#Author:Agnisvāmin
#Text:Lāṭyāyanaśrautasūtrabhāṣya
#Comments:Lāṭyāyanaśrauta
#Edition:Vedāntavāgīśa 1872
#Data entry:Oliver Hellwig
#Notes:Completed: 1-3, 8-10



1.1.2.[1]	tatra mantraśabdaḥ pratītaśabdārthaḥ kartṛpadārthako mahanmevocādiṣu yajaḥṣu varttate /
1.1.2.[2]	vidhīyate vidhānaṃ veti vidhiḥ /
1.1.2.[3]	ādigrahaṇena ādīyate'rtho'neneti ādiḥ /
1.1.2.[4]	ayaṃ sūtrārthaḥ ādigṛhīto mantraḥ kṛtsnaḥ prayoktavya iti /
1.1.2.[5]	atrocyate, yadyevamarthaḥ, satrārambho na karttavyastarhi, ṛtepi etasmādavagamyeta etat, ādigrahīto mantraḥ kṛtsnaḥ prayoktavya iti, paripaṭhitānāmādigṛhīto mantraḥ prayoktavya iti /
1.1.2.[6]	nanu siddhaṃ gṛhyaprāmāṇyādevaitadāmnāyārthatvāt, padārthābhisambandhāccheṣaviśeṣavidhiḥ tadviṣaya iti cet, sthālīpulākavat /
1.1.2.[7]	anyatra yāvadyajurgrahaṇāduttarasūtrārambhācca, gṛhyaprāmāṇyāttāvanmantrāntamavyaktaṃ parasyādigrahaṇena vidyāditi, āmnāyārthatvāditi, yadi hyādigrahītomantraḥ kṛtsno na prayuñjyetāmnāyo narthakaḥ syāt /
1.1.2.[8]	sārthakena cāmnāyena bhavitavyaṃ /
1.1.2.[9]	ataśca gamyate kṛtsnamantraprasaṅga iti /
1.1.2.[10]	padārthābhisambandhādavagamyate kṛtsnamantraprayoga iti /
1.1.2.[11]	iha padānāṃ pāramparyeṇarthopyabhisambandha, tanmāvatvādivat /
1.1.2.[12]	śeṣaviśeṣavidheḥ śeṣe yasmādviśeṣavidhirāgacchati /
1.1.2.[13]	satra eva grahasya bhakṣaye suraindraṁ saha ityudasya harivadaharikāsu cetsuvīranniti, sati kṛtsnamantra prayoge ekadeśoddhāraḥ sambhavati /
1.1.2.[14]	śeṣaviśeṣavidhistadviṣaya eveti, sthālīpulākavat, yathaikenoḍhanasikthena kṛtsnā sthālī parīkṣyā svinnā nasvinneti /
1.1.2.[15]	ekadeśena pulākasthānīyena sthālī sthānīyogranthaḥ kṛtsnaḥ parikṣiṣyata iti /
1.1.2.[16]	anyatra yāvadyajurgrahaṇadyāvadyajuranādiṣṭāntān mantrāniti /
1.1.2.[17]	yāvadyajati samarthantāvat prayoktavyamiti /
1.1.2.[18]	arthavādoddhāraṃ vidadhachāstraṃ kṛtsnamantraprakaraṇaprasaṅgaṃ jñāpayati /
1.1.2.[19]	uttarasūtrārambhācca manyāmahe kṛtsnamantraprakaraṇa prasaṅga iti /
1.1.2.[20]	uttarādiḥ pūrvāntalakṣaṇamiti, uttarasya mantrasyādinā pūrvasya mantrasyāntolakṣyate, sati ca kṛtsnamantraprayoge tallakṣaṇaṃ sambhavati /
1.1.2.[21]	tadevaṃ siddhe kṛtsnamantraprayoge yaducyate mantravidhiścādigrahaṇenetyetadanarthakaṃ, kasmātsūtrārambha, athārabhyate prayojanaṃ vaktavyaṃ, yaducyate sūtrannārabdhavyamārabdhavyamevetyatra brūmaḥ, kasmāt sūtrārambhaḥ asya vidheraprasiddheḥ /
1.1.2.[22]	yattāvaducyate gṛhyaprāmāṇyānnārabdhavyabhityatra brūmaḥ /
1.1.2.[23]	tatrāpyeṣa eva vidhiḥ kṛtsnamantraprayogasya /
1.1.2.[24]	yaduktaṃ āmnāyārthavattvāditi parkādivadetaddraṣṭavyaṃ /
1.1.2.[25]	yathā parkādeḥ simāntasya sāmasamāmnāyasya gavādiṣu sahasrasamvatsarānteṣu na sarvasya prayogodṛṣṭaḥ /
1.1.2.[26]	na ca tāvatā tasyāmnānamanarthakaṃ bhavati padārthābhisambandhāditi yaduktamiti tatra brūmaḥ /
1.1.2.[27]	na hyekasmāt padārthābhisambandhānmantraprayogo bhavati, rūpasampannā api hi śrutyā vidhīyante, taṃ prohedvānaspatyosītivat, durvijñānatyāc ca mantrāṇāṃ na hyeṣu pratyakṣamastyanṛṣṭeratapasā veti /
1.1.2.[28]	śeṣaviśeṣavidhiriti yaducyate, tatra brūmaḥ /
1.1.2.[29]	śeṣaviśeṣavidhistadviṣayopi gamyate /
1.1.2.[30]	sthālī pulākavat tadviṣaya iti yaduktaṃ, anaikāntikoyaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ, vyabhicārakatvāditi, ekenaudanasikthena sthālīna kṛtsnā parīkṣyate, pākavaiṣamyādeva vyabhicāritvādadṛṣṭāntaḥ /
1.1.2.[31]	anyatra yāvadyajurgrahaṇāditi yaduktaṃ, anena vacanena prasakte kṛtsnamantraprayoge ayajati samarthasyoddhārovidhīyate, yadapyuktamuttarasūtrārambhādityetadapi anenaiva pratyuktaṃ /
1.1.2.[32]	evametāni sūtrānārambhakāraṇāni pratyuktāni /
1.1.2.[33]	tatra yaduktamārabdhavyaṃ sūtramiti tadyuktaṃ /
1.1.2.[34]	mantravidhiścādigrahaṇena /
1.1.2.[35]	ayamarthaḥ, ādipradiṣṭomantraḥ kṛtsnaḥ prayoktavya iti /
1.1.2.[36]	atha vidhigrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet, adhikṛta eva vidhirvidhyavyapadeśa iti /
1.1.2.[37]	atrocyate, vidhigrahaṇena tadā etatsubrahmaṇyāmāhūya yajamānaṃ vācayatīti evaṃ trirāhvayeti vidhyādi gṛhyate /
1.1.2.[38]	atha caśabdaḥ kimarthamiti arthādi ca vidhirbhavati idamannamayaṃ rasa imā gāvaḥ sahaśriyeti /
1.1.2.[39]	apara āha, mantravidhiścādigrahaṇeneti yathā yajuḥsamāmnāye mantraḥ paṭhitaḥ tathā prayajyate /
1.1.2.[40]	sammārjane saṃsṛjantvityasya punanvityanena pratyāmnāyomā bhūdairavaditi, mahāntejase brahmavarcasāyeti ca mamāyuṣa ityasya ca pratyāmnāyo mābhūdityata ādigrahaṇenetyāha /
1.1.2.[41]	atha vā caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ /
1.1.2.[42]	ādigrahaṇenāvyapadeśa iti varttate avasṛṣṭatakṣādivat /
1.1.2.[43]	evamuktvārthaṃ sūtraṃ / 2 /
1.1.2.[44]	evaṃ mantravidhiścādigrahaṇeneti siddhe kṛtsnamantraprayoge atha mantrāntaḥ kathaṃ vijñātavya ityatrocyate /
1.1.3.[1]	uttarasya mantrasyādinā pūrvasya mantrasyāntolakṣyate, tallakṣaṇaṃ uttarādiḥ pūrvānta iti /
1.1.3.[2]	siddhe lakṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet, atrocyate/ yadi hyayaṃ lakṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ na kuryāduttarasya mantrasyādiḥ pūrvasya mantrasyāntaḥ syāt, evaṃ pūrvasya mantrasyāntasya uttarasya mantrasya cādeḥ saṃsargaḥ kriyeta, evaṃ mā bhūdityata āha lakṣaṇamiti / 3 /
1.1.3.[3]	iha vṛtapratimantraṇādīni karmāṇyupadekṣyante ekaṃ karttāram adhikṛtya, aviśeṣacoditāśca traya udgātāraḥ /
1.1.3.[4]	yatvityāhurvācānyānṛtvijo vṛṇate kasmādudgātārovṛtā ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti /
1.1.3.[5]	tatredaṃ saṃśete aviśeṣacoditānāṃ sarveṣāṃ prāptau kasyemāni bhavanti, ata āha ācāryaḥ /
1.1.4.[1]	ekavacanaśrutyā ye vidhīyante, ta ekaśrutividhānāḥ mahanmevoca iti kariṣyan pratimantrayetetyevamādyā mantrāḥ /
1.1.4.[2]	karmāṇi ca pṛthaksāvitrīpādairmadhuparkasya pibedityevamādīni udgātaiva kuryādanādeśa iti, ādeśādanyatrānādeśe /
1.1.4.[3]	ādeśaḥ, prastotā havirdhānaṃ gacchet madhyandine huta ādityagrahe pratiharttā bhavati /
1.1.4.[4]	atha vā ekaśrutividhānāddhetoḥ udgātraivoktaḥ ekasya śrutau vidhānaṃ udgātā sāmavedeneti /
1.1.4.[5]	athaivaśabdaḥ kimarthamiti cet, avadhāraṇārthaḥ /
1.1.4.[6]	sāmānyatvādudgātṛśabdasya yasyaivānanyaśabdasaṃyogaḥ sa eva mukhyaḥ /
1.1.4.[7]	anādeśagrahaṇasya prayojanamuktaṃ prathamasūtra eva / 4 /
1.1.4.[8]	utamuttarādiḥ pūrvantalakṣaṇamiti, etallakṣaṇaṃ mahadādīnāṃ yajuṣāṃ utkrāntirasīti paryantānāṃ yeṣu punar idaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ na sambhavati, tām ucchrayatīty evamādivat, teṣāṃ kaḥ prayogaḥ ityatrāha /
1.1.5.[1]	yeṣāṃ mantrāṇām anto nādiśyate tān eva yajuḥ pratīyāt teṣu yāvadeva yajati samarthantāvad eva prayoktavyamiti /
1.1.5.[2]	ye 'rthavādā madhye paṭhitās teṣām uddhāra iti / 5 /
1.1.5.[3]	uktaṃ mantravidhiś cādigrahaṇeneti, tatroktaṃ mahadādiṣu yajuḥṣu mantraśabdosya varttata iti /
1.1.5.[4]	atha ṛksāmnāṃ ko vidhirityatrāha /
1.1.6.[1]	samāmnāye yā ṛk tasyā ṛcaḥ ādigrahaṇena vidhirbhavati /
1.1.6.[2]	avadhūya pavitramudagdaśamavāṅnābhi vitanuyuḥ pavitraṃ ta iti /
1.1.6.[3]	sāmnaśceti ca śabdaḥ, sāmnaścādigrahaṇena vidhirbhavati, adhvaryupreṣitastyagnāyiriti gāyedityādivat /
1.1.6.[4]	ādineti siddhe grahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet, ucyate /
1.1.6.[5]	ādinā ca grahaṇena cetyevamarthaṃ grahaṇaṃ agniṣṭayatītyavabhṛthasāma itivat / 6 /
1.1.6.[6]	iti paribhāṣā /
1.1.6.[7]	uktaṃ karmaṇyudgātaiva kuryādanādeśe, tatrodgātetyukte kiṃ lakṣaṇaṃ punarudgātāraṃ kuryādityucyate /
1.1.6.[8]	tadudgātṛlakṣaṇaṃ vivakṣurācāryaḥ sādhāraṇatvādṛtvigguṇanāṃ sarvartvijo'dhikṛtya lakṣaṇamārabhate /
1.1.7.[1]	ṛtvig iti jātiśabdena /
1.1.7.[2]	ṛtvik, ārṣeyaḥ, anūcānaḥ, sādhucaraṇaḥ, vāgmī, anyūnāṅgaḥ, anatiriktāṅgaḥ, dvayasataśca, anatikṛṣṇaḥ, anatiśvetaḥ, daśapadaṃ sūtraṃ /
1.1.7.[3]	athedānīmarthovakṣyate /
1.1.7.[4]	ṛtvik, ṛtau yajatīti ṛtvik, prajāpatirakāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa ātman vṛttyamapaśyattata ṛtvijo'sṛjata yadṛcyāsṛjata tadṛtvijāmṛtviktvaṃ /
1.1.7.[5]	ṛtvik kasmādīriṇaḥ, ṛgyaṣṭā bhavatīti śākapūrṇiḥ, ṛtuyājī bhavatīti nairuktāḥ /
1.1.7.[6]	ārṣeyaḥ, ṛṣerapatyamārṣeyaḥ, ṛṣidarśanāt stomāndadarśetyaupamanyavaḥ, tadyademāṃstapasyamānān brahma svayaṃ tvabhyānarṣa tadṛṣīṇāmṛṣitvamiti vijñāyate, ādaśamāt puruṣādavyavacchinnaṃ yasya sa yaḥ /
1.1.7.[7]	anūcānaḥ, anūktavānanūcānaḥ śiṣyebhyovidyāsampradānaṃ yaḥ kṛtavān so'nūcānaḥ /
1.1.7.[8]	sādhucaraṇaḥ, sādhviti praśaṃsā, praśastakarmetyarthaḥ, bahu brāhmaṇakarmasvavasthitaḥ /
1.1.7.[9]	vāgmī, vaktuṃ samarthaḥ, atha vā saṃskṛtavāk vāgmī, yohi saṃskṛtāṃ vācamuccārayati sa vāgmī, kaḥ punarvvācaḥ saṃskāraḥ, śabdārthanyāyebhyo'vagamaḥ, yastvevaṃlakṣaṇāṃ vācamuccārayati sa vāgmī, na yo bahutaraṃ vacanamanarthakaṃ bhāṣate taddhi vākchalāyālamityucyate, yohi bahubhāṣaṇaḥ sa na vāgmī vācālo vācāṭa ityucyate, vācogminyālajāracau bahubhāṣiṇīti, sarvathā yaḥ prativacanasamarthaḥ sa vāgmī, yohi pṛṣṭaḥ san nyāyena prativacanaṃ pradadāti, sa vāgmī, matidvaidhe utpanne saṃśayacchettā, udāharaṇaṃ cātra kauṣītakinaḥ, kasmātkauṣītakīnāṃ na kañcanātīva jihīte yajñāvakīrṇāhītyaprativacanadānāt /
1.1.7.[10]	anyūnāṅgaḥ, ūnameva nyūnaṃ na nyūnāṅgaḥ, sa anyūnāṅgaḥ /
1.1.7.[11]	anatiriktāṅgaḥ, aṅgānāṃ cātiriktatā puruṣalakṣaṇe siddhā, tatra coktaṃ, jyotiṣaṃ pūrvaprakṛtamiti, tasya cāṅgaṃ puruṣalakṣaṇaṃ, catuḥṣaṣṭyaṅgatvāt /
1.1.7.[12]	dvayamataśca, pramāṇataśca anyūnaḥ, anatiriktaḥ, pramāṇe pramāṇe dvayaṃ dvayaṃ samaṃ yasya sa dvayamataḥ /
1.1.7.[13]	anyeṣāṃ dve sataśceti pāṭhaḥ /
1.1.7.[14]	teṣāṃ kārikayārtho varṇyate, adhaścorddhvañca nābhestu samoyasmāt pramāṇataḥ /
1.1.7.[15]	pādāṅguṣṭhāṅgaviṣṭabdhaḥ sa vai dvesata ucyate iti /
1.1.7.[16]	anatikṛṣṇaḥ, na atikṛṣṇaḥ anatikṛṣṇaḥ /
1.1.7.[17]	anatiśvetaḥ, na atiśvetaḥ anatiśvetaḥ /
1.1.7.[18]	apare vayasi nipātayanti, kṛṣṇaśvetaśabdo nātibālo nātivṛddha iti evamuktārthaṃ sūtraṃ / 7 /
1.1.7.[19]	ṛtvijāṃ lakṣaṇamuktaṃ, atha yājyaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ syāditi ata āha /
1.1.8.[1]	ārṣeyaḥ anūcānaḥ sādhucaraṇa iti /
1.1.8.[2]	atha vā yājyaśca evaṃ lakṣaṇaḥ yādṛglakṣaṇā ṛtvijaḥ /
1.1.8.[3]	prathamairvā tribhirguṇairvyākhyātaḥ /
1.1.8.[4]	luptavibhāṣaṃ sūtraṃ /
1.1.8.[5]	guṇagrahaṇaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoryathāsambhavaṃ guṇā grāhyāḥ
1.1.9.[1]	sāmprataṃ vidhirvivakṣitaḥ, somaṃ prabrūte, somapravākaḥ, tamakariṣyan karma namaḥ somāya rājña ityetadyajurūktvā pratyākhyānaṃ kuryāt kiñcideva vyākṣepaṃ kṛtvā aparuṣaṃ pratyācakṣīta /
1.1.9.[2]	atha kariṣyata eva, tāvadvidhau vaktavye kasmādakariṣyataḥ pūrvamucyate pratyākhyānamātrasya vaktavyatvādakariṣyataḥ pūrvamuktaṃ, kariṣyato hi vṛtapratimantraṇādiḥ samidādhānāhavanīyopasthānānto vidhirvaktavyaḥ sa ucyate / 8 /
1.1.9.[3]	akariṣyato vidhiruktaḥ atha kariṣyatovidhiṃ vivakṣurāha /
1.1.10.[1]	mahanme voca ityanena yajuṣā kariṣyan pratimantraṇaṃ kuryāt
1.1.11.[1]	tat vṛtapratimantraṇaṃ yajuḥ na jahyāt notsṛjet aprokte 'pi somapravākeṇeti kariṣyāmīti vijñāya /
1.1.11.[2]	kosya viṣayaḥ sādyaktāḥ / 11 /
1.1.11.[3]	atha vṛtapratimantraṇaṃ kṛtvā anantaraṃ somapravāke kiṃ pratipattavyam ityatrāha /
1.1.12.[1]	āvasanti tamityāvasathaḥ somaṃ prabrūte somapravākaḥ, tasmai somapravākāya tādarthye caturtho /
1.1.12.[2]	lavaṇamannaṃ lavaṇena sampṛktamannaṃ lavaṇamannantat dadhnā saha hārayet bhojayet, evaṃ sūtrārthaḥ /
1.1.12.[3]	āvasathaśca somapravākāya karttavyaḥ /
1.1.12.[4]	tatraiva cāsya bhojananneyamiti
1.1.13.[1]	somapravākāyānnaṃ hārayitvāthānantaraṃ prahiṇuyāt prastotṛsubrahmaṇyau purastāt karmabhyaḥ, prahiṇuyāt preṣayedityarthaḥ /
1.1.13.[2]	prastotā ca subrahmaṇyaśca prastotā subrahmaṇyo pūrvaṃ karmaṇa ārambhāt atha vā tādarthye caturthī yāni purastāt karmāṇi tārkṣyasāmādīni tadarthaṃ / 13 /
1.1.13.[3]	uktaṃ prahiṇuyāt prastotṛsubrahmaṇyāviti /
1.1.13.[4]	tayoḥ kamarthaṃ prāgāmanaṃ /
1.1.13.[5]	karmāṇi ca devayajane kriyate /
1.1.13.[6]	ata ācāryo devayajanalakṣaṇaṃ vivakṣurāha /
1.1.14.[1]	prāgudakpravaṇaṃ devajayanaṃ /
1.1.14.[2]	āpaḥ prācya udocyo vā yatra gacchanti /
1.1.14.[3]	athavā prāgudīcīdiśaṃ yatrāpaḥ pravarttante tat prāgudakpravaṇaṃ cātvālasāriṇyo yatrāpaḥ syurityarthaḥ /
1.1.14.[4]	devayajanaṃ devā asminnijyanta iti devayajanaṃ /
1.1.14.[5]	lomaśaṃ, pratilomaśaṃ tṛṇauṣadhibahulamityarthaḥ /
1.1.14.[6]	avṛkṣannāsmin vṛkṣāḥ santyavṛkṣaṃ /
1.1.14.[7]	samaṃ, yatra naviṣamābhūmistatsamaṃ /
1.1.14.[8]	evaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ devayajanaṃ syāt / 14 /
1.1.14.[9]	kiñca /
1.11.15.[1]	purastād iti diṅniyamaḥ kriyate /
1.11.15.[2]	pūrvyapradeśe devayajanasya āpaḥ syuriti ca śabdaḥ kriyate /
1.11.15.[3]	purastān niyamaḥ anyāsu ca dikṣu vipratiṣedha iti /
1.11.15.[4]	asyeti samīpalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī, syuriti svabhāvataḥ syurna kṛtrimā iti / 15 /
1.11.15.[5]	uktaṃ ca svabhāvataḥ syuriti /
1.11.15.[6]	atha punarupapattirna syāt tataḥ kiṃ syāt /
1.11.15.[7]	atrocyate /
1.1.16.[1]	taditi pūrvanirdeśaḥ, tāsāmabhāvaḥ, bhavanaṃ bhāvaḥ, na bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ, apāmabhāve mahāvṛkṣādayaḥ syuḥ /
1.1.16.[2]	mahāṃścāsau vṛkṣaśca mahāvṛkṣaḥ ānmahataḥ samānādhikaraṇajātīyayorityākāraḥ /
1.1.16.[3]	apare varṇayanti udumbara iti /
1.1.16.[4]	prājāpatya udumbaraḥ prajāpatirvāva mahāniti pūrva eva tu sādhīyān /
1.1.16.[5]	mahataḥ samānādhikaraṇa iti /
1.1.16.[6]	udapānaḥ kūpaḥ /
1.1.16.[7]	deśāntaragāmī panthā mahāpathaḥ
1.1.17.[1]	evaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva syāt, na cāsya devayajanasya sthalataraṃ samīpe syāt prātiśāyanikastaraḥ pratyayo devayajanamapi na sthale bhavatītyetaddarśayati /
1.1.17.[2]	sthalataraḥ parvataḥ asyeti sarveṣu kalpeṣu syāt anantarasya vidhirmābhūditi
1.1.18.[1]	na cāsya sthalataramadūre syādityuktaṃ /
1.1.18.[2]	kiñca devayajanapramāṇaṃ cāsya pūrve pradeśe sthitaṃ na syāt
1.1.19.[1]	uktamaviśeṣeṇa devayajanalakṣaṇaṃ /
1.1.19.[2]	athābhicaraṇīyeṣu viśeṣavivakṣurāha /
1.1.19.[3]	viparyasyābhicaraṇīyeṣviti /
1.1.19.[4]	yadidaṃ devayajanalakṣaṇamuktaṃ etadabhicaraṇīyeṣu viparyastaṃ bhavati /
1.1.19.[5]	viparyāsaḥ prātilomyaṃ /
1.1.19.[6]	kiṃ sarvameva viparyastaṃ netyucyate /
1.1.19.[7]	kintarhi, sthalādanyaddevayajanamātrācca/ viparyāse'pi sati naiva sthalataramadūre syāddevayajanamātrañca purastānnaiva syāt
1.1.20.[1]	uta prahiṇuyātprastotṛsubrahmaṇyo purastāt karmabhya iti /
1.1.20.[2]	atha tasya gamanakālaḥ ka iti /
1.1.20.[3]	atrocyate /
1.1.20.[4]	ātmanā gacchet kraye upavasathye punaḥ svayaṃ vrajedanāhūtopi
1.1.21.[1]	atha tasya gamanakriyā ucyate /
1.1.21.[2]	udaṅṅeva tu gṛhebhyaḥ prathamaṃ niṣkrāmet /
1.1.21.[3]	devo devametvityanena yajuṣā /
1.1.21.[4]	athaiva śabdaḥ kimarthaṃ ucyate /
1.1.21.[5]	anyatopi gantavye udaṅṅeva tāvat prathamaṃ prasthānaṃ kuryāt /
1.1.21.[6]	atha tuśabdaḥ kimarthaṃ ucyate /
1.1.21.[7]	anyato dvārepyevaṃ
1.1.22.[1]	dūramadhvanogatvālpevaśiṣṭe vihāya dauskṛtyamityetat yajurjapet /
1.1.22.[2]	vihāya dauṣkṛtyaṃ vrajāmītyasyādhyāhāramapare varṇayanti /
1.1.22.[3]	apare yāvadgrahaṇaṃ kasmādavacanāt
1.1.23.[1]	devayajanagāmī yaḥ panthā tamāpadya ananyagāminaṃ badānāmāsītyetat yajurjapet
1.1.24.[1]	yasyopavasathye'hni āgamanaṃ bhavati sa devayajanamahāvederuttaramantamākramya dakṣiṇamantamīkṣamāṇaḥ pitaro bhūrityetadyajurjapet /
1.1.24.[2]	yasya punaḥ kraye'hni āgamanaṃ bhavati sa patnīsaṃśālāyāṃ vedimākramate mahāvederabhāvāt
1.1.25.[1]	yajuṣāmantaraye 'nvāhārandhānajapyomanyate /
1.1.25.[2]	antarayatyāgaḥ, utsargaḥ /
1.1.25.[3]	anvāharaṇamanvāhāraḥ anutsarga ityarthaḥ /
1.1.25.[4]	kaḥ punar viṣayaḥ /
1.1.25.[5]	sānnipātiko vidhiḥ /
1.1.25.[6]	tatrānujapaḥ alopārthaḥ
1.1.26.[1]	upekṣaṇaṃ varjanam akaraṇam ity arthaḥ /
1.1.26.[2]	evaṃ śāṇḍilyo manyate /
1.1.26.[3]	kasmāt nimittāpāyāt /
1.1.26.[4]	apara āha /
1.1.26.[5]	pitaro bhūr iti kṛtsnaṃ yajuḥ antaritaṃ samāmnāye /
1.1.26.[6]	trayo ha nu vai pitaraḥ avamā ṛrvā kāvyā iti /
1.1.26.[7]	tasyānvāhārandhānaṃjapyo manyate /
1.1.26.[8]	kasmādalopāt /
1.1.26.[9]	upekṣaṇaṃ varjanaṃ śāṇḍilyaḥ kasmādapāṭhāt
1.2.0.[1]	uktaṃ svayaṃ vrajet kraya upavasathyeveti /
1.2.0.[2]	tatra udaṅṅeva tu gṛhebhyaḥ prathamamityudgātṛkarma prakṛtametadādi /
1.2.0.[3]	tatroktamuttaraṃ vedyantamākramya dakṣiṇamīkṣamāṇaḥ pitaro bhūrityetadyajurjapediti /
1.2.0.[4]	asyānantaraṃ madhurpakavidhirvivakṣitaḥ /
1.2.0.[5]	taṃ vivakṣurāha /
1.2.1.[1]	pṛthak nānetyarthaḥ /
1.2.1.[2]	sāvitrīpādaiḥ savitā devatā yasyāḥ seyaṃ sāvitrī tasyāḥ pādaiḥ pibet /
1.2.1.[3]	madhunā pṛktandadhipayaḥkṛtānnaṃ vā madhuparkaḥ /
1.2.1.[4]	dadhani payasi vātha cākṛtānne madhu dadhyānmadhuparkametadāhuḥ /
1.2.1.[5]	dadhimadhuśalileṣu saktavaḥ pṛthageveti vihitāstrayastu manthāḥ /
1.2.1.[6]	tasya madhuparkasya pibet asyeti avayavalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī /
1.2.1.[7]	kathaṃ pibedyathā śeṣaḥ syāditi /
1.2.1.[8]	nanu sāvitrīpādairiti siddhe kiṃ pṛthak grahaṇamiti /
1.2.1.[9]	ucyate /
1.2.1.[10]	uktaṃ, savitṛdevatā sāvitrīti /
1.2.1.[11]	evaṃ sarvāsāṃ savitṛdevatānāṃ prasaṅgaḥ prāptaḥ /
1.2.1.[12]	ata ācāryaḥ pṛthakgrahaṇaṃ karoti /
1.2.1.[13]	yasya ṛksamāmnāye pṛthagāmnānantayeti /
1.2.1.[14]	nanu yadyevamarthaṃ na tasmān mukhyāṃ adya no vedetyetāṃ sāvitrīmutsṛjya gauṇīṃ gṛhṇīyāt /
1.2.1.[15]	tanna, dvayameva mukhyā /
1.2.1.[16]	kathaṃ mukhyeti cet /
1.2.1.[17]	ucyate /
1.2.1.[18]	athopasīdatyabhidhīhi bhoḥ sāvitroṃ me bhavānanubravītviti /
1.2.1.[19]	asminnetasyā evānuvacanaṃ /
1.2.1.[20]	tasyā uttarā ṛksamāmnāyābhivyakteśca sāvitrī caturthī bhavatītyetasyā eva śrutau vidhānaṃ /
1.2.1.[21]	tathā śākhāntarīyāyāmathāvaśiṣṭāyāṃ śrutau etāmeva pratijānate /
1.2.1.[22]	tasmāt pṛthakgrahaṇaṃ nānārthatvādevamuktaṃ
1.2.2.[1]	tatra tasmin madhuparkavidhau etadānayanti /
1.2.2.[2]	viṣṭarādyāharaṇakarma kartavvaniyamārthaṃ bahuvacanaṃ /
1.2.2.[3]	darbhāsanaṃ viṣṭaraḥ /
1.2.2.[4]	pādaprakṣālanārthaṃ udakaṃ pādaprakṣālanaṃ /
1.2.2.[5]	arghārtham udakamarghyaṃ /
1.2.2.[6]	ācamanārtham udakam ācamanīyaṃ /
1.2.2.[7]	madhuparka uktalakṣaṇaḥ /
1.2.2.[8]	atha tatra grahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet /
1.2.2.[9]	ucyate, madhumanthodamanthayor madhuparkakalpārthaṃ /
1.2.2.[10]	te ca vakṣyante /
1.2.2.[11]	tatra tatraitadāharanti viṣṭarādi
1.2.3.[1]	tasya madhuparkasya pibet /
1.2.3.[2]	kathaṃ
1.2.4.[1]	sāvitrīpādasyeti śeṣaḥ /
1.2.4.[2]	tuśabdo viśeṣaṇārthaḥ
1.2.5.[1]	sāvitrīpādasyopariṣṭāditi varttate /
1.2.5.[2]	prathamadvitīyatṛtīyagrahaṇaṃ caturthaniṣedhārthaṃ /
1.2.5.[3]	tūṣṇīṃ caturthamiti prāpte
1.2.6.[1]	sarve bhakṣamantrāḥ svāhākārāntāḥ /
1.2.6.[2]	svāhākārāntā iti bahuvacanāt siddheḥ kimarthaṃ sarvagrahaṇamiti cet ucyate /
1.2.6.[3]	madhumanthādīnāmapi bhakṣamantrāḥ svāhākārāntāḥ syurityevamarthaṃ sarvagrahaṇaṃ
1.2.7.[1]	rasosi vānaspatya iti /
1.2.7.[2]	anena mantreṇa madhumanthasya pibediti gautama ācārya āha /
1.2.7.[3]	yaccoktaṃ viṣṭarādīni dravyāṇyekaikaśastristrirvedayeranniti, tatra madhumanthasyāvedane prāpte /
1.2.7.[4]	vānaspatya iti pravacanamiti /
1.2.7.[5]	vānaspatyo vānaspatya ityāvedanantriḥ
1.2.8.[1]	yathā madhumanthasya tathā dadhimanthodamanthayoḥ pibet /
1.2.8.[2]	tena prakāreṇetyarthaḥ /
1.2.8.[3]	ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ /
1.2.8.[4]	payasyopayasya iti tu rasādeśaḥ /
1.2.8.[5]	vānaspatya ityetasya sthāne syātāmityarthaḥ /

1.2.9.[2]	payasyopayasya iti /
1.2.9.[3]	kālindaḥ sārasvata iti vā, yāthāsaṅkhyena

1.2.11.[1]	śūdravarjaṃ /

1.2.12.[1]	uktaṃ ācāntodakāya gauriti nāpitastrirbrūyāt /

1.2.13.[1]	kuruteti brūyādevaṃ vā
1.2.14.[1]	udgātṛkarmoktaṃ /
1.2.14.[2]	atha sarveṣāṃ sādhāraṇamucyate /
1.2.14.[3]	sarveṣāmudgātṛṇāṃ yajñopavītañca udakācamanañca ete ca nitye karma kurvatāṃ evaṃ yajñopavītī bhavatyevamācāntodako bhavatīti /
1.2.14.[4]	yajñopavītañca udakapūrṇañca kamaṇḍalu /
1.2.14.[5]	ācamanti tasmādityācamanaṃ /

1.2.14.[9]	subrahmaṇyaṃ caturthānāṃ brahmapañcamānāṃ yajamānaṣaṣṭhānāṃ sambandhastadarthaṃ grahaṇaṃ
1.2.15.[1]	na vyavāyaḥ avyavāyaḥ, na vyāvṛttiḥ avyāvṛttiḥ, antarāgamanaṃ vyavāyaḥ, anabhimukhatā vyāvṛttiḥ /
1.2.15.[2]	kenāvyavāyo'vyāvṛttiśca yajñāṅgaiḥ karmopayatāmiti varttate
1.2.16.[1]	prāṅmukhakaraṇamādeśādanyatra syāt, ādeśaḥ pratyaṅmukhastiṣṭhaṃśchirasi gāyatraṅgāyediti /
1.2.16.[2]	caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ, avyavāyo'vyāvṛttiśca yajñāṅgairanādeśa iti
1.2.17.[1]	uktaṃ prahiṇuyāt prastotṛsubrahmaṇyai purastātkarmabhya iti /
1.2.17.[2]	tatra subrahmaṇyaṃ karma vivakṣuridaṃ sūtramārabhate, krīte rājani subrahmaṇya iti /
1.2.17.[3]	atha kasmāt karmabhedaḥ kriyate, prastotrīyaṃ tāvadvaktavyaṃ pūrvvaṃ tārkṣyasāmādīnāmityatrāha kṛtākṛtatvāt tārkṣyasāmādīnāṃ kramabheda iti /
1.2.17.[4]	krīte rājani krīte some, subrahmaṇya iti kartṛnirdeśaḥ uttareṇa somavahanaṃ gatvā uttareṇeti diṅniyamaḥ, gatveti kriyopadeśaḥ /
1.2.17.[5]	antareṇeṣe somavahaneṣayorantarāle śamīśākhāṃ palāśaśākhāṃ vā sapalāśāṃ dakṣiṇena pāṇinā gṛhītvāvatiṣṭheta
1.2.18.[1]	saṃpreṣaṇaṃ saṃpreṣaḥ tam ākāṅkṣet tāvatpratīkṣeta yāvat saṃpreṣaṇamiti sarvatra grahaṇaṃ sarvāsu subrahmaṇyāsu na kevalaṃ śākaśvyāmiti
1.2.19.[1]	raśmī abhīśū pragrahāvityarthaḥ dhārayan savyena pāṇinā śākhayā dakṣiṇena pāṇinā gṛhītayā prasthāpayet gāvau somavahanayuktau dakṣiṇaṃ pūrvam, dakṣiṇasyāṃ dhuri yo yuktasta pūrvaṃ paścāduttaramityarthaḥ
1.2.20.[1]	prāṅmukhe varttamāne subrahmaṇyomiti praṇavaṃ trirbrūyāt, varttatirgatyarthaḥ
1.2.21.[1]	pratyaṅmukhe varttamāne ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ praṇavaṃ brūyāditi varttate
1.2.22.[1]	patnīśālāyāḥ pūrvapradeśe vimukte arddhavimukte sati chadiṣi cchādanakaṭe śākhām avaguhya avalambya tāmevaiṣāmanūtkramya avatīryya tato yathārthaṃ syāditi karmaṇaḥ samāptiṃ darśayati
1.2.23.[1]	dakṣiṇasyāṃ dhuri yo yukto'navān taṃ subrahmaṇyāya dadyāt yajamānaḥ sāmarthyāt
1.2.24.[1]	ubhāvaṣyanaḍvāhau deyāviti śāṭyāyanake śrutiḥ karmasaṃyogāt ubhābhyāṃ hi karma kṛtaṃ hetūpādānaṃ kriyate karmayogāditi yasya yena karmasaṃyogaḥ sa taddravyaṃ labhatityarthaḥ /
1.2.24.[2]	yasmin karmaṇi yaddravyaṃ yasya sannihitaṃ bhavet /
1.2.24.[3]	tattasyaiva pradātavyaṃ hoturgotrapaṭo yathā
1.3.1.[1]	uktā śākaṭī subrahmaṇyā subrahmaṇyomiti trirāhvayet prāci vartamāne ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ pratīcīti praṇavamātrakriyoktā idānīṃ tasyāḥ kāladeśakriyāvidhayo vivakṣitāḥ, tān vivakṣurācārya idaṃ sūtramārabhate, ātithyāyāṃ saṃsthitāyāmiti /
1.3.1.[2]	ātithyā iṣṭiḥ tasyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ samāptāyāmityarthaḥ dakṣiṇasya dvārabāhoḥ patnīśālāyāḥ pūrve pradeśe tiṣṭhan /
1.3.1.[3]	kathaṃ gamyate patnīśālāyā dvārasyeti ucyate, sambandhādātithyāyāṃ saṃsthitāyāmiti pūrveṇa patnīśālāyāṃ tiṣṭhannityūrddhvatā vidhīyate /
1.3.1.[4]	antarvedideśe prakṛtaṃ vedikaraṇaṃ bhavatyato deśa ityāha /
1.3.1.[5]	anvārabdhe yajamāne patnyāñca, anvārambhaṅaṃ sparśanam, saptamī kriyate yasya ca bhāvena bhāvalakṣaṇamiti samāsaḥ kramārthaḥ /
1.3.1.[6]	subrahmaṇyomiti triḥ praṇavamuktvā nigadaṃ brūyāt /
1.3.1.[7]	indrāgacchetyetadādinigadagrahaṇaṃ saṃvyavahārārtham vakṣyatyagniṣṭutvāgneyo nigada iti /
1.3.1.[8]	etāvadahe sutyāmiti yāvadahe syāditi etāvadityatra sutyā nirdeśyā yāvadbhirahobhiḥ sutyā, tāvadbhiḥ parigaṇanāṃ kṛtvā nirdeśaḥ kāryyaḥ
1.3.2.[1]	yasminnahani sutyā bhavati tasminnahany adyeti brūyāt, samānāhanīti kimarthamadyeti sutyāmiti siddheḥ, ucyate, kadāpyekasminnahani kṛtsnaṃ karma kriyate, tasminnapi adya sutyetyevaṃ brūyāt, ko'sya viṣayaḥ /
1.3.2.[2]	sādyaktāḥ
1.3.3.[1]	sutyādeśānantarametadbrūyāt ityevaṃ gautama ācāryya āha
1.3.4.[1]	evaṃ dhānañjaya ācāryo manyate
1.3.5.[1]	eke ācāryyaḥ pūrvaṃ devāhvānānmanyante
1.3.6.[1]	avasyādityarthaḥ, virāmo'vasānam
1.3.7.[1]	etayośca padayorviramet
1.3.8.[1]	āgneyyāṃ subrahmaṇyāyāṃ etau ca virāmau ṣaṇṇe jāre ceti
1.3.9.[1]	viramediti vartate pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ, yajate śabdeṣu ceti ukte kiṃ pṛthaggrahaṇamiti cet ucyate, pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahaśabdānāṃ ca samāmo mābhūditi
1.3.10.[1]	anena prakāreṇa triḥ kriyā subrahmaṇyāyāḥ
1.3.11.[1]	āhūyeti vidhigṛhyate, evaṃ trirāhūya yajamānaṃ vācayati
1.3.12.[1]	patnī ca yajamānaśca patnīyajamānau tāvupavahavaṃ kāmamāṇau subrahmaṇyophvayasvetyevaṃ brūyātāṃ upahvānamupahavaḥ
1.3.13.[1]	subrahmaṇyo yācita upahavaṃ dadyāt, kaḥ punarupahavaḥ upahūta ityupahavaḥ ayamupahavaprakāraḥ
1.3.14.[1]	ṛjyarthaḥ
1.3.15.[1]	bahuvacanasāmarthyāt tatsiddheḥ sarvagrahaṇaṃ nirarthakamiti cet tat kathaṃ pratīṣṭiṣu syāditi upasadgrahaṇādiṣṭidvaye upasatpratyayo mābhūditi
1.3.16.[1]	yāścorddhvamupasadadbhyaścādekṣyanta subrahmaṇyāstāsāmapyeṣa eva vidhiḥ ayantu viśeṣaḥ, utkare tu tatra tiṣṭhanniti, tiṣṭhanniti vaktavye tatra grahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate, mābhūt samīpasaptamī pratyaya iti ārūḍhe notkare vaktavyā /
1.3.16.[2]	apara āha utkare cāha tatra tiṣṭhanniti hi brāhmaṇaṃ tasmādutkare tiṣṭhan subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyāmāhvayatīti
1.3.17.[1]	evaṃ caitā utkare bhavanti kiñca prāk sutyādeśānnāmagrāho bhavati etāvadahe sutyāmiti prāgasmādvacanāt
1.3.18.[1]	agnīṣomīyasya paśorvapāyāṃ hutāyāṃ vasatīvarī pariharaṇe kṛte prātaranuvākasya ārambhaṇavelāyāṃ yajamānanāmadheyāni gṛhṇīyāt pratyekam ekamekaṃ prati pratyekam asāviti sarvvanāmnā yajamānasya nāmadheyāni yajamānanāmadheyānīti bahuvacanaṃ kriyate tatsambandhena sarvāṇyetāni pitṛprabhṛtīni yajamānanāmadheyāni /
1.3.18.[2]	apara āha nakṣatrāśca yaṃ nityaṃ tṛtīyaṃ yattadguhyameva bhavati /
1.3.18.[3]	sarvanāmnaḥ sthāne pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānāṃ nāmadheyāni gṛhṇīyāt amuṣya putraḥ pautro napteti yathāsaṃkhyam /
1.3.18.[4]	yathāmuṣya putraḥ pautro naptetyeteṣāṃ pūrvatve siddhe pūrveṣāmiti kimarthamārabhyate, ucyate, ekaśeṣavidhiprajñāpanārthaṃ, kathamekaśedho gṛhyata iti pūrveṣāṃ ca pūrvāsāṃ ca
1.3.19.[1]	athānantaramavareṣāṃ nāmāni gṛhṇīyāt avare putrapautraprapautrāḥ kathametadgamyate teṣāmapi trayāṇāmeveti athaśabdasāmarthyāt yathājyeṣṭham yo jyeṣṭhaḥ yathājyeṣṭham utpattikramataḥ kimaviśeṣeṇa na jīveyuḥ
1.3.20.[1]	janiṣyamāṇānāmiti siddhe uteti kimarthamārabhyate, ucyate, pṛthagyajate śabdeṣu ca viramedityuktam tadihāpi prāptaṃ tannivṛttyartham ucyate samāsena pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahaśabdaṃ kṛtvā yajata iti brūyāt
1.3.21.[1]	yāgnīṣomīyavapā homānantarakālā subrahmaṇyā sā sādyaḥkteṣu luptā lopaḥ kriyate, atha sāmarthyādeva lope prāpte nimittāpāye naimittikasyāpyapāya iti sūtraṃ kimarthamārabhyate, atrocyate, tisraḥ sanniyogaśiṣṭāḥ sanāmagrāhāḥ tāsāṃ sanniyogaśiṣṭānāṃ satīnāṃ pūrvasyāḥ lope uttarayorapi lopo gamyate /
1.3.21.[2]	sanniyogaśiṣṭānāmanyatamāpāye'pāya iti, apara āha pratinidhau mābhūditi, sādyaḥkteṣvagnīṣomīyasya paśoḥ sthāne agnīṣomīyaṃ puroḍāśaṃ nirvapatīti, athoddeśanirdeśau kimarthamiti cet, atrocyate, sūtrakārasyāyamabhiprāyaḥ saiva luptā /
1.3.21.[3]	anyatra nimittāpāye'pi naimittikāni bhavantīti /
1.3.21.[4]	yathā santatiṣvaprastāvāsvapi kuśāvidhānamiti
1.4.1.[1]	subrahmaṇyāyāḥ sārvakratuko vidhiruktaḥ, sāmprataṃ viśeṣo vivakṣitastaṃ vivakṣurācārya āha, agniṣṭutsvāgneyo nigada iti /
1.4.1.[2]	agniṣṭutsu yajñeṣu āgneyo nigado bhavati agnirdevatā asyetyāgneyaḥ, nigadaśca uktalakṣaṇaḥ agniṣṭutsvāgneyeti vaktavye nigada iti kathaṃ nigadasyaiva pratyāmnānaṃ syānnetarasyeti
1.4.2.[1]	tatra tasminnityarthaḥ /
1.4.2.[2]	gautamasyedaṃ gautamīyam /
1.4.2.[3]	agna āgacchetyetadādirnigadaḥ /
1.4.2.[4]	prāk sutyādeśāt etāvadahe sutyāmiti prāgasmāt
1.4.3.[1]	devānāṃ sthāne agnaya iti brūyāt
1.4.4.[1]	athaśabda ānantarye gautamīyo vidhiruktaḥ, āgneyī ca subrahmaṇyoktā /
1.4.4.[2]	tatrāyaṃ dhānañjapyokto viśeṣaḥ agna āgaccha rohitava ityetadādiḥ prāk sutyādeśāditi vartate, kiñca
1.4.5.[1]	āgneyī subrahmaṇyoktā /
1.4.5.[2]	sāmprataṃ anirukta ucyate, śakrāgaccheti viśve brahmāṇa ityevaṃ brūyāt, anirukteṣu upahavyādiṣu /
1.4.5.[3]	āniruktyaṃ devatānāmadheyaṃ pārokṣyam
1.4.6.[1]	evam eva subrahmaṇyā syāt, aniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ yasya so'niruktaprātaḥsavanaḥ aniruktaprātaḥsavanaścāniruktaprātaḥsavanacāniruktaprātaḥsavanau tayoraniruktaprātaḥsavanayoḥ kathaṃ punargamyate, yathāyaṃ bahuvrīhiḥ samāsaḥ /
1.4.6.[2]	atha punarayaṃ tatpuruṣaḥ kalpeteti /
1.4.6.[3]	yadi hyayaṃ bahuvrīhirabhaviṣyat muktasaṃśayameva sūtramabhaviṣyat /
1.4.6.[4]	aniruktāpūrvavājapeyeṣviti /
1.4.6.[5]	evaṃ kriyamāṇe evaṃ sūtram abhaviṣyat /
1.4.6.[6]	samāse ca saṃśayo nābhaviṣyat /
1.4.6.[7]	yena punarayaṃ pṛthaksūtramārabhyate, aniruktaprātaḥsavanayośceti jñāpayati tatpuruṣaḥ samāsa iti aniruktañca tat prātaḥsavanaṃ cāniruktaprātaḥsavanamiti /
1.4.6.[8]	tenāpūrvavājapeyayoḥ prātaranuvākopakramaṇakālaiva subrahmaṇyā niruktā syāditi ucyate, na ṛtusambandha evāyaṃ gṛhyatāṃ taducyate muktasaṃśayaṃ sūtramabhaviṣyat evaṃ cet aniruktāpūrvavājapeyeṣviti evaṃ kriyamāṇe sūtra ityatra brūmaḥ, yadyevaṃ sūtramabhaviṣyat, vājapeyavicārāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ prasaṅgo'bhaviṣyadevaṃ mābhūdityata āha, aniruktaprātaḥsavanayośceti
1.4.7.[1]	abhiṣecanīyaśca daśapeyaśca abhiṣecanīyadaśapeyau tāvantareṇa yāḥ subrahmaṇyāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ sanāmagrāhāḥ antarāntareṇa yukta iti dvitīyā bhavati /
1.4.7.[2]	sadāgrahaṇaṃ matrādyapekṣyam, apare bruvate nāmagrahaṇamātramevāstviti na nigadaḥ
1.4.8.[1]	dvirātraprabhṛtiṣvahargaṇeṣu ahnaḥ ādau cānte cāhvayet /
1.4.8.[2]	atha kimarthamidamārabhyate, vidyamāne āhvānanimitte pratyahaṃ vastīvarīpariharaṇe prātaranuvāke ca /
1.4.8.[3]	ucyate, vakṣyatyayam ekāṣṭakādīkṣiṇa upasarginaste tūṣṇīmekatriṃśamaharāsīran savanavidhena vā paśunā yajeranniti, yatrāpi kathaṃ syāditi
1.4.9.[1]	yā ahnaḥ ante subrahmaṇyā sottarārthā, uttarārthamahargaṇeṣvaharādyantayorāhvayediti /
1.4.9.[2]	atrātirātrānte prāptā tatpratisedhārthamārabhyate, uttarārthā harantikīti
1.4.10.[1]	agnīṣomīyādi yatkarma ahīneṣu tasmin yāḥ subrahmaṇyāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ sanāmagrāhāḥ syuḥ /
1.4.10.[2]	nanu agnīṣomīyaprabhṛtayaḥ sanāmagrāhā eva bhavanti, tat kimidam agnīṣomīyaprabhṛtītyārabhyate, ucyate, vakṣyatyayaṃ sarvāḥ sanāmagrāhā iti /
1.4.10.[3]	yadyayamagnīṣomīyaprabhṛtīti na brūyāt, tadā śākaṭyā ārabhya sarvāḥ sanāmagrāhāḥ syuḥ, sarvā iti vacanāt, na hi tadasti yadvacanānna bhavati /
1.4.10.[4]	vacanasyātibhāro nāsti vacanamupalabdhuṃ śakyate /
1.4.10.[5]	athāhīnagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet, aikāhiko vidhiruktaḥ /
1.4.10.[6]	sātriko vacyate, dīkṣānupūrveṇa dīkṣitānāṃ satreṣu nāmagrāha ityata ārabhya tadevamubhayatrokte viśeṣa ucyamānaḥ pratyākhyāyāhīnādanyatra na syāt /
1.4.10.[7]	tathā ca sūtre uktam, ekāhāhīnasatrāṇīti caturthī somajātirnāsti /
1.4.10.[8]	ata eva siddhe'hīnagrahaṇaṃ na kartavyam, kriyamāṇe kāraṇaṃ vaktavyam /
1.4.10.[9]	ucyate, kartavyamahīnagrahaṇam, akriyamāṇe mukhyāhīnaśabdo gṛhyate ye'hīnakāṇḍe paṭhitāsta eva gṛhyeran mukhyatvāt gauṇamukhyayormukhye sampratyaya iti kṛtvā so'yamācāryo'hīnagrahaṇaṃ karoti /
1.4.10.[10]	ye'pyahīnakāṇḍe na paripaṭhitāḥ /
1.4.10.[11]	yathā varuṇapraghāsadvidivasākamedhatryahavyuṣṭirdvirātra iti /
1.4.10.[12]	dvādaśāhīnaścāhīnabhūtaḥ katham eteṣu sarveṣu eṣa vidhiḥ syādityato'rthamahīnagrahaṇam
1.8.13.[1]	yadi viśvarūpā gāyet tataḥ jyotīṃṣyapi gāyet, nanu kimarthaṃ punarayaṃ yadyarthaḥ kriyate cediti yadā viśvarūpāṇāṃ gānaṃ yatnena pratiṣṭhāpitamiti ucyate, ayaṃ hyācāryo vacyati etaṃ parikramaṃ sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi, tad viśvarūpāṇaṃ gānaṃ sarvakratuṣu prāpnoti so 'yamācāryyaḥ jyotiṣṭomādanyatra viśvarūpāṇaṃ gānaṃ jñāpayati kathaṃ etat viśvarūpāṇaṃ gānaṃ jyotiṣṭoma eva pravarttate nānyatreti nanu vakṣyatyācāryo na cānyatra viśvarūpāt jyotiṣṭomāditi satyametat asya tu punarvacanasya tatraiva prayojanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ kaḥ punarjyotirganasya kālo gānavidhiśceti
1.8.14.[1]	parihite samāpte prātaranuvāke paridhānīyāyāṃ śastāyāmityarthaḥ aponaptrīyaṃ nāma śastaṃ tasmātpūrvaṃ purā viramyatāṃ tāvadityuktvā āgrayaṇasya vānuhiṅkāraṃ āgrayaṇo grahaḥ tasya gṛhītasya hiṃkārasya paścāt āgrayaṇaṃ gṛhannadhvaryurhiṃkaroti pavitraṃ dhārayan pavitraṃ vigṛhṇanti hastakāryyameva tad yajñasya kriyata iti āstāvaṃ vā prāpya purā bahiṣpavamānasya stomayogāt etatkālatrayamupadiṣṭaṃ jyotirgānasya vikalpena agnirjyotirjyotiragnirityeteṣu yathāsūtriteṣu padeṣu ekaikasmin pade tristrirgāyatraṃ gāyet abhyasyābhyasya abhyāsam
1.11.1.[1]	grahagrahaṇādhikāro varttate, gṛhīteṣu sarveṣu graheṣu dhruvo gṛhyate tatrodgātṛsambandhaṃ kañcidvivakṣurāha, uttarāddhavirddhānāditi havirddhānasaṃjñake dve anasī dakṣiṇaṃ uttarañca tatrottarāddhavirddhānāditi apādānalakṣaṇā pañcamī havirasminnidhīyata iti havirddhānam dhruvo nāma grahaḥ sthālyāṃ gṛhyate tāṃ dhruvasthālīṃ harantaḥ udgātṛṇāṃ paścimena pradeśena hṛtvā gṛhīte some tenaiva punarnayeyuḥ avyavāyārthaṃ nityaṃ parakartṛkeṣu bahuvacanaṃ nainānapareṇa hareyurapi hyakuśalā adhvaryavo bhavantīti
1.11.2.[1]	havirdhānāt niṣkrāmantam adhvaryuṃ prastotā santanuyāt uttarīyaikadeśe gṛhṇīyāt avichedārtham
1.11.3.[1]	taṃ prastotāraṃ udgātā santanuyāt
1.11.4.[1]	santanuyāditi varttate
1.11.5.[1]	taṃ pratiharttāraṃ brahmā santanuyāt
1.11.6.[1]	santanuyāditi varttate vicchede hi prāyaścittaśravaṇātsarve santatā bhavanti
1.11.7.[1]	sāmpratameteṣāmājyahomo vakṣyate taiśca somaḥ pūyamānaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ ata āha na rājānamālabhyānupaspṛśyāpa ājyamālabheranniti
1.11.8.[1]	tathājyam ālabhyānupaspṛśyāpaḥ somaṃ nālabheran sarvaśabdaḥ ṛte 'pyājyālambhāt anupaspṛśyāpo naiva somamālabheran
1.11.9.[1]	adhvaryuṇā hute pravṛttahomau juhuyuḥ pravṛttahomāviti saṃjñā gatyānupūrvyeṇāpi prastotā prathamo 'tisarpet tata udgātā tataḥ pratihartteti gatyānupūrvye bekurānāmāsīti prathamāṃ sūryometi dvitīyāṃ atha gatyānupūrvyeti kimidaṃ yāvatā ihāpyānupūryamuktam evaṃ adhvaryuṃ nikrāmantaṃ prastotā santanuyāttamudgātodgātāraṃ pratihartteti home 'pyetadevānupūryaṃ grahīṣyate vyatikramahetvasambhavāt atrocyate, gatyārambheṇa anyo'pi yo homaḥ tatrāpi gatyānupūrvyameva syāt yathā āgnidhrīye dve āhutī juhuyuriti
1.11.10.[1]	yadi somau saṃsutau syātāmityevamadhikṛtyāha, susamiddhe hotavyamagnirvai sarvā devatāḥ sarvā eva devatāḥ paśyan juhoti saṃveśāyopaveśāyeti chandodevatyāstisra āhutayaśca ucyante tāsāṃ kālo vivakṣitaḥ hotā ca ata āha, saṃsutasome tu pravṛttahomau hutvā adhikāmāhutimudgātā juhuyāt saṃveśāyopaveśāyeti yathāsavanaṃ chandāṃsyādiśan yatra yasmin savane yathāsavanam tuśabdaḥ chandoviśeṣaṇārthaḥ adhikagrahaṇaṃ pravṛttahomayoḥ pratyāmnāyo mābhūditi
1.11.11.[1]	ṛcaṃ sometyetayarcā svāhākārāntayā tṛtīyāmāhutiṃ juhuyāt udgātā sarvatra saṃsutasome ca sa evodgātā juhuyāt netarau tṛtīyāmāhu̍tim
1.11.12.[1]	mahāgiriḥ mahān parvataḥ mahānadī mahatī nadī rathāhaḥ rathasyāhnāgamaḥ vāyurdevatāviśeṣaḥ etairvyavāye asaṃsavaḥ saṃsavo na bhavati pūrvapaścimavātairvāyuvyavāyo gṛhyate anyathā sarvadā sambhavāt vyavāyaśabdaḥ pratyekamabhisambadhyate
1.11.13.[1]	pṛthagjanapade tu punaḥ punaravyavāye'pi mahāgiryādibhiḥ saṃsavo na bhavati pṛthagjanapadaḥ pañcālāḥ kuravaḥ matsyā iti
1.11.14.[1]	avidviṣāṇamātrādevāsaṃsava ityeke ācāryā manyante
1.11.15.[1]	yadā sarvairhutaṃ bhavati atha brahmāhaṃ gāyatrīṃ vācamityetadyajurjapeyuḥ
1.11.16.[1]	yathādhvaryurāvartteta tathaiva āvartteran avyavāyo'vyāvṛttī nādriyeransarpanta ityārabhyate, uttarayorapi savanayorevameva syāditi
1.11.17.[1]	kiñcidgatvā savyairvāmaiḥ pāṇibhistaiḥ pṛthaṅnānā dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi tṛṇāni nirasyeyuḥ nirāśaḥ prakṣepaḥ yo'dya saumya ityanena yajuṣā
1.11.18.[1]	cātvālasannikṛṣṭo deśaḥ taṃ prāpyādhvaryāvupaviṣṭe tasmādadhvaryoḥ paścime deśe upaviśeyuryoma ātmetyetadādinā yajuṣā
1.11.19.[1]	prastotā pratyaṅmukha upaviśet
1.11.20.[1]	prastotaryupaviṣṭe anantaramudgātā udaṅmukha upaviśet
1.11.21.[1]	udgātāramupaviṣṭaṃ paścimena gatvā pratihartā dakṣiṇapūrvamaṣṭamadigbhāgamīkṣamāṇaḥ upaviśet
1.11.22.[1]	savyān vāmānupasthān ūrūn adharān kṛtvā dyauśca pṛthivī ca dyāvāpṛthivyau tayoḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ sandhimīkṣamāṇaḥ samāni mukhāni dhārayantaḥ manaḥsamādhyartham
1.11.23.[1]	yo'yaṃ vidhiruktaḥ pratyaṅmukhaḥ prastotetyata ārabhya samāni mukhāni dhārayanta iti yāvat naiṣa bahiṣpavamānamadhikṛtyoktaḥ ataḥ sarvastrotreṣu bhavati kuta etat yasmādvakṣyatyetatsarvaṃ kuryāduttarayoḥ pavamānayoriti ata āhevaṃ sarvastotreṣvāsīranniti, nanu yadyevaṃ sarvagrahaṇaṃ na kāryaṁ evaṃ stotreṣvāsīranniti siddheḥ uccate, vakṣyati hi evaṃ parikramaṃ sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi pāṭhāntare caiṣa jyotiḥ sarve kāmā iti evaṃ jyotiṣaṃ darśayati evaṃ parikramaṃ sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi jyotiṣaṃ sarvakratuṣu vidhyantaraṃ darśayati vakṣyati ca tadanantaraṃ ṣoḍaśī sāmnā stoṣyamāṇa iti trisaṃsthe'pi jyotiṣṭome prakṛtibhūte ṣoḍaśī nāsti atra ṣoḍaśinyeṣa vidhirna prāpnoti aprākṛtatvāt vikṛtaḥ ṣoḍaśī tathā mānasādiṣu naimittikeṣu ca na prāpnoti ata āha sarvastotreṣvāsīranniti
1.11.24.[1]	udgātṝṇāṃ paścime pradeśe avarārddhyā upagāḥ syuḥ avarārddhyaśabdaḥ nikṛṣṭavacanaḥ trayāṇāmapyadho na bhavantītyarthaḥ
1.11.25.[1]	eke caturavarārdyānmanyante na tasyopadeśaḥ digbhirevodgāyantīti atha parārddhyāḥ kiyanta upagātāra iti ṣaṭ parārddhyā iti
1.11.26.[1]	yadi tryavarārddhyā yadi caturavarārddhyā yadi ṣaṭparārddhyāḥ ta etenākṣareṇopagāyeyurho iti mandrasvareṇa santatam avichinnaṃ yānyudgātṝṇāṃ sahavācyāni teṣu virameyurupagātāraḥ sahavācyāni nidhanāni atha upagāyeyurho iti siddheḥ etenākṣareṇeti kimarthamārabhyate ucyate, sūtrāntaramārabhate api copagātṝṇaṃ bhaktimudgātāra eva kuryuriti etasmin kalpe'pyetenaivākṣareṇeti
1.11.27.[1]	tasmāt mandrāt vyantareṇotkṛṣṭenodgātāraḥ stuyuḥ svare svare saptayavāntarāṇītyantaraparimāṇaṃ tasmāt tryantareṇa stuyuḥ
1.11.28.[1]	upagātṛsvaratulyena vā prātaḥsavane stuyuḥ mandreṇetyarthaḥ
1.11.29.[1]	mandrād ekāntareṇa vā stuyuḥ
1.12.1.[1]	uktamevaṃ sarvastotreṣvāsīranniti anantaramadhvaryuḥ prastaraṃ prastotre prayacchati somaḥ pavata ityanena yajuṣā tataḥ paraṃ adhvaryoḥ sakāśāt pratigṛhya prastotā brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstarityanena yajuṣā udgātre prayachet prastaramiti karmaṇi dvitīyā pratigṛhyeti dīyamānaṃ gṛhītvā prastoteti kartṛnirdeśaḥ prayachediti kriyopadeśaḥ prastaro darbhamuṣṭiḥ uktam adhvaryuḥ prastaraṃ haratīti tasmādadhvaryuṇā prastara īṣadiva vidhūyo vidhūtamiva hi tṛṇampaśava upāvarttanta iti
1.12.2.[1]	etena prastareṇa udgātā dakṣiṇāṃ jaṅghāṃ spṛṣṭvā yuñjyāt stomamagnestejaseti etadādinā yajuṣā prastaramāsādyogāyeddhaviṣo'skandāya yajamānaṃ tu svargalokādavagṛhṇātītyuktvāha aṣṭhīvato'paspṛśatodgeyantenāsya haviraskannaṃ bhavati na yajamānaṃ svargalokādavagṛhṇātītyataḥ sūtrakāraḥ tena dakṣiṇāṃ jaṅghāmupahatyetyāha
1.12.3.[1]	yuktvā stomamanantaram annaṃ kariṣyāmītyetadādi yajurjapet
1.12.4.[1]	tūṣṇīṃ amantrakamityarthaḥ sarve udgātāraḥ tūṣṇīñcātvālamudapātraṃ cāvekṣeran// 4 //
1.12.5.[1]	sāmāsi pratimābhāhītyanena yajuṣā ādityamavekṣeranniti varttate
1.12.6.[1]	yajuṣā vā ādityamavekṣeran tūṣṇīṃ veti vikalpayati
1.12.7.[1]	atrocyate, sakṛditi kimarthamārabhyate, yadā tāvaduktaṃ navabhiḥ stuvanti hiṅkāro daśamo daśākṣarā virāḍiti ucyate ayaṃ hi trivṛtstomakaṃ bahiṣpavamānamadhikṛtya vidhirārabhyate virāṭ sampadarthaṃ yatra punaḥ stomavṛddhiḥ syāt anekasāmānekadaivataṃ vā bahiṣpavamānaṃ syāt tatra hiṅkāraṃ prati saṃśayaḥ syāt kiñca pratisāma pratidaivataṃ vā syāditi, ato'yamācāryo yatnamārabhate sakṛddhiṃkṛtya bahiṣpavamānena stuvīranniti /
1.12.7.[2]	atha bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet atrocyate, vakṣyatyayaṃ etatsarvaṃ kuryāduttarayoḥ pavamānayoriti tatrāpi sakṛdeva hiṅkāraḥ prāpnoti naitat tatra hyayaṃ vakṣyati sāmne sāmne hiṃkuryuriti atrocyate, na hyekavidhau pratyāmnāyo gamyate vikalpaḥ pratīyate ato'yamācāryo yatnamārabhate bahiṣpavamāneneti
1.12.8.[1]	ahiṃkṛtā prathamā stotrīyā sthādbahiṣpavamāne tasyāḥ saṃvyavahārikīyaṃ saṃjñā retasyeti vakṣyati hi retasyaikatrikasya bahiṣpavamānamiti
1.12.9.[1]	retasyā yāḥ parāḥ stotrīyāḥ tāsu hiṅkāraḥ syāditi
1.12.10.[1]	rathantaravarṇo yasyā seyaṃ rathantaravarṇā sā cottamā bahiṣpavamānasya syāt avisṛṣṭahiṅkārā ca syāt hiṅkāro na visṛjyate ākāro visargaḥ
1.12.11.[1]	tasyā rathantaravarṇāyā ūrddhvaṃ prastāvāccatvāryakṣarāṇi rathantaravadabhiṣṭobhet
1.12.12.[1]	annamakaramityetadādi yajurjapedudgātā ekaśrutividhānāt
1.12.13.[1]	śyeno'sītyetadādi yajuḥ prastare'dhikaraṇe yajamānaṃ vācayet ālabdhaprastaraṃ anutvārabhe iti liṅgāt
1.12.14.[1]	taṃ yajamānaṃ sarvastotreṣu stutvopahvayeran sarvagrahaṇaṃ na kevalaṃ bahiṣpavamāne upahava uktalakṣaṇaḥ
1.12.15.[1]	saṃ varcasetyetadādi yajuḥ ye tatrekṣakāḥ ye cāsya sahakāriṇaḥ tān prekṣamāṇo japet
1.12.16.[1]	namo gandharvāyetyetadādi yajurādityamīkṣamāṇo japet
1.12.17.[1]	antarhitaścedādityaḥ syāt deśenaivāvekṣet ko'sya viṣayaḥ sadasi bahiṣpavamānena stuvanti tatprakaraṇe kimarthamiti cet ucyate, anyatrāpi deśenaiva subhūrasītyādityamupatiṣṭheran udvayantamasasyarīti ca etadarthaṃ darśayati
1.12.18.[1]	vakṣyatyayaṃ yathāsavanamupaviśya prastotā havirddhānaṃ gacchenmadhyandine hutaṃ ādityagrahe pratiharttā bhava iti yo'yaṃ havirddhānaṃ gacchet sa eva kuryāduttarayoḥ pavamānayoḥ viṣṇoḥ śira ityata ārabhya sarvagrahaṇaṃ niravaśeṣavāci evamatiprasakte bravīti
1.12.19.[1]	agniḥ prastotāhaṃ mānuṣa ityetadādayaḥ pravarā nivarttante tūṣṇīṃ cātvālamudapātraṃ cāvekṣeranniti etadādi yatkarma tat sarvaṃ prāgghiṅkārānnivarttate
1.12.20.[1]	praveśanañca sammārjanañca praveśanasammārjane iṣa urja iti praveśanaṃ vasavastveti sammārjanantayoḥ praveśanasammārjanayoḥ antarāle yatkarma tṛtīyasavane tacca sarvannivarttate caśabdāt pūrvasūtroktañca
1.12.21.[1]	tatra tṛtīyasavane kumbhasya sammārjanaṃ kuryāt na droṇakalaśasya tuśabdo viśeṣaṇārthaḥ uttare havirddhānasaṃjñake'nasi yaḥ pūrvasthāpitaḥ taṃ sammṛjyāt na paścimaṃ droṇakalaśāvṛtā yo droṇakalaśamamārjanavidhiḥ tena sammārjanavidhinā āvṛtparikramo vidhiriti samānārthaḥ
1.12.22.[1]	taṃ kumbhaṃ yo'sau pūrvaḥ taṃ pūtabhṛdityevamācakṣate ete pūtabhṛdāhavanīyayorapyadhikāraṃ manyanta iti
2.2.1.[1]	uktaṃ etatsarvaṃ kuryāduttarayoḥ pavamānayoriti sarvasminvidhyante prāpte pravarāstu nivarttantiti etadādi yannivarttate taduktaṃ sāmprataṃ stomayogaviśeṣa ucyate stomayogamantre agniryunaktvityetasya padasya sthāne vāyuryunaktu sūryo yunaktviti nānāsavanayorete pade syātāṃ nānā pṛthagityarthaḥ vāyuryunaktu manaseti mādhyandine sūryoyunaktu vāceti tṛtīyasavane
2.1.2.[1]	asminneva stomayojane mantre yāḥ samastāstisro devatā āmnātāstāsāmanusavanaṃ vikṛtāṃ kriyāṃ dhānañjapyo manyate taducyate, agnestejasā bṛhaspatistvā yunaktviti prātaḥsavane indrasyendriyeṇa bṛhaspatistvā yunaktviti mādhyandine sūryasya varcasā bṛhaspatistvā yunaktviti tṛtīyasavane
2.1.3.[1]	sarvairebhirekaikaṃ stomayojanaṃ yathāmnāyaṃ śāṇḍilyo manyate, yathāmnāyagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate, vihāraḥ prakṛtaḥ tanmābhūditi
2.1.4.[1]	sāmārthaṃ sāmārthaṃ hiṃkuryuḥ uktaṃ sakṛddhiṃkṛtya bahiṣpavamānena stuvīranniti tatra sakṛddhiṅkāraḥ iha punaḥ pratisāma hiṅkāraḥ syāt
2.1.5.[1]	vṛṣako'si svaro'sītyetadādiyajuṣī yajamānavācane syātāṃ nānāsavanayoḥ krameṇa śyeno'sītyetasya sthāne
2.1.6.[1]	uttarayoḥ pavamānayorātideśiko vidhiruktaḥ sāmprataṃ yadanantaraṃ prakṛtaṃ karma taducyate, stutvā bahiṣpavamānena anantaraṃ prastarāttṛṇaṃ gṛhītvā tadubhayataḥ parichidya tṛṇaṃ catuṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ taccātvāle pravidhyet prakṣipet prakṣepaḥ pravyādhaḥ yadi stutamityetadādinā mantreṇa ekaśrutividhānādudgātā aṅgulichedanasaṃśaye yena karma kṛtaṃ tasya parimāṇam
2.1.7.[1]	tasminneva cātvāle udapātranninayeyuḥ yattat udapātraṃ tasmin karmaṇyaṅgabhūtaṃ tadeva cātvāle ninayeyuḥ samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomītyetadādinā yajuṣā
2.1.8.[1]	tadudapātraṃ ninīya anantaraṃ bahirvedyudaṅmukhā ayuñji padāni utkrāmeyuḥ gaccheyuḥ prāgdaśabhyaḥ tri pañca sapta nava vā
2.1.9.[1]	āvrajya āgnīdhrīyantasmin bahiṣpavamānaḥ adhīyīran nanu kimidaṃ bahiṣpavamānarco'dhīyīranniti āvrajyāgnīdhrīyamupariṣṭājjapa iti vācye ucyate, stotradharmaḥ pravṛttaḥ pratyaṅmukhaḥ prastotodaṅmukha udgātā dakṣiṇapūrvamaṣṭamadeśamīkṣamāṇaḥ pratihartteti so'yamācāryaḥ punarārabhate bahiṣpavamānarca iti kathaṃ ya eva purastājjapasya dharmaḥ sa eva dharmaḥ syāditi prāṅmukhaiḥ kriyeti
2.1.10.[1]	pratipakṣatayā anuvyāhāriṣīt kṣapaṇavādaṃ kṛtavān ayaṃ pūrvamiti udgāyatāmiti śaṃketa punarapyabhivyāharediti tasmai tadarthaṃ āgnīdhrīye āhutivajraṃ praharet yajñaśañcatityetadādinā yajuṣā āhutivajraḥ abhicārārthī āhutiḥ anuvyāhārapraśamanārthaṃ anuvyāhāro nāma abhidrohābhisaṃhitaḥ praśnaḥ
2.1.11.[1]	yaduktaṃ tasmā āgnīdhrīya nāhutivajraṃ praharediti tanna kuryāt kasmāt yataḥ ya enamanuvyāharati sa ārttimārchatīti śruteḥ akriyamāṇe'pyetasmin ya enamanuvyāharati sa ārttimārchatyeva tasmānna vyabhicareteti iti dhānañjapyasya matam
2.2.1.[1]	bahiṣpavamānasya kṛtsno vidhiruktaḥ sāmpratamahīnasatreṣu deśaviśeṣo vivakṣitaḥ sa ucyate, ahīnabahiṣpavamānairiti ahīnasya bahiṣpavamānāni ahīnabahiṣpavamānāni tairahīnabahiṣpavamānaiḥ sadasī stuvīran deśena deśaḥ pratyāmnāyate prathamāhno'nyatra prathame 'hani cātvāladeśe stutvā śeṣeṣu sadasi stuvīran nanu bahiṣpavamānairiti bahuvacanasāmarthyādahīnavidhau siddhe kasmādahīnagrahaṇaṃ kriyate yāvatā ekāheṣu bahutvāsambhavāt satreṣu ca viśeṣavacanādādyantayośca satreṣviti ataḥ pratyākhyāyāhīnāt na cānyā caturthī yajñajātirasti yasyāmidaṃ vidhānaṃ kalpeta tasmādahīnagrahaṇaṃ na karttavyaṃ kriyamāṇe ca prayojanaṃ vaktavyam ucyate yaducyate'hīnagrahaṇaṃ na karttavyamiti karttavyamiti brūmaḥ kasmāt śeṣavidhiprasiddhaye dvādaśāhe'hīnabhūte ekāhamiśreṣu cāhīneṣu varuṇapraghāsadvidivasākamedhatrirātravyuṣṭidvirātreṣu akriyamāne'hīnagrahaṇe saṃśayaḥ syāt so'yamācāryyo muktasaṃśayaṃ sūtramārabhate, ahīnabahiṣpavamānairiti atha prathamādahno'nyatreti ahargrahaṇaṃ na karttavyaṃ kasmāt prathamādanyatreti siddhe na caikasminnahanyanekabahiṣpavamānaṃ nāsti ucyate, karttavyamahargrahaṇaṃ kasmāt akriyamāṇe prathame'hani naimittikabahiṣpavamānāvṛttau sadasi stavanaṃ syāt bahiṣpavamānānantare somāpahāre somadāhe vā ābhyāsikasaṃskāre sati haviṣaḥ stutyarthatvāt pavamānānāṃ saṃskārāvṛttau pavamānābhyāsavṛttiḥ prāpnoti pavamānābhyāsavṛttiśceti vacanāt havisrutiḥ pavamāne iti ca tasmādahargrahaṇe kriyamāṇe nāsti doṣaḥ
2.2.2.[1]	ādyantayośca ye ahanī satreṣu tābhyāmanyatra sadasi stavanaṃ satreṣu samādhyartham
2.2.3.[1]	sadasi bahiṣpavamānakriyāyāmayaṃ viśeṣaḥ prāgdhiṣṇyeṣvagnīnāṃ viharaṇāt tṛṇaprakṣepaṇādi karma niṣkramya samāpnuyuḥ caturaṅgulaṃ parichidya tṛṇaṃ cātvāle pravidhyedityata ārabhya ā upariṣṭājjapāt
2.2.4.[1]	vaidatrirātre satraṃ nyāyaṃ gautama ācāryo manyate ubhayato'tirātratvāt
2.2.5.[1]	ahīneṣu yo nyāyastaṃ dhānañjapyo manyate ahīnatvāt
2.2.6.[1]	mandraḥ svarastaṃ śritvā prātaḥsavane stuvīran uttaramuttaraṃ śritvā uttarayoḥ pavamānayoḥ stuvīran mandre saptayavāntarāṇi bhavanti ataḥ śritvetyuktam anyathā hi mandreṇa prātaḥsavanaṃ stuvīranniti syāt
2.2.7.[1]	madhyena svareṇa vā ubhayoruttarayoḥ savanayoḥ stuvīran
2.2.8.[1]	etasmin kāle ityarthaḥ stutvā bahiṣpavamānena ṛtvijāmbhojanakāla upadiśyate etasmin kāle bhuñjīrannāntarābhojanaṃ syāt ādadhibhakṣaṇāt
2.2.9.[1]	anusavanantu satreṣu bhojanaṃ savanaśabdo viśeṣaṇārthaḥ kaṃ viśinaṣṭi kālaṃ savanamukhīyān bhakṣayitveti savanamukhīyānāṃ bhakṣaṇamuktaṃ bhavati nahyabhakṣayitvā sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu tato bhuñjīran nanu sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu ityukte savanamukhīyānāṃ bhakṣaṇamuktambhavati nahyabhakṣiteṣu savanamukhīyeṣu nārāśaṃsānāṃ sādanamasti tasmātsavanamukhīyān bhakṣayitvetyatiricyate naitat kutaḥ vakṣyatyayaṃ dvitīyāḥ savaneṣu nārāśaṃsāḥ pūrvayośca tṛtīyāviti tatra saṃśayaḥ syāt kiṃ pūrveṣu nārāśaṃseṣu sanneṣu uttarottareṣviti tadvivecanārthamārabhyate ye savanamukhīyānantaraṃ nārāśaṃsāsteṣu mantreṣviti
2.2.10.[1]	savanīyasya paśorvapāyāṃ hutāyāmanantaraṃ dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭheran taddhiṣṇyopasthānaṃ vakṣyate
2.2.11.[1]	cātvāle tu mārjanaṃ pūrvasatreṣu dhiṣṇyopasthānādbhavati mārjanaṃ mantrapūtābhiradbhirabhyukṣaṇaṃ idamāpa ityetadādinā mantreṇa prakṛtamadhunocyate
2.2.12.[1]	samrāḍasītyanena mantreṇa āhavanīyamupasthāya udaṅmukhā gatvā āstāvacātvālaśāmitrān āstāvaśca cātvālañca śāmitraśca āstāvacātvālaśāmitrāḥ tānupatiṣṭheran udaṅmukhāḥ udaṅmukhā iti prāṅmukhakaraṇaṃ pratyāmnāyate stuto nabhosaṃmṛṣṭa iti etadādibhirmantraiḥ yathāsaṃkhyena
2.2.13.[1]	vibhurasītyanena mantreṇa āgnīdhrīyasyopasthānaṃ kuryuḥ nanu āhavanīyamupasthāyeti prakṛtamupasthānaṃ kasmāducyate upatiṣṭheranniti ucyate udaṅmukhā iti prakṛtaṃ tanmābhūt ataḥ upatiṣṭherannityucyate kathaṃ āgnīdhrīyaṃ gatvā prāmukhā upatiṣṭheranniti
2.2.14.[1]	tamāgnīdhrīyamuttareṇa sañcaraḥ sarvatra enapāyoge dvitīyā sarvatreti na kevalaṃ dhiṣṇyopasthāne tamiti nirddeśaḥ kriyate keṣāñcit pariśrite bhavati keṣāñcidbahirbhavati yadi pariśrite yadi bahistasyaivottareṇa sañcaraḥ
2.2.15.[1]	dakṣiṇenāgnīdhrīyasya sañcaraḥ uttarayoḥ savanayoryasmin kāle havirddhānagamanaṃ bhavati āhavanīyagrahaṇādanyo'pi pṛṣṭhāśrito homaḥ āhavanīya eva syāt yathā vairājamiti
2.2.16.[1]	pūrvasya dvāri kasya sadasaḥ tiṣṭhanto bahirityetadādinā yajuṣāhoturdhiṣṇyamupatiṣṭheran
2.2.17.[1]	dhiṣṇyamupatiṣṭheran
2.2.18.[1]	tutha ityetadādibhiryajurbhiḥ brāhmaṇāchaṃsipotṛneṣṭrachāvākānāṃ udañco dhiṣyāḥ tānupatiṣṭheran
2.2.19.[1]	tasminneva pradeśe tiṣṭhantaḥ śundhyurityetadādinā yajuṣā mārjālīyamupatiṣṭheran
2.2.20.[1]	ṛtadhāmetyanenaudumbarīmupatiṣṭheran
2.2.21.[1]	samudra ityanena yajuṣā brahmaṇaḥ sadanamupatiṣṭheran tatraiva tiṣṭhanta ityetadanuvarttata eva
2.2.22.[1]	uttareṇa sadasaḥ gatvā vederantaḥ antarvedi antarityavyayaṃ na bahirvedītyetaduktaṃ bhavati pratyaṅmukhāstiṣṭhantaḥ ahiriti prajahitamupatiṣṭheran pātnīśālo'gniḥ keṣāñcidgārhapatyādatipraṇayano bhavati keṣāñcidāhavanīyāt yasmādatipraṇayano bhavati sa gārhapatyaḥ yo'nyaḥ sa prajahitaḥ
2.2.23.[1]	aja ityanena mantreṇa gārhapatyamupatiṣṭheran
2.2.24.[1]	sagarā ityetadādinā yajuṣā dakṣiṇāgnerāyatanamupatiṣṭheran
2.2.25.[1]	kavya ityetadādinā yajuṣā mahāvederdakṣiṇamantamupatiṣṭharan
2.2.26.[1]	etasminneva deśe tiṣṭhantaḥ sarvānāhavanīyādīn dhiṣṇyān samanvīkṣamāṇaḥ pātamityetad yajurjapeyuḥ
2.2.27.[1]	āhavanīyādārabhya ekaikaṃ dhiṣṇyamupasthāyaitad yajurjapeyuriti śāṇḍilya ācāryyo manyate tasmin yajuṣi yān bahuśabdāntānekavatsanayantaḥ prayogastu pāhi māgneraudreṇānīkena pipṛhi mā namaste'stu mā mā hiṃsīrityevamādi
2.3.1.[1]	raurukīye pravacane yāni dhiṣṇyopasthānayajūṃṣyāmnātāni yaditāni kuryuḥ tataḥ prāgāhavanīyopasthānādādityantāvadupatiṣṭheran adhvanāmadhvapata ityanena mantreṇa
2.3.2.[1]	āhavanīyaṃ pūrvoktena vidhinā upasthāya tamevopatiṣṭheran apijo'si jāyamāna iti apijo'si navajāta iti vā etayoranyatareṇa yamagninnirmathya āhavanīye praharanti tamagnimābhimukhyena pretya samīpe gatvā upatiṣṭheran
2.3.3.[1]	yadā yasmin kāle cātvālamupatiṣṭheran athānantaramutkaramupatiṣṭheran tumulo'syākranda kṛtvetyanena mantreṇa
2.3.4.[1]	yasmin kāle śāmitramupatiṣṭheran athānantaraṃ yasmin deśe paśoḥ ūvadhyannikhananti taṃ deśamupatiṣṭheran ūvadhyagoho'si pārthiva ityanena yajuṣā
2.3.5.[1]	yasmin kāle āgnīdhrīyamupatiṣṭheran athānantaraṃ yatra yasmin deśe acchāvāka āsīnaḥ hotari upahavamicchati taṃ deśamupatiṣṭheran upahavyo'si namasya iti upahavyo'si tanūpā iti vā etayoranyatareṇa vā
2.3.6.[1]	yasmin kāle brahmaṇaḥ sadanamupatiṣṭheran anantaraṃ sadasyasya sadamamupatiṣṭheran sadasyo'si malimluca ityanena mantreṇa sīdantyasminniti sadanam
2.3.7.[1]	yasmin kāle dakṣiṇaṃ vedyantamupatiṣṭheran tato'nantaraṃ patnīśālādīnyāgnīdhrīyāntāni āgārāṇyupatiṣṭheran yathādiṣṭairmantraiḥ, nanu āgnīdhrīyasya pūrvamevopasthānaṃ kṛtaṃ tat kimidaṃ punarādiśyata iti atrocyate, tadāgnīdhrīyasya kṛtam imāni tu patnīśālādīnāṃ pariśritānāmupasthānāni prakṛtāni tasmādāgnīdhrīyaparicitasyedamupasthānamiti
2.3.8.[1]	atha asmāt karmaṇo'nantaraṃ yathāpūrvaṃ samastopasthānaṃ kṛtaṃ tathaiva tena prakāreṇa sarvānsamanvīkṣamāṇaḥ sarve stha somyāsa ityetadyajurjapitvā anantaraṃ pātametyetadādi pūrvoktaṃ japeyuḥ
2.3.9.[1]	dvayorvvidhānayorantareṇa dhiṣṇyānupasthāya anantaraṃ ṛtasya dvārau stha ityanena mantreṇa sadasaḥ aparau paścimau dvārabāhū saṃmṛjya mā mā santāptamityanena yajuṣā sadasi praviśeyuḥ sammārjanaṃ śodhanam
2.3.10.[1]	dakṣiṇena pradeśenaudumbaryā gatvā tasyā uttare pradeśe upaviśeṣuḥ namaḥ sakhibhya ityanena yajuṣā tasyā iti nirdeśo mābhūt sadasa uttarata iti
2.3.11.[1]	etasyāṃ velāyāṃ dhiṣṇyopasthānānantarāyāṃ pūrveṇa pradeśena prastotāraṃ pratiharttā gacchet apare bruvate etasyāmityetasyāmaudumbaryām ayameva nityaḥ sañcara iti
2.3.12.[1]	etasyāmiti kākākṣinyāyenobhayatra sambadhyate etasyāṃ velāyāmasmin kāle samupahayeran, nanu etasyāṃ velāyāmiti kimarthamārabhyate atha samupahvayerannityānantarye siddhe ucyate, anyadapyasti pūrveṇa prastotāraṃ pratihartuḥ gamanaṃ na tasmin samupahvayeran dhiṣṇyopasthānānantaraṃ praveśanakāla eva samupahvayeram
2.3.13.[1]	yajamānā upahvayadhvamityevopahvānamiti sarve yajamānāḥ satreṣu samupahvayeran
2.3.14.[1]	satrādanyatra mithaḥ dvau dvau samupahvayeran
2.3.15.[1]	satrādanyatra sarve trayo'pi udgātāro yajamānamupahvayeran udgātāra upahvayadhvamiti prārthitāḥ santa upahūta ityanujñāṃ kuryurityarthaḥ
2.3.16.[1]	ṛtasya dvārā stha ityetasmādārabhya etat sarvaṃ kuryuḥ yāvad yajamānasamupahvānamiti yasmin kāle dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭheran, nanu etat sarvamiti kimarthaṃ dvārabāhusammārjanaprabhṛtīti siddhe ucyate, uktaṃ yadā dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭheranniti vakṣyati ca atha dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭherannityetasmin prakaraṇe anupasthānaṃ śāṇḍilya iti taddhiṣṇyopasthānānantaraṃ karma anupasthānena prāpnoti so'yamācāryo niyamārthamārabhate etat sarvaṃ kuryāditi kathaṃ anupasthāne'pi syāditi
2.3.17.[1]	yajamānasya karma yājamānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ karma brahmatvaṃ te yājamānabrahmatve yadyudgātā mūlyena kuryāt tadāgnīdhrīyamupasthāya tasya pūrveṇa gacchet kiṃ viṣayaṃ punaridaṃ karmodgātuḥ ucyate āpatkalpe
2.3.18.[1]	sādasān dhiṣṇyān upasthāya sadasi bhavāḥ sādasāḥ tānupasthāya tasminneva deśe'vasthita īkṣamāṇaḥ pātnīśālān dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭhet patnīśalāyāṃ bhavāḥ pātnīśālāḥ
2.3.19.[1]	itarathā itarau praṣṭī pūrvoktena vidhinā dhiṣṇyān upatiṣṭheyātām
2.4.1.[1]	sādasān pānīśālāṃśca dhiṇyānupasthāya anantaramṛtasya dvārau stha ityanena yajuṣā pūrvau dvārabāhū sadasaḥ saṃmṛjya dakṣiṇasya dvārabāhoḥ pūrve pradeśe udaṅmukha upaviśedityevaṃ dhānañjapyaḥ ācārya āha
2.4.2.[1]	paścime pradeśe dakṣiṇasya dvārabāhoḥ pratyaṅmukha upaviśedityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācārya āha
2.4.3.[1]	praveśanopaveśanārthīye yajuṣī pūrvamevokte mā mā santāpta namaḥ sakhibhya iti ca
2.4.4.[1]	yājamānamuktaṃ sāmprataṃ brahmatvaṃ vivakṣitaṃ taducyate, ṛtvikpathena gatvā samastopasthānādārabhya sarvān samanvīkṣamāṇāḥ pātametyetasmāt sarvaṃ samānam
2.4.5.[1]	ayantu viśeṣaḥ prāgaugātrādupaveśanāt dakṣiṇe pradeśe sadasa upaveśanaṃ prastoturupaveśanaṃ prati tacca brahmopaveśanena, nanu kimidaṃ brahmopaveśaneneti yadā vakṣyatyevopaveśanam ucyate, vakṣyatyayaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prakaraṇe pratipattau dhiṣṇyānupasthāyoktaṃ sadasyupaveśanamiti nirastaḥ parāvasurityanena yajuṣā dakṣiṇātṛṇṇannirasyet āvasoḥ sadane sīdāmītyanena upaviśet
2.4.6.[1]	upaviśyānantaram etadyajurjapet anantaramaudumbarīṃ gatvā pūrvoktena yajuṣopaviśet
2.4.7.[1]	tamupaviṣṭamanantaraṃ prastotṛpratiharttārāvupaviśetāṃ pūrvoktenaiva yajuṣā
2.4.8.[1]	yadi yājamānabrahmatve udgātā kuryāt tadā yājamānaṃ brahmatvamaudgātramityanenānupūrveṇa sarvaṃ yathāsanaṃ upaveśanādi kuryāt
2.4.9.[1]	yadi glāyed audumbaryāmevāsīnaḥ sarvaṃ kuryāt glāniraśaktiḥ
2.4.10.[1]	sadasya evameva yadidamudgātṛṛṇāṃ dhiṣṇyopasthānamuktantamanenaiva prakāreṇa kurvan brahmāṇamanupraviśet
2.4.11.[1]	yadi brahmaṇā yadi vā brāhmaṇachaṃsinā yasyānūpraviṣṭaḥ tena saha sadasyasya samupahavaḥ syāt na kevalaṃ samupahavo bhakṣaśca tenaiva tulyaḥ syāt
2.4.12.[1]	yadi bībhatseyātāṃ nānā camasā syātāṃ bībhatsā nāma ghṛṇā syātāmiti etāveva camasau nānā syātām anyeṣāṃ tu satyāmapi bībhatsāyāṃ naiva nānā camasaḥ syāt
2.4.13.[1]	savanasaṃsthāsu sarpaṇeṣu sarpatsu ṛtvigyajamāneṣu na sadasyaḥ śūnyaṃ sadaḥ kuryāt
2.4.14.[1]	tasya sadasyasya dadhibhakṣāntaṃ karma bhavati norddhvam
2.4.15.[1]	sa dadhibhakṣato nivartteta satreṣu sadasyasya kathaṃ punaretadgamyate yathā dadhibhakṣato nivarttate sadasyasya na sadasya eveti ucyate sadasyo hi satrotpādaka eva āvarttavāḥ sadasyā iti, nanūktamaśuṣomāntamahaḥsatreṣviti satreṣu dadhibhakṣaprāptireva nāsti aśuṣomāntatvādahnām atrocyate, savidhirudgātṛṛṇamukto na sadasyasya sadasyasya hi aviśeṣepoktaṃ dadhibhakṣāntaṃ karma ekāhāhīnasatreṣu so'viśeṣavacanaprāpto dadhibhakṣaḥ satreṣu viśeṣavacanena sa nivartteta satreṣviti
2.4.16.[1]	visaṃsthite arddhasamāpte savane antareṇa hoturdhiṣṇyasya maitrāvaruṇadhiṣṇyañca gatvā pūrvayā dvārā sadoniṣkramaṇakarmārthameṣa sañcaraḥ
2.4.17.[1]	tadyathā gataṃ evaṃ sadasi sañcaraḥ siddho bhavati nānyatprayojanamasti asya sūtrasyārambhe
2.5.1.[1]	dhiṣṇyopasthānamuktam anantaraṃ savanamukhīyāṃścamasānāharanti ata ucyate, camasaṃ pratigṛhyeti camantyasminniti camasaḥ taṃcamasaṃdīyamānaṃ pratigṛhya dakṣiṇa ūrāvādhāya dakṣiṇena pāṇināpidhāyāsīta apidhānamācchādanam
2.5.2.[1]	upahūyamānāyāmiḍāyāntañcamasaṃ iḍāhvānasamīpe dhārayedanupaghnan aspṛśan /
2.5.2.[2]	eṣa upahvānadharmaḥ prāgyājamānāt agnirma ityādi
2.5.3.[1]	vaṣaṭkarttari bhakṣite'smiṃścamase tato bhakṣayeyuḥ svaṃ camasaṃ mithaḥ anyonyamupahvaya, nanu vaṣaṭkartrā camasaṃ bhakṣitaṃ tato'nubhakṣayediti tadayuktaṃ kutaḥ anviti kālāpekṣā na bhakṣaṇaprāptiḥ mitha upahūya ityetasmācca yasya bhakṣaṇaprāptiḥ sa evopahavaṃ yācanīyaḥ anujñārthatvāt upahvānasya sarvagrahaṇānna kevalaṃ savamamukhīyānāṃ sarveṣāñcamasānāṃ eṣa bhakṣaṇadharmaḥ
2.5.4.[1]	camasaṃ bhakṣayet asau camasaḥ prastotrā prathamaṃ pratipannaḥ ato'syaivānantaraṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ prāpnoti ataḥ āhodgātā prathama iti kathaṃ bhakṣayedityucyate
2.5.5.[1]	dakṣiṇaṃ bāhumanu camamasya daṇḍaṃ kṛtvā śyena ityanena yajuṣā avekṣya somam indavityanena dvirbhakṣayedalpaṃ kriyābhyāse sakṛnmantraḥ yadyasminsavane chando yathāsavanaṃ gāyatrachandasa iti prātaḥsavane triṣṭupcchandasa iti mādhyandine jagatīcchandasa iti tṛtīyasavane evamādiśan
2.5.6.[1]	ūrddhva ityanena yajuṣā mukhyān prāṇānabhimṛśeta mukhe bhavā mukhyāḥ prāṇā indriyāṇi, soma rārandhītyanena yajuṣā hṛdayaṃ soma gīrbhirityanena nābhim abhimṛśeteti varttate
2.5.7.[1]	evameva itarau prastotṛpratiharttārau kuryātāṃ
2.5.8.[1]	atha tayoḥ kaḥ krama ityucyate, pratiharttā paścāt
2.5.9.[1]	taṃ camasaṃ sa pratiharttā āpyāyayet abhimṛśya āpyāyasvetyanena mantreṇa ayātayāmārtham atha sagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate, vakṣyati subrahmaṇyacaturthā udgātṛcamasaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ ṣaṭ cānya iti tairapi bhakṣite sa evāpyāyayet pratiharttā
2.5.10.[1]	sarve vā āpyāyayeyuḥ āpyāyasvetyetayā gāyatryā athaitayā gāyatryeti kimarthamiti cet ucyate, saṃvyavahārārthaṃ vakṣyati gāyatrīṃ dvirbrūyuriti gāyatryaivānusavanamāpyāyanamiti ca
2.5.11.[1]	tāṃ gāyatrīṃ tṛtīyasavane somāpyāyane dvirbrūyuḥ sante payāṃsityetayarcā mādhyandine āpyāyanaṃ chandaḥsampadartham
2.5.12.[1]	gāyatryaivāpyāyasvetyetayā sakṛduktayā anusavanamāpyāyanamiti śāṇḍilya āha
2.5.13.[1]	dvitīyāścamasāḥ savaneṣu triṣvapi nārāśaṃsasaṃjñāḥ pūrvayoḥ savanayoḥ prathamadvitīyayostṛtīyau ca
2.5.14.[1]	teṣāṃ nārāśaṃsānāmanavekṣya bhakṣaṇaṃ yadetacye na ityavekṣaṇaṃ etatteṣāṃ na syāt avamairityetadādibhirvihṛtairanusavanaṃ bhakṣayeyuryathākramam
2.5.15.[1]	pitṛbhirbhakṣitasyetyetadādi sarvatrānusaṃharet sarveṣu savaneṣu sarvagrahaṇaṃ anyeṣvapi mantreṣu pitṛśabdamanusaṃharet avamaiste pitṛbhirityetadādi
2.5.16.[1]	yadetadūrddhva iti mukhyān prāṇānabhimṛśetetyetadādi pratyabhimarśanam etat nārāśaṃse kuryānna vā apare varṇayanti pitṛbhiriti sarvatrānusaṃharet ityasya pitṛśabdasyānusaṃharet pratyabhimarśane yathākāmī indraśabdasya sthāne pitṛśabdaṃ vā kuryāt yathāmnātamevābhimarśanaṃ kuryāt sarvaprāptisatatvārthatvādindrasya
2.5.17.[1]	prathamadvitīyau camasau pūrvayoḥ savanayoḥ prātaḥsavanamādhyandinayoḥ āpyāyayet prathamañcamasaṃ tṛtīyasavane āpyāyayet
2.5.18.[1]	āvarttistotreṣu tṛṇe pratigṛhya prastotādgātre prayacchet yathā prastaraṃ yena prakāreṇa prastaradānaṃ brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstariti prastotṛgrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet yathā prastaramityanenaiva siddhe yadā prastarasya prastotaiva sampradātā atrocyate yadāpyanyadupākaraṇadravyaṃ tatrāpi prastotaiva prayacchet yathā vairūpopākaraṇe vyajanamaraṇī vairāje mahānāmnīṣvavakāmiśrā āpaḥ mahāvrate vāṇaḥ ityetadādi
2.5.19.[1]	anāhriyamāṇyostṛṇayormantrannotsṛjet yadā tṛṇābhyāmupakaraṇam
2.5.20.[1]	tathaiva tenaiva prakāreṇetyarthaḥ yathaiva prastareṇa bahiṣpavamāne uktaṃ jaṅghāmupahatya yuñjyāt stomaṃ dīkṣāyai varṇenetyetadādibhiḥ nānā pṛthagityarthaḥ yatra yasminnanantarāṇi catvāri stotrāṇi evaṃ dhānañjapya ācārya āha
2.5.21.[1]	yadetat prajāpatistveti sarveṣāmanantaramāmnātam etat pratyekamanuṣajyate dīkṣāyai varṇena prajāpatistvā yunaktu evaṃ sarveṣu
2.5.22.[1]	alpīyaḥsu stotreṣu uttaramuttaraṃ stomayojanaṃ lupyeta yathāgniṣṭome trīyuttarāṇi luptāni, atha kimarthamidaṃ sūtraṃ ārabhyate yadā nimittāpāye naimittikasyāpyapāyo bhaviṣyatyeva ucyate, sanniyogaśiṣṭānyetāni stomayojanāni yatrānantarāṇi catvārīti tatrākārtsnyena saṃśayaḥ syāt, athālpīyaḥsu kimarthamiti cet ucyate prakāradarśanārthaṃ katham anyatrāpi bahuṣvakṛtsneṣu lopaprāptau uttaramuttaraṃ lupyeta yathā vairāje'gnimanthane āha, abhyātmaṃ prajananaṃ kṛtvā triḥpradakṣiṇamabhimanthedgāyatraṃ chando'nu prajāyasva traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatamānuṣṭubhaṃ vairājamiti gautama ityuktvāha caturbhiriti dhānañjapyastribhiriti śāṇḍilya iti tathā mahāvratāsaṅghārohaṇaṃ chandobhiruktvāha vairājapañcamairiti gautamaścaturbhiriti dhānañjapyastribhiriti śāṇḍilya iti atrāpyuttaramuttaraṃ lupyetālpīyaḥsviti
2.5.23.[1]	prathamena mantreṇa vājapeyasāmnaḥ stomaṃ yuñjyāt ṣoḍaśisāmnaḥ prathamena stomayojanaṃ kṛtam ihānārthāddvitīyasya prāptiḥ tanmābhūdityata āha prathameneti
2.5.24.[1]	prathamaprabhṛtīni rātrau stomayojanāni bhavanti ṣoḍaśimatyatirātre dvitīyaprabhṛtīni rātrau prāpnuvanti tatpratiṣedhārthamāha prathamaprabhṛtīni rātrāviti
2.5.25.[1]	tathaivātiriktastotreṣu prathamaprabhṛtītyeva sandheranantaratvāttatrāpi dvitīyaprabhṛtiprāptau tathetyuktam
2.5.26.[1]	sarvairdīkṣāyai varṇenetyetadādibhirekaikasmin stotre yathāmnātaiḥ stomayojanaṃ syāt yathāpāṭhamityarthaḥ yathāmnāyagrahaṇaṃ vihṛtairmābhūditi
2.5.27.[1]	āvarttistotreṣu yo nyāyaḥ stomayojanādīnāṃ sa sandhau syāt kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ parāktvātsandheḥ
2.5.28.[1]	upavasathye'hani caturdaśyāṃ samānānaṃ na kuryuḥ kva punaḥ samāmnānaṃ prāptamupavasathye'hani niṣidhyata iti ucyate, stotragatasya sāmnaḥ pāñcavidhye bhaktiṣvācāryāṇāṃ anekadhā pratipattiḥ tadyathādāvekaḥ kalponāṅgīkriyate tadā stotrakāle bhaktīḥ prati anyo'nyena vipratipattiḥ syāt sa cānyāyaḥ tadevaṃ mābhūdityata adāvevodgātuḥ kalpo ya iṣṭaḥ sa sampratipattavyaḥ ato'rthaṃ samāmnānamādāveva karttavyaṃ syāt tasyopavasathye'hani pratiṣedhaḥ
2.6.1.[1]	karmasūtramuktaṃ upavasathye'hani na samāmaneranniti kintu prastotā tu kuśāḥ kārayet tuśabdo viśeṣaṇārthaḥ upavasathya evāhani prastotā kuśāḥ kārayet, kārayedityanyaṃ kuśānāṃ karttāraṃ jñāyati, yajñiyasya vṛkṣasya yajñamarhatīti yajñiyaḥ yajñiyasya vṛkṣasyetyavayavalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī khadirasya dīrghasatreṣveke eke ācāryā manyante dīrghasatreṣu khādiryaḥ kuśāḥ syuriti kiṃ kāraṇaṃ dāruprādhānyāt prādeśamātrīḥ prādeśapramāṇaḥ kārayet kuśapṛṣṭhāstvaktaḥ ākṛtirucyate tvacaṃ prati kuśapṛṣṭhāḥ syuḥ samāmajjataḥ majjāṃ prati samāḥ syuḥ aṅguṣṭhaparvapṛthumātrīḥ pṛthutvenāṅguṣṭhaparvamātrāḥ syuḥ prajñātāgrāḥ kārayitvā prajñātāni agrāṇi yathā bhavanti tathā kārayet nanu kārayitveti kimarthaṃ yadā prastotā tu kuśāḥ kārayediti prakṛta eva karaṇe ucyate praṇāśe kuśānāṃ bhaṅge vā punaranyāḥ kārayitvā prayuñjīta nānyat prāyaścittamasti gandhaiḥ pralipya kuśāḥ sarpiṣā satreṣveke eke ācāryāḥ satreṣu sarpiṣā pralepaṃ manyante vaiṣṭutena vasanena pariveśya viṣṭatīṣu yojitaṃ vaiṣṭutaṃ tena vāsasā sarvato veṣṭayitvā kṣaumaśāṇakārpāśānāṃ kenacit kṣumāyāḥ vikāraḥ kṣaumaṃ śaṇasya vikāraḥ śāṇaṃ kārpāśānāṃ vikāraḥ kārpāśam eteṣāṃ vāsasāmekena veṣṭayitvā audumbaryāḥ sādasyāḥ śālāyā upaviṣṭādvāsayet
2.6.2.[1]	tāmaudumbarīṃ śva eva śvobhūta ityevaṃ bruvate tasmin bhūte stotrakāle kuśairurddhvāgrairveṣṭayitvaivaṃjātīyenaiva vasanena yajjātīyaṃ vaiṣṭutaṃ pradakṣiṇamūrddhvadaśena pariveṣṭya pradakṣiṇamiti niyamaḥ kriyate na prasavyam ūrddhvadaśena nādhodaśena pariveṣṭya sarvato veṣṭayitvā spṛṣṭaḥ anapaśrita udgāyet vakṣyati kāraṇaṃ dhiṣṇyo'yaṃ bhavati na dhiṣṇyamāsādayediti
2.6.3.[1]	dhṛṣṭaṃ pragalbhaṃ svalpamityarthaḥ apaśrayeta ityeke tāvatā apaśrayaṇārthā iyaṃ bhavatībhiḥ sa eva tadūrjiśrita iti
2.6.4.[1]	stoṣyamāṇānāmiti pratyupasthitaṃ kālaṃ jñāpayati stoṣyamāṇānāṃ stotrakartṝṇāṃ madhye viṣṭutiprayojanaṃ vasanaṃ dviguṇaṃ kṛtvā prāksamāsaṃ vā deśāntapāśāntayoḥ saṃśleṣaḥ samāsaḥ taṃ samāmaṃ prāṅmukham udaṅmukhaṃ vā kṛtvā uparidaśamāstīryya prastotā kuśānāṃ vinyāsaṃ kuryyāt prastāvānteṣu
2.6.5.[1]	anekaprastāveṣu sāmasu mahādivākīrttyelāndamahānāmnādiṣu sāmasu ādye prastāve kuśāḥ prāsthāpayet
2.6.6.[1]	udagagrābhiḥ kuśābhiḥ prathamaṃ viṣṭāvaṃ vidadhyāt prāgapavargaṃ pratyagapavargaṃ vā
2.6.7.[1]	tasya prathamasya viṣṭāvasya paścime pradeśe dvitīyaṃ viṣṭāvaṃ vidadhyāt udaksaṃsthaṃ prāgagraṃ pratyagagraṃ vā
2.6.8.[1]	tasya dvitīyasya viṣṭāvasya paścime pradeśe tṛtīyaṃ viṣṭāvaṃ vidadhyāt evamekaḥ paryāyo bhavati tasya prathamasya paryāyasya uttare pradeśe dvitīyaḥ tasyāpyuttare tṛtīyaḥ, nanu kimidaṃ bahuvacanam evaṃvidhāḥ paryāyā uttarottarā iti yāvat yāvatā ukta ekaḥ paryāyaḥ anyau dvau vidheyau ucyate, bahuvacanaṃ catuṣṭomārthaṃ vakṣyati catuṣṭomayoścatuṣparyāyā iti sandhau ca pañcadaśādiṣu stomeṣu nānāparyāyaviṣṭāvāḥ syuḥ
2.6.9.[1]	paryāyāṃśca viṣṭāvāṃśca sandadhyāt saṃhatān kuryāt saṃlagnān kuryāt
2.6.10.[1]	paryāyasyādau hiṃkṛtya stuvīran nanu tat kimidamārabhyate yadā pratiparyāyaṃ hiṃkāra āmnāta eva brāhmaṇena tisṛbhyo hiṃkarotītyevamādi, ucyate kṛtaparyāyeṣu stomeṣu tadāmnātam akṛtaparyāyeṣu catuṣparyāyādiṣu ca saṃśayaḥ syādyadyevannārabhyeta
2.6.11.[1]	stotrasya uttamāṃ stotrīyāṃ prastutya prastāvaṃ dattvā prastotā eṣeti bruvan śaṃsitāramīkṣate kālaprajñāpanārthaṃ hotṛṛṇām uttamaṃ pratihāraṃ pratyāhvayantīti śruteḥ tatprajñāpanārthaṃ tadyathaiṣottarameveti
2.6.12.[1]	stutasya stutamasītyetad yajuḥ yajamānavācanamāvarttistotreṣu
2.6.13.[1]	savanasaṃsthāsu savanamamāptiṣvityarthaḥ praśāstrā sarpatetyuktaḥ yathetaṃ yathāgataṃ dakṣiṇenaudumbaryā gatvā aparayā dvārā niṣkramya paścimayā paścimenāgnīdhrīyaṃ bahirvedi mūtraṃ kuryuḥ vederbahiḥ mūtraṃ kuryuḥ yadi mūtritāḥ syuḥ na niyamaḥ avadhirupadiśyate mūtroccārayoḥ atha kimarthaṃ bahirvedīti kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ yathāntarvedimūtroccārayoḥ kriyā syāditi ucyate, bahirvedigrahaṇaṃ deśaprakarṣārthaṃ na vedeḥ samopadeśe prakṛṣṭe syāditi atha bahuvacanaṃ kimarthaṃ savanasaṃsthāsviti yadā prātaḥsavanamādhyandinayoreva savanayoḥ sarpaṇaṃ bhavati tṛtīyasavanasamāptau niḥsarpaṇaṃ tat kimidaṃ bahuvacanamiti ucyate, etadarthaṃ bahuvacanaṃ kriyate savanasamāptau saṃsthāsu ceti kathaṃ saṃsthāsamāptau ca sarpaṇaṃ syāditi yathā atirātre agniṣṭomānte sarpaṇam ukthyeṣu taccastreṣu ca samāpteṣu sarpaṇaṃ syāt ṣoḍaśini stute anuśaste sarpaṇam aptorvyāptyapyevameva
2.6.14.[1]	udakam arhatīty udakyāḥ yāvadakṛtaśaucāḥ syustāvadvāgyamanaṃ kuryuḥ ā upasparśanāt
2.6.15.[1]	yadetaduktaṃ paścimenāgnīdhrīyamiti etasya saṃjñeyaṃ mṛgatīrthamiti mārgatāmetattīrthaṃ yadyarthino bhavanti nirgamane anye bruvate mṛgatīrthamiti uktam āgrāmyān paśūn labhante āraṇyān sṛjantīti tadāraṇyānāṃ paśūnāmanenotsarjanamiti
2.6.16.[1]	tena mṛgatīrthena niṣkramya śamyāprāsātparatā na gaccheyuḥ
2.6.17.[1]	śamyāparāsāt parato yaḥ prakṛṣṭataraṃ deśaṃ gantumicchet āpnānena tīrthena niṣkramya sa gacchet
2.7.1.[1]	uktaṃ savanasaṃsthāsu praśāstroktā yathetamaparayā dvārā niṣkramya paścimenāgnīdhrīyaṃ bahirvedi mūtraṃ kuryuriti tadyadi tāvanniṣkramaṇānantaraṃ mūtroccāre kurvanti tataḥ kṛtaśaucā ācāntodakāḥ yadidamādekṣyate tat kuryuḥ atha mūtroccāre naiva kuryuḥ tadā yathoktena vidhinā niṣkramyāthānantaraṃ dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭheran samastena uktaṃ tatraiva tiṣṭhantaḥ sarvānsamanvīkṣamāṇaḥ pātameti etat samastopasthānam anenottarayoḥ savanayorupatiṣṭheran evaṃ gautamaśāṇḍilyāyanāvācāryāvāhatuḥ
2.7.2.[1]	āhavanīyopasthānādārabhya pratyekaṃ sarveṇa dhiṣyupasthānavidhinā upatiṣṭherann iti dhānañjapya ācārya āha
2.7.3.[1]	na upasthānamanupasthānaṃ etasminneva kāle śāṇḍilya ācāryo'nupasthānaṃ manyate
2.7.4.[1]	evameva niṣkramya yathāsavanasaṃsthāsu ityuktam pṛthak stotrebhyaḥ pṛthaṅgānetyarthaḥ tadarthaṃ samastenopatiṣṭheran yānyūrddhvamukthebhyaḥ katamāni punastāni pṛthakstotrāṇi yadarthamidamucyate yathā ṣoḍaśyarthe vājapeyasāmārthe voktameva sarpaṇaṃ saṃsthāsviti vakṣyati ca paryāyebhyastu rātreriti ucyate, yathā ṣoḍaśyarthe tathātiriktastotreṣu ca stotrāya stotrāya sandhyarthe sarpaṇaṃ syāditi
2.7.5.[1]	rātrau tu paryāyādau sarpaṇaṃ syāditi na pṛthak stotrebhyaḥ etadarthaṃ tuśabdaḥ
2.7.6.[1]	dhiṣṇyopasthānānantaraṃ dvārabāhusaṃmārjanaprabhṛti sarvaṃ kṛtvā yadasya svamāsanaṃ tasmin yajuṣopaviśya prastotā havirddhānaṃ gacchenmadhyandine karmārthamuktam etat sarvaṃ kuryāduttarayoḥ pavamānayoriti
2.7.7.[1]	hute ādityagrahe pratiharttā havirddhānaṃ gacchet ārbhave karmārtham
2.7.8.[1]	ubhayoḥ pavamānayoruttarayoḥ havirddhānaṃ gaccheyuḥ satreṣu sarva udgātāro yajamānatvāt
2.7.9.[1]	pavamānayoruttarayormadhyandinārbhavayordhiṣṇyeṣvagnivihāre mārjālīyamagniṃ carantaḥ paścimena yajamānasya hṛtvā tenaiva punarnayeyuḥ avyavāyārtham udgātṛṛṇāmanena karmaṇa kaḥ sambandha iti cet ucyate uktaṃ yājamānabrahmatve cedudgātā kuryāditi tatra sambandhaḥ
2.7.10.[1]	mādhyandinena pavamānena stutvā satreṣu dadhigharmasya ekadeśaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ sarve samupahūya na mithaḥ dadhikrāvṇa ityetayarcā
2.7.11.[1]	tasyā ṛcaḥ daśame'hani sātrike uttamaṃ padaṃ abhyasyeyuḥ punarbrūyuḥ anuṣṭuppārokṣārtham atha tasyā iti kimarthaṃ prakṛtaiva sā ucyate daśame'hani tārttīyasavanike dadhibhakṣe tasyā ṛcaḥ uttamābhyāsaḥ syāt hetusamatvāt tanmābhūditi
2.7.12.[1]	pūrveṇa patnīśālāṃ gamayitvā āgnīdhrīyasadasorantareṇa dakṣiṇā nayeyuḥ āpnānena tīrthena
2.7.13.[1]	sarvāsāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ devasya tvetyetadādi mantraḥ purastājjapaḥ syāt natu sarvāsāmiti kimarthaṃ dakṣiṇānāmiti bahuvacanāt siddheḥ ucyate, uktaṃ pūrveṇa patnīśālāmantareṇānāgnīdhrīyaṃ sadaśca dakṣiṇā nayeyustīrtheneti, anucyamāne etasminnanena dakṣiṇāpathena nayanaṃ yāsāntāsāmevaiṣa purastāt syāt nānyāsāmiti tanmābhūdityata ārabhyate sarvāsāmiti kathaṃ yāśca na nīyante sarvāsāmeva purastājjapaḥ syāditi yathā nimittaṃ dhānyapalyam udīcīmudgātre mukhyebhyo grāmavarāndadatītyetadādi
2.7.14.[1]	varuṇastvetyetadādi yajurjapitvā yathādevataṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt yathā dakṣiṇāyā devatāṃ nānoddiśya yathā varuṇāyāśvamiti
2.7.15.[1]	pratigṛhṇīyāditi varttate yā yasya jātistāmādiśya yathāvayave mṛgamiti
2.7.16.[1]	aprāṇacca yadravyaṃ yacca yathājāti pratigṛhṇīyāt na prāṇiti tadaprāṇam anindriyamityarthaḥ
2.7.17.[1]	puṃvanmithunāni gṛhṇīyāt yathā aśvaścāśvī cāśvau puruṣaśca puruṣī ca puruṣau anyatrājābhyaḥ ajāṃstu mithunadharmeṇa na pratigṛhṇīyāt nānādevatātvāt anyaivājāyā devatā anyaivājasya agnaye'jam agniṣomābhyāmajāmiti
2.7.18.[1]	sāvitrāderdakṣiṇāpratigrahamantrasya tenāmṛtatvamaśīya ka idaṃ kasmā adādityupariṣṭājjapaḥ
2.7.19.[1]	tatra tasmin dakṣiṇāpratigrahaṇe ūhāpādīni ūhamāpadyante ūhāpādīni ūhitavyaṃ vyaktivacanaiḥ kā vyaktiḥ strīpuṃnapuṃsakādivacanamekatvaditvabahutvāni nanu adhikṛte mantre tatreti kimartham ucyate, ūhanityatādarśanārthaṃ tatra tasmin mantre sati ūhametānyāpadyante tvāṃ devi dakṣiṇe ada iti ca yat tat syāt tena dātre idaṃ viśa etatte iti ca bhuñjatīti ca bhūyāt hiṃsīriti ca ūho vakṣyate devasya tvā devasya vāṃ devasya vaḥ, varuṇastvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe, varuṇo vāṃ nayatu devo dakṣiṇe varuṇo vo nayatu devyo dakṣiṇaḥ varuṇāyāśvaṃ varuṇāyāśvau varuṇāyāśvān varuṇāyāśve varuṇāyāśvaḥ, tenāmṛtatvamaśīya tābhyāmamṛtatvamaśīya tairamṛtatvamaśīya tayāmṛtatvamaśīya tābhyāmamṛtatvamaśīya tābhiramṛtatvamaśīya, vayaḥśabdasya bhūyācchabdena saha sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ tadyadyapyayaṃ ūhapadeṣu na parisaṃkhyātaḥ tathāpyūhayitavyaḥ bhūyācchandena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt vayodātre bhūyāt vayasī dātre bhūyāstāṃ vayāṃsi dātre bhūyāsuḥ vayodātṛbhyāṃ bhūyāt vayasī dātṛbhyāṃ bhūyāstāṃ vayāṃsi dātṛbhyāṃ bhūyāsuḥ vayodātṛbhyo bhūyāt vayasī dātṛbhyo bhūyāstāṃ vayāṃsi dātṛbhyo bhūyāsuḥ, ka idaṃ kasmā adāt ka ime kasmā adāt ka imāni kasmā adāt ka imaṃ kasmā adāt ka imau kasmā adāt ka imān kasmā adāt ka imāṃ kasmā adāt ka ime kasmā adāt ka imāḥ kasmā adāt, samudramāviśet samudramāviśetāṃ samudramāviśan dvivacanabahuvacanayorlaṅ ādeśāt sūtravidhānāt, kāmaitatte kāmaite te kāmaitāni te kāmaiṣa te kāmaitau te kāmaite te kāmaiṣā te kāmaite te kāmaitāste, kāmāya bhuñjatī bhuñjatyo bhuñjatyaḥ mā mā hiṃsīḥ mā mā hiṃsiṭam mā mā hiṃsiṣṭa
2.7.20.[1]	yadyaśvarathaṃ dadyād yajamānaḥ tamaśvarathamudgātā āgnīdhrīyasya pūrve pradeśe samīpe sthāpayitvā purastājjapañjapitvā purastājjapa uktaḥ devasya tveti darbhamuṣṭināśvamukhānāṃ saṃmārjanaṃ kuryāt dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāmaśvanāmabhyāṃ ekaikasyāśvasya aśvo'sītyetatprabhṛtibhiraśvanāmabhiḥ udaksaṃsthandakṣiṇopakramam evaṃ dhānañjapya ācārya āha
2.7.21.[1]	dhuri yuktau dhuryau aśvau tau prathamaṃ saṃskuryādityaparaṃ vidhānam
2.7.22.[1]	dakṣiṇasyāndhuri yoyuktastaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃskuryāt paścāduttaramiti
2.7.23.[1]	yathā dhuryau tenaiva krameṇa praṣṭī saṃskuryāt pārśvavarttinau praṣṭī
2.7.24.[1]	sarvāṇyaśvanāmāni aṣṭāvapi ekaikasminnaśve prayuñjīta dakṣiṇādārabhyānantaryeṇa udaksaṃsthamiti śāṇḍilya ācārya āha
2.7.25.[1]	sarvairaṣṭābhiraśvanāmabhirekāśvasya dakṣiṇasya mukhaṃ saṃmṛjyāt tūṣṇīmitarāṇi saṃmṛjyāt udaksaṃsthameva ityaparaṃ vidhānam
2.7.26.[1]	etānyevāśvanāmāni aśvāsu aśvatareṣu ca aśvatarīṣu ca yathārthamūhet yadyaśvābhiryuktaḥ syāt aśvatarairvā aśvatarībhirvā tatra tatra yathāsambhavamūhet ūha ucyate aśvāsi antyāsi mayyasi hayāsi vājinyasi saptinyasi vṛṣṇyasi arvatyasi iti aśvataro'si śeṣāṇyaśvavat aśvataryasi śeṣāṇyaśvāvat
2.7.27.[1]	tribhiścedyukto bhavati arddhānyekasmin prayuñjīta arddhāni dvyoḥ dve dve nāmanī pūrvoktenaiva krameṇa dvaidhandvayoḥ yadi dvābhyāṃ yukto bhavati tadā dvidhā nāmāni vibhajya yuñjīta pūrvoktenaiva krameṇa
2.8.1.[1]	ādityānāmityetadyajuḥ rathaśira ālabhya japet śiraḥpravṛttīrathakārebhyo jñeyā
2.8.2.[1]	rathasyedaṃ rathyaṃ yatkiñcidrathāṅgaṃ carmaṇyaṃ carmaṇā nirvṛttaṃ carmaṇyaṃ tadvāyoṣṭvetyanena yajuṣā pratigṛhṇīyāt
2.8.3.[1]	yadasthimayaṃ rathyaṃ tannakṣatrāṇāmityanena yajuṣā pratigṛhṇīyāt
2.8.4.[1]	sūryasyetyanena yajuṣā kārṣṇāyamaṃ yatsyāt rathyaṃ tāmrarajatakāṃsyarītikādibhyo lohebhyo nirvṛttaṃ tat pratigṛhṇīyāt
2.8.5.[1]	anenaiva mantreṇa pratigṛhṇīyāt yadrathyaṃ vakṣyati hiraṇyamiti jātarūpaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāditi mantrāmnānasāmarthyādetasmin krameṇa dravyadevatopadeśaḥ kṛtaḥ pratigrahavidhistu prakaraṇe eva vakṣyate sāmprataṃ rathaśira ālabhyānantaram
2.8.6.[1]	dakṣiṇena rathasya gatvā rathantaramasītyanena yajuṣā dakṣiṇaṃ cakramālabhet
2.8.7.[1]	vāmadevyamasītyanena yajuṣā adhiṣṭhānamālabhet rathamāruhya rathī yat sthānamadhitiṣṭhati tadadhiṣṭhānam
2.8.8.[1]	bṛhadamītyanena yajuṣottaraṃ cakramālabhet
2.8.9.[1]	aṅkānyaṅkū ity anena yajuṣā cakrayoḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kuryāt eveti pravṛttāvadhāraṇaṃ kriyate
2.8.10.[1]	vaiśvānara ityanena yajuṣā dakṣiṇena pādena prathamamārohet
2.8.11.[1]	ubhābhyāmāruhya gidaiṣata ityetad yajurjapet
2.8.12.[1]	kṛśetyanena yajuṣā yau rathasya savye pārśve'śvau tayoraśmīnāyacchet āyatan kuryāt raśmīniti bahuvacanamubhayato raśmayo bhavantyaśvānām
2.8.13.[1]	dāsetyanena yajuṣā dakṣiṇayoraśvayoraśmīnavagṛhṇīyāt avagrahaṇamātraṃ nātyantaṃ gacchet
2.8.14.[1]	avatīrya rathāt sakṛdvāruṇaṃ yajuruktvā yathādevatamādiśya uktaṃ vāyoriti carmaṇyaṃ pratigṛhṇīyādityetadādi dravyāmāmaśvānāṃ rathasya gautama ācārya āha
2.8.15.[1]	saṃmārjanaprabhṛtyavarohaṇāntaṃ etat sarvaṃ kṛtvā vimucyāśvau nānā ekaikasmin dravye purastājjapopariṣṭājjapo bhavetāṃ vāruṇantu yajuḥ aśvārthameva syādrathārthañceti evaṃ dhānañjapya ācārya āha
2.8.16.[1]	yady etat karma notsahedyathādeśaṃ kartuṃ tadā audumbaryāmevopaviṣṭa etat sarvaṃ japet
2.8.17.[1]	yadi pṛṣṭhyamaśvandadyād yajamānaḥ pṛṣṭhena vahatīti pṛṣṭhyaḥ, tadā purastājjapaṃ japitvā prāgvāruṇāt mantrādaśvanāmāni japet
2.8.18.[1]	prāgiti prakṛtam
2.8.19.[1]	tathā adānteṣvaśveṣu yathā pṛṣṭhyaḥ tena prakāreṇetyarthaḥ
2.8.20.[1]	rathyamiva rathyaṃ carmaṇyādi yaddravyaṃ rathena tulyaṃ tena tat pratigṛhṇīyāt
2.8.21.[1]	annasyānnapatirityetadyajuḥ prāgvāruṇat mantrādaveḥ pratigrahe japet, nanu tat kimidaṃ prāgvāruṇāditi yadā prāgeva vāruṇāt mantrādayaṃ mantraḥ paṭhitaḥ ucyate vikalpārthaṃ vakṣyati purastājjapādeti
2.8.22.[1]	vāruṇādvā prāk puratastājjapādvā japet
2.8.23.[1]	gnāstvā kṛtaṃ nityetadyajuḥ vāsasaḥ pratigrahe prāgvāruṇāt syāt purastājjapādvā
2.8.24.[1]	tadā gnāstvā kṛtanniti yajuḥ utkṣipet atāntave vasane yanna tantubhyonirvṛttaṃ tadatāntavaṃ navatādi carmaṇyaṃ kucitrādi
2.8.25.[1]	hiraṇyamalpīyaḥ yasya bhogo nāsti tadaudumbaryāmāśleṣayet
2.8.26.[1]	agnīdhrīye vā taddhiraṇyaṃ juhuyāt na bhogāya kalpet
2.8.27.[1]	ekasmin kratau vrīhiyavān samastān pratigṛhṇīyāt na vyastān na pṛthagityarthaḥ, apare bruvate ekakratāviti jyotiṣṭome etat tadyadāhurekāyajña ityetasmāt
2.8.28.[1]	yathā vrīhiyavān tathā tilamāṣān tena prakāreṇetyarthaḥ pratigṛhṇīyāditi varttate
2.8.29.[1]	yāsāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ devatā anādiṣṭāstāḥ prājāpatyena mantreṇa gṛhṇīyāt prajāpataye gardabhamityetadādivat
2.8.30.[1]	yā ayajñe dakṣiṇāḥ tāsu pratigrahaṇamantro nivarttate ityevaṃ dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate kaḥ punarayajñādhikāra iti ucyate yajñasya udgātre kaściddhiraṇyādikaṃ dadāti yathā hiraṇyamalpīyo bhogādāgacchedādumbaryāmāśleṣayediti yajñasya ṛtvijo deva iti ca kanyāpradānādi tatra tūṣṇīṃ pratigṛhṇīyāditi
2.8.31.[1]	bhūrbhuvaḥ svarityanena pratigṛhṇīyāt evaṃ gautama ācārya āha
2.8.32.[1]	omityevaṃ vā pratigṛhṇīyāt evaṃ manyate gautamaḥ
2.9.1.[1]	dakṣiṇāpratigrahavidhānamuktaṃ sāmpratamanantaraṃ pṛṣṭhyasyopākaraṇaṃ tatsambaddhaṃ prastotṛkarmocate dvau nārāśaṃsau mādhyandine tayoḥ pūrvaṃ bhakṣayitvā āhavanīye'gnau prastotā pṛṣṭhahomaṃ juhuyāt tasminnahani yat pṛṣṭhaṃ syāttadādiśya adaḥ pibatu somyaṃ madhvāyurityetadādinā mantreṇa ada iti sarvanāmasthāne rathantaraṃ pibatvityetadādivat
2.9.2.[1]	pūrvaṃ yathoktena mantreṇa hutvā uttarāṃ svāhākāreṇa juhuyāt
2.9.3.[1]	dvaidhaṃ dvidhā kṛtvā evaṃ juhuyāditi dhānañjapya ācārya āha
2.9.4.[1]	hotṛkapṛṣṭhārthamevamabhisambandhaṃ kṛtvā
2.9.5.[1]	revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ pibatu ityeva ṣaṣṭhe'hani pṛṣṭhādeśaṃ gautama ācāryo manyate mahāvrataṃ pibatvitvevaṃ mahāvrate
2.9.6.[1]	revatyaśca vāravantīyañcetyevaṃ ṣaṣṭe'hani pṛṣṭādeśaṃ dhānañjayo manyate yāvanti sāmāni mahāvrate pṛṣṭhasthāni bhavanti sarveṣām eva parisaṃkhyānaṃ kuryāt pibatu dadhaditi caite pade yathārthamūhet prayogastu revatyaśca vāravantīyañca pibatāṃ somyaṃ madhvāyurdadhatīti śeṣo mantraḥ sāmānyaḥ evaṃ ṣaṣṭhe gāyatrarathantarabṛhadrājanabhadrāṇi pibatu somyaṃ madhvāyurdadhatī dadhantīti cetyevaṃ mahāvrate mantraśeṣaḥ sāmānyaḥ evetyuktam ubhayapakṣeṇāmnātaṃ bhadre pucche yajñāyajñīye ca pucche yathārthaṃ na kevalamevaṃ ṣaṣṭhamahāvratayoḥ yatra catrānekamāmapṛṣṭhatā tatra tatraivamarthasamatvāt
2.9.7.[1]	bṛhatā rathantareṇa vā stoṣyamāṇaḥ stotumicchan udgātā stomayogātpūrvaṃ daśa vyāhṛtīrmanasā dhyāyedairamityetadādyāḥ yathāmnānādeva siddhe daśatve saṃkhyāgrahaṇaṃ kimarthaṃ daśeti cet ucyate anuliṅgaṃ vibhāgo mābhūditi, vyāhṛtigrahaṇaṃ saṃvyavahārārthaṃ vakṣyati ṛcaṃ pūrvaṃ vyāhṛtibhya iti
2.9.8.[1]	rathantara eva kevale ṛcaṃ dhyāyet yaste goṣvityetāṃ evaśabdaḥ anyatra prayukte rathantare mābhūditi ṛcamiti saṃvyavahārārthameva ṛcaṃ pūrvaṃ vyāhṛtībhya iti
2.9.9.[1]	yadetaduta prāk stomayogāddaśa vyāhṛtīrmanasā dhyāyedairamityetadādi etayuktvā stomaṃ brūyāditi śāṇḍilya ācārya śraha ayantu kramaḥ ṛcaṃ pūrvaṃ vyāhṛtībhya iti
2.9.10.[1]	yatpūrvamuktaṃ tat dhānañjapyasya matam
2.9.11.[1]	rathantare sāmni prastūyamāne sarvatra sammīlet yāvatkṛtvaḥ prastuyate tāvatkṛtvaḥ sammīlanaṃ kuryāt atha sarvagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate evaṃ brāhmaṇam īśvaraṃ vai rathantaramudgātuścakṣuḥ pramathitaḥ prastūyamāne saṃmīletsvardṛśaṃ prativīkṣeteti prathamāyāmṛcyasya vidheḥ kriyāṃ darśayati svardṛśaṃ prativīkṣeteti tena yadviṣayameva prativīkṣamāṇamādiśyate tadviṣayamevaṃ sammīlanaṃ gamyate so'yamācāryaḥ sarvatretyevamārabhate kathamuttarayorapi stotrīyayoḥ sammīlanaprativīkṣaṇe bhaveyātāmiti yāvatā rathantaradharmo'yaṃ nāyamugdharmaḥ svardṛśaśabdaḥ kālamātrajñāpakaḥ vakṣyati prāk pratihāraṃ caturakṣaraṃ śiṣṭvā tat sarvatra prativīkṣeteti apare varṇayanti vakṣyatyayaṃ tasyāpṛṣṭhasya sato nivartterandharmā iti tatkathaṃ nivarttamāneṣvanyeṣu dharmeṣu sammīlanaṃ syāditi ataḥ sarvatragrahaṇamiti
2.9.12.[1]	ekaikamudgīthākṣaraṃ manasā dhyāyet stobhairvācā saṃyuñjyāt uktaṃ brāhmaṇe balvalā kurvatā geyamiti etat stobharūpaṃ sūtrakāraḥ śrutyantaraṃ dṛṣṭvā vikalpayati prathamasvarairakārairbhakārādibhirakrāntairiti akṣarāṇāṃ stobhānāñca yugapatkriyāṃ darśayati balbalā kurvatā geyamiti prathamasvarairakāraiḥ uktasvarāḥ prathamadvitīyatṛtīyacaturthamandrātisvāryā iti tairakārairbhakārādibhirbhakāra uccāraṇārthaḥ bhakāraiste akārā uccāryyante akrāntaiḥ akrāntāḥ tān prayuñjīta dvitīyasvarottamaiḥ yasteṣāmuttamo varṇaḥ sa dvitīyena svareṇa syāt
2.9.13.[1]	evaṃ prayujyamānaṃ rathantaraṃ yathādhītaṃ prayuktaṃ bhavatīti evamācakṣate etacchrutyantaraṃ yathādhītaṃ prayoktavyamiti atha eke bruvate eteṣāmeva balvaleti stobhānāṃ anukaraṇambhakāra iti aparā śrutiḥ rathantare tvakṣarambhakārāntaravanti vyañjanāni yathākṣaraṃ darśayet tadyathā svareṇa sarvāṇi vyañjanāni vyāptānyevaṃ sarvān kāmānavāpnoti yaścaivaṃ veda yasyaite svaravantaḥ prayujyante yaścaivaṃ vidvān prayuṅkte yathā cāgnicandrasūryyabhāsvanto'pahatatamaskāstaddudgātṛyajamānau bhavata evaṃ hyāha bhātyagnirbhāti candramā bhāti sūryo bhānti jyotīṃṣi bhāti rathantaramiti bhakārāṇāmeva dīptiṃ darśayati svaravatāṃ rathantarasya stobhānāṃ svaravantaḥ prayoktavyā iti yatra tu vyañjanavantaḥ prayujyeran kṣodhukā ca badhyāyināvaprajasāvudgātṛyajamānau syātāntasmādanvakṣaraṃ prayuñjānaḥ svaravanti vyañjanāni yathākṣaraṃ darśayet ekā śrutiḥ tasmādikalpaḥ syāt
2.9.14.[1]	prāk pratihārāccatvāryyakṣarāṇi śiṣṭvā taccaturakṣaraṃ prativīkṣeta sarvagrahaṇasya prayojanaṃ sammīlanavidhāvevoktam
2.9.15.[1]	stutvā rathantareṇa yajamānaṃ varaṃ prati prerayet
2.9.16.[1]	tasya rathantarasya apṛṣṭhasya sataḥ nivartteran dharmāḥ vyāhṛtyṛgvācādayo dharmāḥ sarve nivartteran ato'sya grahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate tasyeti tasyaiva na bṛhadvāmadevyayostu punarapi rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhayoḥ sato nivartterandharmāḥ tathā sata iti pṛṣṭhagatasya tu rathantarasya guṇabhūtasyāpi sato naiva nivartterandharmāḥ tathā bṛhataḥ
2.9.17.[1]	saha stobhairdharmmā nivarttarannityevaṃ gautama ācāryo manyate nanu sarve evāśeṣeṇa dharmā nivṛttāḥ kutastobhanivṛttiryena gautamastobhānnivarttayatīti ucyate, vakṣyati stobhā evānviyuriti dhānañjapyaḥ iti uktaṃ paramatamanumatamapratiṣiddhamiti tena gautamasyāniṣpṛṣṭā eva stobhakriyāḥ
2.9.18.[1]	sarve'nye dharmāḥ apṛṣṭhasya nivartteran stobhā eva kevalā anviyurityevaṃ dhānañjapyo manyate
