2.9.19.[1]	agniṣṭomasāma vā yadā syāt sandhisāma vā tadā apṛṣṭhamapi stobhet evaṃ śāṇḍilya āha
2.9.20.[1]	sarvatra pṛṣṭhagatañcānyat sthānagatañcāsvastotrīyaṃ na stobhediti sthaviro gautama āha
2.10.1.[1]	bṛhadrathantarayoḥ sāmānyaviśeṣadharmāścoktāḥ sāmprataṃ vāmadevyadharmā vivakṣitāḥ tānvivakṣurāha /
2.10.1.[2]	vāmadevyena stoṣyamāṇa iti vāmadevyena sāmnā stoṣyamāṇaḥ stotumichan pūrvaṃ stomayogāt gāvo aśvā ajā ityetadādi manasā dhyāyet anyo'nyadharma uktaḥ yathākulīputrāniti, atha visamāsaḥ kimarthamiti cet go'śvājāvivrīhiyavān manasā dhyāyet ityevaṃ vaktavyamāsīt ucyate yadyevamavakṣyat tadā gavādīnāṃ dravyāṇaṃ dhyānamabhaviṣyat tadevaṃ mābhūdityata āha ācāryo gāvo aśvā ityetadādi tena kiṃ gāvo aśva ityetadādi mantraṃ manasā dhyāyediti
2.10.2.[1]	brahmasāmni stūyamāne yaḥ kāmo yajamānasya bhavet sa sidhyatvityevaṃ dhyāyan yajamāna upāsīta atra sandehaḥ kiṃ kratukāmasya dhyānaṃ utayathākāmyaṃ kāmasya dhyānamiti ucyate, kratukāmasya dhyānaṃ na yathākāmyaṃ kathametadgamyata iti cet ucyate, uddeśanirdeśābhyāṃ yaḥ sa iti yaḥ kratukāmasta dhyāyediti anyathā hi brahmasāmni yajamānaḥ kāmaṃ dhyāyedityevamavakṣyatsūtram
2.10.3.[1]	tathā itara udgātā yajamānasya kāmaḥ sidhyatvityevaṃ dhyāyannudgāyet
2.10.4.[1]	ārbhavena pavamānena stutvā tārttīyasavanikātpuroḍāśāt ekadeśaṃ gṛhītvā ekaikaṃ piṇḍantrīṃstrīnvā aparayā dvārā paścimayā dvārā havirddhānaṃ praviśya adhastātsvasya camamasya samīpe darbheṣu piṇḍānnidadhyuḥ yasmin kāle āsāditaḥ syāt havirddhāne camasaḥ piṇḍānnidhāya japeyuḥ atra pitaromādadhvaṃ yathā bhāgamāvṛṣāyadhvamiti
2.10.5.[1]	taṃ camasaṃ bhakṣārthamāhriyamāṇaṃ pratimantrayerannamīmadanta pitara ityanena
2.10.6.[1]	somyaṃ carumāhṛtaṃ udgātāvekṣeta āyurme prāṇa ityetadādinā yajuṣā sādhyānāṃ vai devānāṃ satramāsīnānāmityetadādi brāhmaṇaṃ somyasyāvekṣaṇaṃ darśayati udgātṛgrahaṇaṃ ācāryaśailī sarveṣāṃ karmaṇi prakṛte avaśyamudgātṛgrahaṇaṃ karoti
2.10.7.[1]	asya somyāvekṣaṇayajuṣaḥ punarasmāsu dadhmasītyeṣo'ntaḥ atrocyate uttarādiḥ pūrvāntalakṣaṇamiti evaṃ vijñāyamāne mantrasyānte tat kimidaṃ vijñāpanaṃ kriyata iti ucyate vakṣyati taṃ daśame'hanyabhyasyeyuriti tatraitāvanmantrābhyāsapradarśanārthamiti
2.10.8.[1]	tamavekṣaṇamantrasyāntaṃ daśame'hani dvirbrūyuḥ
2.10.9.[1]	āyurme prāṇa ityetasya prāṇamantrasya sthāne yanme yamamityetameke ācāryyā manyante
2.10.10.[1]	tuśabdo vyāvṛttyarthaḥ yadetat pūrvoktamavekṣaṇamantraṃ tenaivāvekṣeta na dvitīyena
2.10.11.[1]	tasminnuttaradhṛte somye carau aṅguṣṭhañca anāmikāṅguliñcāvadhāya akṣiṇī vimṛśet yenāhyājimityetadādinā yajuṣā tasmin grahaṇaṃ yadi pūrveṇa yadyuttareṇāvekṣeta kuryādevaitat
2.10.12.[1]	evamanena vidhinā itarā praṣṭī kuryātām
2.10.13.[1]	eṣa kramaḥ prastotā pūrvaḥ paścāt pratiharttā
2.10.14.[1]	tamavekṣitaṃ somyaṃ pratihartturuttareṇa hṛtvā paścimayā dvārā niṣkrāmayeyuḥ yadi vā brāhmaṇoktena vidhinā prāśnīyāt dakṣiṇā sadaso gatvaitaṃ somyātiśeṣaṃ prāśnīyāditi
2.10.15.[1]	patnī codgātāram īkṣeta
2.10.16.[1]	nidhane ucyamāne patnī pātre'ñjalībhiradbhiḥ svaṃ dakṣiṇamūrumabhiṣiñcet tat dakṣiṇānūrūnabhiṣiñcanta iti hi brāhmaṇam
2.10.17.[1]	tṛtīyāyāṃ stotrīyāyāṃ prastutāyāṃ patnī svasminnūrau sarvantadudakaṃ ninayet sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī utpattistotrīyāyāṃ karmastotrīyāyāṃ prastutāyāmiti vivadante tṛtīyāśabdena karmastotrīyāyāṃ nyāyyataram
2.10.18.[1]	stotrasyottamāyāṃ stotrīyāyāṃ bhuvadvājāyi bhuvadvājeṣviti evamabhyāsaṃ kuryāt asya caturakṣarasyābhyāse sati nāmiti ca nidhanaṃ kuryāt yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇam anuṣṭubhamuttamāṃ sampādayatīti akṣareṇāntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpyamiti ca
2.10.19.[1]	anabhyāsamevācāryā manyante caturakṣarasya nidhanañca yathāmnāyameva kuryurityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryo manyate anabhyāsañceti caśabdaḥ tuśabdo hetvarthaḥ ko hetuḥ yasmātpakṣopanyāsabrāhmaṇamevedaṃ prakaraṇādito vā iti hi
2.10.20.[1]	tadyajñāyajñīyaṃ yadā yasmin kāle anuśaṃsan hotāpohiṣṭhīyā ṛcā brūyāt tadā tasmin kāle enaṃ hotāraṃ anvālabheran spṛśeyuḥ apāvṛṇvānāḥ prāvaraṇānyapāsyamānāḥ apāvṛṇvānā iti sarveṣāṃ pūrvaṃ prāvṛtānāṃ kriyāṃ darśayati uktaṃ prāvṛtenodgeyamiti vaiśvānareṇānabhidāhāyeti tat sūtrakāraḥ sarveṣāṃ prāvaraṇaṃ darśayati hetusamatvāt kiṃ hetusamatvam anabhidāhaḥ
2.10.21.[1]	yajñāyajñīyasyāgniṣṭomasāmno'nyasthāne prayujyamānasya sarve dharmā nivartteran
2.10.22.[1]	yadanyadagniṣṭomasāma bhavet tasya dharmā bhaveyuḥ
2.10.23.[1]	ahiṅkāretvagniṣṭomasāmni pratihāravelāyāṃ patnīmudgātā īkṣeta patnī codgātāram
2.10.24.[1]	ye brāhmaṇe ṛcaṃ sāmni pratisannāmā uktāḥ evaṃ kṛtvodgeyaṃ paprīmvayamiti suśaṃsiṣamiti caitān sarveṣvagniṣṭomasāmasu darśayati sarvagrahaṇaṃ pavamānagate'pi yajñāyajñīye bhavati na kevalaṃ yajñāyajñīye apyanyasmin rathantare'pi atha sāmnīti kimarthaṃ ucyate yadā rathantareṣvṛkṣu anyatpṛṣṭhaṃ kriyate tattadāpi asyuṣa iti susṭuṣa iti vā sannāmayet
2.11.1.[1]	tṛtīyasavane sarveṣu stotreṣu samāpteṣu bhakṣayitvā camasaṃ stomavimocanaṃ kuryuḥ ṛtasya tvetyanena yajuṣā, natu tat kimidaṃ tṛtīyasavanagrahaṇaṃ yadā sarveṣu stotreṣu samāpteṣvityuktam ucyate idantāvadyajurupari sandhibhakṣātmamāmnātaṃ tatra vimocanaṃ yajuṣā tasminneva krame prāpnoti ataḥ tṛtīyasavanagrahaṇaṃ tāvatkrayate kathaṃ na kevalamupari sandhibhakṣāt stomavimocanaṃ syāt yasyāṃ yasyāṃ saṃsthāyāṃ kratuḥ samāpyate tasyāntasyāṃ saṃsthāyāṃ syāditi atha sarvagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet stotreṣviti bahuvacanasāmarthyātsiddhe sarvatve idamucyate idaṃ stomavimocanaṃ kratvantastotre dṛṣṭaṃ pratistotrañca stomayojanaṃ bhavati yuktasya ca vimocanaṃ bhavatyeva tasya ca yuktasya stomasya yasmin kāle vimocanamityeṣa saṃśayaḥ ataḥ sarvagrahaṇaṃ karotyācāryaḥ kathaṃ pūrveṣvapi stotreṣu ekaikasmin stotre bhakṣayitvā stomaṃ vimuñceyuḥ atra tu tṛtīyasavane kathamiti
2.11.2.[1]	saṃlobhanaṃ ekatrīkaraṇaṃ kuryuḥ
2.11.3.[1]	yajamānavācanādanantaraṃ yadetat stutasya stutamasīti yajamānavācanaṃ etasmādanantaraṃ etat karma kuryāt tadvakṣyate atra vā asmin kāle kuśānāṃ saṃlobhanaṃ kṛtvā kuryuḥ iti vikalpaḥ tantave mā jyotiṣetyuktvā asāvanumātanuhi jyotiṣeti yathājyeṣṭhaṃ putrāṇaṃ nāmāni gṛhṇīyāt asāviti sarvanāmasthāne nāma gṛhṇīyāt yo yo jyeṣṭho yathājyeṣṭhaṃ prayogastu tantave mā jyotiṣā yajñadatta anumātanuhi viṣṇumitra anumātanuhi somabhūte anumātanuhi jyotiṣā apare pratyekaṃ purastājjapopariṣṭājjapau kurvanti
2.11.4.[1]	ajāteṣu putreṣu janiṣyamāṇa iti sarvanāmasthāne kuryāt prayogastu tantave mā jyotiṣā janiṣyamāṇa anumātanuta jyotiṣā ajātaputrasyaiṣa kalpaḥ apare bruvate jātaputro'pi putrāṇāṃ nāmāni gṛhītvā janiṣyamāṇa iti gṛhṇīyāt āśīryogatvāt janiṣyamāṇa ityajāteṣviti pratipattiriyamiti
2.11.5.[1]	jāteṣu ajāteṣu ca putreṣu satreṣu putrā ityevaṃ nāmagrahaṇaṃ prayogaḥ tantave mā jyotiṣā putrā anumātanuta jyotiṣā yadyekaḥ kuryāt tathāpi bahuvacanaṃ kuryyāt no'haṃ kuryyāt
2.11.6.[1]	vaṣaṭkṛte hāriyojanasya haviṣaḥ hāriyojanasyetyavayavalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī yathetaṃ yathāgatamityarthaḥ dakṣiṇenaudumbaryyā gatvā paścimayā dvārā niṣkrāmanto japeyuḥ some hītyetadādi yajuḥ athāparayā dvāreti kimarthaṃ yadā yathetamityukte siddhamevaitat te hi samastopasthānaṃ kṛtvā aparayaiva dvārā praviṣṭāḥ atrocyate visaṃsthite savane pūrvayā dvārā sañcara ityuktaṃ na cātra savanaṃ santiṣṭhate tadyadyaparayeti na brūyāt visaṃsthite sañcareṇa nirgamaṇaṃ syāt evaṃ mābhūdityata āha aparayeti yathetamiti cokte te piṇḍaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ kṛtvā pūrvayā dvārā praviṣṭāḥ tatraiṣo'pi sañcaro gamyetāparayetyanucyamāne
2.11.7.[1]	subhūrasītyanena yajuṣā ādityamupatiṣṭheran
2.11.8.[1]	yadyastamitaḥ syādādityaḥ tato'nena yajuṣā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭheran ko'sya viṣayaḥ ṣoḍaśīvājapeyau anyasmiṃśca kālātikrame
2.11.9.[1]	āgnīdhrīye'gnau juhuyurgatyānupūrveṇa apāṃ puṣyamityanena yajuṣā pūrvāmāhutiṃ juhuyāt svāhākāreṇottarāṃ athāhutī iti dvivacanena dvitve siddhe kimidaṃ saṃkhyāgrahaṇaṃ dve iti ucyate niyamārtham ekaṃ anena hiraṇyamalpīyo bhogādāgacchedaudumbaryāmāśleṣayedāgnīdhrīye vā juhuyāditi tasya hiraṇyasyāyaṃ homakālaḥ yāsau dvitīyā āhutistasyāmeva hiraṇyaṃ prakṣipya juhuyāditi
2.11.10.[1]	hāriyojanya iti saṃjñā dhānānāṃ droṇakalaśe tāḥ sthāpitā bhavantyadhvaryubhiḥ somamiśrāḥ tāsāṃ dhānānāmavayavamudgātā ādadānaḥ samupahūtā bhakṣayiṣyāma iti brūyāt ādānaṃ grahaṇam
2.11.11.[1]	tathetarau yathodgātā kuryyāt tenaiva vidhinetarau praṣṭī kuryyātām
2.11.12.[1]	unnetari ityadhikaraṇasaptamī upahavamiṣṭvā upahavaṃ yācitvā hāriyojanasya ta ityetena yajuṣā yadvakṣyate tat kuryuḥ tirohyasyetyatirātre etadadhikaṃ kuryyuḥ yathādhītaṃ vā sarvatra atirātre cānatirātre ca dvirupaghrāya āhavanīyasya paścime pradeśe paridhīnāmabhyantarato nivapeyuḥ nāgnau
2.11.13.[1]	yadi paridhayaḥ anuprakṛtāḥ prakṣiptā agnau bhavanti tadā bhasmānte samīpe nirvapeyuḥ
2.11.14.[1]	upadhānāt anantaraṃ apaḥ spṛṣṭvā ekaikaḥ aṣṭau aṣṭau śakalāni āhavanīye prakṣipeyuḥ devakṛtasyetyetatprabhṛtibhirmantraiḥ ikārāntairiti mantrāntajñāpanārtham
2.11.15.[1]	sarvān mantrānuktvā sakṛdeva sarvāṇi sakalāni uttamena mantreṇa prakṣipeyuriti śaucivṛkṣirācārya āha
2.11.16.[1]	apsu ṣomā iti saṃjñā te apsu ṣomāścamasāścātvālasannikṛṣṭe deśe adbhiḥ pūrṇā sthāpitā bhavanti teṣu haritāni tṛṇāni prāstāni bhavantyadhvaryubhiḥ
2.11.17.[1]	te udgātāraḥ svakīyacamasasannidhāvupaviśya dakṣiṇena pāṇinā spṛṣṭvā apsu dhautetyetadādi yajurjapeyuḥ
2.11.18.[1]	madhumantamityanena yajuṣā pāṇīnupajigheran
2.11.19.[1]	śamadbhya ityanena yajuṣā udaṅmukhaṃ camasaṃ kṛtvā tatsthā āpaḥ nīcaiḥ camasaiḥ bhūmau ninayeyuḥ
2.11.20.[1]	kāmetyanena yajuṣā abhimukhamātmanaḥ camasasāvarttayeyuḥ
2.11.21.[1]	ūrgityanena yajuṣā uraḥsu pāṇīnnidadhīran nidhānaṃ sthāpanam
2.11.22.[1]	prāṇasometyanena yajuṣā mukhyān prāṇānabhimṛśeran mukhe bhavā mukhyāḥ prāṇa indriyāṇi akṣiṇī nāsike karṇāviti
2.11.23.[1]	āgnīdhrīyapariśritaṃ gatvā dadhibhakṣaṃ bhakṣayeyurasamupahūya dadhikrāvṇa iti anayā ṛcā asamupahūyeti samupahvānapūrvakāḥ sarve bhakṣā vihitāḥ tadiha bhūyastvaṃ gṛhītvā pravartteta tasya pratiṣedhaḥ asamupahūyeti
2.12.1.[1]	agniṣṭapatīti stobhaliṅgena avabhṛthasāmādeśaḥ ukto grahaṇena ceti
2.12.2.[1]	tasyāvabhṛthasāmna āvṛdvidhiḥ yathā prathamasya pravargyasya sāmnaḥ yena prakāreṇetyarthaḥ prathamaṃ pravargyasāma tyagnāyirityetat atha tasyeti kimarthamiti cet ucyate avabhṛthasāmāntarāṇyupadekṣyante abhiṣecanīyāśca trirātrayoḥ tadarthaṃ tasya grahaṇam
2.12.3.[1]	tasyāvabhṛthasāmnaḥ sarva ṛtvijo nidhanaṃ brūyuḥ sarvagrahaṇaṃ yathā prathamasya pravargyasāmnaḥ ityuktaṃ tasmiṃśca gharmopayuktānāṃ nidhanopapattiḥ tanmābhūdataḥ sarvagrahaṇaṃ kathamiha sarveṣāmṛtvijānnidhanopapattiḥ syāditi
2.12.4.[1]	abhiṣecanīye kratau iṣṭāhotrīyamavabhṛthasāma syāt
2.12.5.[1]	samasyeti vāvabhṛthasāma syādityabhiṣecanīye iṣṭāhotrīyaṃ veti vikalpayati
2.12.6.[1]	uktamahīneṣu dadhibhakṣāntānyahāni prāgudayanīyādatirātrāditi ca ayamaśvatrirātre viśeṣaḥ nānāvabhṛthānyahānīti nānā pṛthagityarthaḥ
2.12.7.[1]	teṣāmāśvamedhikānāmahnāṃ prathamasyāhnaḥ sanādagna ityetadavabhṛthasāma syāt avabhṛthasāmagrahaṇaṃ tatra sāmamātraṃ na kṛtsno'vabhṛtha iti
2.12.8.[1]	yadā uviṣyatirityetat sāma dvitīyasyāhno'vabhṛthasāmeti prakṛtaṃ tyagnāyiriti vā vikalpaḥ tṛtīyasya siddhaṃ prākṛtam
2.12.9.[1]	avabhṛtheṣṭau samāptāyāṃ avabhṛthanicuṃpuṇetyetadādinā yajuṣā yāścāvabhṛtheṣṭiṃ kurvanti tāḥ spṛṣṭvā snātvā nirabhyukṣeran kriyābhyāse sakṛnmantra ityuktam
2.12.10.[1]	abhyukṣaṇānantaraṃ ādityamupatiṣṭheran udvayantamamasparītyetadādinā mantreṇa
2.12.11.[1]	yadyastamita ādityaḥ syāt tadāhavanīyamupatiṣṭheran udvayantamasasparītyetayarcā viśeṣa uktaḥ prāgeva prastamitaścedgārhapatyamityetasmin
2.12.12.[1]	tasminnāhavanīye sarve samidha ādadhyuḥ ādhānaṃ prakṣepaḥ edhosyedhiṣīmahītyetadādibhiryathoddiṣṭairmantraiḥ atha tasminniti kimarthamiti cet yadāstamitaścedāhavanīyamityadhikṛta evāhavanīyaḥ atrocyate upasthite cānupasthite ca tasminsamidha ādadhyureva anyathā tasyopasthāne sati samidādhānaṃ syāt
2.12.13.[1]	tamevāhavanīyamupatiṣṭheran apo adyānvacāriṣamityetadādinā mantreṇa apśabdena somamupacarati somamiṣṭvā bhakṣayanti tameveti prakṛtāvadhāraṇam ādityasya samupasthānamuktam ataḥ tamevāhavanīyamityavadhārayanti
2.12.14.[1]	satreṣu udayanīyādatirātrātpūrvāṇi yānyahāni teṣu dadhibhakṣādikarmaśeṣo na bhavati
2.12.15.[1]	ahīneṣu dadhibhakṣāntānyahāni bhavanti prāgudayanīyādatirātrāditi varttate
2.12.16.[1]	yāvantyahāni rājānaṃ somaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ ṛtvijastāvat svabrājñaṇayocchiṣṭaṃ na dadyuḥ adbhirvā prokṣya chādanaṃ kṛtvā dadyuḥ kimidam ucyate, śrutyantareṣu dṛṣṭaṃ rājanyavaiśyayoḥ somabhakṣābhāvo bhakṣaviśeṣāmnānāditi evaṃ vidhiṃ sūtrakāraḥ prakārāntareṇa darśayāmāsa
2.12.17.[1]	tadeṣa śloka iti etamevārthamanuvadati somametat pibatetyetadādinā ślokena
2.12.18.[1]	yo'yaṃ mantravidhiścādigrahaṇenetyetadādividhiḥ parikrānta etaṃ sarvakratuṣu jānīyāt, nanu uktaḥ sarvakratvadhikāra iti tat kimidaṃ punarucyate sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi ucyate antaprajñāpanārthaṃ kathaṃ atha vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāra iti etadādividherayamanta iti etaṃ sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi apara āha, sarvakratoradhikāraḥ sarvakratvadhikāra iti sarvakratuḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ kutaḥ śruteḥ eṣa vā prathamo yajñānāmityuktvāha yathā vā idamagnerjātādagnayo vijñayanta evametasmādadhyanye yajñā vihriyanta ityuktvāha yo hi trivṛdanyaṃ yajñakratumāpadyate sa tandīpayatītyetadādyuktvāha etadyadāhureko yajña ityetaddhi sarve jyotiṣṭomā bhavantīti etadvidhānamāpadyamānāḥ sarve jyotiṣṭomā bhavantīti sarvakratuṣu jyotiṣṭomaḥ tadādāveva sarvakratvadhikāra iti jyotiṣṭomādhikāraḥ teṣāṃ punaruktadoṣo nāsti evaṃ jyotiṣṭomavidhiṃ sarvakratuṣu vidyāt adhikavidheśca pratyāhāraṃ kuryāt
3.1.1.[1]	uktaṃ sārvakratukaṃ sāmānyavidhānaṃ sāmprataṃ ṣoḍaśino guṇavidhānamucyate sārvakratuko'yaṃ ṣoḍaśī daśarātrike caturtho'hanyutpannaḥ atraiva cāsya hiraṇyaṃ sampradānaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvata ityevamādayo dharmmāḥ paṭhitāḥ teṣāṃ vidhānaṃ vivakṣurāha ṣoḍaśisāmnā stoṣyamāṇa iti, nanu uktaṃ tvayā caturthe'hani ṣoḍaśī utpanna iti tat prakaraṇe caiva dharmā vaktavyāḥ syuḥ tat kimidaṃ viprakaraṇe guṇavidhānam ārabhyata iti yadā ca tasminneva prakaraṇe yasmādanyo na paro asti jāta ityetadādi mantraṃ vidhāyoktam udgātā grahamavekṣeta iti idañcāvekṣaṇavidhānaṃ kimarthamiti cet atrocyate tadidam avekṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇe stotrānte uktaṃ tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ kālaṃ prati tāvat kiṃ tasminneva kāle'vekṣaṇamathānyasminniti tathā kiṃ havirddhānasthasyeva athāvekṣaṇapravṛttiḥ sadasīti avekṣaṇaṃ hi sadasi pravṛttaṃ somānāṃ saumyasya ca tathā ete dharmā hiraṇyasampradānādayaḥ caturthotpādāḥ ayañca ṣoḍaśī prakaraṇāntareṣvapi śrūyate sarvastomātirātrādiṣu tat kimete dharmāḥ prakaraṇasyasya bhavanti uta prakaraṇāntareṣvapi ṣoḍaśinaṃ bhajata iti kutaḥ punarayaṃ saṃśayaḥ ucyate, aprākṛtatvāt ṣoḍaśinaḥ tena kiṃ prākṛto hi vidhirvyakṛtīrbhajata aprākṛtastu na vacanādvikṛtīrbhajata iti ato'yamācārya etānmohān parititīrṣuḥ sārvakratukānantaraṃ ṣoḍaśino vidhānamārabhate katham etaṃ sārvakratukaṃ vidhānaṃ ṣoḍaśinaḥ syāditi yadi hyetaṃ vidhānamācāryaḥ prakaraṇa āmnāyasya tadviṣayamevābhaviṣyat tanmābhūdato viprakaraṇa ārambhaḥ ṣoḍaśisāmnā stoṣyamāṇaḥ yathāsanamupaviśya havirddhānaṃ gatvā ṣoḍaśigrahamavekṣeta udgātā yasmādanya iti eṣa padānāṃ vicchedaḥ artho vakṣyate ṣoḍaśisāmneti karttṛkaraṇalakṣaṇā tṛtīyā stoṣyamāṇa iti bhaviṣyatkālopadeśaḥ yathāsanamupaviśya saṃsthāyāsane niḥsṛpya samastopasthānaṃ kṛtvā kṛtsnena vā akṛtvā vā svasminnāsana upaviśya havirddhānaṃ gatvā ṣoḍaśigrahamavekṣeta udgātā yasmādanya ityanena mantreṇa, nanu ṣoḍaśisāmneti sāmagrahaṇaṃ kimarthaṃ yadāyaṃ ṣoḍaśiśabdaḥ kṛte'pi sāmagrahaṇāt stotravācī bhaviṣyatyeva ayaṃ hi ṣoḍaśiśabdaḥ triṣu varttate stotre grahe saṃsthāyāmiti stotre tāvat yogāya trīṣu dvipadāṣu bṛhatā ṣoḍaśinā stuta iti grahe prātaḥsavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītaṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayatīti sva āyatane ṣoḍaśī gṛhyata iti ca saṃsthāyāṃ so'bravīt ṣoḍaśī te'yaṃ yajñakraturastviti so'yaṃ ṣoḍaśiśabdaḥ prayujyamāna stotragrahasaṃsthāsu ityarthāt pratīyate tadiha ṣoḍaśinā stoṣyamāṇa ityukte ṛte'pi sāmagrahaṇāt stavanasāmarthyāt sāmneti gamyata eva tat kimidaṃ sāmagrahaṇamiti atrocyate asya ṣoḍaśina ukthānantaravidhānaṃ tasminneva krame dharmāḥ prāpnuvanti idañca ṣoḍaśīsāmasaṃsthāntare'pi prayujyate tadasyānyasmin sthāne prayujyamānasya dharmā bhavanti uta netyeṣa saṃśayaḥ so'yamācāryaḥ sāmagrahaṇaṃ karoti kathaṃ sthānāntare'pi prayujyamānasya dharmā bhaveyuriti kva punarasya sthānāntare prayogaḥ atyagniṣṭome ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇīyāditi
3.1.2.[1]	yo'yaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahasyāvekṣaṇe vidhiruktaḥ ṣoḍaśisāmnā stoṣyamāṇa ityetadādi tenaiva prātaḥsavane'pyavekṣeta yadi prātaḥsavane'pi gṛhyeta prātaḥsavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītantaṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayati
3.1.3.[1]	yadyuttarayorapi savanayorgṛhṇīyuḥ tayorapyanenaiva prakāreṇāvekṣeta
3.1.4.[1]	uktaḥ aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa upatiṣṭhati sāmyekṣyāyai tasya sthānanirddeśaḥ kriyate aśva iti pratītapadārthakaḥ śabdaḥ kṛṣṇa iti varṇanirdeśaḥ pūrvasyāṃ sadaso dvāri pratyaṅmukhastiṣṭhediti dhānañjapyaḥ ācārya āha
3.1.5.[1]	aparasyāṃ sadaso dvāri prāṅmukho'śvastiṣṭhedevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācārya āha
3.1.6.[1]	kṛṣṇasyāśvasyābhāve śyāvaḥ syāt śyāva ityanirukto varṇaḥ na kṛṣṇo na śvetaḥ tayorantareṇa varttate
3.1.7.[1]	tasyābhāvaḥ tadabhāvaḥ taditi pūrvanirddeśaḥ tasya śyāvāśvasyā bhāve yaḥ kaścāśvaḥ syāt atha yaḥ kaśca iti siddhe kiṃ punaraśvagrahaṇamadhikaṃ kriyate'śva iti ucyate, anyatrāpyabhāve yaḥ kaścāśvaḥ syāt yathā tasmā amumādityamaśvaṃ śvetaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇamānayanniti tathā aśvaśyāvo dakṣiṇā sahyaniruktaḥ sabrahmaṇe deya iti tatrāpi śvetaśyāvayorabhāve yaḥ kaścāśvaḥ syāt
3.1.8.[1]	yadyaśvo na syāt gaurvājo vā bhavet athehāśvagrahaṇaṃ punaḥ kimartham ucyate, tadabhāve yaḥ kaścāśva ityuktaṃ śvetaśyāvayorapyabhāve madyaktopahavyayoḥ yaḥ kaścāśva iti tayorapi gaurvājo vāśvābhāva iti prāpnoti tannivṛtyarthamaśvagrahaṇaṃ karoti, kathaṃ, ṣoḍaśinyeva gaurvājo vāśvābhāve bhavet na tathātayorapīti
3.1.9.[1]	uta hiraṇyasampradānaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvata iti tadvivekārthamāha, yo yaḥ ṣoḍaśisāmnaḥ aṅgaṃ brūyāt sa sa hiraṇyaṃ dhārayet svasyāṃ svasyāṃ bhakto
3.1.10.[1]	udgātā nidhanaṃ bruvatsu taṃ hiraṇyaṃ dhārayet
3.1.11.[1]	sarve vā hiraṇyamabhimṛśeyurnidhanamupayantaḥ
3.1.12.[1]	avasarpatyāditye ṣoḍaśisāmnaḥ prathamaṃ paryāyaṃ gāyet channam aprakāśam ava adhobhāve sṛgatau nanu kathametadgamyate yathā avasarpatyāditya iti ucyate upariṣṭādvakṣyatyastamite tṛtīyamāviriti
3.1.13.[1]	vigate site visite vigate śukle varṇe dvitīyaṃ paryāyaṃ gāyenmadhyamena svareṇa
3.1.14.[1]	astaṅgate āditye tṛtīyaṃ paryāyaṃ gāyet prakāśam
3.1.15.[1]	iha prathamaṃ kālaniyamaḥ kṛtaḥ avasarpati prathamaṃ paryāyamityetadādi so'yaṃ vikalpayati yadā yasmin kāle upākuryuradhvaryavaḥ tasminneva kāle stuvīran na svaṃ kālamādriyeran apare viniveśaṃ varṇayanti sandhikāle ṣoḍaśini atyagniṣṭome'hani atirātre rātrāviti, apare bruvate vicāritaṃ, kimarthamidam ṣoḍaśina udgāturiti ucyate atrācāryyāṇamubhayathā pratipattiḥ yeṣāmaharante teṣāmahanyupākaraṇaṃ yeṣāṃ rātrī teṣāṃ rātrāviti ato'yamācārya ārabhate yadopākuryuḥ tadā aprakāśaṃ stuvīranneveti atha tatra kaḥ svara ityucyate
3.1.16.[1]	yadāhanyupākuryuḥ tadā aprakāśaṃ stuvīran rātrau prakāśam
3.1.17.[1]	udgātre dadyād yajamānaḥ aśvahiraṇye aśvaśca hiraṇyañcāśvahiraṇye dakṣiṇavatsu yajñeṣu atha dakṣiṇavatsviti kimartham adakṣiṇeṣu dānaprasaṅga eva nāsti ucyate, paśyatyayaṃ satreṣvaṅgadakṣiṇāprasaṅga tena satyapyaṅgadakṣiṇāprasaṅge satreṣu ṣoḍaśinyaśvahiraṇye nivarttayati
3.1.18.[1]	ṣoḍaśigrahasya satra eva bhakṣayeyuḥ nekāhāhīneṣu aindraṃ saha ityanena yajuṣā udasya harivadaharikāsu stuvīran yo'smin yajuṣi harivacchandaḥ tam utkṣipya utsṛjya yadyaharikāsu ṛkṣu ṣoḍaśinaṃ stuvīran atha punaḥ harivatīṣu sṭuvīran naiva harivacchandamudasyeyuḥ harivat kṛtameva mantraṃ prayuñjīran atraivaśabdaḥ kimarthaṃ satra eveti ucyate, na kevalaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahasya anye ye grahāsteṣāmapi ca satra eva bhakṣayeyuḥ naikāhāhīneṣu etasyānyatarasmin tryahe nigrāhyāṇāṃ dravyānāṃ bhakṣayeyurityetadādinā
3.1.19.[1]	ṣoḍaśini stotre yaścamasaḥ tasyānuṣṭupcchandasā bhakṣayeyuḥ
3.1.20.[1]	mantreṇa camamasya bhakṣayeyuḥ aindraṃ maha ityanena udasya harivadaharikāsu stuvīrannityanuṣajyata eva
3.1.21.[1]	tathā kurvan pūrveṇa mantreṇa camamasya bhakṣaṇam indraśca samrāḍvaruṇasya rājetyetadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa grahasya bhakṣayeyuḥ
3.1.22.[1]	indramiddharivadityetayarcā vāgdevī somasya pibatvityetadadhikayā bhakṣayediti vikalpaḥ
3.1.23.[1]	vājapeyasāmni triṣṭupcchandasā ityeva chanda ādeśaṃ kṛtvā bhakṣayediti gautama ācārya āha tacchandastvāt stotrasva
3.1.24.[1]	anuṣṭupcchandasā vājapeyasāmni bhakṣayediti dhānañjapyaśāṇḍilyāvācāryāvāhatuḥ yadūrddhvamukthebhyaḥ anuṣṭubhaḥ sabhāga iti anuṣṭupcchandasā rātrau
3.1.25.[1]	na bhakṣayeyuḥ anuṣṭubhatvāt rātreḥ
3.1.26.[1]	pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ nānātṛcebhyaḥ sandhau hiṃkuryuḥ nānādaivatyatvāttṛcānām
3.1.27.[1]	iṣṭayajuṣa ityanena yajuṣā sandhau bhakṣyaḥ
3.1.28.[1]	atiriktastotreṣu gāyatracchandasā bhakṣaṇamiti evaṃ gautama ācāryyo manyate samāpteṣu bhakṣachandaḥsu punarupakrame ko'nyo gāyatryāt syāditi
3.1.29.[1]	yāni catvāri bhakṣachandāṃsi taiḥ pṛthak pṛthak ānupūrvyeṇa caturṣvanavekṣya tadānupūrvyeṇa bhakṣayeyuriti dhānañjapyaśāṇḍilyāvācāryāvāhatuḥ sambhavācca sarveṣāṃ bhakṣachandasām arthācca, ko'rthaḥ agnyādīnāṃ devatānāñca chandobhāvāt
3.1.30.[1]	mantreṇa bhakṣayeyuḥ anuṣṭupbhāganimittatvāt yadūrddhvamukthebhyaḥ anuṣṭubhaḥ sabhāga iti
3.1.31.[1]	achandasā vā mantreṇa bhakṣayeyuḥ upayuktatvāt bhakṣyachandasām
3.1.32.[1]	yathā vā mantrī tathā vā bhakṣayeyuḥ pravṛttatvāt mantrasya anupadeśādvānyeṣām
3.2.1.[1]	uktāḥ ṣoḍaśino dharmāḥ somasya ca bhakṣavidhānamuktaṃ yāvadatiriktastotrāṇīti sāmpratamupari bhakṣavidhānamucyate āhitāgniḥ āhitā agnayo yena sa āhitāgniḥ somayājī yena somena iṣṭāṃ sa somayājī na somayājī asomayājī param anyaṃ somena yājayitvā aparibhakṣaṃ kurvīta aparibhakṣa iti karmaṇaḥ saṃjñā parasyāgniṣu yena somo bhakṣitaḥ tena svāgnayaḥ paribhakṣitāḥ pitaraśca tadaparibhakṣārthamidaṃ karmārabhyate nanu āhitāgnigrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti yadā avakṣyadasomayājīti nahyanāhitāgneḥ somayāgaḥ syāt anyārthena vāhitāgnitvaṃ vijñāpyate iha gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyeṣu ājyādhiśrayaṇadrapsānidhānājyagrahaṇānyādekṣyante hutāyāṃ prātarāhutāvājyaṃ gārhapatye'dhiśrityodagudvāsayet kaṃse camase vā drapsānavadhāya dakṣiṇāgnāvupasādayet sphyadarbhamuṣṭī ca paścimena gārhapatyaṃ gatvā paścādāhavanīyasyopaviśya sruveṇa srucyājyaṃ gṛhṇīyādyāvadgṛhītī syāditi asya ca karmaṇo nāntareṇāhitāgneḥ prasiddhiḥ tadevamarthādāhitāgnitve siddhe yaducyate āhitāgnirityetadanarthakaṃ tasmādāhitāgnigrahaṇaṃ na karttavyaṃ kriyamāṇe kāraṇaṃ vaktavyam ucyate, yadyāhitāgnigrahaṇaṃ na kuryyāt anāhitāgneryājanaprasaṅgo na syāt so'yamāhitāgnigrahaṇaṃ karoti āhitāgnirasomayājī paraṃ somena yājayitvā itthaṃ karma kuryāt anāhitāgniryājayitvāpi paraṃ na vedaṃ kuryyāt yāvatā tasyāgnayo naiva santi yeṣāmaparibhakṣārthannaivedaṃ karma kriyate athāsomayājīti kimarthaṃ yāvatā vakṣyati somayājyapīti śāṇḍilya iti somayājigrahaṇaṃ kathamucyate aniṣṭaprathamasyedaṃ karma syāt iti somayājī hi anāhitāgnirapi bhavati satreṣu tathāpyasāvasomayājyeva atha paragrahaṇaṃ kimarthaṃ yadā yājayitva siddhametat paramiti ucyate, paragrahaṇaṃ parameva yājayitvā na pitaraṃ vā putraṃ vā bhrātaraṃ veti nirguṇaḥ svajanaḥ ebhyo yo'nyaḥ paraḥ para eva saḥ
3.2.2.[1]	somayājyapyetat karma kuryāditi śāṇḍilyaḥ ācārya āha, sāmpratamasyāparibhakṣasya karmaṇaḥ karttavyatocyate
3.2.3.[1]	hutāyāṃ prātarāhutau ṛte'gnihotre ājyaṃ ghṛtaṃ gārhapatyāgnāvadhiśritya udak udāsayet
3.2.4.[1]	kaṃse vā bhājane dārave vā camase dadhidrapsānavadhāya dadhyavayavān dakṣiṇāgneḥ samīpe sthāpayet
3.2.5.[1]	sphyaśca darbhamuṣṭiśca sphyadarbhamuṣṭī dakṣiṇāgneḥ samīpe sthāpayet
3.2.6.[1]	drapsān sphyadarbhamuṣṭī ca sthāpayitvā anantaraṃ paścimena pradeśena gārhapatyasya gatvā āhavanīyasya paścime pradeśa upaviṣya yattadājyaṃ gārhapatye'dhiśrityodagudvāsitaṃ tasmāt sruveṇa sruci gṛhṇīyāt yāvadgṛhītī sthāt yadi caturgṛhotī yadi pañcagṛhītī
3.2.7.[1]	yadi caturgṛhītaṃ yadi pañcagṛhītaṃ tajjuhuyādimāmagne ityetadādinā yathāsūcitena mantreṇa
3.2.8.[1]	evameva gṛhītvā yadi caturgrahītaṃ yadi pañcagṛhītaṃ apāṃ puṣpamity etadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa juhuyāt
3.2.9.[1]	ājyasya pūrvān grahān gṛhītvā yadi caturgṛhītaṃ trīnājyasya gṛhītvā dadhna uttamaṃ yadi pañcagṛhītaṃ catvāra ājyasya gṛhītvā dadhna uttamaṃ viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ svāheti anena yajuṣā juhuyāt
3.2.10.[1]	dadhno gṛhītāvadānasya avayavaḥ syāt taṃ srucyānīya sruci kṛtvodaṅṅāvṛtya prāśnīyāt tava soma vrate vayamityetadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa
3.2.11.[1]	prāśya dadhiśeṣam ācamya prakṣālya srucaṃ adbhistatkṣaṇaṃ saucaprāpteḥ yathāgataṃ pratyāvrajya dakṣiṇāgneḥ samīpaṃ prācīnāvītitvamuktaṃ gṛhye evaṃ prācīnāvītī bhavatīti tatkṛtvā dakṣiṇāgneḥ dakṣiṇe pradeśe sthaṇḍilaṃ samuhya śodhayitvā adbhiḥ samprokṣya sphyena sakṛdullikhya ullekhanaṃ kṛtvā ulmukaṃ upanidhāya ulmukaṃ lekhāyāḥ samīpe nidhāya darbhānupastīrya apo ninīya darbheṣu amīṣāṃ drapsānānnipṛṇuyāt ye te dadhidrapsāḥ kaṃse camase ca kṛtvā dakṣiṇāgneḥ samīpe sthāpitāḥ teṣāmekadeśaṃ gṛhītvā teṣu darbheṣu nipṛṇuyāt nidadhyāt avamebhya ityanena yathāsūtritena mantreṇa prathamam
3.2.12.[1]	yo'yaṃ vidhiruktaḥ prathamasya niparaṇasya anenaiva vidhinā tasya dakṣiṇārddhe dvitīyasya niparaṇaṃ kuryyādaurvebhya ityanena mantreṇa tadanantaramanenaiva vidhinā tṛtīyaṃ nidadhyāt kāvyam ityanena uktaṃ pitṛbhiriti sarvatrānusaṃharedityetadādi
3.2.13.[1]	evaṃ sarveṣāṃ nidhānaṃ kṛtvā atra pitaro mādayadhvaṃ yathābhāgamityuktvā āsitvā yāvat manyeta tāvat yāvantaṃ manyeta manuṣyāṇāṃ bhojanakālaṃ tāvantamāsitvā bhuktaṃ pitṛbhiriti matvā tataḥ ābhimukhyena paryyāvarttamāno japet amīmadanta pitara ityetaṃ yathāsūtritaṃ mantram
3.2.14.[1]	tān darbhān yeṣu niparaṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tāṃśca drapsān ye nihitāḥ tān dakṣiṇagnau praharet prakṣipet
3.3.1.[1]	iha prācīnāvītinā karmma kṛtaṃ paitṛkamanantaramāha yajñopavītī bhūtveti yajñopavītī bhūtvāpa upaspṛśya apaḥ spṛṣṭvā gṛhān vrajan japati gṛhāmābibhītetyetadādi yathāsūtritaṃ mantram atrocyate gṛhān vrajan japedityāha athedaṃ pūrvaṃ karma kasmiṃsciddeśe kṛtamiti yenedānīmāha gṛhān vrajan japediti tatraike tāvadvarṇayanti so'gnihotra evāsau yajñabhūmigataḥ atastasmin deśe idaṃ karma kṛtamiti ato'nantaraṃ gṛhān vrajannidañjapediti, apare varṇayanti tretāgniśaraṇaṃ havirgṛhebhyaḥ pṛthageva bhavati tasminnidaṃ karma kṛtvā gṛhān vrajannetajjapediti, ubhayamaviruddham
3.3.2.[1]	gṛhān praviśya śālāgneḥ paścime pradeśe upaviśya japediha gāvaḥ prajāyadhvamityetadādi yathāsūtritam
3.3.3.[1]	śālāgneḥ samīpe yāni tṛṇāni prātarhomastaraṇasambandhīni tāni pratyuhya yo'sya suhṛttasya pitā vā putro vā bhāryā vā taṃ prathamamabhibhāṣeta
3.3.4.[1]	goṣu gā apisṛjet yā asya svāgāvaḥ tāsu yā dakṣiṇā prāptāstāmiśrayet upedamupaparcanamiti yathāsūtritena mantreṇa
3.3.5.[1]	sāmpratamasya gavāmayanasya vidhiḥ vivakṣitaḥ taṃ vivakṣuḥ sarvasatrāṇāṃ sāmānyaṃ vidhānamārabhate satreṣu sarvānadhvayurdīkṣayediti satreṣvityadhikaraṇe saptamī sarvāniti niravaśeṣavācī śabdaḥ satreṣu sarvān satriṇaḥ adhvaryurdīkṣayet
3.3.6.[1]	dīkṣiṣyamāṇān svastyātreyādīni darśayet dṛśirau prekṣaṇe svastyātreya ādarśaḥ ṛjvanyat
3.3.7.[1]	kimarthaṃ punareṣāṃ darśanamucyate naitāni parāsuḥ paśyati yeṣāṃ parābhūtāḥ asavaḥ prāṇaḥ mumūrṣavaste svastyātreyādīni na paśyantīti
3.3.8.[1]	tān parāsūnna dīkṣayet kasmādyataḥ asamāpte satre teṣāṃ mṛtyurbhavati etat vidhānaṃ saṃvatsarasatraṃ yāvaddraṣṭavyaṃ ūrddhvaṃ mṛtasya vidhānadarśanāt
3.3.9.[1]	dīkṣākāle upasthite saṃvaderan etat samayaṃ kuryuḥ saha naḥ sādhukṛtyāḥ sādhūnāṃ karmaṇāṃ yā kriyā sā naḥ sādhāraṇī yā pāpānāṃ mā pṛthak asmin satre
3.3.10.[1]	atha yatpurāsannāḥ kṛtavantaḥ karttāsmaḥ yathoktaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ yathopasthitameva nastaditi yadyaḥ karoti tasyaiva taditi, nanu anukte'pyevameva nahyanyena kṛtamanyasminnṛcchati karmakarttāraṃ gacchati atrocyate, prāk satradīkṣāyāḥ teṣāṃ sādhāraṇaṃ iṣṭakāpaśurbhavati ūrddhvañca vakṣyati saṃvatsaraṃ saṃvaseyurdaśarātramahorātrau vā yāvadvā sunuyuriti tatkā svanivṛtyarthamārabhate yāsmin satre iti
3.3.11.[1]	teṣāṃ satriṇāṃ dīkṣāmārabhya patnīśālāyāṃ bhojanaṃ saṃveśanañca bhavetāṃ prabhṛti śabda ādau
3.3.12.[1]	upavasathyāhna ārabhya satriṇāṃ bhojanasaṃveśane āgnīdhrīye bhaveyātām
3.3.13.[1]	dvayor api sandhivelayorvāgyamanaṃ kuryuḥ āsūryodayādānacatradarśanācca
3.3.14.[1]	vāgyamanādanantaraṃ yāṃ vācaṃ bhāṣeran tāṃ vicakṣaṇantāṃ vicakṣaṇamante yasyāḥ mā vicakṣaṇantā, apare bruvate vicakṣaṇantāmiti sādhyantāṃ vācaṃ brūyuriti pūrva eva tu yaḥ śreyān tasya sādhuvacanaprasaṅgo'sti
3.3.15.[1]	yo'pyavaśyamabhivādanīyaḥ tamapi nābhivādayeran canetyayaṃ nipātaḥ netyayaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ
3.3.16.[1]	na śūdreṇa saha sambhāṣaṇaṃ kuryuḥ
3.3.17.[1]	ye parigṛhītā agnayaḥ tānmuktvā anyeṣvagniṣu nottaperan
3.3.18.[1]	ṛjvarthaḥ
3.3.19.[1]	devayajanasya prāgudagvā niṣkramya mūtrapurīṣe kurvīran
3.3.20.[1]	nāprayojanaṃ bahu vadeyuḥ
3.3.21.[1]	na kasyaciddantān darśayeran jāyate vāva dīkṣayeti
3.3.22.[1]	havirucchiṣṭabhakṣāḥ syuḥ
3.3.23.[1]	nainān bhuñjānānanyaḥ paśyet pariveṣṭṛbhyo'nyatra
3.3.24.[1]	sarveṣāṃ savanānāṃ savanamukhīyān bhakṣayitvā mantreṣu nārāśaṃseṣu bhojanaṃ kuryuḥ
3.3.25.[1]	ṛjvarthaḥ
3.3.26.[1]	etāni yathoddiṣṭavratāni dīkṣāsu bhavanti
3.3.27.[1]	athavā dīkṣāsu copasatsu ca
3.3.28.[1]	yāvad vā sattrasamāptir iti etāni yathāsambhavaṃ syuḥ
3.3.29.[1]	ādityasya udayāstamayau abhyāśrāvaṇañca haviṣaḥ prasṛte sutyāsu bahirvedi varjayeyuḥ eteṣu kāleṣu bahirvedisthānamāsanaṃ vā varjayeyuḥ
3.4.1.[1]	teṣāṃ udayāstamayābhyāśrāvaṇānāṃ bahirvedi sthānaṃ kiñcidāgacchet gṛhapatāvupahavamiccheran upahave gṛhapatiradhikaraṇabhūtaḥ gṛhapateḥ sakāśādupahavamiccheyuḥ
3.4.2.[1]	taṃ yadi gṛhapatiḥ eṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ kiñcidāgacchet udgātuḥ sakāśādupahavaṃ gacchet
3.4.3.[1]	dīkṣānupūrvyeṇa vā yo yasyānantaraṃ dīkṣitaḥ ma tasmādupahavamicchet
3.4.4.[1]	vasatīvarīpariharaṇe kṛte tataḥ svapeyuḥ
3.4.5.[1]	teṣāṃ sattriṇāṃ yadi kaścit mriyeta tamatīrthena nirhṛtya niṣkrāmya āhāryyeṇāgninā anāhitāgnindaheyuḥ teṣāṃ satriṇāṃ āhāryeṇa laukikenetyetadvidhānaṃ anāhitāgnerapi satrāsanaṃ darśayati
3.4.6.[1]	araṇyoḥ agnīn samāropaṇaṃ kṛtvā mantravatte araṇī āpnānena tīrthena nirhṛtya nirmanthyenāgninā āhitāgniṃ daheyuḥ te iti kimartham ucyate, preto'trādhikṛtaḥ ataste ityāha, te araṇītīrthena nirhareyuḥ natvāhitāgnimapi tīrthena, nanu yadā tāvaduktaṃ dīkṣiṣyamāṇān darśayet svastyātreyādīni naitāni parāsuḥ paśyatīti tānna dīkṣayediti tadadarśitā naiva dīkṣante tat kimidamārabhyate teṣāñcet kaścit preyādityādi atha punastaddarśito'pi mriyante tataḥ tadvidhānānarthakyam ucyate yānyetāni nimittāni tāni parimitakālāni teṣāṃ dīrghasatreṣvasambhavaḥ ato vidhānaṃ tadartham
3.4.7.[1]	iha satriprakaraṇe madhyame paryāye dve hotṛṣāmanī paṭhite tayośca dvayorekasmin kratau sambhavo nāsti ekārthatvāt ato bravīti daivodāsaṃ hotṛṣāma syādaurddhvasadmanañceti vikalpayati satre
3.4.8.[1]	iha maśakaḥ paṭhatyābhiplavike dvitīye'hni paritoṣiñca tāsu tamiti mādhuchandasañca bhargaśca yaśo veti tat kimayaṃ viniveśārthaṃ vibhāṣitaḥ athaikatra yaddvayameva vikalpayati so'yamācāryo viniveśaṃ vikalpayati abhiplavasya dvitīye'hani bhargo yaśa iti prāgviṣuvatovyatyāsaṃ syātāmiti ye prāgviṣuvato'bhiplavāḥ teṣu bhargasya yaśasīti dvitīye'hani vyatyāsaṃ syātāmiti prathame bhargaḥ dvitīye yaśa iti
3.4.9.[1]	ūrddhvañca viṣuvataḥ ye trayo'bhiplavāḥ teṣu ca bhargo yaśo bharga iti
3.4.10.[1]	teṣāmapyūrddvaṃ ye'bhiplavāḥ uttarasmin pakṣasi teṣu yaśo bharga ityevaṃ vyatyāsaḥ syāt
3.4.11.[1]	aparamanyadvidhānaṃ sakṛddvirvā yaśaḥ purastādbhavet tathopariṣṭādviṣuvataḥ triṣvabhiplaveṣu sakṛddvirvā yaśo bhavet bharga itareṣu abhiplaveṣu syāt
3.4.12.[1]	aparam anyattṛtīyaṃ vidhānaṃ bhargaḥ pūrvasmin pakṣami syāt yaśa uttarasminniti abhiplaveṣviti prakṛtam
3.4.13.[1]	abhiplavika evaṃ caturthe'hani paṭhati vīṅkaśuddhāśuddhīyañceti tayorapyeta eva vikalpāḥ syuḥ ye bhargayaśasaḥ
3.4.14.[1]	viṣuvata ūrddhvaṃ ye'bhiplavāsteṣu vīṅkameva syāt na śuddhāśuddhīyam ityevaṃ dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate evaśabdo'vadhāraṇārthaḥ
3.4.15.[1]	pañcame'bhiplave yasminnahani grāme geyaṃ santatiḥ syāt tasminmānavāt pūrvañcāmraṃ syāt bṛhatyām ajāmyarthena uktamarṣāsoma dyumattama iti gāyatrañca ya evañcāpatyaṃ santatiḥ śākvaravarṇantānyuttareṣviti
3.4.16.[1]	evaṃ maśakaḥ paṭhati ābhilavike ṣaṣṭhe'hani indrāyendo marutvata iti gāyatrañcāśvasūktañca sakṛdiṣovṛdhīyaṃ kuryyāt mṛjyamānaḥ suhatyetyaiḍañcaukṣorandhaṃ trinidhanañcāyyāsya sakṛt samantaṃ kuryyāt sakṛt sakṛdityuktena vai spaṣṭaṃ katarasminnabhiplava iti so'yamācāryyaḥ spaṣṭīkaroti pṛṣṭhyānantarye ṣaṣṭhe'hani iṣovṛdhīyañca samantañca iṣovṛdhīyasamante yasyābhiplavasyānantaraḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ syāttasya ṣaṣṭhe'hani kuryyāt atha ṣaṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet yadā ṣaṣṭhe viṣaye eva ete ukte ucyate āvṛttasyāpyetasmin pakṣasi niyamārtham
3.4.17.[1]	pūrvasmin pakṣasi ṣaṣṭhe māsi trīnabhiplavān paṭhati tatra triṣu karttavyeṣu prathamo lupyatām utānya iti saṃśayaḥ so'yamācārya āha triṣu karttavyeṣu caturtho lupyeta śākvaravarṇavāniti
3.4.18.[1]	ya ete pūrvasmin pakṣasi abhiplavā anukrāntāḥ eta eva sarve uttarasmin pakṣasi āvṛttā bhaveyuḥ uttamāduttamādārabhyeran natu pratimāsam
3.4.19.[1]	teṣāmabhiplavānām āvṛttānāṃ satām ahānyapi prātilomyena kuryuḥ ṣaṣṭhādahna ārabhya prātilomyena yāvat prathamam
3.4.20.[1]	pṛṣṭhyaśca svarasāmānaśca pṛṣṭhyasvarasāmānaḥ teṣāṃ pṛṭhyasvarasāmnāṃ uttarasmin pakṣasi prātilomyena ahānyupeyuḥ
3.4.21.[1]	daśarātrasya sannikarṣe ye goāyuṣaḥ pūrvāstrayo'bhiplavāḥ teṣu caturṇāmāvṛttānāṃ yaḥ prathamaḥ sa lupyeta evaṃ dhānañjapyo manyate uttame cābhiplavike uttame iṣovṛdhīyasamante syātāmiti
3.4.22.[1]	etadvidhānaṃ viparītaṃ śāṇḍilyāyanasya viparyayaḥ prātilomyaṃ uttamo lupyeta prathama iṣovṛdhīyasamante syātāmiti
3.4.23.[1]	viṣuvatsamīpe ca ye'bhiplavāstrayasteṣu caivameva śāṇḍilyāyanasya
3.4.24.[1]	triṣvabhiplaveṣu karttavyeṣu abhāvaḥ akriyā iṣovṛdhīyasamantayoḥ
3.4.25.[1]	iṣovṛdhīyasamantayoḥ bhāvaḥ ācāryyaṇaṃ matena, tuśabda akriyāpekṣānivṛtyarthaḥ
3.5.1.[1]	abhipave ye saṃśayāste nirṇītāḥ sāmprataṃ pṛṣṭhyasya dharmmā vivakṣitāḥ tadvivakṣurāha pṛṣṭhye rathamativaheyuriti iha brāhmaṇaṃ prajāpatirvā etāṃ gāyatrīṃ yonimapaśyat sa ādīdhītāsmādyoneḥ pṛṣṭhāni sṛjā iti sa rathantaramasṛjata tadrathasya ghoṣo'nvasṛjyatetyetadādi ṣaṇṇāṃ pṛṣṭhānāṃ rathantarādīnāṃ ghoṣādayo dharmmā jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe āmnātāḥ teṣāñca samuditānāmasambhavaḥ jyotiṣṭome taiśca dharmmaiḥ pratiprayogamavaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ tataḥ tatpratyanuṣṭheyāḥ yāvatā anubrāhmaṇasyāntarghoṣāḥ pṛṣṭhadharmmāḥ tatpratyanuṣṭheyā iti teṣāṃ samuditānāṃ prayogaviṣayo'yaṃ vidhistamāha pṛṣṭhye rathamativaheyuriti atrocyate, tat kimidaṃ pṛṣṭyagrahaṇaṃ yāvatā abhiplavasyānantaraḥ pṛṣṭhya eva ābhiplavikastu vidhiruktaḥ taccheṣo vidhirucyamānaḥ ānantaryādatra pṛṣṭhyo bhavatyeva vairūpādīnāñcāsambhavādabhiplava iti ucyate pṛṣṭhyagrahaṇaṃ kriyate viśeṣavidhyarthaṃ pṛṣṭhyānāṃ samastānāṃ dharmmārthaṃ pṛṣṭhānyasmin santīti pṛṣṭhyaḥ etaddarśayati yatra yatra samuditāni pṛṣṭhāni bhaveyuḥ tatra tatra dharmā bhaveyuriti yathā viśvajiti viśvajicchilpe'ptoryāmīti pṛṣṭhya ityadhikaraṇe saptamī ādhāro'dhikaraṇaṃ ādhriyate rathaghoṣādayo dharmmā rathamativaheyuḥ śīghraṃ vaheyuḥ paścātprāñcandevayajanasya paścāt prāṅmukhaṃ vaheyuḥ dakṣiṇato vā udañcam ativaheyuḥ bahirvedi vederbahiḥ rathantarasya stotre rathantarasya sāmnaḥ stotre stūyamāne āstotrāntāt
3.5.2.[1]	bṛhataḥ stotre stūyamāne dundubhimāhanyuḥ stanayitnuśabdo'nukarṣaṇārthaḥ nahi śakyaṃ stanayitnuśabdaṃ balādupapādayitum ato dundubhiṃ vādayeyuḥ bahirvedīti prakṛtam
3.5.3.[1]	vyajanena itaretaram upavājayamānāḥ santaḥ vairupeṇa sāmnā stuvīran anyairvopavājyamānāḥ itaretaramekena vyajanena
3.5.4.[1]	katamasyānumantraṇaṃ vyajanasya yo ghoṣavāhaḥ
3.5.5.[1]	vairājasya sāmnaḥ stotre upākṛte purastājjapaṃ japitvā urorupariṣṭāt sakalam ānulomyena nidhāya prasthāpayitvā tṛṇe ca tasya sakalasyopari tiraścīmaraṇiṃ sthāpayitvā abhimukhamātmanaḥ agneḥ prajananaṃ kṛtvā yena pradeśenāgniḥ avatāryyate taduttarāraṇyā triḥ pradakṣiṇamabhimanthet gāyatraṃ chando'nuprajāyasvetyetadādinā mantreṇa evaṃ gautama ācārya āha
3.5.6.[1]	caturbhiśchandobhiriti dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate gāyatraṃ chando'nuprajāyasva traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatamānuṣṭubhamiti
3.5.7.[1]	tribhiśchandobhiriti śāṇḍilya ācārya āha, gāyatraṃ chando'nuprajāyasva traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatamiti kriyāyāḥ sarvatrānuvacanam
3.5.8.[1]	araṇyoḥ sandhānamālabhya spṛṣṭvā upajighrettejo'si tejo mayi dhehītyanena mantreṇa, ghrā gandhopādāne
3.5.9.[1]	mathyamāne'gnau yathāvidhānaṃ stomayojanaṃ kuryyāt
3.5.10.[1]	jāte'gnau stuvīran agnighoṣe
3.5.11.[1]	vācāyitvā yajamānaṃ stutasya stutamasīti punarūrjā nivarttasvetyetadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa agnimanumantrya prāharatyāhavanīye ājyenābhijuhuyāt taduktaṃ brāhmaṇena preddho agne dīdihi puro na iti virājābhijuhotīti
3.5.12.[1]	uttarāmāhutiṃ svāhākāreṇa juhuyāt āgatyopariṣṭājjapaḥ
3.5.13.[1]	apa iti karmaṇi dvitīyā saha avakābhiḥ sāvakāḥ avakāḥ saivālāḥ
3.5.14.[1]	yo yaḥ svabhaktiṃ brūyāt sa udaghoṣaṃ kuryyāt nidhane tu sarve
3.5.15.[1]	vācayitvā yajamānaṃ āpaḥ avakāmiśrā ninayet nikṣipet āstāve anādhṛṣṭāsītyetadādinā yajuṣā yathāsūtritena āstāvaścātvāladeśe prasiddhaḥ
3.5.16.[1]	samanyāyantīti etayarcā vā ninayet
3.5.17.[1]	samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomītyetadādinā yajuṣā vā ninayet
3.5.18.[1]	sarvairvvā ninayanamantraiḥ anādhṛṣṭāsītyetadādibhiḥ ninayet
3.5.19.[1]	sarvairvā aṣṭhīvatoraṅgapradeśayoḥ sthāpayeyuḥ aṣṭhīvatoriti jānubhyāmupari
3.5.20.[1]	chadiṣi chādanasyopari varṣakāmaḥ nidadhyāt evaṃ śāṇḍilya ācārya prāha
3.5.21.[1]	avakā nidadhyāt
3.5.22.[1]	yaśaskāmaḥ sabhāyāmavakā nidadhyāt
3.5.23.[1]	abhicaran abhicāraṃ kurvan śmaśāne avakā nidadhyāt śmaṃ śarīraṃ tadyasmin śete tat śmaśānam
3.6.1.[1]	uktaṃ sa revatīrasṛjata tadgavāṃ ghoṣo'nvasṛjyateti tāśca revatyaḥ pavamāne prayujyante rathantarādīnāṃ pañcānāṃ pṛṣṭhānāṃ pṛṣṭhasthāneṣu prayujyamānānāṃ sannidhau rathavyativarttanādayo dharmmāḥ prayuktāḥ tatsannidhitvāt dharmmāṇāṃ kiṃ sannidhau revatīnāṃ pavamāna eva kriyate dharmāḥ atha pṛṣṭhasthāne ityatrāha, vāravantīyasya stotre dhanūḥ saṃvāśayeyuriti apāṃ vā eṣa raso yadrevatyo revatīnāṃ raso yadvāravantīyamiti revatīnāṃ vāravantīyaṃ rasaḥ sāramiti tadvāravantīyamiti sannidhau prayujyamānā revatyaḥ prāpnuvanti vāravantīyasya sāmnaḥ stotre dhenuḥ saṃvāsayeyuḥ kathaṃ saṃvāsayeyuḥ devayajanasya dakṣiṇe pradeśe kṛtvā gā uttarato vatsān kṛtvā
3.6.2.[1]	samāpte stotre sadasaḥ pūrve pradeśe miśrayitvā vatsaiḥ samādhāya āgnīdhrīyasya paścime pradeśe udīcīndiśaṃ prati prasthāpayeyuḥ niṣkālayeyuḥ idamudgātṛkarma tatsaṃyogāt rathapravarttanādidhenvantāḥ pṛṣṭhadharmāḥ sarvatra bhaveyuḥ teṣāmupadiṣṭatvāt yasya yena karmaṇā saṃyogaḥ sataddravyaṃ labhate pratistotramudgātre etat dadyāt
3.6.3.[1]	vācayitvā yajamānamudgātā gāḥ gonāmabhiranumantrayeta havye kāmye ityetadādibhiryathāsūtritaiḥ atrocyate gonāmabhiriti kimarthaṃ yadā sarvāṇi nirdiṣṭānyeva, ucyate gonāmagrahaṇaṃ saṃvyavahārārtham anyatrāpi yatra gonāmānīti brūyāt tatraitānyeva prāptavyāni yathā dakṣiṇe'syāḥ karṇe gonāmāni japitveti yāni ca prakaraṇāmnātānyeva tāni ca
3.6.4.[1]	saharṣabhā ityetayarcā vā upamantrayet
3.6.5.[1]	saharṣabhā havye kāmye ityetadādinā mantreṇa vānumantrayet
3.6.6.[1]	yadyadbhirupākaraṇaṃ kuryuradhvaryavaḥ tā āpaḥ ninayedāstāve āpohiṣṭhoyābhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ adbhirupākaraṇasya kaḥ sambandhaḥ āpovai revatya iti
3.6.7.[1]	brāhmaṇe ca ūhuṣī vā etarhi vāgyadā ṣaḍahaḥ santiṣṭhate na bahu vadennānyaṃ pṛchennānyasmai prabrūyāt madhu vāśaye ghṛtaṃ vā yathohuṣovahaṃ pratyanakti tathā taditi ete saṃsthādharmmaḥ śrūyante ata āha ṣaṣṭhe'hani saṃsthite'bahuvādinaḥ syuriti ṣaṣṭhe'hani samāpte'bahuvādinaḥ syuḥ na cādhīyīran ā uttarasyāhna upākaraṇāt upākaraṇaṃ nāma prārambhaḥ etaddarśayati anyeṣvahaḥsamāptiṣvadhyayanaṃ kurvīteti atha ṣaṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti ucyate niyamārthameva yadā ṣaḍahaḥ santiṣṭhata iti tadā vṛttasya prathame'hani saṃsthānaṃ tatra saṃsthādharmmāḥ prāpnuvanti so'yamācāryyaḥ ṣaṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ karoti kathaṃ āvṛtte'pyetasmin syuriti etadāvṛtterūpaṃ ya iha upakramadharmmāste āvṛtteḥ saṃsthādharmāḥ ye tatra saṃsthādharmāste iha upakramadharmā iti
3.6.8.[1]	sarpiṣā madhvā ca yajamānaḥ ṛtvijo bhojayedahīneṣu sarpiriti ghṛtasya paryāyaḥ
3.6.9.[1]	sarpiṣā madhvā vā ekena bhojayet
3.6.10.[1]	sarpiṣaiva tṛtīyasavane bhojanaṃ satriṇām evaśabdo madhu nivarttayati atha tṛtīyasavanagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate ṣaṣṭhe'hani saṃsthite etenoktaṃ tat satreṣu yadeva tārttīyasavanīkambhojanamupadiṣṭam tadeva sarpiṣā syāt tat saṃsthite'hani bhojanamastu satriṇāṃ na anusavanantu satreṣviti tadyathākāmyādeveti
3.6.11.[1]	etasya pṛṣṭhyasya ṣaḍahasya anyatarasmiṃstryahe atigrāhyāṇāṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ atigrāhyā grahāḥ atiriktāḥ prakṛtebhyo gṛhyante ityatigrāhyā yasmiṃstryahe gṛhyeran tasmiṃsteṣāṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ, kasmin kāle stutvā pṛṣṭhena
3.6.12.[1]	viṣuvadgagatayoñca atigrāhyāṇāṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ
3.6.13.[1]	triṣṭupchandasā mantreṇa bhakṣayeyuḥ
3.6.14.[1]	pūrvaṃ sarvacamasebhyo bhakṣyeyuḥ
3.6.15.[1]	anyatra ca anyayajñeṣu ca etasmin kāle yān grahān bhakṣānāhareyusteṣāṃ triṣṭupacchandasā pūrvaṃ camasebhyo bhakṣayeyuḥ
3.6.16.[1]	ete pṛṣṭhyasya dharmā gavāmayanaprakaraṇa āmnātāḥ ete yatra yatra pṛṣṭhāḥ prayujyante tatra tatra syurna kevalaṃ gavāmayane
3.6.17.[1]	daśamañcāhavratañca yatra yatra kriyetāṃ tatra tatra sahadharmaiḥ
3.6.18.[1]	ye ābhīvarttastotrīyāḥ ābhiplavikāḥ tān sarvatra pṛṣṭhye saṃśayet brāhmaṇācchaṃsinā yadābhīvarttapavamāne syāt kāleyasyarcaḥ acchāvākena saṃśayet yadā tat pavamāne syāt na kevalaṃ pṛṣṭhye kāleyasya anyatrāpi yadā kāleyaṃ pavamāne syāt tatrā'pyetasya stotrīyaṃ śaṃsayedacchāvākena yathā viśvajitīti
3.6.19.[1]	ūrddhvaṃ viṣuvataḥ yānyahāni teṣu sarveṣvindrakratuṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ śaṃsayet prāgatirātrāt udayanīyam atirātraṃ varjayitvā sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī
3.6.20.[1]	uktaṃ yatra yatra samuditāni pṛṣṭhāni prayujyeran tatra tatra eṣāṃ rathavyativarjamānādayo dharmāḥ syuriti tadiha sarvapṛṣṭhaviśvajit tasmin viśvajiti rathantarādīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ pṛṣṭhyādīnāṃ vairāje'dhikaraṇe dharmān kuryyāt etaddhi dharmāṇāṃ sthānaṃ hotāpi sarveṣāṃ tasminneva yonīḥ saṃśati
3.6.21.[1]	itareṣvapi pṛṣṭheṣu dharmān kuryyāt eṣā ācāryyāṇāṃ matiḥ sannikṛṣṭanyāyatvāddharmāṇam itareṣu triṣu pṛṣṭheṣu mahānāmnīvairūparevatīṣu svadharmāḥ syuḥ bṛhadrathantaravairājānāṃ vairājā dharmāḥ syuriti
3.6.23.[1]	iha brāhmaṇe aṣṭamanavamayorahnoḥ svāśirāmarkadīrghatamaso'rkāvāmnātau agnerarko'ntaritaḥ tamagnerarkaṃ saptame'hani kalpayatyācāryyaḥ saptame'hanyagnerarko'dhyarddheḍañca somamāma maukṣasya pūrvayoriti yaste madovareṇya iti gāyatraṃ tṛce kṛtvā etasminneva sāmatṛcaḥ syāt agnerarko'dhyarddheḍañca somasāma maukṣamiti
3.6.23.[1]	athavā gāyatramekarce kṛtvā tasyottarayormaukṣasomasāmanī kṛtvā tasminneva tṛce agnerarkastisṛṣu kurvyāt araṇye geyamidamapavitramiti
3.6.24.[1]	sākamaśvasya iḍānāṃ saṃkṣārasya ca aṣṭamanavamayorahnorvyatihārameke ācāryyāḥ kurvanti āṣṭamikī iḍā vibhaktirnavame'hani kṛtvā aṣṭama eva kalpayati iḍā saṃkṣāro'ṣṭamasya vibhaktirnavame'hani kriyata iti vyatihāro nāma anyo'nyasthānopādānaṃ iḍānāṃ saṃkṣārau sākamaśvasya sthāne kurvanti sākamaśvamiḍānāṃ saṃkṣārasyeti
3.6.25.[1]	aṣṭame'hani surūpaṃ gāyatryatṛcasthamāmnātaṃ krauñcaṃ cānuṣṭubhi uṣṇikkakubhāvekarcau kṛtau tadeke ācāryyā liṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā vikalpayanti prāṇāśiśurmahīnāmiti prāṇavatyo bhavantīti asya ca bahuvacanasya uṣṇikkakubhorekarci kriyānarthakyaṃ tadeke uṣṇikkakubhau tṛcayoḥ kurvanti uṣṇikkakubhostṛcaikarcatvamanyathā teneti surūpakrauñce ekarcayoḥ
3.6.26.[1]	navame'hani bahiṣpavamāne evaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ paṭhati savā uttamaḥ ṣaḍṛco bhavatītyuktvāha tṛca uttamo bhavatīti na ca tasyānantarastṛco'sti ṣaḍṛcaḥ tasyānantaraḥ nacāvacchedaṃ kṛtvā kalpanā yuktā ṛte vacanāt so'yamācāryyaḥ prākṛtaṃ paryyāsaṃ vidhitsurāha navamasya jyotiṣṭomaḥ paryāsa iti anādeśe prakṛtipratyayāt
3.6.27.[1]	eke ācāryāḥ sāptamikaḥ paryyāsaḥ syādityevamāhuḥ kasmāt saprabhṛtitvāt uktaṃ saprabhṛtayo bhavantīti tāḥ śvasanādayaḥ
3.6.28.[1]	tasya grahaṇaṃ yadi jyotiṣṭomaḥ paryyāsaḥ yadi sāptamikaḥ tasya bṛhatyāmekādaśasāmāni paṭhitāni teṣāṃ tṛcaikarcatvaklṛptiḥ kalpayati yānyaranye geyāni tāni tṛceṣu syuḥ pṛṣṭhyañca anyānyekarceṣu
3.6.29.[1]	tat kimidamārabhyate anuprāptameva vāsiṣṭhamadhyāsyāyām ācāryyairapi prakaraṇe'dhyāsyāyāmeva gītam ucyate niyamārthamārabhyate vakṣyate saptaiva tṛceṣu yairajāmītyaparamiti na tat kalpe vāsiṣṭhaṃ syāt adhyāsyāviṣayameva vāsiṣṭhamiti
3.6.30.[1]	pāṭhakramaṃ vikalpayati ajāmyarthena vaiyaśvaṃ prāgabhargādbhavet abhīśavaṃ yaśasaḥ prāgiti varttate
3.6.31.[1]	aparaḥ kalpaḥ bṛhatyāṃ saptaiva tṛceṣa syuḥ yaiḥ kriyamāṇairjāmi na bhavati etadaparaṃ ācāryamataṃ prathamaḥ kalpo yathāmnātānāṃ kriyāśeṣe vikalpaḥ
3.6.32.[1]	ante dīrghatamaso'rkaḥ sāmarājañca tayośca dvayorekasmin sambhavo nāsti tasmād vikalpaḥ syāt ekārthatvāt
3.6.33.[1]	yadā tāvat dīrghatamaso'rko'ntyaḥ syāt tadā sāmarājasyābhāva eva yadā punaḥ sāmarājamantyaṃ syāt tadā pṛṣṭhasyottarayoḥ stotrīyayoḥ dīrghatamaso'rkaḥ syāt māṇḍavaṃ caiḍaṃ dīrghatamaso'rkaḥ arko'nugrahārthaḥ māṇḍavaṃ stomapūrṇārtham
3.7.1.[1]	daśānāṃ pūraṇaḥ daśamaḥ daśamasyeti sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭho bahiṣpavamānamiti stotropadeśaḥ dvitīyaprabhṛtīnāmiti nidadhyurupadeśaḥ prabhṛtiśabdaḥ ādyābhidhāyī pañcānāmiti saṃkhyā ahnāmiti aharnirdeśaḥ anurūpā iti bahiṣpavamānaṃ tannavarcaṃ navarcamiti saṃjñā bahiṣpavamānasya ādyadvitīyāntyāstṛcaḥ pratipadanurūpaparyāsaḥ prathamāccāhnaḥ bahiṣpavamānantannavarcaṃ navarcamiti saṃjñā etaddaśamasyāhno bahiṣpavamānam atrocyate yadā tāvadeva bahiṣpavamānaṃ dāśamikaṃ klṛptameva sarvaṃ brāhmaṇe pañcānāmahnāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti navarce bhavanti yā evāmūḥ prayacchan yā āvadadhātīti ca sambandho'sya darśitaḥ prāthamikasya navarcasya vāruṇyekā bhavati ādityekā bhavatīti ca liṅgacodanā tat kimidaṃ siddhe sati punarārabhyate daśamasya bahiṣpavamānamiti ucyate, ācāryyasyeyaṃ pravṛttiḥ yatra hi kālo vā viśeṣo vā kañcidvivakṣito bhavati tatra siddhasyāpi sato vidhiḥ punarupādānaṃ karoti yathā ekatrike sadyaḥ sarvaṃ kuryurekadīkṣastryupasatka iti gautamastasya gāyatrapārśvamārbhavo yā ruceti purojityamiti śāṇḍilya iti etad vivakṣuḥ siddhamidaṃ gāyatrapārśvaṃ punarāmanati evamiha vidhiśeṣaṃ vivakṣuḥ siddhopādānaṃ karoti kaḥ punarvidhiḥ śiṣyate yo vaktavyaḥ ucyate, brāhmaṇaṃ pañcānāmahnāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavayantīti tathā vaktavyam etadarthaṃ siddhamapi santaṃ punarādadate ucyate yadyevaṃ siddhe'pi sati punarādadate daśamagrahaṇaṃ tāvanna karttavyaṃ kasmāt nāvamikaṃ vidhānamuktaṃ śeṣo'pi vidhirucyamānaḥ saṃkhyānāt daśamādanyatra ca bhavet tasmāddaśamagrahaṇaṃ śakyamavaktuṃ bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ śakyameva vaktuṃ bahiṣpavamānasya grahaṇasya kiṃ kāraṇaṃ tacchakyatvāt tat vivaktavyam atra hoturājyādārabhya susamiddho na āvahetyetasmāddāśamikāni stotrāṇi pratyakṣaśiṣṭāni tasmāt kāraṇaṃ na vaktavyaṃ dvitīyaprabhṛtīnāmityetadapyanārabdhavyameva yasmāddvitīyaprabhṛtiṣvahaḥsu bahiṣpavamānadvitīyāstṛcasteṣāmanurūpā iti saṃjñā pavasvendovṛṣāsuta ityetadādīnāṃ ahnāmanurūpā ityetacca na vaktavyaṃ kasmāt uktaṃ pañcānāmahnāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavayantīti prathamācca bahiṣpavamānantannavarcamityetadapi na vaktavyaṃ kasmāt uktaṃ navarce bhavatīti yā evāmūḥ prayacchan yā avadadhāti tā etā udasyatīti prāthamikenaiva bahiṣpavamānena sambandhaṃ darśayati tasmāt sarvameva sūtraṃ nārabdhavyam ārambhe vā prayojanaṃ vaktavyam atrocyate, yaduktaṃ nārabdhavyamityārabdhavyamiti brūmaḥ śeṣavidhyarthaṃ yattāvaducyate daśamagrahaṇaṃ na kartavyamiti atra brūmaḥ karttavyameva chandomā iti paṭhati abhyasaṅgyaḥ pañcāhaścatvāraḥ chandomā viśvajidatirātra iti tatredaṃ saṃkhyānato navamaṃ tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimatra dāśamikaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavatyata utpattikatvāt nāvamikaṃ mābhūditi yāvatā nidānakāreṇāpi vicāritaṃ kathaṃ daśamadharmā mānasamiti karttavyā ityeke taccāharjāyata iti akartavya ityaparamadaśamañca luptaśca daśarātra iti so'yamācāryyo'niyamārthaṃ daśamagrahaṇaṃ karoti kathaṃ adaśame'pyetasmin bahiṣpavamānaṃ syāditi, atha yaduktaṃ bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ na karttavyamityatra brūmaḥ bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ kriyate niyamārthaṃ kathaṃ etasminnahani na kadācidanyaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ syāditi kutaḥ punarāśaṅkā yathānyaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ syāditi ucyate, maśakaḥ paṭhati dvādaśāhavicāreṣu api vā pratipadāvevānyonyasyāḥ sthānaṃ vyatiharediti na kadācidapi bahiṣpavamānasya vikāraḥ syāt daśame'hanīti, atha yaduktaṃ dvitīyaprabhṛtīnāmiti na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ anyonyasya sthānaṃ dvitīyaprabhṛtīnāmeva syuḥ, atha yaduktaṃ pañcānāmityatra brūmaḥ avidyamāneṣvapi pañcānāmeva kuryuḥ yathā chando bhavati daśarātre, atha yaduktamahnāmiti na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ aharvyatyāso'pyānupūrvyeṇa syāt, atha yaduktamanurūpā iti na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ anurūpagrahaṇaṃ sāptamikapratiṣedhārthaṃ kathaṃ samūhite dvādaśāhe etā anurūpā na syuriti yeṣāmevānurūpā saṃjñā tā eveti, atha yaduktaṃ prathamācca bahiṣpavamānaṃ tannavarcamityetadapi na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ avachinnabahiṣpavamānaṃ klṛptaṃ chandomā mati daśarātre tanmābhūditi tasmāt sūtramārabdhavyam
3.7.2.[1]	uktaṃ pañcānāmahnāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti yathābhyāruhya pratyavarohettathā taditi tatpratyavarohaṇaṃ kiṃ ṛkprātilomyena athavā tṛcaḥ prātilomyeneti ucyate anurūpeṣu tṛcā pratilomā ṛcā navarce ṣāṣṭikādanurūpādārabhya prātilomyena tāvadyāvaddvitīyaka iti taiḥ pratyavarohaḥ na ṛcāmapi asṛkṣata pravrājinaḥ pavamānasya viśvavitpavamāno ajījattadete asṛgramindavaḥ pavasvendovṛṣāsuta ityeṣa karmakramaḥ tata ṛcaḥ pratilomāḥ syuḥ upāsmai gāyatānara ityata ārabhya yāvadasya pratnāmanudyutamiti evaṃ pratyavarohaṇaṃ gautama ācāryo manyate
3.7.3.[1]	sarvatra sarvasmin bahiṣpavamāne tṛcā prātilomyena dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate anurūpāṇāṃ yathoktaṃ navarce tu upaśikṣāya tasthuṣa eṣa pratnena janmanāsya pratnāmanudyutamityevantṛcaḥ prātilomyam
3.7.4.[1]	anurūpāṇāṃ yathoktameva prātilomyaṃ navarce tu yathādhītameveti evaṃ śāṇḍilyāyana ācāryo manyate
3.7.5.[1]	sarvatrānurūpeṣu navarceṣyṛcaḥ pratilomāḥ syurityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryyo manyate, dvitīyakādanurūpādārabhya yāvat ṣāṣṭika iti ete ṛkpratilomāḥ syuḥ anyathā hi yadi ṣāṣṭikādārabhyeran evamubhayaprātilomyaṃ syāt ṛkprātilomyantṛcaprātilomyañca navarce tu sarvamṛkpratilomameva syāt upāsmai gāyatā nara ityata ārabhya yāvadasya pratneti
3.7.6.[1]	apratibhāṃ na pratibhām anavasthānamityarthaḥ yadetasminnahani pratibhāyāḥ stotrāṅgaṃ kiñcittadanuṣṭummātrāṃ kṛtvācakṣīran uktaṃ yāvatyanuṣṭuptāvatīṃ vācaṃ sampādya vibrūyuriti atha mātrāgrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti ucyate ṛknyāyannādriyeran dvātriṃśanmātrāṃ kṛtvācakṣīran
3.7.7.[1]	jyāyastvaṃ nāma vṛddhiḥ kanīyastvaṃ hrāsaḥ jyāyasi indasyākhyātavye anuṣṭummātrāṃ kṛtvā adhikānyakṣarāṇi lumpeyuḥ kanīyasī abhyasyeyuḥ ke yeṣāmudgātṛṛṇāmidaṃ karmma upadiṣṭam
3.7.8.[1]	agniṣṭomasāmnā stutvā prāk patnīsaṃyājebhyaḥ yadebhirudgātṛbhiḥ prastute some prasavādārabhya sarvairdūraṅgataṃ syāt tadgatvā pratyāvrajya manasānutsāhe yadyutsāho na syāt gamanāgamane manasā gamanāgamane kṛtvā huteṣu patnīsaṃyājeṣu gārhapatya udgātā juhuyāt upasṛjandharuṇaṃ mātra etadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa udgātṛgrahaṇaṃ na sarve eva
3.7.9.[1]	uttarāmājatiṃ svāhākāreṇa juhuyāt
3.7.10.[1]	gārhapatye udgātā hutvā adhvaryuṇā sampreṣite āhavanīye gatvā tasya paścime pradeśe tiṣṭhanto yadvakṣyate tat kuryuḥ kiṃ punastat ayaṃ sahohā ityetatsāma trirudgātā gāyet nidhanamitarau prastotṛpratihattarau udgātāramupayantaṃ anupeyātāṃ gānagrahaṇaṃ uktamatichandasāhavanīyamupatiṣṭhanta iti ṛcā mābhūditi
3.7.11.[1]	yajamānasya yaḥ sañcarastena gatvā nodgātṛsañcareṇa pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ praviśeyuḥ
3.8.1.[1]	yasmin kāle adhvaryurupākaraṇaṃ karoti athānantaraṃ mānasena stotrena stuvīran manasā kriyata iti mānasam uktaṃ manasopāvarttayatyetadādi ayaṅgauḥ pṛśnirakramīdityetasmiṃstṛce gāyatreṇa sāmnā uktaṃ sārparājñā ṛgbhiḥ stuvantīti etā sārparājñyaḥ pṛthak stotrīyābhyo hiṅkāraṃ pṛthak nānetyarthaḥ stotrīyābhyo hiṃkāraṃ kuryuḥ trikeṇa stomena uktaṃ parācībhiḥ stuvantīti evaṃ parāktvam astomayogā yajamānavācanena nātra stomayojanaṃ syāt na ca yajamānavācanam
3.8.2.[1]	pratihāradeśakāle pratiharttā apānyāt uktaṃ tasmāddvayaṃ prāṇena karoti prāṇiti cāpāniti ca tadapānasaṃjñakavāyurantaḥ praveśayet
3.8.3.[1]	uttamāṃ stotrīyāṃ prastutyaiṣetyanena hotāramīkṣet
3.8.4-5.[1]	yatkiñcidasmin stotre purastājjapādi tatsarvaṃ mānasaṃ kuryuḥ samīkṣaṇena vijñāpayantaḥ brahmaṃstoṣyāmaḥ praśāstarityataḥ ārabhya samīkṣaṇamātreṇa vijñāpanaṃ kurvantaḥ sarvapraiṣeṣu prajñāpanaṃ manasaiva syāditi / 4
3.8.6.[1]	yamadhvaryurbhakṣaṃ prayacchanmanyeta yadi grahaṃ yadi camasaṃ tasya manasopahūya kastvā kaṃ bhakṣayāmīti bhakṣayeyuḥ manasaiva uktaṃ grahaṃ vā gṛhītvā camasaṃ vonnīya stotramupāvarttayatīti na bhakṣaṃ stotreṇa sambadhyate'taḥ punarmanasetyāha
3.8.7.[1]	uktaṃ brahmodyaṃ vadanti brahmavarcasa eva pratitiṣṭhantīti kiṃ punarbrahmodyamiti ucyate gāyatrīṃ trirbrūyuriti dhānañjapya iti gāyatryāstrirvacanaṃ brahmodyaṃ sā ca gāyatrī paribhāṣitā taṃ sa āpyāyayedabhimṛśyāpyāyasvetyuktvāha sarve vaitayā gāyatryeti
3.8.8.[1]	caturhotāraṃ brahmodyamabhipretya etadbrāhmaṇam iti gautama ācāryo manyate
3.8.9.[1]	svāhākṛtibhiśca ṛte pūrveṇa sada upaviśya brahmodyaṃ vadeyuriti etadbrahmodyamihāpi syāditi śāṇḍilya āha
3.8.10.[1]	etasyāṃ velāyāṃ varān vṛṇīranmanasā yo yasyepsitaḥ sa taṃ varaṃ vṛṇīte
3.8.11.[1]	uttare pradeśe'vasthita udgātā audumbarīṃ gṛhṇīyāt anvārabhet paścātpratiharttā paścime pradeśe cāvasthitaḥ pratiharttā anvārabhet dakṣiṇato brahmā anvārabhet pūrvapradeśe'vasthitā itare sarve anvārabheran
3.8.12.[1]	athaśabda ānantarye anvārabhyāthānantaraṃ japeyuḥ iha dhṛtirityetadādi yathāsūtritaṃ mantraṃ mayi dhṛtirityetadādi vā
3.8.13.[1]	ubhau vā mantrau japeyuḥ
3.8.14.[1]	evaṃ japitvānantaraṃ vāgyatā vācaṃ yamayitvā apidhāya dvāre āsīran ākutaḥ kālāt ā nakṣatrapravacanāt yāvannakṣatraṃ proktamiti uktaṃ vācaṃ yacchanti dugdhānīva vai tarhi chandāṃsi yātayāmānyantagatāni tānyeva tadrasenāpyāyayantyatho'śvastanāmevābhisantanvantīti
3.8.15.[1]	uktam āsīran ānakṣatrapravacanāditi tato'nyena prokte nakṣatre pūrvayā dvārā sadaso niṣkramya subrahmaṇyāpraṇavaiḥ subrahmaṇyomityebhiḥ vāgvisargaṃ kuryuriti dhānañjapyaḥ ācāryo manyate
3.8.16.[1]	vasatīvarīpariharaṇasyānte subrahmaṇyenāhūyamānāyāḥ subrahmaṇyāyāḥ praṇavān śrutvā vācaṃ visṛjeyurityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryo manyate na svayaṃ praṇavaṃ brūyuriti
3.8.17.[1]	varavaraṇañca vāgyamanañca te varavaraṇavāgyamane yajamāna eva kuryādahīneṣu evaśabdo'vadhāraṇārthaḥ sarvakarttṛkamidaṃ karmopariṣṭaṃ tad yajamānaḥ kuryādahīneṣu iti sarvartvijo na kuryuḥ nanu yadā dvāvevāhīnau tāṇḍake yayordaśamamahaḥ tayośca ahīnadvādaśāhachandomavāṃśca daśarātraḥ tat kimidaṃ bahuvacanaṃ ahīneṣviti ucyate śākhāntarābhiprāyeṇa athavā pauṇḍarike catuṣṭome ca vicāritaṃ kathaṃ daśamadharmā mānasamityakarttavyā ityeke tatsvena nāmadheyenaikāha ādiśyate catuṣṭomo'gniṣṭome ityathāpi na dāśamikaṃ liṅgaṃ dṛśyate yathaitad bahiṣpavamānasyāvṛttisāmnāṃ vipracyāvanamanuṣṭubhaṃ parokṣīcikīrṣediti śāṇḍilyaḥ karttavyā ityācāryā ye'nye mānasasaṃyuktebhyaḥ saṃsthāpanīyaṃ mānasaṃ catuṣṭome'gniṣṭoma iti so'yamācārya anenaiva bahuvacanena evaṃ vidhimādarśayatīti
3.8.18.[1]	varavaraṇavāgyamane yajamāna eva kuryādahīneṣu itare ṛtvijaḥ varavaraṇavāgyamanābhyāṃ yadanyatkarmoktaṃ tat kṛtvā yathārthaṃ syuḥ iti karmaṇaḥ samāptiṃ darśayati
3.9.1.[1]	iha mahāvrataprakaraṇe trayodaśaparimādaḥ paṭhitā brāhmaṇena purastādāhavanīyamupatiṣṭhanta ityata ārabhya yāvadgārhapatyopasthānamiti tadanantaraṃ paṭhati āsandīmāruhyādgāyatīti parimādagānānantaraṃ mahāvratasya stavanaṃ darśayati teṣāṃ parimādāṃ kriyāvidhiṃ vivakṣuridaṃ sūtramārabhate mahāvratasya pṛṣṭhe upākṛte yuktvā stomaṃ parimādo gāyediti mahāvrata iti karmaṇo nāmadheyaṃ tasyeti sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī pṛṣṭhamiti stotrasaṃjñā tasmin pṛṣṭhe upākṛte upākaraṇaṃ nāmādhvaryavaṃ karma upāvarttadhvamiti yuktvā stomaṃ stomayojanaṃ kṛtvā yathoktena mantreṇa parimāda iti saṃjñā parimādbhiścaranti tvak ca vā etalloma ca mahāvratasya yatparimāda iti gāyediti kriyopadeśaḥ bhāṇḍitāyana ityācāryamatasaṃkīrttanaṃ eṣa sūtrārthaḥ mahāvratasya kratoḥ hotṛpṛṣṭhe upākṛte stomayojanaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ parimādagānamiti ucyate, daśamamahaḥ niravaśeṣamuktaṃ tasmādanantaraṃ mahāvratasāmnā taṃ dvādaśāhasya dvādaśāhāni mahāvratañceti tadevamānantaryādeva prāpte mahāvratake vidhau parimādasambandhācca yāvatā mahāvratādanyatra parimādo na bhavanti tat kimidaṃ mahāvratagrahaṇaṃ mahāvratasya pṛṣṭhe iti ucyate niyamārthaṃ mahāvratagrahaṇaṃ mahāvratasyaiva prāptāvetasmin pṛṣṭha upākṛte nānyatra pṛṣṭhamātre yathā vakṣyati mahendrasya mahāvratapṛṣṭha iti
3.9.2.[1]	pratigṛhya tṛṇe upākaraṇike ayuktvā stomaṃ parimādo gāyedityevaṃ gautamaśāṇḍilyāvācāryāvāhatuḥ dhānañjapyaśca
3.9.3.[1]	eke ācāryyā manyante prāgeva stotropākaraṇāt parimādo gāyediti
3.9.4.[1]	āgnīdhrīyasya dakṣiṇena gatvā iṣṭakācitasyāgneḥ uttareṇa gatvā prāṇaprabhṛtibhi ṛṣyasya sāmāntaiḥ āhavanīyādigārhapatyāntāni brāhmaṇoktāni upatiṣṭheran taduktamupasthānavidhānaṃ brāhmaṇena prāṇena purastādāhavanīmupatiṣṭhanta ityetadādi
3.9.5.[1]	sarvāpyetāni prāṇaprabhṛtīni sakṛtsakṛdudgātā gāyet atha kiṃ sakṛtsakṛditi ucyate, uktaṃ ayaṃ sahohā iti trirudgātā gāyediti taddarśanamapi gamyate ata āha sakṛtsakṛditi
3.9.6.[1]	itarau praṣṭī udgātrā saha nidhanamupeyātāṃ prāṇena purastādāhavanīyamupatiṣṭhantiti sarveṣāmupasthānamuktantatsūtrakāra udgātuḥ prāṇadīni vidhāya itarayornidhanamupetya bahuvacanasyārthavatvaṃ darśayati
3.9.7.[1]	madhye nidhaneṣvapi sāmasu itarāvanūpeyātānnidhanāni
3.9.8.[1]	yānyādyantasrubdhāni sāmāni teṣvanupadaṃ stobhaṃ kuryāt tat kimidaṃ siddhe sati punarārabhyate ucyate, eteṣāṃ satrasyarddhyādyantasrubdhaṃ padyate ayañcānupasaṃhāra āvikeṣu pādeṣu vihitaḥ tatra ca daivatāni tiṣṭhanti teṣvapi padāya padāya stobhedityata ārabhyate
3.9.9.[1]	yenaiva gatāstenaiva pratyāvrajya pucchamupatiṣṭheran yathoktenaiva sāmnā prāṅmukhāḥ
3.9.10.[1]	uktaṃ vratapakṣābhyāṃ pakṣāvupatiṣṭhanta iti tayorvratapakṣayoḥ pūrveṇa dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣamupatiṣṭheran arthādāpannamuttareṇottaramiti
3.9.11.[1]	uktaṃ prajāpaterhṛdayenāpi kakṣe upatiṣṭhanta iti tatra dvāvapi kakṣau katarasyopasthānamiti atrāha, uttaramapi kakṣamupatiṣṭheranniti
3.9.12.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ vasiṣṭhasya nihavena cātvālamupatiṣṭhate vaiśvadevyāmṛci bhavatīti so'yamāha, viśvedevā ityetasyāmṛci vasiṣṭhasya nihavamūhediti asya hi anyatrotpattiḥ ata ūhedityuktam
3.9.13.[1]	cātvālamupasthāyāgnīdhrīyasyottareṇa pradeśena gatvā paścime pradeśe tiṣṭhantaḥ tasyopasthānaṃ kuryuḥ uktaṃ satrasyarddhyāgnīdhramupatiṣṭhanta iti
3.9.14.[1]	cātvālasyopasthānaṃ kṛtvā tasminneva deśe'vasthitāḥ pratyaṅmukhāḥ āgnīdhrīyamupatiṣṭherannityevaṃ dhānañjapyaḥ ācāryo manyate
3.9.15.[1]	yadi paścāttiṣṭhantaḥ yadi cātvāladeśe tasya satrasyarddheḥ uttamanidhanamātamitoḥ upeyuḥ tāvadarddhayeyuryāvannāntaḥ uktam ātamitornidhanamupayantīti
3.9.16.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ ślokānuślokābhyāṃ havirddhāne upatiṣṭhanta iti havirddhānayoḥ pūrve pradeśe'vasthitāḥ pratyaṅmukhāḥ ślokānuślokayoḥ sāmnoḥ pūrveṇa ślokenetyarthaḥ havirddhānayorupasthānaṃ kuryuḥ
3.9.17.[1]	paścime pradeśe tayoreva sthitāḥ pratyaṅmukhāḥ anuślokenopatiṣṭheran ta eva havirddhāne
3.9.18.[1]	tatraiva deśe'vasthitāḥ īkṣamāṇā mārjālīyaṃ yāmenopatiṣṭheran uktaṃ yāmena mārjālīyamupatiṣṭhanta iti tatra sarveṣāṃ yāmānāṃ prāptau niyamayati yaddvandveṣviti yāmānāmanekatvānniyamayati yannāke suparṇamiti yāmantat syāditi
3.9.19.[1]	yathā havirddhāne upasthite tenaiva prakāreṇa sada upatiṣṭheran uktamāyurnavastobhābhyāṃ sada upatiṣṭhanta iti pūrve pradeśe sadasaḥ pratyaṅmukhā avasthitāḥ tamāyuṣā sāmnopatiṣṭheran paścāditareṇa paścime pradeśe prāṅmukhā avasthitāḥ navastobhena sāmnopatiṣṭheran
3.9.20.[1]	uktaṃ ṛṣyasya sāmnā gārhapatyamupatiṣṭanta iti antarvederantarvedi pratyaṅmukhāstiṣṭhanta gārhapatyamupatiṣṭheran yathoktenaiva sāmnā
3.9.21.[1]	tasyaiva gārhapatyasya paścime pradeśe'vasthitāḥ prāṅmukhā upatiṣṭherannityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryo manyate
3.9.22.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ yatparokṣaṃ nidhanamupeyurhrītamukhaṃ pratimuñceran yatpratyakṣamupayanti hrītamukhamevāpajayantīti indraśabdādārabhya pratyakṣaṃ nidhanaṃ brūyuḥ lokavat pratyakṣaparokṣe āmantritaṃ pratyakṣaṃ nirddiṣṭaṃ parokṣaṃ devadattaḥ saḥ devadattaḥ indreti pratyakṣam sa indra iti parokṣam
3.10.1.[1]	parimādaḥ gītvā athānantaraṃ rājānaṃ sannāhayet athaśabda ānantarye rājānamiti kṣattriyaṃ sannāhayet anyat uktaṃ sannaddhāḥ kavacinaḥ pariyantīti
3.10.2.[1]	tasya rājñaḥ dvyavarārddhyau rathau anuyāyinau syātāṃ bhaveyātāṃ paścādyāyinau sarve nikṛṣṭau dvau yadi bahavo rathā na syuḥ nanu tasya dvyavarārddhyā rathā anuyāyinaḥ syurityevaṃ sūtraṃ karttavyamāsīt tatraivamapare varṇayanti dvyavarārddhyau manuṣyau yasmin rathe so'yaṃ dvyavarārddhyo rathaḥ dvyavarārddhyaśca dvyavarārddhyaśca dvyavarārddhyau ekasminneva ekasmin rathe bahavo manuṣyā abhipretāḥ tata āha dvyavarārddhyā iti
3.10.3.[1]	devayajanasya pūrve pradeśe sannahyeran rājānaṃ muktvānye anuyāyinaḥ
3.10.4.[1]	sannaddhāḥ santaḥ dakṣiṇena devayajanaṃ parigaccheyuḥ
3.10.5.[1]	udgātā patnīśālāyāḥ pūrveṇa pradeśena gatvā mahāvederdakṣiṇe vedyante darbhān prāgagrān āstīrya teṣu darbheṣu enaṃ rājānaṃ prāṅmukham upaveśayet
3.10.6.[1]	athaśabda ānantarye prāgagreṣu darbheṣūpaveśya rājānam anantaramasmai varma badhnīyāt uttiṣṭha rājannityetadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa anyaṃ vābhiharantam enaṃ mantraṃ brūyāt
3.10.7.[1]	rājānaṃ paścimena devayajanaṃ pariyāhītyuktvā yenaiva gatastenaiva punarāvrajya uttare vedyante enaṃ rājānam avasthāpya brūyāt hastatraṃ badhnīṣva ujjyamāyudhaṃ kuruṣva trīniṣūnupakalpayasva anugṛhṇīṣva āyasmāyān kārṣṇāyasān yameva kañca caturthamiti yaṃ kañceṣucaturthanna niyamaḥ
3.10.8.[1]	iṣuṃ pratidhatsveti brūyāt
3.10.9.[1]	taṃ rājānaṃ pratidadhānam iṣuṃ sandadhānaṃ anumantrayeta vaiṇavatāya pratidhvatsva śaṃkumityetadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa
3.10.10.[1]	saṃhateṣu rathamāroheti brūyāt rājānam
3.10.11.[1]	dakṣiṇena pradeśena rathapathaṃ kṛtvā kasya dakṣiṇena vakṣyati pūrvāpare carmaṇī vibadhnīyuriti tayoścarmaṇordakṣiṇena uttareṇāgnīdhrīyam enaprayoge dvitīyā āgnīdhrīyasya uttare pradeśe pūrvāpare carmaṇī vibadhnīyuḥ pūrvañca aparañca pūrvāpare carmaprahārāntanaṃ te carmaṇī dve vibadhnīyuḥ
3.10.12.[1]	taṃ rājānaṃ brūyādudgātā pradakṣiṇaṃ devayajanaṃ parīyāt pūrvaṃ carma yattadāgamaneṣu vidhyeḥ āgamanāgamaneṣu ekaikeneṣuṇā vidhyeḥ uktaṃ trīniṣūnupakalpayasveti uttarottarā vedhasya vedhasyopariṣṭāduttarottarī prathamasyopariṣṭāddvitīyaḥ dvitīyasyopariṣṭāt tṛtīya iti anatipātayan bhūmāvapātayanniṣuṃ tathā vidhyedyathā tasminneva carmaṇi saṃsaktā bhavanti
3.10.13.[1]	aparasmai carmaṇi itare rathinaḥ yathābhipretaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ kṣipeyuḥ
3.10.14.[1]	evaṃ brūyād rājānaṃ tṛtīyeneṣuṇā viddhvā udaṅmukhaḥ prayāyāḥ gacchet
3.10.15.[1]	tadā tasmin kāle udaṅ gacchat caturthamiṣum uktaṃ yameva kañca caturthamiti yāndiśaṃ manyethāḥ icchā bhavet tāmasyeḥ etaduktaṃ bhavati udaṅgacchan caturthabāṇaṃ yāndiśaṃ prati icchā bhavati tāṃ diśaṃ kṣipet yasmin deśe gāḥ paśyeyuḥ tasminneva deśe avatiṣṭhethā avasthānaṃ kurvīran
3.10.16.[1]	tatra yasmindeśe avatiṣṭheran tasmin deśe tvā viśrambhayeyuḥ varmādisannahanamapanayeyuḥ
3.10.17-19.[1]	evaṃ sampreṣya rājānaṃ anantaraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brūyāt yadidaṃ mayā rājñe upadiṣṭam etatsarvaṃ rājānaṃ hiṅkāravelāyāṃ kārayeriti evamuktvā bhūmidundubhimāvrajet kva bhūmidundubhirbhavatītyata āha / 17 / 18
3.11.1.[1]	uktaṃ bhūmidundubhirbhavatīti sa bhūmidundubhirucyate agnīdhrīyasya paścime pradeśe vederantaḥ antarvedi arddhaṃ śvabhrasya khātaṃ syāt śvabhraḥ garttaḥ arddhaṃ bahirvedi śvabhrasya khātaṃ syāditi
3.11.2.[1]	sa śvabhraḥ ārṣabheṇa carmaṇā ṛṣabhasya avayavamārṣabhaṃ tena ārṣabheṇa uttaralomnā upari lomāni yasya carmaṇaḥ tadidamuttaralomnā tena ārṣabhena uttaralomnā carmaṇā abhivihitaṃ syāt sarvataḥ avanaddhaḥ syāt
3.11.3.[1]	tvaṃ vāgasītyetadādibhiḥ yathāsūtritairmantraiḥ itikaraṇaprajñāpitāntaiḥ etairbhūmidundubhiṃ pṛthagāhatya bāladhānena pṛthak nānetyarthaḥ vālā asmin dhīyante iti bāladhānaṃ pucchaṃ tena bāladhānena vādayitvā anyaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vādayamānaṃ anumantrya apaḥ sṛṣṭvā paścāttiṣṭhanto'gnimupatiṣṭheran paścime pradeśe iṣṭakācitasyāgneḥ tiṣṭhantaḥ śiraādīnāmaṅgānāmātmanaścopasthānaṃ kuryuḥ namaste gāyatrāya yatte puro yatte śira ityetadādibhiryathāsūtritairmantraiḥ pṛthak nānetyarthaḥ arthamanu anvarthaṃ arthānusāreṇa namaste gāyatrāyeti śiraḥ namaste rathantarāyeti dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣaṃ namaste bṛhata ityuttaraṃ namaste yajñāyajñīyāyeti pucchaṃ namaste vāmadevyāyeti ātmānam
3.11.4.[1]	vyastānāmupasthānaṃ kṛtvā athānantaraṃ samastānāṃ sāmastyenaiva mantreṇopasthānaṃ kuryuḥ tasmai ta ityetadādinā mantreṇa yathāsūtritena
3.11.5.[1]	upasthāya vyastasamastaistato'nantaraṃ sadaḥ praviśeyuḥ
3.12.1.[1]	uktam upasthāya sadaḥ praviśeyuriti sāmprataṃ pṛṣṭhena stavanamuktam āsandīmāruhyodgāyatīti tasyā āsandyāḥ praveśanamucyate aparayā dvārā sadasaḥ paścimayetyarthaḥ audumbarīmāsandīmūdumbarasya vikāraḥ audumbarī āsandī saṃjñā āsyate asyāmityāsandīṃ mauñjavivānāmatihareyuḥ mauñjaṃ vivānaṃ muñjebhyo nirvṛttāṃ mauñjavivānāmatihareyuḥ praviśeyuḥ
3.12.2.[1]	yadyudumbaro na syāt yasya kasyacit yajñiyasya vṛkṣasyāvayavaniṣpannā syāt āsandī yajñamarhati yajñiyaḥ
3.12.3.[1]	yadi muñjo na syāt darbhamayaṃ vivānaṃ syāt abhāvo'nupapattiḥ
3.12.4.[1]	uktaṃ prādeśamātrī bhavatīti tasyā āsandyāḥ prādeśamātrāḥ pādā itararāsyaṅgāni aratnipramāṇani syuḥ aṅgulaṃ prādeśo'ratnirityetadādīni parimāṇāni siddhāni granthāntare
3.12.5.[1]	tāmāsandīmaudumbaryyā dakṣiṇena pradeśena hṛtvā tasyā uttarārddhe sannikarṣe sthāpayeyuḥ tasyā iti kimartham ucyate, sadohyadhikṛtam atastasyā iti bravīti tasyā audumbaryyā uttarato na sadasaḥ
3.12.6.[1]	tasyā āsandyā uttareṇa pradeśenodgātā gatvā paścime pradeśe upaviśya bhūmispṛśaḥ asyā āsandyāḥ pādān kṛtvā kūrcau tasyā adhastādupohya tānabhimṛśet bṛhadrathantare te pūrvau pādāvityetadādibhiryathāsūtritairmantraiḥ pṛthagāsandyaṅgānyanvarthaṃ pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ arthamanu anvarthaṃ yathāliṅgamityarthaḥ
3.12.7.[1]	yadi mauñjaṃ yadi dārbhaṃ vivānamālabhya spṛṣṭvā ṛcaḥ prāñca ityetadādinā yathāsūtritaṃ mantraṃ japet
3.12.8.[1]	tāmāsandīṃ mukhenorasā bāhubhyāñca spṛṣṭvodgātā ārohet vasavastvetyetadādibhiryathāsūtritairmantraiḥ tāmiti kimartham ucyate, vivānamālabhyeti prakṛtam atastāmityāha
3.12.9.[1]	athaśabdo vikalpārthaḥ athāgamaparaḥ vikalpa etaireva mantrairdevatā utkṣipya padānāmanviṣya rājaśabdañca amunā tvā chandasā rohāmītyārohet prakāramupadiśyate gāyatreṇa vā chandasā rohāmi traiṣṭubhena tvā chandasā rohāmi jāgatena tvā chandasā rohāmi ānuṣṭubhena tvā chandasā rohāmi iti
3.12.10.[1]	etaiḥ udasya devatārājāśabdaiḥ vairājapañcamairārohet ityevaṃ gautama ācāryyo manyate vairājena vā chandasā rohāmītyeva pañcame prayogaḥ
3.12.11.[1]	eteṣāmevodasya devatārājaśabdānāṃ caturbhiḥ pūrvaiḥ stomairārohedityevaṃ dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate
3.12.12.[1]	eteṣāmeva pūrvaistribhiriti śāṇḍilya ācāryo manyate uktārthānāmeva, nanu ānantaryārtho athaśabdaḥ kasmānna bhavati athānantarametairudasya devatārājaśabdaḥ ārohediti ucyate, ukta chandobhirārohatīti tadekenaivārohaṇasyārthavattvaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati atha punaḥ samuccayaḥ kalpyate tadā pūrveṇa kalpenāruhya punarārohaṇārthamavarohaṇaṃ syāt tanmābhūdityato vikalpārtho'thaśabdaḥ kalpyate
3.12.13.[1]	āruhya āsandīṃ syonāmāsadamityetaṃ mantraṃ japet
3.12.14.[1]	tasminnudgātari ārohati āsanārthān pūrvakalpitān kūrcānāroheyuḥ ke praṣṭī pārśvavarttino praṣṭī prastotṛpratihattarau brahmā gṛhapatiśca
3.12.15.[1]	āsandyā vyākhyātam uktaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ vāṇasya uktaṃ vāṇaṃ vitanvantīti tat kiṃmayo vāṇo bhavati taducyate āsandyā vyākhyātaṃ dravyaṃ vāṇasyeti audumbaro vāṇaḥ syāt udumbarābhāve yajñiyavṛkṣasya
7.13.1.[1]	gautama ācāryo manyate sarvāsāṃ dhurāṃ samastānāmetadbrāhmaṇaṃ syāditi kasmāt yasmāt triṣṭubjagatīsaṃjñayoḥ stotrīyayorakṣarāṇāṃ nirvacanaṃ kṛtam evaṃ samastānāṃ dhurāṃ niruktāniruktatā dṛṣṭā
7.13.5.[1]	udasyodasyodāsaṃ tadudastagānaṃ paṭhitameva
7.13.9.[1]	iḍādīni kāmyāni nidhanāni yāvatprayogaṃ gāyatrasya bhavanti tāni sadādīni bahiṣpavamāna eva bhavanti nordhvam
7.13.11.[1]	gāyatryāḥ triṣṭubhaśca vyatikramaṃ dhānañjapyo manyate triṣṭubhaṃ kṛtvā gāyatrīṃ kuryyāt
7.13.13.[1]	etasminneva hoturājyagāne triṣṭubhaṃ gītvā tasyottarāṃ gāyatrīṃ gāyet tatastasyāṃ triṣṭubha uttarāṃ gāyatrīṃ gītvā tasyā eva yā dvitīyā ṛk tasyāmanuṣṭubhaṃ gāyedityevantāḥ sarvā hoturājye gītā bhavanti evaṃ dhānañjapya ācārya āha
8.1.2.[1]	yatra saṃkhyāmātraṃ dakṣiṇāmādiśyate dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ sahasraṃ vā'yutamiti na dravyaṃ viśiṣyate tatra dakṣiṇā gāvaḥ pratyetavyāḥ atha mātragrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate, grahaṇamātraṃ yasmāt tatrāpi gāva eva pratyetavyāḥ yathā itarebhyaḥ kiñciddadyāt kuladakṣiṇa indrāgnyoḥ kulā yatra iti caśabdo na deśānukarṣaṇārthaḥ
8.1.22.[1]	tadviśvajito devayajanaṃ prati patnīśālā bhavet prāgviśvajitaḥ
8.1.27.[1]	kāmantu pṛthagbhṛtābhyāmeva yajeta na yamābhyām
8.1.28.[1]	abhijiti pṛthagbhūte sahasraṃ dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ viśvajiti pṛthagbhūte śatāśvaṃ sahasraṃ sarvavedasaṃ vā yasmin sahasre śatamaśvānāntacchatāśvaṃ sahasraṃ tadā śatāśvaṃ sahasraṃ dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ viśvajiti sarvavedasaṃ vā sarve vedasaḥ sarvavedasaṃveda iti dhananāma sarvasvamityarthaḥ
8.2.1.[1]	uktaṃ śatāśvaṃ sahasraṃ sarvavedasaṃ vā viśvajiti dakṣiṇā evaṃ viśvajiteṣṭvā tatastasya viśvajito 'vabhṛthādudetya rohiṇīṃ vatsacchavīṃ paridhāya dharmān kuryāt rohiṇīmiti varṇanirdeśaḥ vatsacchavīmiti jātasya vatsasya chatrī carma tāṃ vatsacchavīṃ paridhāya yajamāno dharmān kuryyāt te dharmā uktā brāhmaṇena paśubhirvā eṣa vyṛdhyata ityāhuryaḥ sarvaṃ dadātīti chavīṃ paridhatte paśubhireva samṛdhyata ityetadādayaḥ atha tasyeti nirdeśaḥ kimarthamiti cet ucyate abhijit viśvajitāvadhikṛtau pūrvaṃ viśvajidabhijidbhyāṃ yajamāna iti tayośca sāmānyo vidhirutaḥ tadya ete dharmā nirddiśyante te sāmānyadharmā eva gamyeran evaṃ mābhūdityata āha tasyeti apare bruvate tasya sarvavedasadakṣiṇasyeti na śatāśvasahasradakṣiṇasyeti pūrva evamityarthaḥ evamapyartham upariṣṭāt jñāpayiṣyāma iti yathā syāditi
8.2.8.[1]	niṣādeṣu tisro vasatīti brāhmaṇaṃ niṣādagrāmasya pārśve vaset niṣādīṣviti janopalakṣaṇaṃ bahuvacanam
8.2.16.[1]	athavā vratavatsu kratuṣu rātrisatreṣu dīkṣābhireva saṃvatsare samāpte rājānaṃ krīṇīyuḥ
8.2.18.[1]	dhānañjaya ācārya āha sarveṣu vratavatsu yathājāti dīkṣeran yadyanyatra karmaṇi vratamupetaṃ syāt prathamaṃ vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ
8.3.2.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha praga evartvigbhyaḥ preṣayet kutaḥ yena sādyaḥkrīma iti dīkṣāprabhṛti yatkarma tatsadyaḥ sarvaṃ kuryuḥ prathamadvitīyayoḥ sādyaḥkrayoḥ śyenasya ca eteṣāṃ sadyaḥ prathamā sadyaḥ dvitīyā syāt
8.3.6.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ khale vālīyūpo bhavatīti khale vālīyūpa ityukte lāṅgaleṣā yūpaḥ syāt lāṅgalaṃ halam etayā hitaṃ rasamutkṛṣantīti lāṅgaleṣā yūpaḥ syāditi prokṣaṇādiyūpadharmān karoti kalāpī dhānyamuṣṭiḥ kalāpīkṛtaḥ caṣālasthāne karttavyaḥ atha kiṃ bhāgagrahaṇaṃ kalāpī caṣālabhāgeti ucyate caṣālaḥ bhāgo yasyāḥ sā caṣālabhāgā yāvantaṃ deśaṃ yūpasya caṣālā bhajate tāvadeva kalāpo bhajatīti
8.3.7.[1]	yadyatītāyāṃ vrīhivelāyāṃ yajeta yaveṣu lūneṣu brīhiṣu vātīto dhānyapātrānuptvābhikṛṣeyuḥ alī trījīsā vediḥ syāt
8.3.10.[1]	yo vā tisro gāḥ pibet sa vā trivatsa iti tisṛṇaṃ vatsaḥ trivatsaḥ
8.4.1.[1]	etenaiva prathamena sādyaḥkreṇa uttaro vyākhyāto 'yaṃ vidhyanta uktaḥ mādyaḥkreṇa yakṣyamāṇa ityata ārabhya eṣa eva sarva uttarasminnapi bhavati
8.4.4.[1]	tasyānukrayaḥ krayādārabhyottaramahaḥ syāditi gautamaḥ taṃ sadyaḥ parikrīyeti hi ādityānadhikṛtyāhaitadbrāhmaṇaṃ nāṅgirasaḥ
8.4.13.[1]	tasya viśvajicchilyasya dakṣiṇā yānāni yānti tairiti yānāni ārohaṇāni śakaṭagantryudarṣakādīni yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt yāvānutsāho 'sya yathotsāhaṃ tasmin janapade yānyabhidhyātatamāni syuḥ kāṅkṣitatamāni syurīpsitatamāni kimarthaṃ punarayaṃ yānaśabdaḥ aśvādiṣvapi na varttate ucyate eteṣāmeva śakaṭādīnāṃ parārthā pravṛttirna svārthā nīyate ca tāni na svayaṃ gacchanti aśvādayastu svayañca gacchanti tasyeti nirdeśaḥ sarveṣu kalpeṣu tasyaiva dakṣiṇā
8.5.1.[1]	ukto viśvajicchilyaḥ sāmprataṃ śyenasya vidhirvaktavyaḥ taṃ vivakṣurāha vrātīnānāmiti nānājātīyā aniyatavṛttaya utsedhajīvinaḥ saṅghātāḥ vrātāḥ vrātānāṃ karma vrātakarmaṇā jīvanti vrātīnāḥ yodhanāt yodhaḥ yodhabhavā yaudhaḥ teṣāṃ vrātīnānāṃ yaudhānāṃ putrānanūcāntān putraśabdaḥ pratītapadārthakaḥ uktavānanūcānaḥ tānanūcānān vrātīnānāṃ putrānṛtvijo vṛṇīta śyenasya athānūcānāniti kimidamityārabhyate yadā ṛtvikprakaraṇa evoktamṛtvigārṣeyonūcāna iti ucyate ṛtvikśabdena yo 'yamṛtvijo guṇasamudāyaḥ sa kṛtsnaḥ prāptaḥ tasmin prāpte ekenaiva parisaṃkhyānaṃ karoti kevalam anūcānāḥ syuḥ anyeṣāmaniyamaḥ syāditi athavā nivarttayatyevānyānekadeśaparisaṃkhyānaṃ siddhe satyārambho niyamārtho niyamaścātra nivarttako bhavati na parisaṃkhyānādanyanivṛttiriti
8.5.3.[1]	abhivātāsu goṣu vyādhitāsu yā anabhivātā avyādhitāḥ syustā dohayitvā tatkṣīraṃ manthayet tato yadudgacchet ghṛtaṃ tenājyaṃ kuryāt
8.5.6.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ śavanabhye adhiṣavaṇa iti śavanabhye iti kimuktaṃ bhavati ucyate yena yānena mṛtaṃ nirvaheyuḥ śavantasya yānasya nabhye nābhyā nirvṛtte adhiṣavaṇaphalake kuryuḥ
8.5.7.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ tailvako vā bādhako vā yūpasphāgra iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kathaṃ sphyāgra iti kiṃ sphyāgraḥ upamārtho 'yamatha sphyāgra evāgre so 'yaṃ sphyāgra iti so 'yamācārya āha acaṣālā yūpaḥ sphyāgra iti nāstyasya caṣālamityacaṣāla iti
8.5.19.[1]	gautama ācārya āha ekadīkṣastryupasatkaḥ syāt
8.6.1.[1]	uktāḥ sādyaḥkrāḥ sāmprataṃ vrātyastomā ucyante tān vivakṣuridaṃ sūtramārabhate vrātyastomairiti vrātyānāṃ stomāḥ kiṃlakṣaṇāḥ punarvrātyā iti ucyate paṭhitā brāhmaṇena hīnā vā ete hīyante ye vrātyāṃ pravasanti na hi brahmacaryaṃ racanti na kṛṣiṃ na vaṇijyamiti tathā garagirā vā ete ye brahmādyaṃ janma mantramadantyaduruktavākyaṃ duruktamāhuradaṇḍyaṃ daṇḍena ghnantaścarantyaḥ dīkṣitā dīkṣitavācaṃ vadantīti evaṃprakārāḥ vrātyāḥ paṭhitāḥ ye cānye śākhāntareṣu paṭhyante te sarve vrātyāḥ vrātyastomairiti karaṇe tṛtīyā yakṣyamāṇa iti bhaviṣyatkālopadeśaḥ te vrātyā vrātyastomairyakṣyamāṇāḥ pṛthagagnīnādhāya pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ pṛthagagnyādhānāni kṛtvā yajñopakaraṇāni ceṣṭvā yajñopakaraṇāni yajñasādhanāni dravyāṇi arjayitvā ya eṣāṃ vrātyānāmadhyayane 'bhikrāntitamaḥ syāt abhikrāntā adhyayanena sarva ime abhikrāntinaḥ ayameṣāmabhikrāntitamaḥ atiśayena tamatiṣṭhinau abhijanena vā yo'tiricyate abhijanaḥ kulaṃ yaḥ kulena vādhikaḥ syāt tadabhāve 'pi bhogalābhena tayorabhāvastadabhāvaḥ tayoḥ svādhyāyābhijanātirekayorasambhave bhogalābhena ye 'tiricyate dravyavattamaḥ syāt tasya gārhapate dīkṣeran sa teṣāṃ mukhyaḥ syāt bhakṣāṃśca tasyānu sarve bhakṣayeyuḥ
8.6.2.[1]	ete vrātyastomāścatvāraḥ paṭhitāḥ tatra prathamo 'viśeṣeṇa sarvān vrātyānadhikṛtya paṭhitaḥ anye tu dvitīyādayo viśiṣṭaviṣayā uktāḥ te yathāmnānaṃ bhavati sāmprataṃ prathamasya tāvadvidhirucyate ye kecidvrātyāḥ sampādayeyuriti nātra niyamaḥ ye kecit sampādayeyuḥ saṃkhyāṃ te prathamena vrātyastomena yajeran kiyantaṃ stomasaṃkhyayā uktaṃ trayastriṃśaddhi devā ārdhnuvanniti
8.6.8.[1]	uktaṃ jyāhnoḍaśceti kaḥ punarjyāhnoḍa iti ucyate dhanuṣkeṇa aniṣuṇā vrātyāḥ prasedhamānā yanti alpakaṃ dhanuḥ dhanuṣkaṃ tena dhanuskeṇa aniṣuṇā akāṇḍena vrātyā lokaṃ prasedhamānāḥ āsedhantaḥ trāsayanto yanti sa jyāhnoḍaḥ
8.6.10.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācārya āha prācyaratho na vipathaḥ kampramiśrābhyāmaśvāśvatarābhyāṃ yuktaḥ syāt sa vipathaḥ kampanaśīlaḥ kampraḥ aśvaśca aśvataraśca aśvāśvatarau tayorekaḥ kampanaśīlaḥ kaścana tābhyāmavaśyamevotpathaḥ kriyate gativaiṣamyāt evamasau vipatho bhavati
8.6.13.[1]	gautama ācārya āha śuklaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇadaśaṃ vā etatkṛṣṇadaśamiti so 'yaṃ madhyavarṇalopī samāsaḥ
8.6.14.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha evamahammanye kṛṣṇameva kṛṣṇaśamiti svārthe taddhita iti
8.6.17.[1]	niṣkaḥ prajñātaḥ niṣko nāmālaṅkāra iti sarājato bhavati
8.6.22.[1]	dve dve dāmanī iti brāhmaṇam ekaikasya vasanasya dve dve daśe syātām uktaṃ granthiḥ pārśe ceti
8.6.24.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha yāḥ kāścopānahaḥ syuḥ aniyamo varṇakarṇayoḥ
8.6.29.[1]	vrātyastomair iṣṭvā te vrātyā yā traividyavatāṃ vṛttistāṃ samātiṣṭheyuḥ dvijānāmadhyayanamijyādānamityetadādi
8.6.30.[1]	teṣāṃ vrātyānāmiṣṭavrātyastomānāṃ tata ūrdhvaṃ bhuñjīta api cainān kāmaṃ yājayediti etadādarśayati ato arvāk caiva teṣāṃ pūrvaṃ yājanaṃ kṛtaṃ bhuktaṃ veti avyavahāryyāḥ akṛtaprāyaścittā iti
8.7.1.[1]	uktā vrātyastomāḥ anantaramagniṣṭuta āmnātāḥ teṣu na kiñcidavaśivyate yadvaktavyaṃ sarvamevoktaṃ dakṣiṇāyane agniṣṭutsviti sarvānagniṣṭuto 'dhikṛtya saptamī teṣu agniṣṭutsu anaḍuhāmaśvānāmajānāmiti yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt ano vahatītyanaḍvān yathotsāhamiti śaktyapekṣā kutaḥ vākyāt yathā asamāsaḥ kimarthamiti cet anaḍuhāśvājahiraṇyānāṃ yathotsāhaṃ dadyāditi vaktavye ucyate yadi samāsaḥ kriyate pratidravyaṃ bahutvaṃ na gamyate yathotsāhamityucyate pratidravyaṃ bahutvāniyamaḥ syāt anaḍuhāmaśvānāmajānāmiti yo yaḥ pratidravyaṃ bahuvacanaṃ karoti bahulavacanāddṛśyate kathaṃ pratidravyaṃ bahūnāṃ dānaṃ syāditi yathā hiraṇyasyeti yathotsāhamiti prakṛtam
8.7.2.[1]	iha brāhmaṇaṃ trivṛdagniṣṭomaḥ tasyāniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanamiti tatra paṭhati grāmakāmo yajeteti so 'yamācāryaḥ tasyāharaṇe aparamapyarthaṃ darśayati kañcidarthamarhanyo na prāpnuyāditi arhanyo 'pyasau tamarthaṃ naca prāpnoti tasya prāptaye anena trivṛtāṃ prathamena yajet
8.7.5.[1]	tasya bṛhaspatisavanasya prātaḥsavane āsāditeṣu nārāśaṃseṣu camaseṣu ekādaśadakṣiṇā vyādiśedṛtvigbhyaḥ vyādeśamātraṃ kuryyāt apākaraṇaṃ na kuryyāt ṛtvigbhyo vyādiśet apākaraṇamarpaṇam
8.7.7.[1]	yāśca prātaḥsavanīyāyāḥ tā aśvadvādaśāḥ ubhayormadhyandine dadāti sannihiteṣu nārāśaṃseṣviti prakṛtam evaṃ brāhmaṇam
8.7.8.[1]	evaṃ brāhmaṇam ekādaśatṛtīyasavane tā vaśāyāmapākarotīti tṛtīyasavane ekādaśadakṣiṇāḥ tā anubandhyasya paśorvapāyāṃ hutāyāmapākuryyāt vaśāpakṣe brāhmaṇat tatrāpyekādaśa eva
8.7.10.[1]	ya enaṃ yajamānaṃ puraskarvīran anvagbhūteṣu yā vṛttiḥ tata ūrddhvaṃ tāṃ vṛttiṃ teṣu vartteran anvagbhūtā nāma ye āśritāḥ tān bibhṛyāt yogakṣemamanteṣu kalpayet
8.7.11.[1]	te anvagabhṛtā enaṃ yajamānaṃ sthapatiriti ācakṣīran
8.7.12.[1]	iṣuḥ śyenenaiva vyākhyātaḥ yāvān śyenasya sūtrakāreṇa vidhiruktaḥ sa sarva eva iṣorbhavati ayantu viśeṣaḥ aikāhikyo dīkṣopasada iti iṣorbhavanti śyenyastu sadyopakramaḥ
8.8.1.[1]	agniṣṭutaḥ prakṛtāḥ tatra sarvasvārasya brāhmaṇaṃ trivṛdagniṣṭomaḥ sa sarvasvāro yaḥ kāmayetānāmayatāmuṃ lokamiyāmiti sa etena yajeteti tasya sarvasvārasya vidhirucyate sarvān yasmin svārāṇīti sa sarvasvāraḥ tena sarvasvāreṇa yakṣyamāṇo dīkṣābhya ārabhya prayateta prayatnaṃ kuryāt yathā sautye 'hani preyāṃ mriyeyamiti dīkṣāstasyā parimitāḥ kuryyāt
8.8.2.[1]	dīkṣābhya ārabhya yāvanto bhakṣāḥ sarvān prāṇabhakṣān bhakṣayet na pratyakṣabhakṣān sarvagrahaṇāt vratamapi prāṇabhakṣa eva
8.8.3.[1]	tān bhakṣānapobhyavahārayet anu prakṣipet karte vā prakṣipet khāte vā anuṣecayet
8.8.5.[1]	iha brāhmaṇam ārbhave pavamāne stūyamāna audumbaryā dakṣiṇe pradeśe kṛṣṇājinamupastīrya dakṣiṇāśirā nipadyeta saṃviśet tadeva saṅgacchate tadeva mriyata iti saṅgamanaṃ maraṇam
8.8.8.[1]	śāṇḍilyāyana āha yadi samāpayeyuḥ śeṣaṃ karma tato yadyajamānasya kṛṣṇājinaṃ tatputro bhrātā vā yo vā nediṣṭo syāt sa tat pratimucya āvṛtya yājamānaṃ karma kuryāt bhakṣāṃśca bhakṣayet tatra hi yajamānasya prāṇabhakṣaṃ sarvatra bhakṣān bhakṣayedityuktam ayantu punarbhakṣaṃ bhakṣayet
8.8.15.[1]	anubandhyasya paśoḥ śeṣaṃ samāpya devayajanasya madhye kāṣṭhaiścitāñcinuyuḥ
8.8.18.[1]	śirasi yajamānasya kapālāni kuryāt kapālāni yeṣu puroḍāśāḥ saṃskriyante
8.8.27.[1]	udare pātrīṃ sthāpayet
8.8.39.[1]	etat tāvatkṛtsnaṃ sārvasvārikamuktaṃ karma yāvatparimāṇamiti atha punarjīvennaiva mriyeta yajamānaḥ tata udavasānīyayā yajeta udavasānīyāntaṃ kṛtsnaṃ karma samāpayeyuriti etaduktaṃ bhavati mṛte tu parigānāntameva karma nodavasānīyāntam
8.8.48.[1]	itareṣāṃ vaiśvadevādīnāṃ ekaikasyāḥ pañcāśat pañcādaśaddakṣiṇāḥ varuṇapraghāse śataṃ dakṣiṇā iti paṭhitaṃ sākamedhe pañcāśacchatamiti tāḥ pratyahaṃ samatvavibhāgena kalpayati
8.9.1.[1]	upahavyasya brāhmaṇaṃ saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomo devāśca vā asurāśca prajāpaterdvayāḥ putrā āste 'surā bhūyāṃso balīyāṃsa āsan kanīyāṃso devāḥ te devāḥ prajāpatimupādhāvan sa etamupahavyamapaśyan sa aikṣata yanniruktamāhariṣyāmyasurā me yajñaṃ haniṣyantīti so 'niruktamāharediti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimāniruktyamiti tadvivakṣurācāryaḥ idaṃ satramārabhate upahavya iti upahavye kratau devatānāmadheyāni parokṣaṃ brūyuḥ svasthānāsu devatāsu parokṣatā parokṣaṃ devatāśabdamuddhṛtyānyena śabdāntareṇoccāraṇaṃ devatāyāḥ anirvacanam etadāniruktyam evaṃ svasthānāsu kuryāt
8.9.2.[1]	aśvasthānāsu pratyakṣameva śabdaṃ prayuñjīta devatāsthānāni nyāyyānyuktāni kimudāharaṇaṃ somātirekāditi
8.9.3.[1]	uktaṃ svasthānāsviti devaśabdaṃ sarvatra varjayeyuḥ
8.9.5.[1]	brāhmaṇenādiṣṭā dakṣiṇā yāvat yasya ceti aśvaḥ śyāvo dakṣiṇā sa hyaniruktaḥ sa brahmaṇe deya iti
8.9.6.[1]	itarebhyaśca ṛtvigbhyaḥ kiñciddadyāt caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ brahmaṇe cāśvaṃ dadyāditarebhyaśca kiñciddadyāditi kiñcicchabdoktam
8.9.7.[1]	ṛtapeye paṭhati tasya dvādaśadīkṣopasada iti tatra asamaśruteḥ dīkṣopasadāṃ vibhāgasaṃśaye viśinaṣṭi tisra upasada iti nava dīkṣā iti sāmarthyātsiddham
8.9.8.[1]	ghṛtavrato bhavatīti brāhmaṇam etaddīkṣāsu yāvadutsāhantāvat ghṛtasya prāśnīyāt yāvatāsya śarīraṃ noparudhyate
8.9.10.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācārya āha ekāṅgulyā pṛthak parvabhiḥ pṛthaṅgānetyarthaḥ sarvāndeśān prati camasā mitāḥ syuḥ ekaikenāṅguliparvaṇā ekekaścamaso mitaḥ syāt taiścamasairanulobhaiḥ prāśnīyāditi
8.9.13.[1]	yā devatācamasairijyeran tābhirdevatābhiste camasāḥ pītā bhavanti tasmātpītavadeva bhakṣamantrānūheyuriti ṛtapeyatvāt evaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryo manyate
8.9.14.[1]	nārāśaṃsānāṃ camasānām avikāreṇa bhakṣamantraḥ syāt
8.9.17.[1]	taṃ camasaṃ dakṣiṇākāle āhavanīyasya pūrveṇa pradeśena anirgamayanto vedeḥ yūpāhavanīyāntareṇa hṛtvā sado havirddhānayośca dakṣiṇena hārayitvā pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ praveśayeyuḥ
8.9.18.[1]	saṃsthite samāpte 'hani ṛtvigbhyaḥ kiñciddadyāditi
