8.10.1.[1]	ṛtapeya uktaḥ tadanantaraṃ paṭhitaṃ saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomastasya dīkṣaṇīyāyāmiṣṭau dvādaśamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ dadātīti somasaṃsthā dakṣiṇā phalāṇi śrūyante karmanāmadheyañca śrūyate so 'yamācāryyaḥ sarvajñaḥ śrutyantaraṃ dṛṣṭvā nāmadheyaṃ kalpayatīti ādiṣṭā dakṣiṇā brāhmaṇena dūṇāśasyeti kathamādiṣṭā tasya dīkṣaṇīyāyāmiṣṭau dvādaśamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ dadātītyata ārabhya yāvadaṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni vaśāyāṃ vapāyāmiti
8.10.2.[1]	yatra syādetāvantyaṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānānīti yathā dve aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamāne agnīṣomīyasya paśorvapāyāñcatvāryaṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni prātaḥ paśorvapāyāmaṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni prātaḥsavaneṣu nārāśaṃsesvityetadādi tatra caturviṃśatiśatamānānāntāvanti tāvatparimāṇāni aṣṭāviṃśatiśatāni dadyāt
8.10.3.[1]	uktaṃ rukmo hotuḥ sragudgāturiti rukmo hoturityuta niṣkonāmālaṅkāraḥ sauvarṇastaṃ dadyāt
8.10.6.[1]	tasya vaiśyastomasya dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ sahasraṃ vā vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ ayantu viśeṣo yathārūpāḥ pañcaśāradīye paśava ālabhyante tadrupā dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ
8.10.7.[1]	tīvrasuti yajñe aneke adhikṛtāḥ śrūyante somātipavitaṃ yājayedityata ārabhya tatra anye śabdāḥ pratītapadārthakāḥ somātipavita iti ucyate
8.10.8.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācārya āha iṣṭvā yaḥ pāpīyān bhavet sa somātipavita iti sarvathā iṣṭvā śreyasā bhavitavyaṃ yastu pāpīyān bhavati sa somātipavitaḥ atipavanaṃ nāma asamyak pariṇāmaḥ tasya samyak somaḥ pariṇataḥ
8.10.9.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha yaḥ somaṃ pītvā chardayeta viricyeta vā sa somātipavita iti vājasaneyyaparā śrutiḥ
8.10.11.[1]	anena prakāreṇa sarveṣu savaneṣu camasānāṃ bhakṣaṇavidhiḥ
8.10.13.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ śatamāśiraṃ duhantīti dhenūnāṃ śatandohayitvā traidhantatkṣīraṃ vibhajya tena somaṃ miśraṃ kuryuḥ yena prakāreṇa vaiśyastome sadyo dugdhena prātaḥsavane śṛtena madhyandine dadhnā tṛtīyasavane
8.10.14.[1]	tasya tīvrasutaḥ yadetacchatamāśiraṃ duhantīti tadeva dhenuśataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ evaṃ hi brāhmaṇamāha tā u eva dakṣiṇa iti
8.11.1.[1]	tīvrasuduktaḥ sāmprataṃ vājapeyena vājapeya āmnātaḥ sa ucyate yaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ yamityuddeśaḥ rājānaśca puraskurvīran sa puraskāro nāma pūjā mahaḥsthāpanaṃ puraskṛtaḥ san vājapeyena yajet yathoddeśena nirdeśaḥ kimarthaṃ yaṃ sa iti brāhmaṇaṃ rājabhiḥ puraskṛto vājapeyena yajetetyevaṃ vaktavyamāsīt ucyate taittirīyake śrutiḥ brāhmaṇakṣatriyayoreva vājapeyo na vaiśyasyeti yathā etasmin kalpakāra āha vājapeyaḥ śaradyo 'vaiśyasyeti so 'yamācāryya etaṃ vidhiṃ uddeśanirddeśābhyāmāha
8.11.2.[1]	tasya vājapeyasya paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitvā trayodaśa dīkṣā bhaveyuḥ
8.11.3.[1]	saptadaśa vā dīkṣā bhaveyuḥ
8.11.4.[1]	gautama ācārya āha amāvāsyāyāṃ dīkṣitvā māsandīkṣāḥ syuriti
8.11.6.[1]	idaṃ purastāt tathopariṣṭāccāsya vājapeyasya vidhānamucyate pārṣṭikān stomān jyotiṣṭomatantre kalpayitvā trivṛdādīṃstrayastriṃśāntān tantralakṣaṇamuktaṃ tairjyotiṣṭomādibhirjyotiṣṭomenaiva vyavetaiḥ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrvapakṣeṣu yajeta prathame pūrvapakṣe jyotiṣṭomaṃ kṛtvā dvitīye pūrvapakṣe jyotiṣṭomatantre trivṛtaṃ kalpayitvā tena yajeta evameteṣāṃ pārṣṭikānāṃ stomānāṃ jyotiṣṭomena vyavahitānāṃ tantrapūrveṇa kriyā tatastrayodaśe pūrvapakṣe vājapeyena yajeta tata iṣṭvā vājapeyena etairevāvṛttairye pūrvasmin saṃvatsare kṛtāstairaparaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ yajeta taistrayastriṃśādibhirjyotiṣṭomavyavahitaiḥ prātilomyena yathotsāhadakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ te sarve caturviṃśati yathotsāhaśabdaḥ śaktyapekṣaḥ
8.11.7.[1]	lāmakāyana ācārya āha rājasūyavidhena yajeteti yadvidho rājasūyastadvidheneti rājasūyasadṛśeneti
8.11.8.[1]	abhyārohaṇaṇīyasya sthāne trivṛt pañcadaśastomo jyotiḥ syāt
8.11.9.[1]	abhiṣecanīyasya sthāne vājapeyaḥ syāt
8.11.10.[1]	keśavapanīyasya sthāne pañcadaśatrivṛt stomaḥ jyotiḥ syāt
8.11.11.[1]	vyuṣṭidvirātrasya sthāne kṣatrasya dhṛteśca jyotiṣṭomau syātāṃ pṛthak
8.11.12.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha vājapeyasya purastādupariṣṭācca bṛhaspatisavenaiva yajeta evaśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ bṛhaspatisavenaiva nānyeneti
8.11.13.[1]	śāṇḍilyāyana cācārya āha māsamātre purastāt jyotiṣṭomena yajeta tathopariṣṭājjotiṣṭomenaiveti
8.11.14.[1]	gautama ācārya āha pratyavarohaṇīyenaivāntato yajeta itareṣāṃ na kenaciditi itare kalyāstvekeṣāmeva gautamasyāniṣṭāḥ
8.11.15.[1]	ekaikasya pṛthaktvena varaṇaṃ kuryāt athartviggrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti sadasyasaptadaśān vṛṇīteti vaktavye na cānyeṣāṃ varaṇapravṛttiḥ ucyate asyopariṣṭāt prayojanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
8.11.16.[1]	tasya vājapeyasya dakṣiṇāḥ dāsyādīnāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ saptadaśa saptadaśa ekaikasyaikaikasya jātasya syuḥ dāsyaḥ karmakāryyaḥ niṣka uktalakṣaṇaḥ sauvarṇā alaṅkārāḥ rathāḥ prajñātāḥ tathā hastinaḥ yānāni śakaṭādīni gāvaḥ prasiddhāḥ pṛṣṭhena vahantīti pṛṣṭhyāḥ aśvāḥ eteṣāṃ yathoddiṣṭānāṃ jātānām ekaikasya saptadaśa saptadaśa syuḥ tasya grahaṇaṃ kriyate tasya sarveṣu kalpesviti
8.11.17.[1]	uktaṃ saptadaśaikaikasya jātasyeti tadgavāmapi prāptaṃ tathaiva tato viśinaṣṭi sahasrāṇi gavāṃ saptadaśa syuḥ śatāni veti
8.11.18.[1]	saptadaśa vaiva gāvaḥ syuḥ anyāḥ sarvāni varttante tadevaṃ kuruvājapeya ityācakṣate eke tāvata bruvate karttā vājapeyaḥ taṃ kuruvājapeya iti athavā taṃ kuruvājapeya ityācakṣate alpako vājapeyaḥ yathā alpikā nadikā kurunadikā ityucyate supūrā vai kunadiketi
8.11.19.[1]	tā dakṣiṇāḥ samamṛtvigbhyo vibhajet etat jñāpayati anyāsāntvanādeśāt tat sārvatriko vibhāga iti tā iti nirdeśaḥ kriyate saptadaśagāvo 'dhikṛtāḥ śataṃ sahasraṃ tasmādāhṛtā iti tāstāḥ athartviggrahaṇaṃ kimartham ucyate yo 'sāvṛtvijāṃ madhye vṛtaḥ pūrvasadasyaḥ tasyāpyatra vibhāgaḥ syāditi
8.11.20.[1]	athavā teṣu dakṣiṇājāteṣu yadyacchreṣṭhaṃ tanmadhyataḥ kāribhyo dadyāt itarebhyaḥ samaṃ vibhajet
8.11.21.[1]	yena rathenājindhāvettaṃ rathamudgātre dadyāt āsandīñca sāstaraṇāṃ yāmāsandīmabhiṣiktaḥ sannārohet āsandī uktalakṣaṇā
8.11.22.[1]	bastasya carma bastacarma bastaḥ chāgaḥ taccarma sarukmaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ hotre dadyāt yasmin carmaṇyāsīno 'bhiṣicyet
8.11.23.[1]	vāsobhirnirvṛttā rasanāḥ tā adhvaryave dadyāt
8.11.24.[1]	sauvarṇaṃ sthālaṃ pātraṃ madhunaḥ pūrṇaṃ madhu iti dravyanirddeśaḥ tadbrahmaṇe dadyāt
8.11.25.[1]	athavā kaṃsasthāle hiraṇyatuṣāḥ hiraṇyaśakalāḥ tānmadhumiśrān dadyāt
8.12.1.[1]	tasya vājapeyayājinaḥ vratānyādiśyante vratamiti karmanāma kṣatravṛttiṃ varttayet kṣatrasya yā vṛttistāṃ vṛttiṃ varttayet adhīyīta nādhyāpayet dadyāt na pratigṛhṇīyāt etāṃ kṣattravṛttiṃ varttayet
8.12.2.[1]	pratyavarohaṇañcābhivādanañca pratyavarohaṇabhivādane pratyavarohaṇaṃ pratyutthānaṃ yadyanyavrajyāṃ kim ādeśakāritvena gamanaṃ samānaśayyatāmekasminneva śayane śayanam etānyavājapeyayājinā saha na kuryāt
8.12.3.[1]	ye vājapeyayājinaḥ tairyathāvayasam etāni kuryāt ye jyeṣṭhāsteṣāṃ pratyavarohaṇādi kuryādityarthaḥ
8.12.4.[1]	kiyantaṃ punaḥ kālametāni vratāni bhavantītyatra lāmakāyana ācārya āha pratyavarohaṇīyeneṣṭvā tato naitāni vratāni carediti pratyavaroṇīya uktaḥ klṛpto jyotiṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohaṇīya iti
8.12.5.[1]	tasya vājapeyasya vikalpā ārabhyata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
8.12.6.[1]	yo 'yaṃ prākṛto vājapeyaḥ pathyaḥ etasminneva ekiprabhṛtīn dvyuttarān saptadaśasaṃkhyātastrayastriṃśāntān stomān kalpayet sa vājapeya evaṃ stomaklṛptaḥ san mayūro nīkarṣītyevamucyate mayūraḥ kalāpī atha saptadaśagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ekiprabhṛtayo dvyuttarībhāvena kalpamānāḥ trayastriṃśāntāḥ saptadaśaiva sampadyante vakṣyatyayaṃ brahmasāmaiva pratyeteneṣṭvā svargaṃ lokamākrameteti so 'yamācāryo niyamārthaṃ saptadaśagrahaṇaṃ karoti pratyavarohaṇavidhāne saptadaśaiva trayastriṃśāntāniti
8.12.7.[1]	tasyaivaṃ klṛptasya vājapeyasya upāsmai gāyatā nara ityetadbahiṣpavamānaṃ syāt
8.12.8.[1]	dhānañjaya ācārya āha brahmasāmaiva prati etena iṣṭvā svargaṃ lokamākrameteti iva brahmasāmnā kāmānavāpnotīti
8.12.9.[1]	aparo vikalpaḥ jyotiṣṭomo 'tirātraḥ aṣoḍaśikaḥ syāt anatirātro vā jyotiṣṭomaḥ syāt ṣoḍaśimān
8.12.10.[1]	prākṛte hi śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhat klṛptaṃ tena iha svāsvityāha
8.12.11.[1]	agniṣṭomo vā syāt jyotiḥ
8.12.12.[1]	tasyāgniṣṭomasaṃsthasya jyotiṣaḥ abhīvarttī brahmasāma syāt anuṣṭubhi yajñāyajñīyamanukalpayet bṛhadagniṣṭomasāma syāt yajñāyajñīyasyarkṣu
8.12.13.[1]	pañcaviṃśastomaṃ pṛṣṭhānāṃ brahmasāma syāt achāvākasāma vā itaratsarvaṃ caturviṃśam
8.12.14.[1]	athavā etasyaiva yathāklṛptasya sāmadravyasya catustriṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni syuḥ agniṣṭomasāma ca catustriṃśameva itaratsarvaṃ saptadaśaṃ syāt
8.12.15.[1]	gautama ācārya āha ya ete jyotiṣṭomo 'tirātraṣoḍaśika ityārabhya vikalpā uktāḥ naiteṣāṃ kaścidapi vā vājapeya iti nātra pratiṣedho yajamānasyeti ebhiryajamāno na vājapeyadakṣiṇā dadyāditi
9.1.1.[1]	ukto vājapeyaḥ anantaraṃ rājasūyo vaktavyaḥ taṃ vivakṣurārabhate rājā rājasūyena yājya iti ayaṃ sūtrārthaḥ prāptābhiṣekakṣatriyo rājasūyena yajeteti
9.1.2.[1]	phalgunībhyāṃ yuktā phālgunī phālgunyāḥ pakṣaḥ phālgunīpakṣaḥ tasya phālgunīpakṣasya yā prathamā tithistasyāṃ dīkṣeta abhyārohaṇīyāya jyotiṣṭomāya uktam agniṣṭomaṃ prathamamāharatītyādi maśakenāpyuktaṃ klṛpto jyotiṣṭoma iti so'bhyārohaṇaṇīyāya jyotiṣṭomaḥ syāt tasmai tadarthaṃ dīkṣeta
9.1.3.[1]	tasya abhyārohaṇīyasya jyotiṣṭomasyaikā dīkṣā syāt dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ evaṃ paribhāṣitaṃ teṣāmekā dīkṣā'nādeśe tisraścatasro'parimitā veti so'yamācāryo niyamayati tasyaikā dīkṣeti nanu dakṣiṇāparimāṇaṃ na karttavyaṃ kutaḥ tasyānatirātrasya dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇā iti paribhāṣitatvāt ucyate tatra tasya pradhānasyoktam ayantvaṅgabhūto'svatantrastasmādatra vaktavyam
9.1.4.[1]	iṣṭvābhyārohaṇaṇīyena saṃvatsaramāsitvā tato'bhiṣecanīyena yajeta abhiṣecanīya iti saṃjñā tasminneva kāle yasmin kāle'bhyārohaṇīyeneṣṭaṃ phālgunīpakṣasya prathamāyāmiti
9.1.5.[1]	tasvābhiṣecanīyasya yathaivābhyārohaṇīyasya tathaiva dīkṣā syāt eketyarthaḥ
9.1.6.[1]	gautama ācārya āha dve dīkṣe syātāmabhiṣecanīyasyeti //
9.1.7.[1]	tathā sati kalpe abhyārohaṇīyasyāpi dve dīkṣe syātām abhiṣecanīye ca parasya matam
9.1.8.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācārya āha ekābhyārohaṇīyasya dīkṣā syāt abhiṣecanīyasya tisraḥ syuḥ ayantu viśeṣaḥ trayodaśyāpamarapakṣasya dīkṣeta
9.1.9.[1]	tasyābhiṣecanīyasya dakṣiṇā ucyante dvātriṃśataṃ sahaśrāṇi madhyataḥ kāribhyaḥ ekaikasmai dadyāt madhyataḥ kāriṇastu hotradhvaryubrahmogātāraḥ
9.1.10.[1]	ṣoḍaśasahasrāṇi prastotrādibhyo dadyāt ekaikasmā iti varttate
9.1.11.[1]	tā etā ṛtvijaḥ arddhinya ucyante
9.1.12.[1]	aṣṭau sahasrāṇi pratihartrādibhyo dadyāt ekaikasmā iti prakṛtaṃ tāstṛtīyinya ityucyante
9.1.13.[1]	catvāri sahasrāṇi subrahmaṇyādibhyo dadyāt ekaikasmā ityanuvarttata eva tā etā hotrāḥ pādinya ityucyante tā etāḥ saṃjñā madhyataḥ kāribhyo'rddhinyastṛtīyinyaḥ pādinya iti saṃjñā saṃvyavahārārthāḥ vakṣyati cāyamaṣṭācavāriṃśaṃ śataṃ vā madhyataḥ kāribhyaḥ sahasrāṇi dadyādityevamādi tathā gargastrirātrādiṣu dakṣiṇāprativibhāgaṃ vakṣyati etaddarśayati yatra yatra dakṣiṇānāṃ saṃvibhāgaḥ prativiśiṣṭo nocyate tatrāyaṃ saṃvibhāganyāya dūti madhyataḥ kāribhāgāt etā utpadyante
9.1.14.[1]	asya rājño yajamānasya jñātayaḥ pratirājānaḥ tān abalān kṛtvā nirjitya saha vittenānayeyuḥ rājabhṛtyāḥ
9.1.15.[1]	tānabalānānītān rājā jinīyāt dakṣiṇāvelāyām
9.1.16.[1]	iṣūṃścaibhyaḥ asyetkṣipet dakṣiṇāvelāyāṃ yajamānaḥ
9.1.17.[1]	tāniṣūn kṣiptān ta eva rājānaḥ pratyāhareyuḥ vijayasva rājanniti bruvantaḥ
9.1.18.[1]	teṣāṃ rājñāṃ vittasya tṛtīyaṃ bhāgamṛtvigbhyo dadyāt
9.1.19.[1]	daśapeye'nuprasṛptibhyaḥ tṛtīyaṃ bhāgaṃ vibhajya dadyāt anuprasarpakā vakṣyante śeṣaṃ tebhya eva pratyutsṛjet tasya vittasya
9.1.20.[1]	tasya vittasya śeṣantebhya eva rājabhyaḥ pratyutsṛjet pratidadyāt //20
9.1.21.[1]	grāmāṃścaibhyo dadyāt
9.1.22.[1]	tata ūrddhvante rājanyāḥ syuḥ rājasamānatvaṃ prāpnuyuḥ na abhiṣekārhāḥ syuḥ
9.1.23.[1]	tenābhiṣecanīyeneṣṭvā na pratyakṣamavabhṛthamabhyaveyāt avabhṛthaṃ nāpsu majjet kṛṣṇaviṣāṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇājinasya pādaṃ vā apsvavadadhyāt majjayet
9.1.24.[1]	ito devayajanādavabhṛthaṃ vārāhībhyāmupānadbhyāṃ vrajet varāhacarmaṇā nirvṛttā vārāhī kārṣṇībhyāṃ kṛṣṇasāracarmaṇā nirvṛttābhyāmupānadbhyāṃ pratyāvrajet
9.2.1.[1]	uktaṃ teneṣṭvā na sākṣādavabhṛthamabhyaveyāditi sāmpratañcāsminneva dīkṣito'bhiṣecanīyasya daśāhānte tato daśapeyena yajeta daśāhe saptadīkṣeṣṭayastisraścopasadaḥ daśapeya iti saṃjñā
9.2.2.[1]	tasya daśapeyasya brāhmaṇaṃ daśa daśa camaśamabhiyantīti yat, abhiyantītyasya padasya ko'rthaḥ atrāha
9.2.3.[1]	subrahmaṇyaḥ caturtho yeṣānta ime subrahmaṇyacaturthāḥ te udgātāraḥ subrahmaṇyacaturthā udgātṛcamasaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ ṣaḍvānye brāhmaṇāḥ yadetadbrāhmaṇaṃ daśa daśa camasamabhiyantītyasyāyamarthaḥ daśa daśa camasaṃ bhakṣayantīti tatkathametadgamyate abhiyantītyukte bhakṣayantīti gamyate ucyate liṅgāt daśapeya iti athodgātṛgrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti camasaṃ bhakṣayantīti siddhe prakṛte udgātāra iti ucyate anyatrāpi yatra subrahmaṇyaḥ somaṃ bhakṣayet tatrodgātṛcamasenaiva
9.2.4.[1]	evamitareṣāñcamasānāṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ yāvatā daśapūryeran tāvatā brāhmaṇān gṛhītvā ekaikaṃ camasaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ yajamānacamasantu yajamāna eva bhakṣatet nānyaḥ
9.2.5.[1]	te brāhmaṇā ye camasān bhakṣayanti daśamātṝrdaśapitṝniti anvākhyāya prasarpeyuḥ mātṝḥ pitṝniti dvitīyā karmaṇi ādaśamāt puruṣādanvākhyāya prasarpantītyevaṃ brāhmaṇamāha mātṛtaśca daśa pitṛtaśca daśa ācakṣīran
9.2.6.[1]	yasyā ārabhya brāhmaṇatvaṃ pravṛttantāmevābhyasyeyuryāvaddaśamaḥ pūrṇa iti kaḥ punarasya viṣayaḥ varṣāntarāgamanamutkarṣābhyāmiti
9.2.7.[1]	asmarantaśca nāmāni yataḥ smareyustasyaivābhyāsaṃ kuryurnāmni
9.2.8.[1]	te prasarpakā ṛtvigbhiḥ saha dhiṣṇyopasthānaṃ kuryuḥ
9.2.9.[1]	sragudgāturiti brāhmaṇaṃ srapsyate'smai udgāturbahiṣpavamānamarpaṇakāla ityarthaḥ sauvarṇīṃ srajaṃ mālāṃ tripuṣkarāṃ tribhiḥ sauvarṇapadmaiḥ saṃyuktāṃ pratimuñcet badhnīyāt
9.2.10.[1]	āstāva upaviṣṭāya kasmai udgātre yajamāna audakīṃ udake bhavāmaudakīṃ dvādaśapuṣkarāṃ dvādaśapadmasaṃyuktāmābadhnīyāt yāsya yajamānasya svā bhavet
9.2.11.[1]	stutvā bahiṣpavamānena audakī dvādaśapuṣkarā tāṃ yajamānāyaiva punardadyāt
9.2.12.[1]	itarayā hiraṇyasrajā āvṛddhayā sarvamahaḥ kṛtvā sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī yāvat samidādhānamiti sa evodgātā gṛhṇīyāt
9.2.13.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ prākāśāvadhvaryvoriti sauvarṇaḥ prākāśo'dhvaryordakṣiṇe pradeśe śirasā ābaddhaḥ syāt prākāśa ādarśaḥ prakāśakaraḥ prākāśaḥ apare bruvate karṇotsānū prākāśāviti pratiprasthātuḥ raupyaprakāśaḥ savye pārśve syādābaddhaḥ
9.2.14.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ vāsaḥ poturiti tadvāsaḥ kārpāsaṃ syāt kārpāsasya vikāraḥ kārpāsam
9.2.15.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ barāsī neṣṭuriti sā barāsī kṣaumī syāt kṣumāyāḥ vikāraḥ kṣaumī
9.2.16.[1]	itarā dakṣiṇāḥ yāśca deyā yebhyaśca tā brāhmaṇenaiva vijñātā vispaṣṭāḥ paṭhitāḥ
9.2.17.[1]	tasya daśapeyasyāvabhṛthādudetya saṃvatsaraṃ devavratāni caret tasya grahaṇamabhiṣecanīyo'pi adhikṛta iti /
9.2.17.[2]	kāni punardevavratāni ucyate
9.2.18.[1]	unmardanaṃ kuryyāccharīrasya udakena snānaṃ na kuryyāt
9.2.19.[1]	śodhayet dantān dantakāṣṭhaṃ bhakṣayet
9.2.20.[1]	nakhāṃśchedayet
9.2.21.[1]	śmaśrūṇi vāpayet na keśān
9.2.22.[1]	vyāghrasya vikāro vaiyāghraṃ tasminvaiyāghre carmaṇyuttaralomni āstṛtasyaivopariṣṭāllomāni syuḥ agnyagāre'gniśaraṇe tasmin carmaṇi śayīta
9.2.23.[1]	ahanyahanyagnau samidha ādadhyāt
9.2.24.[1]	na grāmāntaḥ praviśet etat jñāpitaṃ bhavati yathā devayajanamaraṇye bhavatīti apare bruvate nānugrāmaṃ praviśediti maithunapratiṣedhaḥ grāmyaṃ karma na kuryāditi
9.2.25.[1]	asya rājño rāṣṭre nābrāhmaṇā vāpayeran keśaśmaśruromanakhāni na kārayeyuḥ
9.2.26.[1]	aśvānāñca keśacchedanaṃ na kuryuḥ
9.2.27.[1]	tejaninā dantānna cchindyuḥ tejanī vikaṭaḥ
9.2.28.[1]	prasravaṇāni na cchindyuḥ
9.2.29.[1]	brāhmaṇāstu yathābhipretaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ chedanaṃ kuryuḥ tathā ye cānyān brāhmaṇānāśritā anye varṇāste'pi yathābhipretaṃ kuryuḥ
9.3.1.[1]	uktaṃ daśapeyaḥ tasyāvabhṛthādudetya saṃvatsarandevavratāni carediti tatastasmāt saṃvatsarādūrddhvaṃ keśavapanīyāya dīkṣeta keśavapanīya iti saṃjñā saṃvatsaradhṛtānāṃ keśānāṃ tasmin vapanaṃ kriyate keśavapanīyāyeti tādarthye caturthī dīkṣeteti yajamānasya kriyopadeśaḥ yasmin kāle'bhiṣecanīyena yajeteti abhiṣecanīyasya kāla uktaḥ
9.3.2.[1]	tasya keśavapanīyasya paurṇamāsyāmatirātraḥ syāt
9.3.3.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha daśapeyeneṣṭvā yastasyottaraḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ anantarantasminneva keśavapanīyena yajeteti paurṇamāsyāmeva cātirātraḥ syāditi
9.3.4.[1]	tasya keśavapanīyasya sahasraṃ dakṣiṇāḥ tasya grahaṇaṃ yadi saṃvatsarādūrddhvaṃ yadyanantaraṃ pūrvapakṣa iti
9.3.5.[1]	tasya keśavapanīyasya udavasānīyayeṣṭvā yadanantaraṃ paurṇamāsaṃ prāptaṃ aniṣṭvā tena vyuṣṭidvirātrāya dīkṣeta yadyamāvāsyāyāṃ pūrvamahaḥ karttumicchet uktam amāvāsyāyāṃ pūrvamaharudvṛṣṭaṃ uttarannānaivārddhamāsayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati paurṇamāsyāṃ pūrvamaharvyuṣṭakāyāmuttaraṃ nānaivamāsīt pratitiṣṭhatīti
9.3.6.[1]	paurṇamāsyāṃ pūrvamaharityevañceccikīrṣet pūrvapakṣa eva dīkṣeta kṛtvādarśam
9.3.7.[1]	ubhayorvicārayoryadyamāvāsyāyāṃ yadi paurṇamāsyāṃ yajanīye'hni uttaramahaḥ syāt pratipadītyarthaḥ kutaḥ punarayaṃ saṃśayaḥ yathā amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā pūrvasminnahni kṛtena yajanīye'hni uttaramahaḥ syāditi ucyate brāhmaṇam amāvāsāyāṃ pūrvamaharudvṛṣṭa uttaramiti tadyasminnahani darśanaṃ bhavati candramasastadudvṛṣṭaṃ nāma tasya tu darśanaṃ kadācidyajanīye'hani bhavati nityantu dvitīyāyāṃ tadatra darśanaśaṅkayā kadācidyajanīyamaharlaṅghayet so'yamācāryo niyamārthamārabhate yajanīye'hanīti yadyapi tasminnahani na dṛśyate kāla evāyaṃ sādhudarśanastasyāvikṛṣṭā eva dvitīyā bhavati tasminnahani
9.3.8.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ vyaṣṭakāyāmuttaramiti tāmisro'parapakṣaḥ vigatā vyāptirasminnityaparapakṣapratipadi candramasastasmādasau vyaṣṭaketyucyate tena sarvavyāpterekayā kalayonobhavati atha tisro vyaṣṭakā iti kimidaṃ yadā vyaṣṭakārthaḥ kṛtaḥ pratipadyeva ucyate etaddarśayati yathaiva pūrvapakṣa utthānāya tathaiva tāmisraprathamāni trīṇyahānyutthānīyāni bhavanti loke hi yāni pūrvapakṣakāryyāṇi tānyeteṣvahassu kriyeranniti
9.3.9.[1]	athavā ubhe evaite'vyuṣṭidvirātrasyāhanī pūrvapakṣe syātāṃ yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇamāha ye evetyādi
9.3.10.[1]	asya vyuṣṭidvirātrasya pūrveṇa keśavapanīyena dakṣiṇā vyākhyātāḥ tasya sahasraṃ dakṣiṇā iti
9.3.11.[1]	iṣṭvā vyuṣṭidvirātreṇa yadi tasminneva pūrvapakṣaṃ avakāśaḥ syāt antaraṃ syāt tasminneva pakṣe kṣattrasya dhṛtinā yajeta uktaṃ klṛpto jyotiṣṭomaḥ kṣatrasya dhṛtiriti
9.3.12.[1]	avidyamāne avakāśe ya uttaraḥ pūrvapakṣastasmin kṣatrasya dhṛtinā yajeta
9.3.13.[1]	sa kṣattrasya dhṛtirabhyārohaṇīyena jyotiṣṭomena vyākhyātaḥ yo'bhyārohaṇīyasya vidhiḥ sa tasya tasyaikā dīkṣā dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇā ityetadādi
9.3.14.[1]	tayoḥ kṣattrasya dhṛtyabhyārohaṇīyayoḥ pṛthak sahasre dakṣiṇāḥ pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ ekasminnapi sahasramanyasminnapi evaṃ gautamadhānañjapyāvācāryāvāhatuḥ keśavapanīye ca dve sahasre dakṣiṇaḥ syuḥ caśabda ācāryamatānukarṣaṇārthaḥ tathā vyuṣṭau vyuṣṭidvirātre dve sahasre dakṣiṇāḥ tayorevācāryyayormatam
9.3.15.[1]	abhiṣecanīye catvāri sahasrāṇi dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ iti gautama ācāryo manyate
9.3.16.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha abhiṣecanīye pañcasahasrāṇi dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ atrābalānāṃ jñātīnāṃ vittaṃ syāt nityaṃ dānaṃ tuśabdo viśeṣaṇārthaḥ sarveṣu dakṣiṇaṇakalpeṣu
9.4.1.[1]	ukto rājasūyaḥ sāmprataṃ dvandvā vaktavyāḥ teṣāṃ rājyakāmayajñaḥ prathamo rāṭ sa ucyate rājītyadhikaraṇā saptamī tasmin rāji ekaviṃśativargān kṛtvā yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt liṅgaṃ aṣṭāvekaviṃśaḥ saṃstuto bhavatīti aindra ṛṣabhaḥ indro devatā asyetyaindra ṛṣabha iti gauścodyate vayoviśiṣṭastena purastāccopariṣṭācca yajeta pariśabda ubhayatovācī
9.4.2.[1]	virāji kratau daśaśaḥ daśavargān kṛtvā yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt atrāpi sāmānyāddaśa daśa bhavantīti trayantu viśeṣaḥ āgneyena paśunā purastādupariṣṭācca pariyajeta aviśiṣṭaḥ paśuśabdaśchāge varttate
9.4.3.[1]	aupaśade kratau vaiśvadevena paśunā purastāduparitācca yajeta
9.4.4.[1]	tasyaupaśadasya caturviṃśamekaśataṃ dakṣiṇaḥ atrāpi sāmānyam ekaikā stotrīyopajāyata iti dvādaśastotrīyā upajāyante prākṛtebhya ūrddhvaṃ dakṣiṇā api dvādaśaivopajāyante
9.4.5.[1]	uktaṃ punaḥ stomamadhikṛtya yo bahu pratigṛhya garagīriva manyate sa etena yajeteti taducyate pūrve vayasi uccāvacānyājayitvā upanīya vā tebhyaḥ samāvartsyan nivarttayiṣyamāṇaḥ punaḥ stomena yajeta
9.4.6.[1]	tasya punaḥ stomasya dvādaśamithunā dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ dvādaśaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanamiti sāmānyatā punaḥ dvādaśa mithunā dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ mithunaśabdastrīpuṃsasambhavaḥ striyaḥ pumāṃsaśca evaṃ dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate
9.4.7.[1]	śāṇḍilyo dakṣiṇaṃ vikalpayati śīrṇo yo rathaḥ punaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ punarutsyūtaṃ śāmūlaṃ jīrṇaṃ śāmūlaṃ punaḥ sūtreṇa saṃskṛtaṃ śāmūlamiti ūrṇaṃ vāsaḥ punardhenuḥ viśuṣkā gauḥ pravṛttakṣīrā punardhenuḥ punarvatsaḥ stanapānānnivṛttaḥ san punaḥ pravṛttaḥ eteṣāṃ dravyāṇaṃ yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt ityetacchāṇḍilya āha punastvasāmānyāt
9.4.8.[1]	dvau catuṣṭomau tayoḥ pūrvasmiṃścatuṣṭome ekakhurāṇaṃ aśvāśvataragardabhānāṃ yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt ubhayeṣāmuttarasmin catuṣṭome ekakhurāṇāñca dvikhurāṇāñca yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt
9.4.9.[1]	udbhicca balabhicca udbhidbalabhidau tābhyāmudbhidbalabhidbhyāmaviprayogeṇa yajeta udbhidā iṣṭvā avaśyaṃ balabhidā yajeta sambandhena phalaśruteḥ arthaśeṣatvācca
9.4.10.[1]	tāvudbhidbalabhidau saptāpavargau syātām apavargaḥ samāptiśca ubhāviti pratyekaṃ saptāpavargo vasante ca svātāmubhāvapi
9.4.11.[1]	arddhamāsaḥ enayorantareṇa syāt māso vā saṃvatsaro veti kālavikalpaḥ antarāntareṇa yukte iti dvitīyā
9.4.12.[1]	tayorudbhidbalabhidoścaturviṃśativargān kṛtvā yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt pṛthaṅgānetyarthaḥ pratyekaṃ caturviṃśativargān yathotsāhaṃ dadyāt caturviṃśativargasāmānyāt gāyatrī sampadyate iti
9.4.13.[1]	apacityoḥ kratvoḥ pṛthak nānā caturyujāvaśvarathau dadyāt caturbhiryuk catvāro vāsmin yuktāścaturyuk
9.4.14.[1]	tau rathau ubhayataḥ kāṃsyakavacau syātāṃ kāṃsyaiva kavace ekaikasya rathasyobhayataḥ syātāṃ kaṃsasya vikāraḥ kāṃsyaṃ kavacaṃ sannahanam
9.4.15.[1]	tayorathayoścatvāro'pi śatārhāḥ aśvā yuktāḥ syuḥ śatam ekaiko'rhati mūlyamiti śatārhaḥ śatakriyo vā śatenaiva vā ekaikaḥ krītaḥ syāt
9.4.16.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryo manyate rājaitābhyāmapacidbhyāṃ yajeteti sa hi sarvasmāt pūjāṃ kāmayate
9.4.17.[1]	śāṇḍilya āha yaḥ kaścāpacitikāmaḥ sa etābhyāṃ yajeteti
9.4.18.[1]	agneḥ stomayoraikāhikena vratenokta upāyaḥ ekāheṣu bhava aikāhikā upagamanamupāyaḥ tisra upasado vratasyaikāhikasya gautamīyena ṣaḍ vā dvādaśa veti
9.4.19.[1]	tayoragneḥ stomayoḥ pṛthak ekaikasmin catvāri dhānyācitāni dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ dhānyācitānīti dhānyapūrṇāni śakaṭāni ekaikasminnapi catvāri anyasminnapīti kathametadgamyate yathā catvāri catvāri na dve dve ityucyate bahuvacanasāmarthyāt ṣaḍgavāni caturgavānīti catvāri dhānyācitānīti pūrvasya ṣaḍgavāni dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ uttarasya caturgavānīti ṣabhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ gobhiryuktāni ṣaḍ gavāni caturbhiścaturbhiryuktāni caturgavāni
9.4.20.[1]	ṛṣabhāṇāmanaḍuhāṃ dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ ṛṣabhe sahasraṃ vā vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ rājayajñatvāt
9.4.21.[1]	avidyamāneṣvapyṛṣabheṣu sarveṣu katipayā apyṛṣabhāḥ syuḥ itare vatsatarāḥ syuḥ vatsatareṣu bahutvamatantraṃ vatsatarāḥ sāṇḍāḥ syuḥ secanasamarthāḥ
9.4.22.[1]	vaiśyamiti varṇanirdeśaḥ vaiśyaṃ yaṃ vaiśyāḥ svarājānaḥ puraskurvīran svarājānaḥ yeṣāṃ svo rājā vaiśyānāṃ yathā trāyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ puraskāraḥ ādhipatye sthāpanaṃ sa gosavena yajñena yajeta
9.4.23.[1]	sa gosavo bṛhaspatisavenokto vyākhyātaḥ abhiṣekādividhyantasāmānyaṃ ya enaṃ puraskurvīrannanvagbhūtavṛttiṃ tata ūrddhvaṃ teṣu varttayet sthapatiriti cainanta ācakṣīraniti
9.4.24.[1]	ayutantu asya dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ śrutatvāt tuśabdo viśeṣaṇārthaḥ anyat samānaṃ bṛhaspatisavena syāt dakṣiṇāstu atrāyutaṃ syuḥ
9.4.25.[1]	marutstome brāhmaṇaṃ paṭhati etenaiva trīnyā yajediti ata ārabhyate sakhāyo bhrātaro vā ye sampādayeyuḥ te marutstomena yajeranniti sakhitvaṃ nāma prītipūrvakaṃ bhavati tadye samānajātīyā ekatra sampādayeyuḥ bhrātaro vā te marutstomena yajeranniti
9.4.26.[1]	tasya marutstomasya dakṣiṇāḥ tadrūpāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ yathotsāhaṃ dadyuḥ tasyeti nirddeśaḥ kriyate ayamekamasya vā bhavati trayāṇāṃ veti tadyadekasya syādyadi trayāṇāṃ tasya tasya pañcaśāradīye sāmānyaṃ marutstomatvam
9.4.27.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha yeṣāṃ keṣāñca paśūnāṃ yathotsāhaṃ dadyuriti
9.4.28.[1]	indrāgnyoḥ kulāye gavāṃ kulāni kṛtvā sarasvatyāḥ kulamidaṃ viśvarūpāyā idaṃ gaṅgāyāḥ ityevamādisaṃkhyaṃ prakṛtiṃ pūrayet kulādāne prayojanaṃ kulāya iti śabdasāmānyāt
9.4.29.[1]	indrastome sahasraṃ dakṣiṇāḥ rājayajñatvāt
9.4.30.[1]	rājā ca purohitaśca rājapurohitau tāvekatra yajeyātāmindrāgnyoḥ stomena evaṃ hi brāhmaṇaṃ rājā ca purohitaśca yajeyātāmiti
9.4.31.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ gāyatrīñca jagatīñca sampadyata iti brāhmaṇe gāyatrīsampannā dakṣiṇā dadyāt gāyatrīsampaccaturviṃśatiḥ rājā jagatīsampannā dakṣiṇā dadyāt jagatīsampannā aṣṭācatvāriṃśat
9.4.32.[1]	kāmantu pṛthaṅnānā yajeyātāṃ tayorevameva dakṣiṇaḥ syuḥ gāyatrīsampannā brāhmaṇasya jagatīsampannā rājñaḥ
9.4.33.[1]	vighanau dvau paṭhitau tābhyāṃ paśukāmo yajetābhicaranvā ubhayathā śrutiḥ paśukāmasyāpi tau bhavataḥ abhicarato'pi śrutisāmarthyāt
9.4.34.[1]	maśakaḥ paṭhati somasāmātharvaṇaṃ veti tatkimayaṃ tulyavibhāṣā atha viniviṣṭavibhāṣeti so'yamācāryo viniveśaṃ kalpayati yadā paśukāmaḥ syāt tadāsminnātharvaṇaṃ kuryyāt abhicarataḥ somasāma kuryyāt
9.4.35.[1]	paśukāmasya bṛhatīsampannāḥ dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ ṣaḍviṃśadakṣarā bṛhatīti
9.4.36.[1]	abhicarata etau vighanau iṣuṇa vyākhyātau iṣoryovidhiruktaḥ sa sarvo'pi bhavatīti
9.4.37.[1]	sandaṃśavajrau ca kratū iṣuṇā vyākhyātau
9.4.38.[1]	rājānaṃ sandaṃśena kratunā abhicaret janapadaṃ vajreṇa
9.4.39.[1]	rājānamabhicaran enau sandaṃśavajrau vyatyāsaṃ prayuñjīta vyatyāsaḥ sandaṃśaṃ kṛtvā vajraṃ vajraṃ kṛtvā sandaṃśaṃ anena nyāyena
9.4.40.[1]	etābhyāṃ sandaṃśavajrābhyāmiṣṭvā jyotiṣṭomena yajeta śānyarthaḥ nanu maśakenoktaṃ klṛpto jyotiṣṭomaḥ śāntyartha iti ucyate tatra sandaṃśavajrāvanadhikṛtyoktaṃ iha sandaṃśavajrāvadhikṛtau ataḥ punarāha
9.5.1.[1]	uktā ekāhāḥ sāmpratamahīnā vivakṣitāḥ teṣāṃ paribhāṣāmārabhyate paurṇamāsīdīkṣetyādinā paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitvā māsenāpavargo yeṣānta ime paurṇamāsīdīkṣāmāsāpavargā iti apavargaḥ samāptiḥ ahīnā iti vyāvahārikī saṃjñā trikāṇḍo yajñaḥ ekāhāhīnāḥ matrāṇīti ayaṃ niścayaḥ jyotiṣṭomātirātrādayaḥ ete sarve paurṇamāsīdīkṣāmāsāpavargāśceti kecittu pralobhanāṃ kurvanti ye māsāpavargāste paurṇamāsīdīkṣā iti māsāpavargā tayā paurṇamāsīdīkṣātvamupapadyata iti ke punarmāsāpavargā ityucyate ye sutyābhyuccayinaste māsāpavargā iti vakṣyati ekatriṃśe'hani yajñapuchaṃ triṃśe vā sutyābhyuccaya iti sūtraṃ kṛtvā vayantu brūmaḥ ye ca sutyābhyuccayino ye ca na sarveṣāmahīnaśabdaḥ sāmānyaḥ śrutiprāmāṇyāt jyotiṣṭomātirātrādārabhya yāvatpauṇḍarika iti ucyate yadi ca ye sutyābhyuccayinaḥ teṣu paurṇamāsīdīkṣatā māsāpavargatā ceṣṭābhaviṣyat na śeṣeṣu vidhirārapsyeta asmin kāle dīkṣā iyatyaśca dīkṣopasada iti yena punarviśeṣeṇa vidhirārabhyate tena ca manyāmahe sarveṣāmayaṃ sāmānyo vidhiriti
9.5.2.[1]	teṣāmahīnānāṃ dvādaśopasadaḥ syuḥ teṣāmiti nirdeśaḥ kriyate anyatrāsmāt samāhṛtyānādeśa iti iha punaḥ kimanādeśa iti na pratītiḥ anādeśāgrahaṇāt sāmānyasya vidherviśeṣakasya ca vikalpaḥ prāpnoti jamadagnipañcaśāradīyādivat tena teṣāmityārabhyate teṣāmeva paurṇamāsīdīkṣāṇāṃ māsāpavargāṇaṃ dvādaśopasadaḥ syuḥ anyatra yathādeśameveti apare punarbruvate anādeśagrahaṇavikalpa eveti
9.5.3.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha ṣaḍupasadaḥ syuriti
9.5.4.[1]	yajñapucchamatirātraḥ seyaṃ viniviṣṭaviṣayā vibhāṣā triṃśini māse ekatriṃśe'hani yajñapucchaṃ syāt ekonatriṃśini triṃśe evaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitasya paurṇamāsyāmeva yajñapucchaṃ bhavati
9.5.5.[1]	upasadāṃ niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ dvādaśa ṣaḍiti vā sutyāsvapi niyataviṣaya eva tatsutyopasatsu śeṣeṇa dīkṣā bhavati dvirātraprabhṛtiṣu sutyābhyuccayena pratisutyaṃ dīkṣāṇāṃ hrāsaḥ syāt
9.5.6.[1]	sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī sarve'tirātrā ahīnāḥ siddhe sati vidhyantaramārabhate dvirātrādayaścāhargaṇāḥ sarve'hīnā aśvamedhādanye sarve sahasradakṣiṇāḥ prākcatūrātrebhyaḥ sarvagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate ye'pyahīnakāṇḍena santyatirātrāḥ yathā keśavapanīyasākamedhavyuṣṭidvirātrādayaśceti ye cānye śākhāntaradṛṣṭāḥ santyatirātrādayaḥ sarve sahasradakṣiṇā iti kaḥ punarviśeṣa āhīnikye yadā dīkṣākālo'pi prativiśiṣṭaḥ dakṣiṇā api rātriviśeṣe pṛthak samāmnāyāntaratayā nivṛttā tadāhīnikye sati ko viśeṣaḥ syāditi ucyate upasadastāvadāhīnikyaḥ syuḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ sambhavo'sti evaṃ kṛtvā nidānakāro'pi siddhamahīneṣvityupakramya keśavapanīyaprakaraṇamāha prācīnastoma uttaraḥ ityevamadhikṛtya athāpīdaṃ dvitīyaṃ yajñasthānaṃ yadahīno dvitīyo varṇaḥ kṣatriya iti
9.5.7.[1]	yaditi pūrvanirdeśaḥ catūrarātraprabhṛtīnāṃ bhūyasyaḥ sahasrā dakṣiṇāḥ syuḥ sutyābhyuccayena yathā yathā sutyā varddhayeran tathā tathā dakṣiṇā varddhayeran kaḥ punarupajanaḥ syāditi ucyate dvau nyāyau dṛṣṭau ekastrairātrikaḥ prativināśo dṛṣṭaḥ trayastriṃśacca trīṇi ca śatāni prathame'hani deyāstathā dvitīye tathā tṛtīye tathānukāravacane atha caturthādiṣvapi pratisutyaṃ aparonyāyaḥ yathā dīyamānāsu pauṇḍarīke ayutamupapadyate tathopajanaṃ kuryyāditi pañcaviṃśaṃ śataṃ sahasrañcopajana iti ekā evamayutotpattiḥ pauṇḍarika iti
9.5.8.[1]	vibhajya vibhajya vibhājam
9.5.9.[1]	yatra samapravibhāgonopapadyate tatra uttame'hani bhūyiṣṭhā dadyāt yāḥ samaṃ vibhāgaṃ nopapadyeran, tāḥ sarvā uttame'hani dadyāt
9.5.10.[1]	ekādaśarātre pauṇḍarīke ayutaṃ dadyāt nanu tatkimidamārabhyate yadā prayutameva śrutaṃ tatra ucyate, pravibhāgārthamārabhyate
9.5.11.[1]	navanavaśatāni pūrveṣvahaḥsu prathamādiṣu yāvaddaśamamiti uttame ekādaśe sahasraṃ dadyāt tatra hi yaddaśamamadhikaṃ śataṃ tatra samaṃ pravibhāgaṃ karttumekādaśasu ahaḥsu nava nava bhavanti ekāvaśiṣyate sā uttame'hani dīyate evaṃ pravibhāgo mābhūdityata āha yadyevaṃ nava nava pūrveṣvahaḥsu śatānīti ukte sahasramavaśiṣyate taduttama eva dāsyate tatkimidamārabhyate sahasramuttama iti ucyate uttame'hani dvādaśāhe upajananyāyena dakṣiṇāvibhāgāḥ prāptāḥ tāṣu prāptāsvāha sahasramuttama iti ucyate naitadyuktaṃ pradhāne jñāpakajñāpitā dakṣiṇā iti na yuktā janyāḥ praviṣṭā dvāreṇa sucinānāhatāḥ tasmādatra pratyahaṃ sahasraṃ dadyāt dakṣiṇā pravādamātraṃ bhavati sahasrāṇyāditsatāmiti
9.5.12.[1]	aptoryāmṇi paṭhati viśvajitāni pṛṣṭhānāṃ garbhā iti
9.5.13.[1]	bhavatyaptoryāmṇi vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ
9.5.14.[1]	tasya rathantarasya sthāne yatprakṛte'toryāmṇi bṛhatyāṃ kalpitaṃ tasya sthāne bārhataṃ vājajit syāt bṛhatyāṃ bhavaṃ bārhataṃ tasya grahaṇaṃ kriyate anyatrāpi rathantaraṃ kalpakena bṛhatā rathantarasthāne bārhataṃ vājajit syāt yathā caturviṃśe caturviṃśamarathantarapṛṣṭhaṃ vā bṛhadanuṣṭupkamiti
9.5.15.[1]	etasmin kalpe bṛhadvāravantīye uttare pṛṣṭhe syātāṃ tṛtīyacaturthe
9.5.16.[1]	kāleyasyarkṣu vāravantīyaṃ syāt caturthaṃ pṛṣṭham
9.5.17.[1]	tasya vāravantīyasya sthāne atiriktastotreṣu pūrvaṃ vāravantīyaṃ syāt
9.5.18.[1]	samaṃ tasya sthāne yadbṛhatyāṃ kalpitaṃ tasya sthāne kāleyaṃ syāt caśabdo vikalpānukarṣaṇārthaḥ
9.5.19.[1]	pārthasya sthāne mādhyandināntyamauśanaṃ syāt
9.5.20.[1]	pṛṣṭheṣu ta eva garbhāḥ syuḥ ye maśakenoktāḥ
9.5.21.[1]	aparaṃ vikalpaṃ dhānañjapya ācārya āha maśakaklṛpte'ptoryāmṇi vaiśvajitā nyāyānyājyeṣu garbhān kuryyāditi viśvajiti bhavāni vaiśvajitāni ṣāṣṭhikāni utthānyuktheṣu garbhān kuryyāditi ṣaṣṭhe'hani bhavāni ṣāṣṭhikāni aparaḥ pakṣaḥ
9.5.22.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācārya āha yathaivārṣeyakalpena kṛtaṃ vidhānaṃ tathaiva sthāt avadhāritamiti aparaḥ pakṣaḥ
9.5.23.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācārya āha yathā maśakena klṛptaṃ tathaiva svāt athavā jyotiṣṭome vātirātre ṣoḍaśimati atiriktastotrāṇi kuryyāt ṣoḍaśimatīti aṣoḍaśiko jyotiṣṭomo'tirātro'pi ityajyotiṣṭomo'pītyeva jñāpayati
9.5.24.[1]	ta eva garbhā maśakoktāḥ syuḥ yajñāyajñīyañca bṛhadgarbhaṃ syāt caśabda evamapi sūtrakārasya kalpaṃ darśayati api vā sarvāṇyāvarttāni vaiśvajitairāvarttibhiḥ garbhavanti kuryyāt tatra bṛhatsañcarate tasya vairūpaṃ vidhṛtyā iti
9.6.1.[1]	trirātre sahasraṃ śrutaṃ dakṣiṇāḥ tāḥ prativibhāgaṃ praviśiṣṭovibhāga ucyate uktam aśvamedhādanye sahasradakṣiṇā iti tat ye'śvamedhādanye trirātrāsteṣāmayaṃ dakṣiṇapravibhāga ucyate trirātrāṇāṃ prathame'hani vaṣaṭkāribhyo dadyāt hotṛmaitrāvaruṇabrāhmaṇachaṃsipotṛneṣṭrachāvākāgnīdhrebhyogrāvastute ca prathama eva dadyāt sā ca mātrā vakṣyate yasya yāvatī deyā
9.6.2.[1]	uttame'hani chandogebhyo dadyāt
9.6.3.[1]	ye anuktāstebhyo madhyame'hani dadyāt
9.6.4.[1]	ekaikasmai madhyataḥ kāribhyo hotrādibhyo mahartvigbhyaḥ śataṃ śataṃ dadyāt
9.6.5.[1]	arddhinībhyo hotrādibhyaḥ pañcāśataṃ pañcāśataṃ dadyāt ekaikasmā iti prakṛtam arddhinya uktāḥ arddhinyastṛtīyinyaḥ pādinyaḥ iti
9.6.6.[1]	tṛtīyinīnāṃ hotrāṇaṃ viṃśatiṃ potre dadyāt tathā neṣṭre viṃśatiṃ dadyādityetaduktaṃ bhavati
9.6.7.[1]	itarābhyāṃ tṛtīyinībhyāṃ hotrābhyāṃ triṃśataṃ dadyāt āgnīdhrāya ca pādinīnāṃ triṃśatameva dadyāt
9.6.8.[1]	pādinīnāmunnetre nava dadyāt itarābhyāṃ pādinībhyāṃ daśa daśa dadyāt
9.6.9.[1]	yāstakrāḥ unnetre nava dakṣiṇāstā eva vibhajyānvahaṃ dadyāt tisrastisraḥ
9.6.10.[1]	sadasyāya prathame'hani daśa dadyāt dvitīye'hani saptatiṃ dadyāt tṛtīye viṃśatiṃ dadyāt
9.6.11.[1]	ārṣeyapravādibhyo daśa daśa dadyāt ye brāhmaṇenoktāḥ ya ārṣeyo vidvānityevamādayaḥ, vidvānavidvānityetasmin saṃśaya āha
9.6.12.[1]	vidvāṃsau pūrvayorahnoravidvānuttame
9.6.13.[1]	daśādhikaṃ śatameva śiṣyate dakṣiṇanāṃ tāḥ sarvebhyo ṛtvigbhyo vibhajya dadyāt prasarpakebhyo vā dadyāt
9.6.14.[1]	sahasrasya pūraṇī sahasratamī tāṃ sahasratamīṃ madhyame'hani brahmaṇe dadyāt āgnīdhrāya ca dadyāt uktam athaiṣā dvidevatyā trirūpā brahmaṇo dve tṛtīye tṛtīyamagnīdhra iti kāni punastāni rūpāṇītyucyate
9.6.15.[1]	śuklādīni asyāḥ sahasratamyāḥ trīṇi rūpāṇi
9.6.16.[1]	tāṃ sahasratamīṃ ṣoḍaśadhā kalaśo vibhajya yajamāno daśa kalā brahmaṇe pañcāgnīdhrāya ekā mama ityapākaraṇaṃ kurvīta
9.6.17.[1]	tāṃ sahasratamīṃ yajamānaḥ anyayā gavā niṣkrīya dakṣiṇe asyā goḥ karṇe gonāmāni japitvā kāmyāsītyetadādīni anyāsu goṣvapi sṛjeta
9.6.18.[1]	iha brāhmaṇaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jyotiṣṭomavidhimāmnāyānantaraṃ dādaśāhavidhimāmanati tato dvādaśāhānantaraṃ punarekāhādau punarjyotiṣṭomavidhiṃ samāmanati tata ekāhān samāpyāhīnānāmādau punarjyotiṣṭomavidhimāmanati tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimayaṃ jyotiṣṭomavidhiḥ anantarāmnānāt dvādaśāhabhūtasyaiva jyotiṣṭomasya bhavati uta svatantrasya jyotiṣṭomasyeti kiṃ punaretasyāñcintāyāḥ prayojanamiti cet ucyate yadi tāvaddvādaśāhabhūtasyaiva jyotiṣṭomasya syāt tadā uttarayorāmnāyayordravyāntaraṃ kalpayitavyam atha punaḥ sārvatrikaḥ tataḥ punarāmnāye prayojanaṃ vaktavyam etasmin saṃśaye'yamācāryyaḥ śāstramārabhate jyotiṣṭomavidhirityādinā jyotiṣṭomasyāsau vidhiḥ dvādaśāhabhūtasya syāditi kiṃkāraṇam anantarāmnānāditi yasmādanantaro dvādaśāha āmnātaḥ
9.6.19.[1]	kiñcānyat dvādaśāhikaliṅgadarśanāt thāl prakāravacane yathā pṛṣṭhānāṃ yathā stomānāñca
9.6.20.[1]	kiñcānyat yasmāccāhīnaikāhādau punarjyotiṣṭomavidhirāmnātaḥ tasmāt dvādaśāhabhūtasya syāditi
9.6.21.[1]	natvevaṃ syāt tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣavyāvarttakaḥ yaduktaṃ dvādaśāhabhūtasya syāditi tatra nānā pṛthak tasmin svasmin prakaraṇe coditānāṃ krameṇa ānantaryyāt sambandho na syāt nahyānantaryaṃ sambandhakāraṇaṃ yathā upahavyasya ca ṛtapeyasya ca prakaraṇavaccoditayorna sambandho bhavatyānantaryyāt
9.6.22.[1]	atha yaduktaṃ talliṅgadarśanāccetyatra brūmaḥ liṅgagrahaṇaṃ anyārthena kṛtaṃ kiñcidevārthamuddiśyānyantadarthena kṛtaṃ yathā ṣaṣṭhe'hani śakvarīṇāṃ grahaṇaṃ kṛtaṃ mṛjyamānaḥ suhasyeti simānāṃ rūpaṃ samānaṃ vai simānāñca rūpaṃ revatīnāñca simābhyo hyadhirevatyaḥ prajāyanta iti
9.6.23.[1]	atha yaduta punarāmnānāccāhīnaikāhādāvityatra brūmaḥ śeṣasya vidheḥ punarāmnānaṃ na sarvasya śeṣavidheriti sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī kaḥ punaḥ śeṣavidhiriti ucyate pratisavanaṃ tāvat stomavinyāsaḥ trivṛtpañcadaśau prātaḥsavanamiti tasya navatiśataṃ stotrīyā iti saṃsthādeśaḥ tasya dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇā iti dakṣiṇāniyamaḥ tathā ahīnādau trivṛdbahiṣpavamānamityata ārabhya pratistotraṃ stomavinyāsaḥ atirātreṇeti saṃsthācodanā ṛddhikāmaphalacodanā etadarthaṃ punarāmnānam
9.7.1.[1]	tasmin jyotiṣṭome'tirātre svatantre nāṅgabhūte āhīnikī rātriḥ syāt yasmādaviśeṣeṇa ahīneṣu codyate hiśabdaḥ kāraṇopadeśārthaḥ sarve'tirātrā ahīnā iti
9.7.2.[1]	prākṛtī tveva syāt prākṛtau bhavā prākṛtī tuśabdaḥ pakṣāntaranivṛttaye yaduktamāhīnikī syāditi tanna evaśabdo'vadhāraṇārthaḥ naivāhīnikī syāt kiṃkāraṇam adhikṛtyāmnānāt yasmādadhikṛtya jyotiṣṭomaṃ sā rātrirāmnātā
9.7.3.[1]	atha yaduktamaviśeṣeṇa hyahīneṣu codyata iti tatrocyate aviśeṣacodanā śeṣe syāt sarvastomādiṣu yathā caturavattaṃ sarvatrāviśeṣeṇa bhavati pañcāvattantu bhṛgūṇāmiti taccaturavattvaṃ bhṛguṇāviśeṣeṇa bhavati evamaviśeṣacodanā jyotiṣṭomaśeṣe bhavati
9.7.4.[1]	etena nyāyenoktamākhyātam oṅkārasya pratyāmnānaṃ vācā rathantare aviśeṣacoditaṃ sarveṣāṃ sāmnāmoṅkāreṇodgīthādānantadrathantare pratyānātaṃ vācā vāgityādeyamiti
9.7.5.[1]	tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣanivṛttyarthaḥ yaduktamoṅkāro vācā nivarttitaḥ tatra samuccayaḥ syādvāgoṅkārayoḥ kasmāt nānārthatvāt vākprayogaḥ prastāvaśāntyarthaḥ udgīthāderoṅkāraḥ śāntyarthaḥ kathaṃ punarvāgoṅkārayoḥ śāntyarthateti ucyate evaṃ brāhmaṇamāha vajreṇa vā etat prastotodgātāramabhipravarttayati yadrathantaraṃ prastauti samudrakaṃ tarhyodgāyet vāgityādeyaṃ vāgvai samudraḥ samudramevāntardadhātyahiṃsāyā iti tat yat vajreṇābhipravarttanaṃ tasyaṃ vācā samudrabhūtāyāṃ antarddhānaṃ kriyate ahiṃsārthaṃ oṅkārastūdgīthādeḥ śāntyarthaḥ prastutaṃ vai sāmāvasīdati tadudgātauṅkāreṇa viṣṭanoti tatprasutaṃ sāmāvasīyamānamudgātauṅkāreṇa kṣipati tadevaṃ nānārthatvāt vāgoṅkārayoḥ samuccayaḥ syāt ubhayoḥ kriyā
9.7.6.[1]	evaṃ vāgoṅkārayorekatra samuccayībhūtayoḥ kasya pūrvaṃ prayogo'stvityata āha vāk tu pūrvaṃ syāt evaṃ kriyamāṇe yadarthaṃ vāk prayujyate so'rthaḥ pratyāsannataro bhavati prastāvānantaraṃ vāci kriyamāṇayām
9.7.7.[1]	uttarā vā vāk syāt yasmādādita ārabhya stotrāṇām oṅkāreṇa pravṛttamudgīthādānaṃ vācā jaghanyavidhānaṃ rathantare kiñcānyat samācāraśca dṛśyate ācāraḥ pāramparyyamavichinnaḥ loke'pi brahmaṇa ādānamoṅkārapūrvakameva bhavati tasmādoṅkāra eva pūrvamuttarakālā vāk
9.7.8.[1]	iha trivṛtātirātreṇa brahmavarcasakāmo yajetetyārabhya catura ekastomānāmanati tathā trayastrivṛto tirātrāḥ sarve ṣoḍaśimanta iti vaidatrirātre śrutiḥ tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimayamahaḥstomo vidhīyate bhūyastvādakṛtsnasaṃyogaḥ rātriryathāklṛptastomaiva athavā kṛtsnasaṃyogāt sarātrikāṇyahāni tatstomānyeveti etasmin saṃśaye ācāryyaḥ śāstramārabhate ekastomesviti ekastomeṣu caturṣu vaidatrirātre ca svastomārātrirbhavet yathā sandhiḥ svastomakaḥ kaḥ punaḥ rātreḥ svastomaka iti ucyate svajātitaḥ pañcadaśī rātristrivṛtsandhiriti
9.7.9.[1]	atha vyāvṛttaḥ pakṣaḥ yaduktamekastome vaidatrirātre ca svastomā rātriḥ syāditi tathā sandhiriti tatra trivṛtātirātreṇeti tvaviśeṣacodanā nāyaṃ viśinaṣṭi ahastrivṛtāṃ svastomā rātristathā sandhiriti kṛtyāha trivṛteti
9.7.10.[1]	yaduktamubhayaṃ hyavikāreṇa varttata ityatra brūmaḥ ādeśe vṛtyapekṣā na vidyate ādeśo hi balavān yathā ṣoḍaśaṃ prathamaṃ rātriṣāmeti ādeśena sāmānyāvṛttiḥ pratyāmnātā
9.7.11.[1]	yaduktaṃ parātkañca trivṛto'nyacca sandhernopapadyata ityatrāpyarthoktaḥ āvāpaḥ syāt ko'rthaḥ parāktvañca
9.7.12.[1]	abhyāso vā syāt arthokta eva kathamarthoktaḥ na hi parāktvaṃ śrutaṃ sandhau trayastṛcācoditāḥ teṣāṃ stomavaśena parāktvaṃ kṛtaṃ ihāpi stomavaśenābhyāsaḥ kriyatāṃ
9.7.13.[1]	ājyadohānāṃ brāhmaṇamagnimupanidhāya stuvata iti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kasmin deśe tadupanidhānaṃ kutaścāgnirāharttavya iti ata āha heturdhiṣṇye'gniṃ dhārayeyuḥ prathame'hani yaṃ madhyandine dhiṣṇyaviharaṇa ānayeyuḥ yāvadājyadohakāla iti tatra hyārbhave ājyadoham
9.7.14.[1]	dvitīyatṛtīyayoḥ prātaḥsavane dhiṣṇyapraviharaṇāya yamānayeyuḥ taṃ dhārayeyuḥ yāvadājyadohakāla iti tayorhi madhyandine ājyadohe
9.7.15.[1]	stotravelāyāmenamagniṃ prajvalayeyuḥ sarveṣvahaḥsu
9.7.16.[1]	tamagnimanumantrayetodgātā prajvalitamagnirasīti mantreṇa yathā sūcitena
9.8.1.[1]	gargatrirātrasyānantaraṃ śabalīhomasya brāhmaṇam tasya vidhānamucyate sahasrapoṣaṃ kāmayate sahasrapoṣakāmaḥ yaḥ kāmayate sahasraṃ mama poṣaḥ syāditi sa śabalīhomaṃ kurvīta kiṃ tatsahasraṃ paśūnāmityapare varṇayanti sahasrapoṣakāma iti sahasraṃ bibhṛyāditi pūrva evatvarthaḥ kathaṃ gamyate vakṣyati prathamataścettu śvā gardabho vā prativāśyeta na paśūnāmāśāstīti vidyāditi tena paśukāmasyeti sutarāmupapadyate
9.8.2.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācārya āha na atrirātrayājī śabalīhomaṃ kurvīta yasmādbrāhmaṇaṃ sambandhaṃ darśayati trirātro vā etāṃ pradāpayatīti
9.8.3.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha yaḥ kaśca sahasrapoṣakāmaḥ syāt trirātrayājī atrirātrayājī vā śabalīhomaṃ kurvīteti nāsya trirātro nimittaṃ kāmo nimittam
9.8.4.[1]	vasante prathamāyāṃ pūrvapakṣasyeti niyamaḥ keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayitvāhataṃ vasanaṃ paridhāya ahatam abhuktapūrvam anantarhite sthaṇḍile āstaraṇenāstṛte dvādaśarātrīradhaḥ śayīta brāhmaṇaṃ dvādaśarātrīradhaḥ śayīteti tatrāstaraṇe prāpte sūtrakāra āhvānantarhi te sthaṇḍila iti brāhmaṇaṃ taptaṃ pibanniti tatkintaptamiti tadgavyaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ so'yamācārya āha kṣīramiti
9.8.5.[1]	asyāvasathe'gnirnityābhyāhitaḥ syāt na jāgarayet dvādaśāhāni
9.8.6.[1]	enaṃ karmiṇaṃ suhṛt yaḥ syāt praiṣakṛt evainamanupraviśet nānyaḥ kaścit praiṣakṛdanye suhṛdaḥ syāt
9.8.7.[1]	alpavyāhārī ca bhavet nāsadbahu bhāṣet
9.8.8.[1]	na ca dūraṃ yāyāt avaśyakāryyārthaṃ vā samidarthaṃ vā
9.8.9.[1]	dvādaśyā rātrerūpavyuṣam uṣārātreraparaḥ kālaḥ vigatā uṣā vyuṣā vyuṣāyāḥ samīpe upavyuṣaṃ parisamuhyāgniṃ paristīryya parisamūhanaparistaraṇe siddhe audumbaraḥ idhmaḥ syāt udumbarasya vikāraḥ audumbaraḥ sruksruvau ca audumbare dārave syātāṃ tathā camasaḥ audumbaraḥ syāt tathā camasa iti kimarthaṃ sruksruvacamasāñceti vaktavye ucyate vakṣyatyayaṃ tasmāddadhimadhusarpiriti sruveṇa sruci gṛhṇīyādityetadarthaṃ pṛthak camasagrahaṇañcamantyasminniti camasaḥ tasmāccamasāddadhimadhusarpirityetāni dravyāṇi saṃyutāni sruveṇa sruci gṛhṇīyāt caturgṛhītamaṣṭagṛhītaṃ vā
9.8.10.[1]	taditi nirdeśaḥ yadi caturgṛhītaṃ yadyaṣṭagṛhītaṃ tajjuhuyāt śabaliḥ samudro'sītyetadādinā yajuṣā yathāmnātena uktaṃ mantravidhiścādigrahaṇeneti
9.8.11.[1]	tathaiva gṛhītvā caturgṛhītamaṣṭagṛhītaṃ vā uttarāmāhutiṃ svāhākāreṇa juhuyāt
9.8.12.[1]	tasya dravyasya yaḥ śeṣaḥ syāt ācamya taṃ camase kṛtvā prāśnīyāt
9.8.13.[1]	sthāpayet
9.8.14.[1]	śāṇḍilyāyana ācārya āha kṛtārthatvāt sruksruvacamasānāṃ prakṣālyāsminnevāgnau prakṣipediti
9.8.15.[1]	sruksruvacamasānnidhāyāgnau vā pratikṣipyānantaraṃ prāṅvodaṅvā grāmānniṣkramya yasmin deśe grāmyasya paśoḥ śabdaṃ na śṛṇuyāt tadaraṇyaṃ paretya gatvā darbhastambamālabhya śabaliśabalītyanena kṛtarūpeṇa mantreṇa triḥparamakaṇṭhena krośet āhvāyet parameṇa svareṇeti na tasmātparataro'nyaḥ syāt
9.8.16.[1]	tasminnāhvāne kriyamāṇe kṛte vā śuno vā gardabhādvā yadanyat sarvaṃ prativāśyeta samṛddhaṃ karmeti jānīyāt
9.8.17.[1]	evamanena prakāreṇa ātṛtīyaṃ saṃvatsarātyāsaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ kṣiptvā kurvīta uktaṃ yadi na prativāśyeta saṃvatsareṇa punarāhvayediti
9.8.18.[1]	yadi prathamataḥ śvā gardabho vā na prativāśyeta saṃvatsare punarāhvayet yadi prativāśyeta na paśūnāmāśāstīti vidyāt
9.8.19.[1]	ātṛtīyaṃ yāvat tṛtīyaṃ karmeti tāvadanyasminna prativāśyamāne sa tena paśūnāmāśāstīti vidyāt
9.8.20.[1]	ante karmaṇaḥ śāntyarthaṃ vāmadevyaṃ gāyet samṛddhe cāsamṛddhe ca nityaṃ vāmadevyagānam
9.9.1.[1]	sabalihoma uktaḥ sāmpratamaśvamedha ucyate sahyanantaraṃ tasyāmnānaḥ rājā prāptābhiṣekaḥ kṣattriyaḥ pṛthivīśvaraḥ aśvamedha iti karmaṇo nāmadheyam aśvamedhena yajeteti vidhāyakaṃ vākyam
9.9.2.[1]	tasyāśvamedhasya upāyaḥ upagamanamupāyaḥ yathā yena prakāreṇa mahāvrate gautamīyaṃ vidhānam amāvāsyāyāṃ dīkṣitvetyetadādi
9.9.3.[1]	tisra upasado vratasyaikāhikasya gautamīyena ṣaḍvā dvādaśa veti prāpta āha upasadastvasyāhīnikya iti ṣaḍvā dvādaśa vopasadaḥ syuḥ iti upasatpakṣaṃ nivartayati
9.9.4.[1]	dīkṣitvā yajamānaḥ niyamaṃ gṛhītvā yadetadvratāvalambanādi dīkṣaṇīyāyāmiṣṭāvāsamāptestasyā etat sarvaṃ kṛtvānuṣṭhīyāśvamutsṛjet aśvasyotsargavidhānamādhvaryave dṛṣṭaṃ śvetaṃ kṛṣṇamaṇḍalaṃ śvetamiti varṇanirdeśaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ yasya śarīre etadakṣṇo rūpam uktaṃ prajāpatervā yattatparāpatattadaśvo'bhavaditi yo javena sampannaḥ syāt javatirgatyarthaḥ śīghragatitama ityarthaḥ
9.9.5.[1]	tamevaṃlakṣaṇamaśvaṃ kāmataścarantaṃ anāvartayanto rakṣeyuḥ digbhyaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ somasya rājñaḥ kraye badhnīyuḥ atha digbhya iti kimartham ucyate digbhya anāvartayanto rakṣeyuḥ viṣamebhyaśca śvabhrebhyaḥ parvatādibhyaśca āvartayeyuḥ atha kraya ityukte rājagrahaṇaṃ kimarthaṃ rājakraya iti ucyate etadādi darśayati sarvakarmasu pratyakṣaṃ somamupalabhya dīkṣeta pratinidhinā ārambho na syāditi
9.9.6.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya māha grīṣme ārabhyeteti
9.9.7.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācārya āha vasante upakrameteti grīṣme vasanta iti kālanirddeśaḥ
9.9.8.[1]	caitravaiśākhayoranyatarasya caitravaiśākhasya vā saptamyāntithāvaṣṭamyāṃ vā yajamāno madhyataḥ kāriṇa ṛtvijo hotrādhvaryubrahmodgātṝn brahmaudanaṃ bhojayitvā brahmaudanaḥ siddhaḥ adhvaryyave tebhyo mahartvigbhyaḥ pṛthagekaikasmai sahasrāṇi dadyāt uktaṃ saṃkhyāmātre ca dakṣiṇa gāva iti atha pṛthakgrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet ucyate sahasrāṇīti bahuvacanasāmarthyāt siddhe ucyate triprabhṛtibahutvāt sahasrāṇītyukte tribhya ārabhya aniyamaḥ sahasrāṇāṃ syāt so'yaṃ niyamārthamārabhate pṛthagiti caturṇāmiti
9.9.9.[1]	tenaiva vidhinā rakṣeyuḥ yathoktena dīkṣitvā'śvamutsṛjedityetasmin kalpe pūṣā devatā asyeti pauṣṇī tasyāṃ pauṣṇyāmiṣṭau vitatāyāṃ prārabhyāyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ samāptāyāṃ vāśvamutsṛjet tantayaivāvṛtā rakṣeyuḥ
9.9.10.[1]	anantaramaśvotsarjanāt tisra iṣṭayaḥ sāvitryo bhavanti savitā devatā āsāmiti sāvitryaḥ tāsu saṃsthitāsu samāptāsu āhavanīyasya dakṣiṇe pradeśe hiraṇmaye kūrce sauvarṇe pīṭhe prāṅmukha āsīno yajamānaḥ saṃvatsaramaharahaḥ ahanyahani pāriplavamākhyānaṃ hoturācakṣāṇasya śṛṇuyāt
9.9.11.[1]	sauvarṇe kaśipuni brahmā udgātā ca pṛthak udaṅmukhāvāsīnau saṃvatsaramevāharaharhotuḥ pāriplavamācakṣāṇasya śṛṇuyāt hiraṇyakaśipuni sauvarṇe vicitre amale
9.9.12.[1]	tatpāriplavaṃ śrutvā yajamānaḥ śataṅgāḥ hotre dadyāt daśādhvaryave
9.9.13.[1]	itarābhyāṃ brahmodgātṛbhyāṃ kiñciddadyāt kiñcicchabdo'niyame vāśabdaḥ ubhayakalpārthaḥ
9.9.14.[1]	tasya yajamānasya pāriplavaṃ śṛṇvataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ devavratāni bhavanti yathā rājasūye unmṛhnītānāplavamāna ityetadādīni
9.9.15.[1]	pāriplavākhyānike saṃvatsare prāpte tasmādūrddhvaṃ badhvā aśvamedhāya dīkṣeta niyamaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
9.9.16.[1]	tadahastasminnahani etānyāsanāni hiraṇyakapipuprabhṛtīni yathāsvaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ yadyasya yathāsvaṃ tasminneva kāle darśayati yathā teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pṛthak hiraṇyakaśipuprabhṛtyāsanānīti
9.9.17.[1]	uktam ahīnabahiṣpavamānaiḥ sadasī stuvīran prathamādahno'nyatreti so'yamatra viśeṣa ārabhyate sarveṣāmeteṣāmahnāṃ bahirbahiṣpavamānaiḥ stuvīranniti atha sarvagrahaṇaṃ kimarthaṃ bahuvacanātsiddhe bahiṣpavamānairiti ucyate ubhayoḥ kalpayoḥ saṃvatsaradīkṣe dvādaśadīkṣopasade ca
9.9.18.[1]	madhyame'hani aśvasya bāladhim ālabhya gṛhītvā bahiṣpavamānaṃ sarpeyuḥ bālā asmindhīyanta iti bāladhiḥ
9.9.19.[1]	sarpatsu bahiṣpavamānaṃ yajamāna udgātāraṃ brūyāt udgātarapa tvā vṛṇe śatena ca niṣkeṇa ca apavṛṇe tvā gavāṃ śatena ca sauvarṇena ca niṣkeṇa cakāreṇa kṛtaparimāṇena aśvo ma udgāsyatīti
9.9.20.[1]	evamutkvāthānantaram aśvamāstāvamākramayya vaḍavāṃ darśayeyuḥ
9.9.21.[1]	tāṃ vaḍavāṃ aśvam ābhimukhyena yadā krandet śabdaṃ kuryyāt athānantaraṃ yajamānaḥ udgātāraṃ brūyāt udgātarupa tvāhvaye śatena caiva niṣkena ca tvameva ma udgāsyasīti
9.9.22.[1]	udaṅmakhamaśvantasmādāstāvādutkramayya nītvā āstāve upaviśyodgātā aśvavratena sāmnā ātmanā stuyāt abhivājī viśvarūpa ityetāsvṛkṣu udgātṛgrahaṇaṃ itarayornivṛtyartham
9.9.23.[1]	astāve hiraṇyakaśipuni āsīno bahiṣpavamānena stutvā sa evodgātā gṛhṇīyāditi āsanam evaśabdaḥ kriyate vacanāt gṛhṇīyāditi
9.10.1.[1]	yā patnīnāṃ priyatamā yajamānasya patnīnāṃ priyatamā rājaputrī rājaduhitā kṣatriyā tasyāḥ sāṃvyavahārikī saṃjñā vāvāteti saṃvyavahāraṃ vakṣyati brahmā vāvātāmabhimethediti
9.10.2.[1]	yajamānasya yā anapacitā patnī syāt apūjitā tasyāḥ sāṃvyavahārikyeva saṃjñā parivṛktīti vakṣyati udgātā parivṛktīmabhimethediti
9.10.3.[1]	saṃjñapteṣu paśuṣu śamitrā sarveṣu hotrābhimethite sati brahmā vāvātāmabhimethet ūrddhvāmenāmucchrayatādityetadādinā yathodiṣṭena abhimethanaṃ nāma tadākrośanamabhimethanam asaṃyatayā vācā mantravatyā uktipratyuktiḥ
9.10.4.[1]	śatam asyā vāvātāyāḥ rājanyānāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ duhitaraḥ anucaryyaḥ anugāminyaḥ syuḥ tāstaṃ brahmāṇaṃ pratyabhimetheyuḥ pratibrūyuḥ ūrddhvamenamucchrayatādityetadādinā yathāsūtritena mantreṇa
9.10.5.[1]	udgātā parivṛktīṃ yajamānasya patnīmabhimethet yadasyā aṇuhodbhyā aṇusthūlamityetadādinā yathāsūcitena mantreṇa
9.10.6.[1]	asyāḥ parivṛktyāḥ śataṃ sūtagrāmaṇīnāṃ duhitaraḥ anucaryyaḥ anugāminyaḥ syuḥ sūtāśca te grāmaṇyaśca sūtagrāmaṇyaḥ grāmannayatīti grāmaṇīḥ tāstamudgātāraṃ pratyabhimetheyuḥ pratibrūyuḥ yaṃ devāso lalāmagumityetadādinā yathāsūtritena
9.10.7.[1]	tadabhimethanaṃ kṛtvā brahmā udgātāraśca vāmadevyaṃ sāma gāyeyuḥ udgītvā ṛco'syānujapeyuḥ asyābhimethanasyaitacchāntyarthaṃ vāmadevyagānam atha tasyeti kimartham ucyate yatra yatra vāmadevyagānamādiśyate śākhāntare'pi tatra tatra gītvā tasyarco'nujapeyuḥ
9.10.8.[1]	svāhākṛtayo nāma paśuprajayājeṣu taiḥ karmaṇi kṛte hotradhvaryubhiḥ sadasaḥ pūrte pradeśe brahmodyaṃ vadeyuḥ brahmodyaṃ vakṣyati kiṃ tadbrahmodyam
9.10.9.[1]	hotrādhvaryuṇā ca ukte brahmodye brahmā pṛcchedugātāraṃ pṛcchāmi tvācitayaṃ devasakhetyetadādi yathāsūcitaṃ praśnam
9.10.10.[1]	taṃ brahmāṇaṃ prati brūyādudgātā api teṣu triṣu padeṣvasminnetadādi yathāsūtritaṃ prativacanam
9.10.11.[1]	udgātā brahmāṇaṃ pṛcchet kiṃsvidantaḥpuruṣa āviveśetyetadādi yathāsūcitaṃ praśnam
9.10.12.[1]	tamudgātāraṃ prati brūyādbrahmā pañcasvantaḥpuruṣa āviveśetyetadādi yathāsūtritena prativacanena
9.10.13.[1]	sarve brahmodyavaktāro yajamānaṃ pṛccheyuḥ pṛcchāmastvā paramantaṃ pṛthivyā iti yathāsūcitaṃ praśnam
9.10.14.[1]	tān sarvān prati brūyāt yajamānaḥ iyaṃ vediḥ paro antaḥ pṛthivyā ityetadādi yathāsūtritena prativacanena
9.10.15.[1]	tasya aśvamedhasya dakṣiṇā ucyante prathame'hani sahasraṃ dadyāt tathottame sahasrameva dadyāt paribhāṣitamidaṃ saṃkhyāmātre ca dakṣiṇāgāva iti tasya grahaṇamanekān vikalpānasya vakṣyante tasya tasya ca syāt
9.10.16.[1]	ayaṃ rājānekajanapadeśvarastadekasmin janapade'brāhmaṇānāṃ vittaṃ syāt tat dadyāt janapadāḥ pañcālāḥ kuravo matsyāḥ sūrasenīyāḥ cedyamālavādayaḥ
9.10.17.[1]	athavā na kevalaṃ pṛthivīśvaro rājāśvamedhena yajeta maṇḍaleśvaro'pi yajeta yo yasya deśo vijitaḥ syāt sa tasya madhye yajeta
9.11.1.[1]	dakṣiṇā ucyante aśvamedhe vihitā pṛthivī dakṣiṇā śrūyate tadyadi tāvatpṛthivīśvaraḥ sākṣāt pṛthivīmeva dadyāt caturddhāṃ kṛtvā yo nyāyo vakṣyate atha maṇḍalīkaḥ syāt yasya deśasyeśvarastasya madhye yajamāno madhyame'hani hotre prācīndiśaṃ dadyāt dakṣiṇāṃ brahmaṇe dadyāt adhvaryave pratīcīṃ dadyāt udgātre udīcīṃ dadyāt yadanyakṣetrācca puruṣebhyaśceti bhūpuruṣavarjamityetaduktaṃ bhavati bhūmiśca na deyā puruṣaśca puruṣaśabdena jātigrahaṇaṃ yat tatra rājagāmibhogaphalaṃ dadyādityetaduktaṃ bhavati bhūmiśca na deyā ubhayorvicārayoretat asmiṃśca kalpe yaccoktaṃ madhyame'hanyekajanapade yadabrāhmaṇānāṃ vittaṃ syāt tat dadyāditi tatra ca
9.11.2.[1]	aparo vikalpaḥ tāvadvā dānaṃ sthāt yāvadbrūyurneto bhūya icchāma iti tṛptāḥ sma iti
9.11.3.[1]	aparaḥ kalpa ucyate aṣṭācatvāriṃśataṃ vā sahasrāṇi madhyataḥ kāribhyaḥ ekaikasmai dadyāt caturviṃśatimarddhinībhyaḥ caturviṃśatisahasrāṇi arddhinībhyo dadyāt ekaikasmā iti varttate dvādaśa tṛtīyanībhyaḥ tṛtīyinībhyo hotrābhyo dvādaśasahasrāṇi dadyāt ṣaṭpādinībhyaḥ pādinībhyo hotrābhyaḥ ekaikasmai ṣaṭsahasrāṇi dadyāt uktaṃ saṃkhyāmātre ca dakṣiṇā gāva iti
9.11.4.[1]	ya ete dakṣiṇavikalpā uktāḥ eteṣāmaṣṭācatvāriṃśādayo dakṣiṇā avarāḥ sarvanikṛṣṭāḥ bhūyastve bahulaṃ kutaḥ punariyamāśaṅkā yathā niyamitābhyo na avarārdhyā iti ucyate uktamanena yāvadvā brūyurneto bhūya icchāma iti tadetasmin vikalpe avarārdhyā evaibhyo'pi naiva dadyāt avarārdhyā etāḥ
9.11.5.[1]	tasya aśvamedhasya vikalpā varttiṣyanta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
9.11.6.[1]	etānyeva prathamakalpitānyahāni pañcadaśastomavikṛtāni kalpayet sapatantako'śvamedhaḥ śrutyantaradṛṣṭaḥ aśvamedhagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti ucyate na tatkarmāntaraṃ draṣṭavyam aśvamedhavicāro'śvamedhena yajeta yo'sau prakṛto'śvamedhaḥ saṃvatsaramaśvasya cāraṇakālaḥ sa vikalpyate
9.11.7.[1]	arddhamāsamaśvaṃ cārayitvā etena patantakena yajeta
9.11.8.[1]	jyotiṣṭomo vā atirātraḥ etasya patantakasya
9.11.9.[1]	gaurvātirātrastṛtīyamahaḥ syāt tena yajamānastrīnmāsānaśvaṃ cārayet
9.11.10.[1]	āyurvātirātra etasya patantakasya tṛtīyamahaḥ syāt tena yajamānaḥ ṣaṇmāsānaśvaṃ cārayet
9.11.11.[1]	prākṛtasyāśvamedhasya vā eteṣāṃ jyotiṣṭomādīnāṃ yathoddiṣṭānāṃ trayāṇāṃ kiñcidekaṃ tṛtīyamahaḥ syāt
9.11.12.[1]	atha vā prākṛtasyaiva viśvajidādīnāṃ yathoddiṣṭānāṃ kiñcit tṛtīyamahaḥ syāt atirātrāṇameva
9.11.13.[1]	teṣāṃ jyotiṣṭomādīnāmaptoryāmāntānāṃ stomacodanaiva syāt na dravyacodanā yathā catuṣṭomasarvastomayoḥ pratyakṣaśiṣṭayoḥ stomacodanāmātraṃ bhavati evameteṣāṃ stomacodanāmātraṃ syāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt trirātreṣu tantravilopo na vidyate
9.11.14.[1]	atha yaduta yathā catuṣṭomasarvastomayoḥ pratyakṣaśiṣṭayoḥ stomacodanāmātraṃ bhavati evameteṣāṃ stomacodanāmātraṃ syāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt trirātreṣu ca tantravilopo na vidyata iti tanna natvevaṃ syāt tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣanivṛttyarthaḥ yaduktaṃ teṣāṃ stomacodanaiva syāditi tanna svatantrā eva syuḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt purastāt kṛtalakṣaṇā hi codyante teṣāṃ kṛtalakṣaṇaṃ na codyamānānāṃ stomacodanāmātraṃ pratīyāt atha yaduktaṃ yathā catuṣṭomasarvastomayorityatra brūmaḥ pratyakṣavikārāt catuṣṭomasarvastomayoḥ stomacodanāmātraṃ pratīyate pratyakṣavikāraḥ kṛta eva maśakena
9.11.15.[1]	atha yaduktaṃ trirātreṣu ca tantravilopo na vidyata ityatra brūmaḥ tantravilopo vacanādbhavati vacanaṃ balīyaḥ na hi tadasti yadvacanānna bhavati pratyakṣaśiṣṭatvāt jyotiṣṭomādīnāṃ śrutyantare
9.12.1.[1]	aśvamedha uktaḥ anantaraṃ vaidatrirātrādayaḥ paribhāṣāsiddhāḥ sarve yāvajjāmadagna iti, sāmprataṃ jāmadagniviśeṣo vivakṣitaḥ sa ucyate trayodaśyāmaparapakṣasya dīkṣeta jāmadagnāyeti trayodaśyāmiti tithinirdeśaḥ aparapakṣasyeti sāmānyavidhiprāptasya pūrvapakṣasya pratyāmnāyaḥ dīkṣeteti kriyānirdeśaḥ jāmadagmāyeti jāmadagnārthaṃ tāda caturthī eṣa sūtrārthaḥ jāmadagnena catūrātreṇa yakṣyamāṇastrayodaśyāmaparapakṣasya dīkṣeta
9.12.2.[1]	tasya jāmadagnasya viṃśatiḥ dīkṣā dvādaśopasadaḥ syuḥ iha sāmānyaparibhāṣā paurṇamāsī dīkṣā māsāpavargā ahīnāḥ teṣāṃ dvādaśopasadaḥ ṣaḍiti dhānañjapya iti tadidaṃ sarvavacanāt vikalpyate
9.12.3.[1]	tatropasatsu pṛthagghomāḥ puroḍāśāḥ bhavanti uktaṃ jāmadagnibrāhmaṇe puroḍāśinya upasado bhavantīti tattasmin jāmadagna upasadiṣṭiḥ pṛthagghomāḥ puroḍāśā bhavanti pṛthakśabdo nānārthavācī nānā upasadāni pradhānāni pṛthagghomā eva te bhavanti tānadhvaryurjuhuyāt puroḍāśānte brāhmaṇenaivoktāḥ āgneya ekakapāla ityetadādayo dvādaśakapālāntāḥ adhvaryugrahaṇaṃ chāndogya āmnānāt teṣāṃ pavamānādevakoṣṇatusau syātāṃ paurvāhnikyām upasadyāmāparāhṇikyāñca
9.12.4.[1]	samānadevatau tulyadevatau puroḍāśau syātāṃ pūrvāhṇikyāmupasadi āparāhṇikyāñca
9.12.5.[1]	agneverhotramityetadādibhiryathāmnātairmantraiḥ anupūrve homā bhavanti ekaikena mantreṇa ekaikaḥ puroḍāśo hūyate
9.12.6.[1]	tasya jāmadagnasyāvabhṛthādudetya dvādaśāhamiṣṭibhiryajeta tasyeti punaḥśabdo niyamārthaḥ nāsau sāmānyena vidhinā vikalpite niyamārthaḥ tasyaśabdaḥ
9.12.7.[1]	tāsviṣṭiṣu eta eva puroḍāśā ye upariṣṭāt uktāste syuḥ tenaiva vidhinā samānadaivatau pūrvāhṇāparāhṇayoriti ayantu viśeṣaḥ pratilomā dvādaśakapālādayaḥ ekakapālāntāḥ na mantraiḥ prātilomyam ayaṃ dīkṣopasanniyamo viṃśatiḥ dīkṣā dvādaśopasada iti sampadarthaḥ uktaṃ hyasya brāhmaṇe jagatīcchandobhiḥ sampadyata iti na dīkṣābhirupasadbhiḥ upariṣṭāt dvādaśabhiriṣṭibhiḥ jagatī sampadyate kathaṃ puroḍāśairupasatsu ca caturviṃśatiranyāsviṣṭiṣu caturviṃśatyeva jagatī sampadyate
9.12.8.[1]	uktaṃ vasiṣṭhasya janitre bhavata iti te kalpayatyācāryyaḥ saṃsarpasya kratoḥ caturthe'hani bṛhatyanuṣṭubhoḥ pṛthaṅnānā anupūrvam anukalpayet bṛhatyāṃ pūrvam anuṣṭubhi uttaraṃ yasmāccaturthamaharjanitrasya sthānam
9.12.9.[1]	vasiṣṭhasya janitre maśakenānukalpite tayorācāryyakalpena vikalpaḥ syāt na tayorniyamaḥ
9.12.10.[1]	pañca śāradīye viśeṣa ucyate tasmin pañca śāradīye brāhmaṇena paśava āmnātāḥ saptadaśa pṛśnīnukṣṇaḥ pañcavarṣānityevamādayaḥ teṣāṃ vidhiviśeṣa ucyate pañcaśāradīye kratau pratisaṃvatsaraṃ paśubandhairyajeta saptamyām aṣṭamyāṃ vāśvayujīpakṣeṣu
9.12.11.[1]	uktaṃ saptadaśa pṛśnīnukṣṇaḥ pañcavarṣān saptadaśa pṛśnīstrivatsā apravītāstān paryagnikṛtān prokṣitānetarā labhante pretarān sṛjantīti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ ke'trālabdhavyāḥ ke cotsraṣṭavyā iti tadayamācāryyo viśiṣṭavatsatarīrevālabherannukṣṇo visṛjeyuḥ yāstatra vatsataryyastā ālabdhavyāḥ ye ukṣāṇaste utsraṣṭavyāḥ teṣāmālambhanaṃ some bhaviṣyati
9.12.12.[1]	paṭhitaṃ yadi rudrībhiḥ manyetāgnaye rudravate puroḍāśamaṣṭākapālaṃ nirūpyāthānyamālabheta ityevamādayobhreṣāḥ paṭhitāḥ anyeṣāṃ cālambhanaṃ teṣāmutsṛṣṭānāṃ ukṣṇaṃ yāvanto yāvatparimāṇaḥ bhreṣamāpadyeyuḥ tāvantaḥ anyānayajuṣkṛtān akṛtasaṃskārān teṣvapi sṛjeyuḥ tadrapāste pṛśniḥ citrāḥ apravītāḥ anāmitāḥ navanītavaccitrā rājīvā padmavaccitrā sāraṅgyovarṇantarāṣadhvastāḥ piśaṅgyo māṃsavarṇāḥ aruṇā garuḍakapilā bhreṣamāpannāḥ yadrūpāneva yāvadvarṣāstāvadvarṣāneva ca
9.12.13.[1]	pañcasu saṃvatsareṣu gateṣu yā ṣaṣṭhī śarat tasyāṃ kārttike māsi pañcaśāradīyena yajeta
9.12.14.[1]	tasya pañcaśāradīyasya dvādaśopasadaḥ syuḥ ṣaḍiti dhānañjapyaḥ ityetannivarttayati
9.12.15.[1]	dvau ṣaḍahau paribhāṣitau kratau ṣaḍaha āyuḥkāmaṣaḍahañca tṛtīye kiñcidvivakṣitaṃ taducyate tatra paṭhati abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāha iti tṛtīye ṣaḍrātre pañcamasyāhnaḥ pratyavarohīṇyukthāni syuriti evamācāryyā manyante kasmāt yasmādatrābhyāsaṅgyaścodyate yathā devānāṃ pañcarātre tatra pañcame'hani pratyavarohīṇyukthāni tasmādihāpi tathaiva syāt abhyāsaṅgyātideśāt
9.12.16.[1]	gautama ācārya āha devānāṃ pañcarātre pañcame'hani rātrirbhavati tatkāritastatra pratyavarohaḥ iha punaḥ pañcamamahaḥ ukthasaṃstham eva bhavati tasmāt tatra trayastriṃśānyeva syuriti yātu pratyavarohasya nimittaṃ rātriḥ sā viśvajiti kariṣyati tatra pratyavaroho bhaviṣyati
9.12.17.[1]	saptarātrāṇāṃ prathame paṭhati pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho mahāvratamatirātra iti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ mahāvrate kimukthāni vratastomamanuvarttatām athaikaviṃśastomāni bhavanti etasmin saṃśaye ayamācāryya ārabhate saptadaśarātrāṇāṃ prathamasyātirātra ekaviṃśānyukthāni syuriti yasmāt jyotiṣṭomapradeśaḥ kriyate tasya jyotiṣṭomo'tirātraḥ ṣoḍaśimāniti śeṣā ahīnāḥ paribhāṣāsiddhā yāvatpauṇḍarīka iti
10.1.1.[1]	ahīnānantaraṃ satrāṇi vaktavyāni tāni vivakṣurācāryyaḥ paribhāṣāmārabhate dīkṣākrayaprasavotthānāni sarvasatreṣu pūrvapakṣa upapādayeyuriti dīkṣā ca krayaśca prasavaśca utthānañca dīkṣākrayaprasavotthānāni tasminnahani dīkṣeran yathaitāni sarvāṇi pūrvapakṣe bhavanti sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī
10.1.2.[1]	teṣāṃ dīkṣādīnāmekasyānupapattau krayaḥ aparapakṣe syāt anupapattirasāmarthyaṃ kālasya sampādane
10.1.3.[1]	yadi dve na sambhaveyātāṃ prasavaśca aparapakṣe syāt krayaśca iti prakṛtam
10.1.4.[1]	triṣvanupapadyamāneṣu utthānameva pūrvapakṣe syāt eṣāmudāharaṇamātramucyate kṣullake dvādaśāhe tathā viśvasṛjāmayane saptatriṃśatsamākhye catvāri syuḥ yathākramaṃ kṣullakatāpaścite tāvaddīkṣākrayaprasavotthānāni sarvāṇi paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pūrvapakṣe upapadyante dvādaśāhe pūrvapakṣasya saptamyāṃ dīkṣitvā dvādaśadīkṣāstataḥ aparapakṣasya caturthyāṃ krayaḥ sampadyate evaṃ dīkṣākrayaprasavotthānāni trīṇi pūrvapakṣaṃ sampadyante viśvasṛjāmayane pūrvapakṣasya ṣaṣṭhyāṃ dīkṣitvā parapakṣasya tṛtīyāyāṃ krayaḥ sampadyate amāvasyā prasave sahasrasaṃvatsara iti saptatriṃśadrātreṣu vratavatsu sarveṣvamāvāsyāyāṃ dīkṣitvā tasmin kāle saha sṛtyābhiḥ ṣaḍahāni samvatsarādadhikāni kṛtvottiṣṭheyuriti amāvāsyāyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ dīkṣākrayaprasavā aparapakṣe bhavanti utthānameva kevalaṃ pūrvapakṣe sampadyate
10.1.5.[1]	teṣāṃ satrāṇāṃ dvādaśadīkṣāḥ syuḥ tathopasado dvādaśaiva anādeśe teṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ triṣūtthānameva pūrvapakṣe syādetadanantaram ādeśaḥ māsaṃ dīkṣitā bhavanti saṃvatsaramupasadbhiścaranti
10.1.6.[1]	sāṃvatsarikebhyaśca satrebhya ūrddhvaṃ dīkṣāṇaṃ yathākāmī syāt yāthākāmyamiṣṭataḥ pravṛttiḥ sāṃvatsarikāni gavāmayanādīni satrāṇi
10.1.7.[1]	prathame pañcadaśarātre ekānnaviṃśatiḥ dīkṣāḥ syuḥ ityevaṃ ācāryya āha evaṃ hi brāhmaṇamāha ekāṣṭakāmahāvratamamāvāsyātirātra iti evaṃ kriyamāṇe eṣa kalpaḥ sampadyate paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ ekānnaviṃśatiḥ dīkṣāḥ kṛtvā pūrvapakṣasya caturthyāṃ krayaḥ tataḥ aparapakṣasya pratipadyatirātraṃ kṛtvā ṣaḍahaṅkṛtvā aṣṭamyāṃ mahāvrataṃ tataḥ punaḥ ṣaḍahaṃ kṛtvā amāvāsyāyāmatirātraḥ
10.1.8.[1]	gautama ācāryya āha aṣṭādaśadīkṣāḥ syuriti yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇamāha paurṇamāsyatirātra iti atrāpi paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ aṣṭādaśadīkṣāḥ kṛtvā tṛtīyāyāṃ pūrvapakṣasya krayo bhavati tataḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ prāyaṇīyo'tirātraḥ tataḥ ṣaḍahaṃ kṛtvā saptamīṃ laṅghayitvā aṣṭamyāṃ mahāvrataṃ kṛtvā amāvāsyāyāmatirātraḥ natveṣa nyāyo yuktaḥ na hi laṅghanamahno yuktaṃ santānavirodhāt tasmāt nyūnamaparapakṣaṃ vidhāya kalpaṃ kuryyāt
10.1.9.[1]	jātikalpo vā syāt dīkṣopadāṃ jātikalpastu teṣāṃ dvādaśadīkṣāstathopasado'nādeśa iti
10.1.10.[1]	ṣoḍaśarātrādārabhya yāvat triṃśadrātramiti etāni sarvāṇyaṣṭādaśadīkṣāṇi syuḥ ekānnapañcāśadrātrāṇi ca sarvāṇi aṣṭādaśadīkṣāṇi syuḥ eteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ paurṇamāsī dīkṣā krayaprasavotthānāni sarvāṇi pūrvapakṣe sampadyante
10.1.11.[1]	dvādaśāhaprabhṛtisatrasyārabhante prabhṛtiśabdaḥ ādau varttate idaṃ hi dvādaśāhaprakaraṇaṃ tenārabhyate dvādaśāhaprabhṛtīnīti viśeṣañca vivakṣitaḥ
10.1.12.[1]	tena dvādaśāhenāpyahīnabhūtena yajeta api satrabhūtena apiśabdaḥ apyahīnabhūtena yajeta kiṃ punaḥ satrabhūteneti yasmāt asminnahīnaliṅgāni brāhmaṇaṃ darśayati yathā eko vā dīkṣeteti yadgaurīvitenāhīnānīti yajamānaṃ vā anupratiṣṭhantamityevamādīni
10.1.13.[1]	yaḥ purā puṇyo bhūtvā paścāt pāpīyān syādācāraṃ brahmasāma kurvīteti tadākṣāraṃ prathame'hani brahmasāma kurvannaudhasasyarkṣu kuyāt
10.1.14.[1]	tasyācārasya yatkiñcidauṣṇihaṃ sāma ekākṣaraṇidhanaṃ syāt ākṣāraṃ hyekākṣaraṇidhanaṃ naudhasaṃ vā tasya sthāne syāt
10.1.15.[1]	nanvevaṃ syādanācāraṇi bārhatānāṃ akriyā kiñca anekākṣaraṇidhanāni cātra uṣṇihi dṛśyante bhūyiṣṭhāni sāmāni kriyamāṇani
10.1.16.[1]	tatra tasyāmuṣṇihi pauṣkalaṃ kuryyāt yasmāt tasminnahani jyotiṣṭomaprāyāṇi sāmāni prāyeṇa jyotiṣṭomasāmāni
10.2.1.[1]	ṣoḍaśiprakaraṇe caturthe'hani paṭhati gaurīvitamadhikṛtya śarkvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīteti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimatra śarkvaryyaḥ gaurīvitasya ṛcaścodyanta atha sāmacodanaiveyam iti kutaḥ punarayaṃ saṃśayaḥ codanāt eva śarkvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīteti adhikaraṇe pakṣaṇe saptamī śrūyate śarkvvarīṣu ṛkṣu gaurīvitena sāmnā stuvīranniti atha dṛṣṭā etā mahānāmnyaḥ ṣoḍaśisāmeti kṛtvā agniḥ sāmacodaneti ṛgbhirāśrayeṇa sāmna āśrayeṇa ca codaneti saṃśaye ācārya idaṃ sūtramārabhate śarkvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīteti yadetadbrāhmaṇaṃ tatra gaurīvitaṃ mahānāmnīṣu ṛkṣu syāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ tasya prakaraṇe yasmādṛkcodanā
10.2.2.[1]	tuśabdaḥ pakṣanivṛtyarthaḥ yaduktaṃ gaurīvitaṃ mahānāmnīṣu syāditi tanna mahānāmnya eva ṣoḍaśisāma syuḥ yasmādetāsu na kadācidapi anyatsāmāpadyate anyāsu ṛkṣu dṛśyante anyāni sāmāni āpadyamānāni etāsu na kadācidapyanyatsāmāpadyate
10.2.3.[1]	apiha maśakācāryyaḥ pṛṣṭhastotrīyeṣu parokṣāṇi kalpayan pañcamātparokṣāṇi pratyakṣāṇi pratyakṣeṣu pṛṣṭhastotrīyeṣu kalpayati pāñcamikaṃ parokṣaṃ nityavatsāḥ naitāsu karoti etameva nyāyamanupaśyan
10.2.4.[1]	kṛtā mahānāmnyaḥ ṣoḍaśisāma vajrasya na hyetāsvanyatsāma kiñciddṛṣṭaṃ pratīyate dṛṣṭapratyayonyāyatastasmānmahānāmnya eva ṣoḍaśi sāma syuḥ na tāsu gaurīvitaṃ syāt
10.2.5.[1]	virāṭsvanuṣṭupsu codyamānaṃ gaurīvitameva syāt yasmātsvāraprāyāṇi hi ṣoḍaśisāmāni dṛṣṭāni āsitādīni
10.2.6.[1]	śarkvarīṇaṃ kāmyāni nidhanāni coditāni gāyatramayanaṃ svarṇidhanaṃ brahmavarcasakāmasya traiṣṭubhamayanammathakāranidhanamojaskāmasya jāgatamayanamiḍānidhanaṃ paśukāmasya iti tadeteṣāṃ nidhanānāṃ kiṃ sthānamiti ucyate yāvatya iḍā mahānāmnīṣu tāsāṃ sthāne'pyetāni nidhanāni syuriti tasmādbhūyiṣṭhaṃ nidhanamiḍāmahānāmnīṣu
10.2.7.[1]	gotamadhānañjapyāvācāryyāvāhatuḥ etāni kāmyāni nidhanāni ūdhaḥsveva syuḥ yasmādetasminnidhanavādaṃ vadatīti iḍe abhito'thakāramiti etadadhikṛtya kāmyāni nidhanāni paṭhanti
10.2.8.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācāryya āha athakārasthāne kāmyāni nidhanāni syuriti evaṃ kriyamāṇe alpīyān vikāro bhavati ūdhaḥsu kriyamāṇeṣvanalpo vikāro bhavati athakārasthāne ca kriyamāṇe alpīyān vikāro bhavati
10.2.9.[1]	kautsa ācāryya āha na niyamitamamuṣya nidhanasya sthāne kāmyāni nidhanāni syuriti ataḥ aniyamātsarveṣu nidhanasthāneṣu syuriti
10.2.10.[1]	tisraḥ stotrīyāḥ paṭhitvā purīṣaṃ paṭhati tatkiṃ purīṣaṃ mahānāmnīṣu sakṛtprayoktavyam atha pṛthageva taditi ucyate uttamayā stotrīyayā saṃyuktaṃ purīṣam ānantaryyāddhetostasmin saṃyojyam uttamayā saha yujyeta yāvatkṛtva uttamatā prayujyate tāvatkṛtvaḥ purīṣāṇi prayujyante
10.2.11.[1]	śarkvarībhiḥ stutvā purīṣeṇa stuvate paśavo vai śarkvaryāgoṣṭhaḥ purīṣamiti brāhmaṇaṃ śarkvarībhistutvetyapavarjya apavargaṃ kṛtvā samāptiṃ kṛtvā purīṣeṇetyāha tasmādasaṃyuktaṃ syāt sakṛtkuryyādityarthaḥ
10.2.12.[1]	purīṣaprayoga iti śeṣaḥ
10.2.13.[1]	uktaṃ bārhadgiraṃ brāhmaṇāya rāyovājīyaṃ vaiśyāyeti tat yadā pañcame'hani rāyovājīyaṃ brahma sāma syāt tat kurvan tasya sthāne kuryyāt yat kalpavṛttenopapannaṃ tadetat kalpavṛttaṃ sāma yadaraṇye geyam athavā kalpena ca vṛttena ca vṛttaṃ chandaḥ
10.2.14.[1]	bārhadgirameva kuryyāt brahmasāma yasmādaraṇye geyaṃ tat sacchandasyañca tasminnevāhani dṛṣṭaṃ tadeva kalpavṛttenopapannam
10.2.15.[1]	pārthuraśmaṃ brahmasāma kurvan bārhadgirasya kuryyāt ṛcāmasañcārārthaṃ yadi hi svāsu kuryyāt ṛcāṃ sañcāraḥ syāt ata eva rāyovājīyaṃ kariṣyante
10.3.1.[1]	gavāmayanaprakaraṇe dādaśāhasya daśāhāni bhavantītyevamadhikṛtyāha athaitat daśamamahariti tasminnadhikaraṇe mānasampaṭhati tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimetanmānasaṃ daśamasyāṅgam athānaṅgamiti kutaḥ punarayaṃ saṃśayaḥ aṅgamanaṅgamiti tatkāraṇamasminneva vacyate athāṅgamanaṅgamiti kiṃ punaretasyāścintāyāḥ prayojanaṃ yadyanaṅgaṃ tataḥ ko viśeṣaḥ syāditi ucyate maśakena dvādaśāhavicāreṣu athāpare daśa bhavanti yathā stomaṃ prathamamahastathā stomo'yaṃ sarvo daśarātraḥ syāt tena tejaskāmo brahmavarcasakāmo vā yajeteti evaṃ dvitīyādiṣvahaḥsu ye stomāstaiḥ pratikāmamekaikena stomena sarvāṇi daśāhāni bhavanti tadyadi tāvanmānasaṃ daśamasyāṅgaṃ tatastrivṛdādibhiḥ stomaiḥ pratikalpaṃ mānasenāpi bhavitavyam tathā dāśamikena stomena daśarātre kriyamāne mānasenāpi stomenātra bhavitavyam atha punaranaṅgaṃ tataḥ mānasikena stomena nātra bhavitavyaṃ so'yamācāryya evamarthaṃ parivivakṣuḥ punarārabhate daśamasyāhno'naṅgamiti daśamasyāhaḥ eke ācāryyāḥ mānasam anaṅgaṃ bruvate guṇapradhānamekadeśo'ṅgam avayava ityekorthaḥ na aṅgam anaṅgaṃ kasmādanaṅgaṃ bruvate bahiṣpatnīsaṃyājatvādete yasmāt patnīsaṃyājebhyo bahiretat stotrasthāne hyetat stotrāṇi sarvāṇi prāk patnīsaṃyājebhyo'pavṛjyante ūrddhvaṃ patnīsaṃyājebhyaḥ stotrānāmapravṛttiḥ tasmādanaṅgam
10.3.2.[1]	dvādaśāhabrāhmaṇaṃ aṣṭau madhya ukthyā agniṣṭomāvabhita iti yadi hi mānasaṃ daśamasyāṅgamabhaviṣyat agniṣṭomatvena tasyāpavarṇanaṃ nābhaviṣyat daśamasya mānasaṃ hi tattrayodaśaṃ stotraṃ tatra daśamamaharatyagniṣṭomo'bhaviṣyat
10.3.3.[1]	kiñcānyat asya mānasasya avayavena ekadeśena sargaṃ vadati sargaḥ sṛṣṭirityanarthāntaram iha stotrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ ātmābhyāsakriyā asya punarmānasasya avayavena ekadeśena kriyāṃ vadati manaso'pāvartayati manasā hiṅkaroti manasā prastauti manasodgāyati manasā pratiharati manasā nidhanamupayantīti evaṃ ebhiḥ kāraṇairanaṅgaṃ sadityucyate
10.3.4.[1]	tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ vyāvartayati yaduktaṃ daśamasyāhnaḥ anaṅgaṃ mānasamiti tanna aṅgameva syāt yasmādadhikṛtya daśamamahaḥ mānasamāmnātaṃ kathamanaṅgaṃ syāt
10.3.5.[1]	na hi kadācit paśyāmaḥ ekastotrasya svatantrabhāvo vartamānaḥ tasmādastotrasthānamityāha
10.3.6.[1]	atha yaduktamagniṣṭomāvabhita iti cāhetyatra brūmaḥ vādamātrametat yathā gavāmayane atirātrasya vādamātraṃ jyotiṣṭomo bhavati yajñamukhaṃ tadṛdhnuvanti yadukthyo yajñakratoranantarayājeti na kadācit jyotiṣṭomaḥ ukthyaḥ prāyaṇīyo bhavati gavāmayane ukthāni dṛṣṭvā vādamātraṃ pravṛttaṃ evametadvādamātraṃ agniṣṭomāvabhita iti
10.3.7.[1]	yaduktaṃ avayavena cāsya sargaṃ vadatītyatra brūmaḥ aheturayaṃ na hi adhikṛtyāmnātaṃ sargāvayavamātrādanaṅgaṃ syādyathā rathantaraṃ jyotiṣṭomasya jyotiṣṭomamadhikṛtya āmnātaṃ rathantaraṃ sāvāgrathantaramanvapadyatetyekadeśāmnānāt na hi rathantaraṃ jyotiṣṭomasya anaṅgaṃ bhavati prajāpatirakāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tūṣṇīṃ manasā dhyāyet tasya yanmanasyāsīt tadbṛhatsamabhavatsa ādīdhīta garbho vai me'yamantarhitastaṃ vācā prajanayā iti sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sā vāgrathantaramanvapadyateti evamete hetavaḥ prasaktāstasmādaṅgameva mānasaṃ syāt daśamasyeti
10.3.8.[1]	iha satreṣu prāyaṇīyodayanīyāvatirātrau paṭhati tatra kasmiṃścit ṣoḍaśinamādiśati kasmiṃścitpratiṣedhati yatra punarnādeśo na pratiṣedhaḥ tatra kathaṃ ṣoḍaśī karttavyo na karttavya ityetasminnarthe ācāryyaḥ parīkṣāmārabhate atirātrayoḥ prāyaṇīyodayanīyayoḥ ṣoḍaśini anādiṣṭe apratiṣiddhe kriyamāṇe'sminyatra virāṭ upapadyate kuryyādenaṃ ṣoḍaśinaṃ tatra ityācāryyā āhuḥ yasmāt dvādaśāhe kriyate na gavāmayane tatra tathopapadyate tatra tayordvādaśāhagavāmayanayoḥ kriyamāṇe cākriyamāṇe ca ṣoḍaśini virāḍupapadyate tatra daśāhe yadi ṣoḍaśi kriyate ato virāṭ sampadyate gavāmayane kriyamāṇe prāyaṇīyodayanīyayoratirātrayoḥ ṣoḍaśini virāṭ sampadyate
10.3.9.[1]	pratipakṣe yaduktaṃ sampatkāraṇaṃ ṣoḍaśina iti tatra na kāraṇam akāraṇam animittaṃ sampat hetuḥ nimittaṃ pramāṇaṃ kāraṇamityanarthāntaraṃ bahavo hyavirāṭsampannāḥ bahavo hi yajñā na virāṭsampannāḥ kiñcānyatkāraṇamapūrvasya vidherna vidyate apūrvasya prathamautpattikasya vidheḥ kāraṇaṃ na vidyate yasmāt dvādaśāhagavāmayanayoḥ ṣoḍaśikā ṣoḍaśitvaṃ na virāṭsampadartham apūrva evāsau tayorautpattiko vidhiḥ prākṛtasya
10.3.10.[1]	atirātrasya tu jyotiṣṭomasya prākṛtasya tatra yāthākāmī bhavatīti ṣoḍaśini kriyamāṇe akriyamāṇe vā yāthākāmyaṃ nāma iṣṭataḥ pravṛttiḥ jyotiṣṭomo'tirātraḥ ṣoḍaśimāniti tasmāt yeṣu satreṣu prāyaṇīyodayanīyayoratirātrayoḥ ṣoḍaśī nādiśyate nāpi pratiṣidhyate teṣu yāthākāmyaṃ syāt
10.3.11.[1]	yau tau vidhipratiṣedhau kvacidvidhānaṃ kvacitpratiṣedhaḥ to niyamārthau
10.3.12.[1]	pūrvasmiṃstrayodaśarātre paṭhati atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhyaṣaḍahaḥ sarvastomo'tirātraścavāraśchandomā atirātra iti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ chandomā vyūḍhā bhavanti na vyūḍhā iti sarvastomena vyavadhānāt ata ācāryya ārabhate pūrvasmiṃstrayodaśarātre vyūḍhāśchandomāḥ syuriti kasmāt somasānna ādeśāt gaurīvitasya cānādeśāt yadi hi samūḍhā abhaviṣyan iha somasāma nādekṣyat tasmāt samūḍheṣu chandomeṣyavasthitaṃ somasāma gaurīvitañcādekṣyat yasmāt samūḍheṣu śchandomeṣu gaurīvitaṃ nāsti na hi samūḍho'sti chandomānāṃ prakṛtau prāk gaurīvitaḥ svaraḥ tasmāt vyūḍhāśchandomā bhavanti
10.3.13.[1]	gavāmayananyāyena pṛṣṭhyaḥ syāt yo gavāmayananyāyaḥ saḥ vyūḍho vā samūḍho vā tṛcaklṛptabahiṣpavamāmaḥ tasmāt yatra yatrāvachinnastatra tatra tathā pravarttate
10.3.14.[1]	daśarātravat tu syāt na gavāmayananyāyena avyatirekāt nāyaṃ vyatirikto daśarātrāt
10.3.15.[1]	avyatirekāt
10.3.16.[1]	vyūhasamādhirhetuḥ vyūḍhāśchandomāḥ pṛṣṭhe'pi vyūḍhe kriyamāṇe samādhiḥ kṛtā bhavati
10.3.17.[1]	pratnavaccādyabahiṣpavamānaṃ siddhaṃ yasmātpareṇa etanmātraṃ trayodaśarātram asya pratnānurūpa ityāha maśakaḥ apavṛjya trayodaśarātraṃ asya pratnānurūpa iti paṭhati dvādaśāhasya ṣoḍaśimantāvatirātrau trayodaśarātre prathamasya chandomasya kaṇvarathantarasya loke somasāma punānaḥ soma dhārayetyetatsāṃvatsarikaṃ vrataṃ satreṣu yatrātirātrātpṛṣṭhyamupayanti prathamasyāhno'sya pratnānurūpa iti
10.3.18.[1]	chando bhavati daśarātre
10.3.19.[1]	bhavatyetadbahiṣpavamāne navāhasya yuktyā iti sa ceha navāho'sti
10.3.20.[1]	saṃvatsare'bhiplavasyābhyāso dṛṣṭaḥ tatra ca viśeṣo dṛṣṭaḥ arṣāsomadyumattama iti gāyatrañca ya evañcāpatyasantaniśākvaravarṇānyuttareṣviti tadabhiplavasyābhyāsaḥ rātrisatreṣvapi keṣucidbhavati tatsaṃvatsare ādeśādviśeṣasya rātrisatreṣvevābhyāsastathaiva syāt evaṃ gautama ācāryo manyate
10.3.21.[1]	trayastriṃśadrātre satre nivṛttimuttareṣām apatyādīnāṃ darśayatīti aparaṃ mataṃ nāsya paramaparam athavā idamanyat idamaparaṃ tasmādanyeṣu sāṃvatsariko abhyāsaḥ syāditi
10.4.1.[1]	kathaṃ nivṛttimuttareṣāṃ darśayatīti taducyate āvṛttānāṃ pañcāhānāṃ trayastriṃśadrātre prathamasya pañcāhasya prathamasyāhno mānavādirbṛhatī bhavati athaitayaiva pañcāhā āvṛttā āvṛttānāṃ pañcāhānāṃ prathamasya pañcāhasya prathamasyāhno'bhisomāsa āyava iti mānavamekasyāṃ tasyāmevānūpa iti tat yadyapatyādīnāṃ pravṛttiḥ syāt tatra tṛtīye pañcāhe santani syāt tadāvṛttasya prathamaṃ tadevaṃ santanimānavayorjāmi syāt anena kāraṇena manyāmahe apatyādīnāṃ rātrisatreṣu nivṛttirbhavati
10.4.2.[1]	vaikṛtatvāttu teṣu pañcāheṣu apatyādīnāṃ nivṛttiḥ pañcāhāstena te ṣaḍahāsteṣu pañcāheṣviti
10.4.3.[1]	pañcāheṣvabhiplavaprasaṅgaṃ na kuryyāt tasmādabhiplavābhyāso rātrisatreṣu syāt sāṃvatsarikebhyo'yaṃ viśeṣaḥ
10.4.4.[1]	ya ete pañcāhāstrayastriṃśadrātre coditāḥ te anādeśe prakṛtipratyayādityetadādibhirhetubhiḥ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhāniti pakṣaḥ pratigṛhyate tān pratyekamunmīlayiṣyāmaḥ tān pañcāhāneka ācāryyāḥ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhān manyante kiṃ kāraṇam anādeśe prakṛtipratyayāt yatra hyādeśo nāsti tatra prakṛteḥ pratyayo bhavati iha sarve vilopāddaśarātrādbhavanti ucyate yadyevaṃ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhānityevaṃ na vaktavyaṃ na hi pṛṣṭhyaḥ stomaḥ prakṛtiḥ ucyate pṛṣṭhyapañcāhā evāsya vivakṣitāḥ bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭhyatāmabhipretya samūḍhañca pṛṣṭhyastomena pradeśaṃ karoti yadi tu pṛṣṭhyena pradeśaṃ kuryyāt pṛṣṭhyāni prasajyeran vyūḍhasamūḍhatāyāñca vikalpaḥ syāt evaṃ mābhūdityataḥ pṛṣṭhyastomena pradiśati pṛṣṭhya eva tvasya prakṛtitvenābhipretaḥ viśvajidanvavāyāt iha ca manyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti yenaiva viśvajidanvavaiti ya ete pṛṣṭhyavilopā etān sarvān viśvajidanvavaiti tathā tṛtīye ṣaḍrātre abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho viśvajidatirātraḥ tathā dvitīye navarātre jyotiṣṭomo'gniṣṭomo gaurukthya āyurukthyo'bhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho viśvajidatirātra iti daśarātre'bhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāhāśvān vā yaśchandomā viśvajidatirātra iti eteṣāṃ pṛṣṭhyavilopaṃ kṛtvā viśvajidanvavāyo bhavati pṛṣṭhyānugrahārthaṃ nānā brahmasāmatvācca manyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti na hi nānā brahmasāma abhiplavaḥ śyaitanaudhasabrahmasāmatvāt tena pradeśaḥ nānā brahmasāmānyupayantīti nityānuvādo'yaṃ yadi hyapūrvo bhavet vidhirevābhaviṣyat vidhāyakena vākyena vyavāyaḥ syāt nānā brahmasāmānyupeyuriti ṣaṣṭhasyālopavacanāt itaśca manyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti yasmāt pṛṣṭhyaṃ prati ṣaṣṭhasyālopavacanaṃ lupyate vā etat ṣaṣṭhamaharyatpañcāhānupayanti narttavaḥ kalpante yatpṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahastena ṣaṣṭhamaharna lupyate narttavaḥ kalpanta iti tadyadi pārṣṭikaṃ ṣaṣṭamaharna luptaṃ tataḥ pṛṣṭhyasya ṣaḍahasya kriyāyāmalopavacanaṃ nopapadyate atha punarābhiplavikaṃ ṣaṣṭhamaharna luptaṃ tasya pārṣṭikena ṣaṣṭhenāhnā alopavacanaṃ nopapadyate jyotirgaurāyurityanādeśāt yadyasyābhiplavikaḥ pañcāha iṣṭo bhavati tatropadiśyate vātirātrojyotigaurāyugaurāyuḥ pañcāha iti iha punastasyānādeśāt manyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti trivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyantoti cāha evaṃ brāhmaṇamāha trivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyantīti tasya trivṛtstomaṃ prathamamahaḥ āvṛttasya tadevohanīyaṃ bhavati evametairhetubhirmanyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti
10.4.5.[1]	samāstvete hetavaḥ ya ete pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhatve hetava uktāstān samīkariṣyāmaḥ tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣanivṛtyarthaḥ yaduktaṃ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti tanna ya evaite hetava uktā ubhayatraite samāḥ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāheṣvabhiplavapañcāheṣu ca yattāvaduktam anādeśe prakṛtipratyayādityatra brūmaḥ naiva pṛṣṭhyaḥ stomaḥ prakṛtiḥ yaduktaṃ tvayā pṛṣṭhyamabhipretya pṛṣṭhyastomena pradiśatyetannopapadyate kathaṃ hi pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā ityukte pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti pratīyeran tadyathaiva pṛṣṭhyastomasya dāsarātrikānyahāni prakṛtirevamabhiplavasyāpi tānyeva prakṛtiḥ tasmādanādeśe prakṛtipratyayāditi ubhayatrāyaṃ samohetuḥ ubhāvetau ṣaḍahāvabhiplavapṛṣṭhyastomau vikṛtī tasmādubhayordaśāhikaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ prakṛtiḥ atha yaduktaṃ viśvajidanvavāyādityatra brūmaḥ nātra pṛṣṭhānāṃ vilopoyadarthaṃ viśvajidanvavaitīti atra hi daśarātraprayogo vakṣyate tatprayogādeva pṛṣṭhānāmavilopaḥ na cāpi pṛṣṭhārthena viśvajidāgacchati viṣuvadarthenāgacchati atra viśvajit tato ayamapi samohetuḥ atha yaduktaṃ nānā brahmasāmatvādatra brūmaḥ nātra nānābrahmasāmānīti anityārthavādaḥ apūrvameva nānā brahmasāmatvaṃ vidhīyate nityānuvādavadvidhānāni dṛśyante yathā rathantaraṃ bhavati cārkṣaṃ cāsmai daṇḍaṃ prayacchanvācayediti atha yaduktaṃ pṛṣṭhyataḥ ṣaṣṭhasyālopavacanāditi atrāpyucyate yathaiva pṛṣṭyastomasya bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭhasya sataḥ ṣaṣṭhamaharlupyate evamevābhiplavasthāpi tasmāt samānolopaḥ ṣaḍahatantre atha yaduktaṃ jyotirgaurāyurityanādeśādityatra brūmaḥ yatra hyasya pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iṣṭāḥ tatrāpyādiśatyeva yathā pṛṣṭhyasya na labdhiḥ abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāha iti yathā dvitīye navarātre daśarātre chando bhavati tadyathaivātra jyotirgaurāyurityanādeśe iti evaṃ pṛṣṭhyastome'pyanādeśa iti yaduktaṃ trivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyantīti cāheti atra brūmaḥ ayaṃ trivṛchandaḥ na kevalaṃ stomavācīti tritvañcāpekṣya bhavati yathā agninā pṛthivyauṣadhibhistenāyaṃ lokastrivṛt tathā agne vivasvaduṣasa iti sandhinā stuyurityadhikṛtya trikaṃ stomaṃ vidhāyāha prāṇāvai trivṛtstomānāmiti evamayaṃ trivṛcchandastrivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyantīti uttame ca trayastriṃśadrātre tritvamiha samākhyābhipravarttate trivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyantīti purastāttrayaḥ pañcāhāstraya upariṣṭāditi tasmādayamapi heturubhayatra samaḥ ata ete hetavaḥ samīkṛtāḥ pratyuktāḥ svapakṣamidānīṃ sthāpayiṣyāmaḥ
10.4.6.[1]	gautama ācārya āha abhiplavapañcāhā eva bhavantīti eva śabdoavadhāraṇarthaḥ abhiplavapañcāhā eva na pṛṣṭhāstomapañcāhā iti yasmādadhikṛtaḥ satreṣu abhiplavapañcāhaḥ atirātro jyotirgaurāyuḥ pañcāha iti yaduktamanādeśe prakṛtipratyayāditi anādeśajātireṣā bhavati yadadhikāraḥ kiñcānyat itaraścādṛṣṭaḥ itaraśca pṛthyastomapañcāhaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ satreṣu kiṃ dṛṣṭārthaḥ pratīyatāmadṛṣṭārthaḥ pratīyatāmiti dṛṣṭapratyayo nyāyata iti
10.4.7.[1]	abhyāsaścādṛṣṭaḥ prākṛtasya tāvat pṛṣṭhyastomasyaiva kutaḥ pañcāhasyābhyāsaḥ syāditi yāvatā nidānakāro'pyāha athāpi kṛtsnāveva pṛṭhyastomau nābhiprayogaṃ labhete kuto viluptau labheyātāmiti
10.4.8.[1]	yadapyuktaṃ jyotirgaurāyurityanādeśāditi iva pareṣāṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jyotirāyurgaurāyuḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīya iti
10.4.9.[1]	ete pañcāhā bhavanti tata eṣa pratnā vā anurūpaḥ pratipañcāhaṃ vārkajambhaṃ vā prathame'hani
10.4.10.[1]	āñjanābhyañjanāsu gārhapatye'gnau sarpīṃṣi gṛhītāni phāṇayeyuḥ pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ devasurabhibhiḥ saha devasurabhīṇi yānyuktāni brāhmaṇena gaulgulavena saugandhikena paitudāraveṇa ghṛtaṃ saha ekīkaraṇaṃ devasurabhibhiḥ
10.4.11.[1]	taiḥ sutyāsūpākaraṇavelāyāṃ havirddhānayoḥ pūrve pradeśe āsīnāḥ satriṇaḥ āñjīran akṣīṇī gātrāṇi ca abhyañjīran uktaṃ gaulgulavena prātaḥsavane saugandhikena mādhyandine savane paitudāraveṇa tṛtīyasavana iti
10.4.12.[1]	gautama ācāryyo manyate bhuktvāgnīdhrīya eva tat kuryyuriti
10.4.13.[1]	ānupūrvyaṃ brāhmaṇenoktaṃ gaulgulavena prātaḥsavane saugandhikena mādhyandine savane paitudāraveṇa tṛtīyasavane
10.4.14.[1]	dhānañjapyaśāṇḍilyāvācāryyāvāhatuḥ aharaharetat kuryyuriti
10.4.15.[1]	sarvastoma evaitat kuryyuriti eṣa ūrddhvaṃ stomataḥ saṃsthātaḥ
10.4.16.[1]	eke ācāryyā bruvate pṛṣṭhya eva tatkuryuriti
10.5.1.[1]	saṃvatsarasaṃmitāsu paṭhati tadāhuryaccaturviṃśamahaḥ prāyaṇīyaṃ kuryyuḥ saṃvatsaramārabhya na samāpayeyuriti trivṛdeva kāryamiti tatra kimidaṃ trivṛtā liṅgena dāśarātrikaṃ prathamamahaścodyete athavā tata adhikṛtasyaiva prāyaṇīyasya stomavikāra iti so'yametasminnarthe śāstramārabhate saṃvatsarasaṃmitāsvityādi saṃvatsarasaṃmitā iti saṃjñā tāsu saṃvatsarasaṃmitāsu prathamamahaḥ dāśarātrikaṃ prāyaṇīyaṃ syādityeke ācāryyā ūcuḥ yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇamāha trivṛdeva kāryyamiti
10.5.2.[1]	natvevaṃ syāt prāyaṇīyaṃ caturviṃśamahaścodayitvā atirātraścaturviṃśaṃ prāyaṇīyamahariti trivṛdeva kāryyamiti tasya stomavikāraṃ gṛhṇāti
10.5.3.[1]	kiñcānyat dāśarātrikāṇāñcāhnāṃ avayavaprayogaḥ ekadeśasammitāsu prayogo na vidyate
10.5.4.[1]	saṃvatsarasaṃmitāsu uttare pakṣasi abhiplave asmin āvṛtte śārkaravarṇaṃ syādityācāryyā manyante sāṃvatsarikasya dravyasyānugrahārthamiti pūrvasmin pakṣasi trayo'bhiplavāḥ prayuktāḥ yaṇvāpatyaṃ santaninimittam ayaṃ caturthaḥ śārkvaravarṇavān uttare pakṣasi tasmin prayujyamāne sarvasāṃvatsarikaṃ dravyamanugṛhītaṃ bhavati
10.5.5.[1]	natvevaṃ syāt yaścaturthaḥ sāṃvatsariko'bhiplavaḥ pūrvasmin pakṣasi sa iha luptaḥ tena saha śārkvaravarṇamapyupeyāt yathā pṛṣṭhyena lupyamānena janitramapi luptaṃ nanu sarva eva pṛṣṭho luptaḥ tatkimidaṃ yathā pṛṣṭhyena janitramiti ucyate pṛṣṭo daśarātre prayokṣyate janitrantu samūhāgataṃ tat luptameva
10.5.6.[1]	ucyate yadi śārkvaravarṇaṃ kriyate kiṃ tarhi tatra karttavyamiti bravīti santani karttavyaṃ taddhi pūrvasmin pakṣasi prayuktantadiha karttavyaṃ āvṛttisādhutvāt uttarasya pakṣasya āvṛttisādhuruttare pakṣa iti
10.5.7.[1]	yaṇvantu syāt tatra na santanini upariṣṭādhyabhiplāvānāṃ lopasthānaṃ purastādbhavati tasmāt yaṇvameva syāt
10.5.8.[1]	uttarasmin pakṣasi āvṛttasyābhiplavasya etenoktaṃ vidhānam ekaṣaṣṭirātre
10.5.9.[1]	śatarātre paṭhati abhiprayāyamabhiṣuṇvantyabhikrāntyai samānatrābhiṣuṇvanti pratiṣṭhityā iti sa vikalpaḥ syāt bhavet abhiprayāya vā syādabhiṣavaḥ abhiprayāyābhiprayāya samānatra samānatra vā samānadeśe ekasmin ubhayasyāśakyatvāt
10.5.10.[1]	abhiprayāyaṃ sunvantaḥ yāntaḥ sunuyuḥ yathā yena prakāreṇa sārasvateṣu śamyāprāsanena
10.5.11.[1]	yatra kvaca deśe nātra niyamaḥ yathā sārasvateṣu sarasvatyāstīreṇeti
10.5.12.[1]	ekasminvā deśe sunuyuḥ samāne ayānta eva
10.5.13.[1]	śrutyarthatvāt kalpyante cakrīvanti sadohavirddhānāni kārayitvā sadaśca havirddhāne ca sadohavirddhānāni teṣāmahaḥsaṃsthāsu ahaḥsamāptiṣu cakrāṇi viparivarttayeyurityācāryyā āhuḥ tadabhiprayāttasya rūpam aprayāṇāśca samānatrābhiṣavaḥ aprayāṇāśca ekatra deśe samāne abhiṣavaḥ kṛto bhavati evamubhayoḥ śrutyorarthaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati
10.5.14.[1]	dhānañjapyaśāṇḍilyāvācāryyāvāhatuḥ yadetadabhiṣavasya vidhānamuktam etadahanyahani kuryyuriti
10.5.15.[1]	gautama ācāryya āha abhiplaveṣveva tat kuryurnāhanyahani iti
10.5.16.[1]	eke ācāryyā āhuḥ trikadrukeṣvityevaitatkuryyurnānyatreti
