10.5.17.[1]	uktaḥ kāloyasyāḥ seyamuktakāladīkṣā kāla ukto brāhmaṇena gavāmayanasya ayane vikalpaḥ
10.5.18.[1]	vaiśākhajyaiṣṭhau tu vikalpete asamāsa iti kimartham āṣāḍhaśceti ucyate vakṣyati ṣaṣṭhyāṃ vā dīkṣitvā saptadaśadīkṣāḥ kurvīranniti tadāṣāḍha eva syāt
10.5.19.[1]	ṣaṣṭhyāṃ vā āṣāḍhasya dīkṣitvā saptadaśadīkṣāḥ kurvīran
10.5.20.[1]	etena gavāmayanikena vidhinā sāṃvatsarikāṇāṃ satrāṇām uktaṃ vidhānam ādeśādanyatra ādeśe yathādeśam
10.6.1.[1]	uktakālādīkṣā brāhmaṇena gavāmayanasyetyetadadhikṛtaṃ tasmin gavāmayane paṭhati abhīvartto brahmasāma bhavatītyevamadhikṛtyāha pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthā āpyanta iti teṣāṃ pragāthānāntu viṣayaḥ kalpyate pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthāḥ samāpyante prāpyanta iti yadidaṃ vidhānante pragāthā abhīvarttastotrīyāḥ syuḥ kiṃ viṣayasyābhīvarttasya brahmasāmabhūtasya yasmāttasya prakaraṇe śrūyante
10.6.2.[1]	samānaṃ sāma bhavatyanyonyaḥ pragātha ityetadbrāhmaṇamabhīvarttasya nānā pragāthatāṃ darśayati
10.6.3.[1]	kutaḥ punaste pragāthā āhartavyā iti ucyate catuḥśatamaindrā bārhatāḥ pragāthā daśatayīṣviti catvāraśca śataṃ catuḥśataṃ aindrāḥ devatayā bārhatāḥ chandasā daśatayīṣu daśāvayavāsvṛkṣu rugveda ityarthaḥ
10.6.4.[1]	teṣāṃ pragāthānāṃ catuḥśatasya catvāraḥ anyatra sthānāḥ caturṇāmanyatra sthānaṃ brahmasāmnaḥ bṛhadrathantarayoḥ stotrīyayoḥ kāleyastotrīyāḥ indrakratumauttarapākṣika iti
10.6.5.[1]	evañcānyatra sthānāṃ caturuddhṛtya śataṃ pragāthāḥ śiṣyante tasya śatasyaikaṃ pragāthaṃ prāyanīye'hani caturviṃśe kuryyāt itarānyekonaśatam abhiplaveṣu kuryyāt pañcasu māseṣu viṃśatirabhiplavāḥ teṣu ekaikasminnabhiplave pañca pañca pragāthā bhavantīti teṣāmekasmiṃścatvāra evamevaiṣāṃ pragāthānāṃ vināśaḥ
10.6.6.[1]	tāsveva daśatayīṣu ekonaviṃśatsātobārhatāstṛcāḥ tān āharet
10.6.7.[1]	teṣāṃ sātobārhatānāṃ tṛcānāṃ ekaikaṃ tṛtīye tṛtīye'hani kuryyāt abhiplaveṣu prathamadvitīyatṛtīyacaturthapañcamaṣaṣṭheṣu pragāthā na kṛtā hi satobṛhatyaḥ tṛtīye'hanyārṣeyakalpena ātvā sahasramāśatamityetāḥ
10.6.8.[1]	pañcamasya māsasya ya uttamo'bhiplavastasminneva pragātho na saṃpūryyate pañcame'hani satobṛhatīḥ kuryyāt dvau sātobṛhatau tṛcau catvāraśca pragāthāḥ evamekaviṃśatiḥ sātobṛhatyaḥ prayuktāḥ pragāthāśca sarve aṣṭau sātobārhatāstṛcāḥ avaśiṣyante
10.6.9.[1]	uktaṃ pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthā āpyante teṣvāpteṣu chandasi saṃyujyaitavyantisṛṣu uṣṇihaḥ syurekā gāyatrī tāstisro bṛhatyo bhavantīti yāvat teṣu pragātheṣu āpteṣu sarveṣu chandasī saṃyujyaitavyamiti brāhmaṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsi gāyatrīpādamekaikamuṣṇahāmupariṣṭāt kuryyāt evante bārhatāstṛcā bhavanti anyathā hi viṣṭāvānopapadyante
10.6.10.[1]	gautama ācāryya āha sātobārhatānāṃ tṛcānām ekaviṃśatiḥ pañcasu māseṣu prayuktāḥ anye'ṣṭau śeṣā anuprayuktāḥ tān ṣaṣṭhasya māsasya prathame'bhiplave kṛtvā dvitīyasya cārthe dvyahe tataśchandasī saṃyujyā diti
10.6.11.[1]	yasmāt bṛhatīkṣayādevamāmanati teṣvāpteṣu chandasī saṃyujyaitavyam
10.6.12.[1]	uktaṃ tadāhuḥ saṃśara iva vā eṣa chandasāṃ yaddve chandasī saṃyujyantīni caturuttareva chandobhiretavyamiti etasmiṃścaturuttarakalpe gāyatrīṃ caturviṃśe'hani kuryyāt abhiplavike prathame'hani uṣṇihaṃ kuryyāt anuṣṭubhaṃ dvitīye'hani kuryyāt itareṣu sarveṣvahaḥsu bṛhatīṃ kuryyāt
10.6.13.[1]	kiñca uddharetpañcamādahnaḥ satobṛhatīḥ yasmāt pragāthāḥ prabhavanti vidyanta ityarthaḥ caturviṃśāt prāyaṇīyādekaḥ ābhilavikau dvau dvitīyaprathamābhyāmahobhyām ekaḥ pañcamāt
10.6.14.[1]	tatra pañcame'hani ṣaṣṭhe vā paṅktīḥ kṛtvā
10.6.15.[1]	triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsaṃ gaccheyuḥ
10.6.16.[1]	tṛtīye svarasāmni jagatī karttavyā evameteṣāṃ chandasāṃ kriyā yasmādāha ekāṃ gāyatrīmekāhamupeyurekāmaṣṇihamekāhamekāmanuṣṭubhamekāhaṃ bṛhatyā pañcamāsamīyuḥ paṅktimekāhamupeyuḥ triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsamīyuḥ śvoviṣuvān bhaviteti jagatīmupeyuriti
10.6.17.[1]	gautama ācāryya āha sātobārhatā navāvasiṣṭā dvau ca pragāthau tān ṣaṣṭhasya māsasya prathame cābhiplave dvitīyasya cābhiplavasvādye pañcāhe tān kṛtvā tataḥ paṅktimupeyuriti athavā teṣāmeva bārhatānāṃ pragāthānām uttamasya sthāne paṅktiṃ kṛtvā tata ūrddhvaṃ triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsamīyuḥ yāvasiddham
10.7.1.[1]	iha paṭhati tadāhuranavaklṛptāni vā etāni chandāṃsi madhyandine bṛhatyā caiva triṣṭubhā caitavyamiti cāturuttaryamapodya triṣṭupbṛhatībhyāṃ vidadhāti taducyate bṛhatyā caiva triṣṭubhā caitavyamiti triṣṭubhaṃ caturviṃśe'hani prāyaṇīye kuryyāt abhīvarttastotrīyaṃ prathame ābhiplavike'hani bṛhatīṃ kuryyāt abhīvarttasya
10.7.2.[1]	eṣa viparyyāsaḥ anena nyāyena eṣa viparyyāsaḥ sarvasminnayane
10.7.3.[1]	ya ete vidhaya uktāḥ pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthā āpyanta ityārabhya etāni mahānānātvānītyucyante śrutyantare mahānānātvāni śrūyante
10.7.4.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācāryya āha ya eṣa caturuttara prayogaḥ chandasāṃ chandobhiretavyamiti yaśca bṛhatītriṣṭubhośca viparyyāsaḥ bṛhatyā caiva triṣṭubhā caitavyamiti etau kalpau kriyamāṇa ṣaṣṭha eva māsi syātāmiti yasmādāha saṃśara iva vā eṣa chandasāṃ yaddve chandasī saṃyuñjantīti caturuttaraireva chandobhiretavyamiti tasmin ṣaṣṭhe upodya chandaḥsaṃyogaṃ kalpo vidadhāti ṣaṣṭhaviṣayaḥ chandaḥsaṃyogaḥ yadviṣayaścāpavādaḥ tadviṣayenaivetareṇa vidhinā bhavitavyam
10.7.5.[1]	ācāryyā āhuḥ sarvasminnevāyane pūrvasminnetau kalpau syātāmiti yasmāccaturuttarāṇi chandāṃsi anupūrvaṃ prayuñjānaḥ gāyatryuṣṇiganuṣṭubhau vidhāya triṣvahaḥsu bṛhatīṃ madhya āmanati yāvatpañcamāsāḥ samāptā iti kiñcānyat triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsamiti cāha brāhmaṇaṃ kṛtsnaṃ saṃyogaṃ darśayati
10.7.6.[1]	yasmāt bṛhatya eva na santi kena vyatyāsaḥ kariṣyati
10.7.7.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācāryya āha syādeva ṣaṣṭhe māsi bṛhatītriṣṭubhorviparyyāsaḥ yattāvaducyate caturuttarāṇi anupūrvaṃ prayuñjāno bṛhatīṃ madhya āmanatīti sā prāyyādbṛhatīgrahaṇaṃ na hyatra bṛhatyaḥ kṛtāḥ atra yaduktaṃ triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsamiti cāha ayaṃ bhūyasovādaḥ bhūyastvaṃ gṛhītvā pravṛttaḥ prayogo hi vādānānniyāmako bhavati atha yaduktaṃ bṛhatīkṣayācca bṛhatyā vyatyāsonopapadyate iti akṣīṇāśca bṛhatyaḥ naca bṛhatyaḥ, kṣīṇāḥ satyo bṛhatyaḥ kathaṃ santītyucyate
10.7.8.[1]	ya ekonatriṃśatsātobārhatāstṛcāsteṣāmekaviṃśatipragāthaiḥ sahopayuktāḥ aṣṭau śiṣyante tairaṣṭabhiḥ bṛhadrathantarakāleyastotrīyaiśca taiḥ taistriṣṭubhaiḥ ṣaṣṭhe māsi triṣṭubhovyatyasyet ekādaśasu rāthantareṣvahaḥsu ekādaśabṛhatyaḥ daśasu bārhateṣu daśa triṣṭubhaḥ triṣvabhiplaveṣu ca svarasāmasu ca
10.7.9.[1]	yasminnahani kāleyastotrīye'bhīvarttaḥ syāt tasminnahani taraṇiritsiṣāmatīti kāleyaṃ syāt asañcārāddhetoḥ
10.7.10.[1]	athavā svaramānnoḥ prathamatṛtīyayoranyatarasminnekasmin rathantare stotrīyaṃ brahmasāmni kuyāt yasmāttatra pṛṣṭhagatasya rathantarasya anyā eva ṛcaḥ kṛtā evamācāryyā vyācakṣate
10.7.11.[1]	viṃśatiśca śatañca viṃśatiśataṃ viṃśatiśatantvapi pragāthā na dhīyate apare tuśabdo hetvarthaḥ yasmāt tatra sa eva prayujyate catuḥśate saṃrodhaḥ svasya pakṣa eva
10.7.12.[1]	tatra tasmin kalpe tathaiva satobṛhatīḥ kuryyāt yathā catuḥśate tṛtīye'hani
10.7.13.[1]	yathā satobṛhatyaḥ pañcame māsi asyābhiplavasya pañcame'hani kṛtāḥ tā uddharet prabhavanti hi pragāthāḥ hiśabdo hetvarthaḥ yasmāt prabhavanti pragāthāḥ
10.7.14.[1]	yaḥ punarayaṃ śaucivṛkṣeḥ bṛhatītriṣṭubhorviparyyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhe māsi ayamanyāyena kṛtaḥ kathamanyāyaḥ yasmādakṛtakriyā hi ya āstutaṃ kurvato yathādugdhāmupasīdedevantaditi aprayuktapratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ punarbṛhadrathantarakāleyastotrīyāḥ teṣāṃ kṛtānāṃ satāṃ sveṣu sthāneṣu kṛtāḥ punarbrahmasāmni prayogaḥ
10.8.1.[1]	viṃśatiśatasya pragāthānāṃ śeṣo vidyate teṣāṃ saptabhiḥ pragāthaiḥ ye ca nava sātobārhatāstacaḥ teṣāṃ caturbhiḥ ṣaṣṭhe māsi triṣṭubho'vyatyasyet
10.8.2.[1]	anantaraṃ paṭhati trayastriṃśatā pragāthairetavyaṃ trayastriṃśaddevatāsveva pratitiṣṭhantoyanti caturviṃśatyaitavyaṃ dvādaśabhiretayaṃ ṣaḍbhiretavyaṃ caturbhiretavyaṃ tribhiretavyaṃ dvābhyāmetavyamiti trayastriṃśatprabhṛtayaḥ kalpāḥ śrūyante tān cayastriṃśatprabhṛtīn pragāthān saha caturviṃśeṣvabhiplaveṣu kuryyāt uttame ca svarasāmni ityevamācāryyā āhuḥ yasmādete trayastriṃśatpragāthādayaḥ kalpāḥ abhīvarttaprakaraṇe śrūyante so'trāpyabhīvartta iti caturviṃśe svarasāmasu ca uttamaṃ svarasāmānaṃ udgṛhṇāti tatra tu satobṛhatītvanna bhavati satobṛhatī uddharatīha
10.8.3.[1]	natvevaṃ syāt antareṇa caturviṃśasvarasāmnoḥ ārṣeyakalpena maśakena kṛtaṃ ṣaṭpragātham ayane ihāpi tathaiva syāt
10.8.4.[1]	teṣāṃ pragāthānāṃ yatra samaprayoge kriyamāṇe ye tṛtīye'hani satobṛhatya upapadyeran kuryyādenāstatra
10.8.5.[1]	anupapadyamānāsu samaprayogeṇa pragāthā eva syuḥ tṛtīyeṣvahaḥsu yathā anācāraḥ ṣaḍahe'nyatra tṛtīyādahnaḥ satobṛhatīnām ayaṃ hi samaprayogaḥ ṣaṭpragāthe evopapadyate
10.8.6.[1]	sa yenaiva kalpena pūrvasmin pakṣasi abhīvarttastotrīyaṃ kuryyāt ādikalpādārabhya yāvaddhi pragātha iti tathaitasmin pakṣasi indrakratau pragāthe brahmasāmāni nidhanavanti evaṃ kalpayet yasmādevamārṣeyakalpena kṛtaṃ pūrvasmin pakṣasi ṣaṭpragātheṣu abhīvarttaḥ kṛtaḥ uttarasmin indrakratau ṣaṭ sāmāni kṛtāni
10.8.7.[1]	pūrvasmin pakṣasi atirātracaturviṃśe paṭhitvā pañcāyanamāsān paṭhati tataḥ ṣaṣṭhe māsi vrataṃ paṭhati uttarasmin pakṣasi prathamaṃ vrataṃ paṭhitvā caturayanamāsān paṭhati tato daśarātramiśraṃ māsaṃ paṭhati tatra vratātirātramadhikaṃ paṭhati tat ṣaṣṭhasaptamayormāsayoḥ pūraṇaṃ dadāti atirātracaturviṃśābhyāṃ saha pūrvasmin pakṣasi ṣaṣṭhomāsaḥ sampūrṇo bhavati uttarasmin pakṣasi prathamovratātirātrābhyām
10.8.8.[1]	uktaṃ ye vai vācamannamādayantyannādā bhavantīti ye vitarṣayanti rūkṣā bhavanti gaurīvitaṃ śyāvāśvannihava etāni vai sāmāni vāco'nnameteṣāṃ vāgannaṃ yadetāni sāmāni na cyavante vācameva tadannamādayanti tena sarve'nnādā bhavanti tadyadetāni sāmāni na cyavanta iti gaurīvitasyottarayostotrīyayornihavaśyāvāśve syātāṃ sarvasmin gavāmayane hi yasmādanārabhya eteṣāṃ sthānam acyavanañca vidadhāti evameke ācāryyā manyante
10.8.9.[1]	anvavetyānvagatya gaurīvitaśyāvāśvayoḥ ārṣeyakalpena vidhiḥ kṛtaḥ anugamanamanvavāyaḥ nihavasya ca anvavetya vidhiḥ kṛto brāhmaṇena tathā sati kalpe teṣām acyavanaṃ syāt
10.9.1.[1]	mahāvrataprakaraṇe sarve mahartvijo mahāvratena stuvīrannityevamadhikṛtyādhvaryuḥ śirasodgāyediti parisaṃkhyānaṃ karoti tatra kiṃ sarvaśabdasya niravaśeṣavācitvāt sarveṣāṃ stavanaṃ atha parisaṃkhyānādadhvaryvādayo ye parisaṃkhyātāsteṣāmiti etasmin saṃśaya ācāryya ārabhate sarve mahartvijo mahāvratena stuvīranniti tadetadbrāhmaṇam ayamudgātṛvikāra eva syāt yenodgātā vikriyate adhvaryumaitrāvaruṇabrāhmaṇāchaṃsigṛhapatibhista eva syuḥ aśrutibhūtā hyanye na śrutibhūtā aśrutibhūtāḥ anya ṛtvijaḥ na śrutibhūtāḥ ucyante nanviyaṃ śrutiḥ sarve mahartvija iti atrāha
10.9.2.[1]	yo'yaṃ sarvaśabdaḥ ayanteṣvevāvāpyate etaddhi brāhmaṇam adhvaryvādīn manasi kṛtvā sarvaśabdaṃ prayuṇkte tena tasyādhikṛteṣu sarvaśabdo'rthavān yathā sarva odanabhutaḥ sarvairbrāhmaṇairbhuktamiti / 2
10.9.3.[1]	saha stuvīranniti yadetat tadetasmin karmaṇi samavāyāt paurvāparyyacodanādanupūrvaṃ stavanaṃ syāt yattu stavanaṃ tadeva ānupūrvyeṇa syāt pūrvāparabhāvaḥ paurvāparyyam
10.9.4.[1]	tisṛbhirudgātātmana udgīyeti caitadādi brāhmaṇam ātmanā jaghanyastavanaṃ darśayati evaṃ caitatsarvaṃ bhavati yathānupūryeṇa stavanamiti
10.9.5.[1]	yadetannānādeśastavanañcoditaṃ havirddhāne śirasā stutvā ityetadādinā tacchandogānāmeva syāt netareṣāṃ yasmāt atho khalvāhuḥ kathamadhvaryyurbahvṛcaḥ sāma gāyedityudgātaiva sarveṇodgāyediti hyuktvā tasya deśānvidadhāti tasya sthānāni vidadhāti udgātuḥ kiñcānyat havirddhāne śirasā stutvā saṃrabdhāḥ pratyañca eyuste dakṣiṇena dhiṣṇyān parītya paścāt maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyasyopaviśyeti caiṣa samānakarttṛka ādeśaḥ ye śirasi stuvate teṣāmevetaraiḥ stavanaṃ darśayati
10.9.6.[1]	ilāndamagniṣṭomasāma kāryyamiti brāhmaṇaṃ tadilāndamagniṣṭomasāma kriyamāṇam agne tava śravo vaya ityetāsāṃ ṣaṇṇāmṛcāṃ pūrvāsu tisṛṣu ṛkṣu syāt
10.9.7.[1]	tāsāntisṛṇāmṛcāṃ daśākṣareṣu ārcikānyanugānāni syuḥ daśākṣarāṇi daśākṣare daśākṣare ekaikamārkṣikamanugānaṃ syāt evaṃ kriyamāṇantṛce bhavati yathānyāni sāmāni
10.9.8.[1]	ṣaḍṛce sarvasmin kāryyamityevamācāryyā manyanta evaṃ kriyamāṇe asaṃrodhataraḥ parvaṇāṃ kṛto bhavati ayamatisaṃrodhaḥ pūrvasmiṃstu kalpe saṃrodhaḥ tatastvakriyā
10.9.9.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha dvādaśarcaḥ syāt tatra tasmin bahvṛcāvuttarau aparāvāgneyau tṛcāvāharedāte agne'gniṃ taṃ manya iti evaṃ kriyamāṇe ṛgutpannānyanugānāni sarvāṇi kṛtāni bhavanti
10.9.10.[1]	vārṣagaṇya ācāryya āha caturthamevānugānantṛce syāt yasmādatra hi nidhanavādaṃ vadati vratamiti bhavati svariti bhavati śakuna iti bhavatīti eṣa nidhanavādaḥ bhaktayaśca sarvāḥ prastāvādayaḥ asminneva kalpyante eke ca chandogā etāni pañcāpyanugānāni nānāsāmavadevādhīyate
10.10.1.[1]	gavāmayane yatkiñcitsandigdhaṃ tadvicāritam anantaramādityānāmayanamaṅgirasāmayanañca tayoḥ sāmānyaṃ vicāryate ādityānāmayane aharvyūhaṃ vidhāya paṭhati chandomadaśāho'ṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ prathamamahariti evaṃ daśasvahaḥsu aṣṭācatvāriṃśādibhiḥ stomaiḥ prakṛtān stomān pratyāmanati daśame'hani caturviṃśastomamāmanati evamevāṅgirasāmayane ca caturviṃśādīṃstomān paṭhati punardaśame caturviṃśamevāmanati maśakena prāyaṇīyādṛksāmadravyaṃ kalpayitvā chandomadaśāhayorekatra daśame'hani paṭhati maśakaḥ atha yadeva chandomavato daśarātrasya mahāvratāntimamahastadatra daśarātramiti aparatra paṭhati atha yadeva pūrvasya chandomadaśāhasya daśamamahastadatra daśamamiti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ maśakena daśamapradeśāt trikatrayastriṃśo mānasāgniṣṭomasāmnoḥ stomo karttavyo atha pratyakṣavidhānāt sarvatraiva caturviṃśa iti etasmin saṃśaye ayamācāryya ārabhate chandomadaśāhayordaśamasya trayastriṃśamagniṣṭomasāma syādityeke trikaṃ sārparājñaṃ daśamapradeśāditi chandomadaśāhayorubhayorapi daśamasyāhnaḥ trayastriṃśamagniṣṭomasāma syādityeke ācāryyā manyante trikañca sārparājñam ete ubhe mānasāgniṣṭomasāmano trikatrayastriṃśastomayoḥ syātāṃ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ daśamapradeśāt yasmāt daśame ubhayorapyetayoḥ prākṛtena daśamenāhnā pradeśaṃ karoti anyonyaṃ syāt yadyevaṃ tadidaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ caturviṃśamiti asya kṛtsnasaṃyogasthānarthakyaṃ prāpnoti ucyate
10.10.2.[1]	yadetadbrāhmaṇaṃ caturviṃśamiti eṣa yathā bhūyasovādaḥ bhūyastvaṃ gṛhītvā pravṛttaḥ āmravanavat brāhmaṇagrāmaḥ yasminnanyepi vṛkṣā vidyante tathāpi āmravanamiti ucyate tathā anye'pi varṇā vidyante tathāpi brāhmaṇagrāma ityucyate na caturṣvityanye'pi varṣā na santi kintu bhūyastvādvādaḥ sanniviṣṭo yathā prādhānyabhūyastvānnityatvācca vādāḥ sanniviśante evamayaṃ caturviṃśamiti bhūyastvādvādaḥ sanniviṣṭaḥ
10.10.2.[1]	tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣanivṛtyarthaḥ yaduktaṃ trayastriṃśamagniṣṭomasāma syāt trikaṃ sārparājñamiti tanna ṛksāmamātraṃ pradiśyate daśamastomastu caturviṃśastomaṃ prathamamaharadhikṛtya aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ prathamamaharadhikṛtya sarveṣāmahnāṃ kṛtsnādhikāraḥ
10.10.4.[1]	yaduktaṃ bhūyasovādacaturviṃśamiti evaṃ na syāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt pratyakṣavikāro balīyān yathā bhūyasovādāt caturviṃśamiti pratyakṣeṇa śabdena vikaroti trikatrayastriṃśe
10.10.5.[1]	yaduktaṃ maśakena pradeśāditi brāhmaṇavihitena stomena kalpapradeśena ṛksāmnāṃ bhavati maśako hi brāhmaṇaṃ upaklṛptasya stomasya vaśena pradeśasyeṣṭena hi brāhmaṇavihitaṃ stomaṃ maśakasya vikalpayituṃ īśitam
10.10.6.[1]	sarvasatreṣu triṃśinaḥ sutyā māsān sarvatra sañcakṣīran kauṇḍapāyine ca hāviryajñikān māsān kauṇḍapāyine cāgnihotrādayo vihitāḥ śunāsīryyāḥ māsamagnihotraṃ juhvatītyata ārabhya tāṃśca hāviryajñikān māsān kauṇḍapāyine triṃśinaḥ sañcakṣīran tāpaścite paṭhati saṃvatsaraṃ dīkṣitā bhavanti saṃvatsaramupasadbhiścaranti saṃvatsaraṃ prastuto bhavati tāṃśca daikṣopasadānmāsāṃstāpaścite triṃśinaḥ sarvān sañcacīran sautyāstu sarvaśabdenaiva siddhāḥ
10.10.7.[1]	dṛtivātavatorayane atirātrastrivṛtā māsamityadhikṛtya pārṣṭikaiḥ yajñastomairekena stomena kriyāvidhānaṃ pūrvasmin pakṣasi tadanantaramuttarasmiṃstaireva pratilomaiḥ tatra gautama ācāryya āha dvau māsau prathamottamau trivṛtau ekonau sunuyuratirātrābhyāntayoḥ pūraṇamiti
10.10.8.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryya āha trayastriṃśau māsau ṣaṣṭhasaptamau ekonau sunuyuriti gavāmayane hitau ekonau dṛṣṭāviti
10.10.9.[1]	athavā ubhāveva triṃśinau syātāṃ prathamottamau vā ṣaṣṭhamaptamau vā yathaitadbrāhmaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ samadhikāvevātirātrau paṭhati
10.10.10.[1]	tathā sati kalpe aṣṭamyāṃ dīkṣitvā pañcadaśadīkṣāḥ kurvīran
10.10.11.[1]	maśakaḥ paṭhati vidhṛtibhiḥ klṛptaṃ dṛtivātavatorayanamātriṇavebhyaḥ trivṛdbhyaḥ uddharatyukthāni pañcadaśebhyaḥ ṣoḍaśinamiti ṣoḍaśina uddhāraṃ paṭhati tatra ca vidhṛtīnāṃ daśame'hani pañcadaśānāṃ nārmedhamukthāneva paṭhati yadi ṣoḍaśinamuddharati tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ nārmedhasya tatra ṣoḍaśī nimittam atha vacanaṃ kāraṇamiti tadiha ācāryyairvicāryate pañcadaśastomānāmahnāṃ daśamasyāhnaḥ āṣṭādaṃṣṭrānyukthāni syurityevamācāryyā manyante kasmāt ṣoḍaśyapāyāt nārmedhasya hi tatra ṣoḍaśī nimittaṃ sacet ṣoḍaśī tasmādevamapi syāt avayavānāṃ nivṛttiḥ syāt
10.10.12.[1]	tuśabdaḥ pakṣavinivṛtyarthaḥ yathā anyāni sāmāni nivṛttāni bhavanti tatpradeśādevameva nārmedhamapi syāt na hi vacanamasti yena nārmedhaṃ nivarttata iti yaccoktaṃ ṣoḍaśino nivṛttaṃ na tatra nārmedhamityevaṃ vacanam
10.10.13.[1]	vacanañca tatra kāraṇaṃ nārmedhasya na ṣoḍaśī nimittaṃ bhavati
10.10.14.[1]	dṛśyate caitadevamābhīkṣṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ prayujyamānam aṣoḍaśikeṣu yajñeṣu yathā gūrdaḥ traikakubhañca nārmedhamityutthānānītyetadādivat
10.10.15.[1]	tasyāyanavicārā varttiṣyante pṛṣṭhyenaikaiko māso varttetetyevaṃ śrutiḥ trivṛtāmāsamityevamādi atra pṛṣṭhyena ṣaḍahastomena trivṛdādi stomavikṛtena ekaiko māso vartteta evameke ācāryyā manyante liṅgāt yasmāt pārṣṭikāḥ stomāścodyante
10.10.16.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha pṛṣṭhyastomena trivṛdādistomavikṛtena krameṇa ekaikomāso varttate
10.10.17.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācāryya āha abhiplavapṛṣṭhyābhyāṃ trivṛdādistomavikṛtābhyām ekaikomāso vartteteti saṃvatsaraprakṛtitvāt
10.10.18.[1]	śāṇḍilyāyanadhānañjapyāvācāryyāvāhatuḥ pṛṣṭhyāhnaikaikena trivṛdādiḥ ekaiko māsaḥ vartteteti yasmāt tena liṅgena tasya tasya hi stomacodanā
10.10.19.[1]	lāmakāyana ācāryya āha jyotiṣṭomena trivṛdādistomavikṛtena ekaikomāso vartteta yasmāt sarveṣāmahnāmasau prakṛtiḥ ayantu viśeṣaḥ tasya rathantarapṛṣṭhaṃ bṛhacca pṛṣṭhānugrahārthaṃ tatprakṛtīni hi sarvāṇi
10.10.20.[1]	kṣairakalambhiḥ ācāryya āha yathaivārṣeyakalpenoktamayanaṃ tathaiva syāditi paraṃ naḥ pramāṇaṃ maśaka iti evamete sarve kalpāḥ pramāṇam
10.11.1.[1]	vicāritaṃ dṛtivātavatorayanaṃ sāmprataṃ kauṇḍapāyinaṃ vicāryyate tatra paṭhati māsaṃ dīkṣitā bhavanti māsaṃ soma krīṇanti teṣāṃ dvādaśopasada upasadbhiścaritvā somamupanahya māsamagnihotraṃ juhvati māsaṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajante māsaṃ vaiśvadevena māsaṃ varuṇapraghāsairmāsaṃ śākamedhairmāsaṃ śunāśīryeṇa trivṛtā māsaṃ pañcadaśena māsaṃ saptadaśena māsamekaviṃśena māsantriṇavena māsamaṣṭādaśatrayastriṃśānyahāni dvādaśānyahāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvratañcātirātrañceti tatra upasadbhiścaritvā somamupanahya vidhāya prāyaṇīyamatirātrāgnihotrādīn haviryyajñānupadiśati trivṛnmāsādīṃścānyān māsān tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ satranyāyena prāyaṇīyo'tirātreṣu athāśravaṇān mābhūditi etasmin saṃśaye ācāryyaiḥ svaṃ svaṃ mataṃ parigṛhyāyamartho vicāryyate paurṇamāsīprabhṛtayo dīkṣāḥ kauṇḍapāyinasyeti paurṇamāsārambhāḥ paurṇamāsīprabhṛtayaḥ dīkṣāḥ prabhṛtiśabdaḥ ādyarthaḥ kauṇḍapāyinasyeti sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī
10.11.2.[1]	kauṇḍapāyinasya upasadanta upavasathakarma kṛtvātirātramupeyuriti śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yasmādevaṃ vṛttirgṛhyate sarvasatrāṇam
10.11.3.[1]	tatastasmādatirātrādūrddhvaṃ prātarāhutyupakramāḥ prātarāhutyārambhaṇāḥ sāyamāhutisaṃsthāḥ sāyamāhutyapavargāḥ ekānnatriṃśatamahānyagnihotraṃ juhuyuḥ evaṃ śāṇḍilyo manyate
10.11.4.[1]	gautama ācārya āha māsamevāgnihotraṃ juhuyuḥ māso hi śrutaḥ tasya kutaḥ khaṇḍanamṛte vacanāt kintu sutyānāntu purastādagnihotrādīn śunāsīryyāntān haviryajñān upariṣṭātkrameṇa samāpya tataḥ sutyānāntu purastādupavasathakarma syādatirātraścaivañca gṛhyate vṛttiḥ sarvakarmasu sutyānāṃ purastādupavasathakarma bhavati kiñcānyat avyavāyaśca haviryajñairevaṃ kriyamāṇe sutyānāṃ bhavati
10.11.5.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryya āha aśravaṇādatirātro na syāditi yadi atirātro dṛṣṭo'bhaviṣyat aśrauṣat yena punasteṣu satreṣu pratimatrañcodayan yāvadanta iti neha vidadhāti tasmādakalpo na śrutamatirātraṃ kalpayitum
10.11.6.[1]	upasadanta eva upavasthakarma bhavet na sutyānantaram
10.11.7.[1]	athavā'nekadīkṣāṇāmanantaraṃ somakrayo na syāt śaunāsīryyānyahānyaṣṭādaśa kṛtvā tataḥ somaṃ rājānaṃ krīṇīyuḥ evaṃ tat rājakrayādi karma anantaraṃ sutyābhyo bhavatīti
10.11.8.[1]	śāṇḍilyāyana ācāryya āha dīkṣopasadāṃ vyavāyaḥ anyāya iti kiñcānyat te māsi somaṃ krīṇantīti caitat brāhmaṇamanantaraṃ dīkṣābhyaḥ krayaṃ darśayati
10.11.9.[1]	upavasathakarmaivānantaraṃ sutyābhyaḥ syādatirātro na syāt
10.11.10.[1]	darśe pitṛyajñā bhavanti teṣāṃ vidhirucyate āgnīdhrīyādaṅgārān mārjālīyaṃ hrtvā pṛthaṅnānā sthālīpākāñchrapayitvā pitṛyajñān kurvīran
10.11.11.[1]	tatastasmānmārjālīyāt dakṣiṇe pradeśe atipraṇayeyuḥ paitṛyajñikāyāṃ pitṛmedheṣu
10.11.12.[1]	kṛta upavasathānantaraṃ āhavanīyapraṇayanaṃ bhavati varuṇapraghāseṣu yo dvitīyo'gniḥ praṇīyate dakṣiṇatastamāhavanīyasya dakṣiṇe pradeśe praṇayeyuḥ tasmin kuryyuryyat karma dakṣiṇāhavanīye kṛtyaṃ tadupavasathakarmapūrvakaṃ syāt
10.11.13.[1]	atha punarupavasathakarma naiva kṛtaṃ syāt tathā satyanantaraṃ prakṛtaṃ tata iha āgnīdhrīyādaṅgārādityetadādi yathā prakṛtyeva syāt
10.11.14.[1]	agnihotramāse prakṛtānāṃ satriṇāṃ agnihotrācchiṣṭena vṛttirna kalpate tadeva darśayati teṣāmannaṃ kriyata iti dīkṣitārthamannaṃ tasya dīkṣitānnasyādhvaryurjuhuyāt uktannāhutasyāśnīyuriti itare'dhvaryyumanvārabheran juhvānam
10.11.15.[1]	iṣṭyayaneṣu havīṃṣvevopāvadyeyuḥ nātra dīkṣitānnamagnihotramāsavat syāt tatkimidamārabhyate yathā uktamevāgnihotramāse dīkṣitānnasyeti tat kathamiṣṭyayaneṣu na syāt ucyate anyārthamevaitadityādiśyate havīṃṣyeveṣṭyayaneṣūpāvadyeyuriti haviṣāmāvṛttiparimāṇamuktam iha tu tathā upāvadyeyuḥ yathā iṣṭīnāṃ haviḥśeṣeṇa yajamānavṛttiḥ syāt
10.12.1.[1]	somamupanahya māsamagnihotraṃ juhvati ityuktaṃ tasmin karmaṇi yat prāptaṃ karma tatra kiñcidvacanena nivartyate agnihotraṃ tāvadupasthānamiṣṭiṣu viṣṇukramāḥ samiṣṭayajūṃṣi avabhṛthanyaṅgaśceti etāni na kriyeran ityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryyo manyate eteṣāṃ prāptapratiṣedhaḥ
10.12.2.[1]	samidhastvādadhyuryyā asminnavabhṛthanyaṅgeṣu purastāduktāḥ avabhṛthanyaṅgaṃ prāpyābhyukṣaṇaprabhṛti sautyaṃ karma samāpayeyurityetasmin prakaraṇe tatra hi samidādhānāntaṃ bhavati
10.12.3.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryya āha agnihotropasthānādi sarvaṃ kriyeteti
10.12.4.[1]	māsandarśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajerannityuktaṃ tatrāmāvāsyena haviṣā pūrvapakṣaṃ yajeran itaramaparapakṣaṃ paurṇamāsena yajeran
10.12.5.[1]	āmāvāsye karmaṇi pitṛyajñaḥ sakṛdbhūtvā prathame itareṣu na syādityevaṃ gautama ācāryyo manyate sati daśāṅgatve kāle'pi na syāt pitṛyajñaḥ amāvasyāyām
10.12.6.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha asakṛdapi na syāt pitṛyajñaḥ nāṅgametaddarśasyeti
10.12.7.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha yāvatkṛtva amāvasyā tāvatkṛtvaḥ pitṛyajñaḥ syāt darśāṅgaṃ hi sa iti
10.12.8.[1]	māsaṃ sākamedhairyyajeranniti brāhmaṇaṃ tatra gṛhamedhīyeneṣṭvā pūrvedyuḥ karma saṃsthāpayeyuḥ evaṃ kriyamāṇena sākamedhīyaṃ karma triṃśatkṛtva upetaṃ bhavatīti
10.12.9.[1]	tuśabdo hetvarthaḥ eṣāṃ śākamedhānāṃ prakṛte dvyahenāpavargo dṛṣṭaḥ ihāpi dvyahāpavargatāmeva kalpayitvā pañcadaśakṛtvo'bhyasyeyuḥ samāso bhavati evaṃ māsaśabdasyārthavattvaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati
10.12.10.[1]	agnihotraṃ daśahotā darśapūrṇamāsaṃ caturhotā cāturmāsyāni pañcahotā saumyādhvare sadā hoteti brāhmaṇaṃ tatra agnihotraṃ daśahoteti daśahotāraṃ nāmādhvaryyavaḥ agnihotrasyopasthānamadhīyate tadabhipretyaitadbrāhmaṇam
10.12.11.[1]	uttarairvacanairyaduktaṃ tatra ṛtvijo'bhipretāḥ darśapaurṇamāsayoścatvāro hotāraḥ cāturmāsye tu pañca
10.12.12.[1]	adhvare some vaṣaṭkāriṇaḥ saptatāmanabhipretyaitadbrāhmaṇaṃ saumyo'dhvaraḥ saptahoteti
10.12.13.[1]	te sarve kuṇḍapāyino'tsarukaiścamasairbhakṣayantīti atsarukairadaṇḍacamasaiḥ kuṇḍapratirūpaiḥ kuṇḍasadṛśairbhakṣayeyuḥ
10.12.14.[1]	yo hotā so'dhvaryuḥ sapotetyetadādi samāsaḥ saṅkṣepa ekībhāvaḥ
10.12.15.[1]	svasmādāsanādupasañcāre'pi sañcāryya itare hotre maitrāvaruṇīyapratikartre kuryāt etat jñāpitaṃ bhavati brahmatvenāsau dīkṣitaḥ itare hotre karoti
10.12.16.[1]	tathā udgātā ca svasmādāsanādupasañcāramitare hotre neṣṭrīyācchāvākīye kuryyāt tathā prastotā itare hotre grāvastut brāhmaṇāchaṃsīye svasmādāsanādupasañcāraṃ kuryyāt tathāgnidhrīyeṇāsau dīkṣitaḥ itare unnetre pratiprasthātre kuryyāt
10.12.17.[1]	gṛhapatirgṛhapatiḥ subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇya ityanayā vīpsayā brāhmaṇamasamāsantayordarśayati vijñāpayati
10.13.1.[1]	uktaṃ kauṇḍapāyināmayanam anantaraṃ tāpaścitasya brāhmaṇaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ dīkṣitā bhavanti saṃvatsaramupasadbhiścaranti saṃvatsaraṃ prasṛtā bhavatīti tasya dīkṣākāla ucyate etenoktastāpaścitasya dīkṣādiriti etena kauṇḍapāyinena uktovyākhyātastāpaścitasya dīkṣādiḥ paurṇamāsīprabhṛtayo dīkṣā iti
10.13.2.[1]	vakṣyanta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ayanasya vikalpitaṃ maśakena gavāmayanena klṛptaṃ tāpaścitāmayanaṃ jyotiṣṭomena vā viklṛpteneti tasya vikalpa ucyate
10.13.3.[1]	jyotiṣṭomo'tirātraḥ ṣoḍaśimānahanyahani syāt saṃvatsaramiti śeṣaḥ
10.13.4.[1]	catvāro jyotiṣṭomāḥ jyotiṣṭomaścaturabhyastaḥ abhijideṣa pañcāhaḥ ṣaṭsu māseṣvabhyasyeta mahāvrataṃ viṣuvān syāt athaita eva māsā āvṛttāḥ syuḥ ayantu viśeṣaḥ viśvajittvabhijitaḥ sthāne syāt tatpuruṣasya nārāyaṇasyāyanam
10.13.5.[1]	tenābhijidvikalpena rathantarapṛṣṭhamiti niyamārtham
10.13.6.[1]	bṛhatpṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaramaharahaḥ syāttadindrasyāyanam
10.13.7.[1]	vyatyāsaṃ jyotiṣṭome saṃvatsaraṃ bṛhadrathantare pṛṣṭhe syātāṃ tadindrāgnyorayanam
10.13.8.[1]	ubhayasāmā jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ syāt tadbrahmaprājāpatyorayanaṃ syāt
10.13.9.[1]	vairūpapṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt mahāvrataṃ vā saṃvatsaramaharahaḥ syāt tadvāyorayanam
10.13.10.[1]	vairājaṣpṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt viśvajidvā tadādityasyāyanam
10.13.11.[1]	śarkvarīpṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ svāt tadapāmayanam
10.13.12.[1]	revatīpṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt tadgavāmayanaṃ syāt
10.13.13.[1]	vāmadevyaṣpṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt tatprajāpaterayanam
10.13.14.[1]	svarapṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt etadviśveṣāṃ devānāmayanam
10.13.15.[1]	divākīrttyapṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt tatsūryyasyāyanam
10.13.16.[1]	mahāvratapṛṣṭho jyotiṣṭomaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ syāt etanmahendrāyanam ete vicārāstāpaścitasya
10.13.17.[1]	tasya tāpaścitasya yāni trīṇyuttarāṇi dvādaśasaṃvatsaraṃ ṣaṭtriṃśatsaṃvatsaraṃ śatasaṃvatsaramiti etāni jyotiṣṭomena abhyastāni bhavanti tasya jyotiṣṭomasya rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bṛhacca vyatyāsaṃ vyatyasya vyatyasya vyātyāsam
10.13.18.[1]	kṣairakalambhirācāryya āha eteṣāmayanavidhānaṃ yathaivārṣeyakalpenoktaṃ tathaiva syāditi iti vātavatorayane tat klṛptaṃ prajāpaterdvādaśasaṃvatsaraṃ ṣaṭtriṃśatsaṃvatsaraṃ śatasaṃvatsaramiti
10.14.1.[1]	iha jyotiṣṭomena trīṇyuttarāṇīti prakṛtaṃ teṣu sarveṣu saṃvatsaracodanā na ca prāyaṇīyodayanīyāvādiṣṭau nāpi viṣuvān tatrāyaṃ śaṃsayaḥ kiṃ saṃvatsaranyāyaṃ gṛhītvā prāyaṇīyodayanīyātirātravanto bhavanti athāgrahaṇānna bhavantīti etasmin saṃśaye'yamācāryya ārabhate agniṣṭomāstrivṛta ityetadādi sūtraṃ maśaka eteṣu ye trivṛdādistomāḥ saṃvatsarān agniṣṭomasaṃsthān kalpayati yān pañcadaśān tānukthyasaṃsthān so'yamācāryya etadarthaṃ gṛhītvā tu parīkṣitumārabhate agniṣṭomāstrivṛta ukthyāḥ para ityetasmin kalpe avacanādatirātrā na syuḥ viṣuvantaśceti evaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha
10.14.2.[1]	dhānañjapya ācārya āha itaroyo vakṣyate satranyāyaḥ sa bhaveta iha kaḥ punarityucyate
10.14.3.[1]	prāyaṇīyodayanīyāvatirātrau syātām ādyantayoḥ satrasya syātāṃ madhye viṣuvān syāt bṛhatpṛṣṭho rathantaramadhyandinaḥ pañcadaśasaptadaśau stomau stotreṣu vyatyāsena syātām ekatrika iva
10.14.4.[1]	trivṛdādivargeṣu ādyantayoḥ prāyaṇīyodayanīyāvatirātrau madhye viṣuvān
10.14.5.[1]	vargāṇamuttame vā saṃvatsare etat syāt uttamasyottamasya saṃvatsarasyādyantayoḥ prāyaṇīyodayanīyāvatirātrau madhye viṣuvān
10.14.6.[1]	pṛthaksaṃvatsareṣu ekekasmin saṃvatsara ādyantayoḥ prāyaṇīyodayanīyāvatirātrau madhye viṣuvān
10.14.7.[1]	teṣāṃ saṃvatsarāṇāṃ yathāstomaṃ viṣuvantaḥ syuḥ yo'yaṃ sastomaḥ saṃvatsarastasmin sastome viṣuvān syāt
10.14.8.[1]	trivṛtāṃ saṃvatsarāṇāṃ rathantarapṛṣṭho bṛhadbrahmasāmā viṣuvān syāt bṛhatpṛṣṭho rathantaramadhyandinaḥ pareṣu pañcadaśādiṣu saṃvatsareṣu viṣuvān syāt
10.14.9.[1]	yajanīye'hani pratipadi prasavo bhavet prathamaḥ plavaḥ prasavaḥ yadyaviṣuvatkāḥ syuḥ tataḥ pūrvapakṣe syāt samārddhamāsātivarttinaśca yadi bhaveyuḥ
10.14.10.[1]	yadi viṣamārddhamāsātivarttinaḥ aviṣuvatkāśca tato aparapakṣe prasavaḥ syāt
10.14.11.[1]	sahasrasāvye paṭhati atirātraḥ sahasramahānītyatirātra iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ sahātirātrābhyāṃ sahasramahāni syuḥ uta vinātirātrābhyāmiti kutaḥ saṃśaya utpanna iti cet pratyakṣāyāṃ śrutau atirātraḥ sahasramahānītyatirātra iti ucyate samākhyātaḥ sahasrasāvya iti sahasramasmin sāvyā sahasrasāvyam ata ācārya prārabhate sahasrasāvye satre sahātirātrābhyāṃ sahasramahāni syuriti yasmādāha sahasrasāvyamiti
10.14.12.[1]	śaucivṛkṣirācāryya āha antareṇātirātrau anyāni sahasramahāni syuriti yasmādantareṇatirātrāvāha sahasramahānīni atirātraḥ sahasramahānyatirātra iti atha yaduktaṃ samākhyātaḥ saṃśaya utpanna iti na hi pratyakṣāyāṃ śrutau samākhyā grāhyā prathamaṃ hi viniyogakāraṇaṃ śrutiḥ durbalā samākhyā
10.14.13.[1]	tasya sahasrasāvyasyāyana ucyate atirātrau tāvatpratyakṣaśiṣṭau anyadatra sahasramayanaṃ yaccoditaṃ tat maśakena vikalpitaṃ jyotiṣṭomenāviklṛptena klṛptam agneḥ sahasrasāvyaṃ gaurīvitasya svareṇa vā tatrāyaṃ vikalpa ucyate pratirātrau tāvat pratyakṣaśiṣṭau anyattrikadrukāścatuḥṣaṣṭhaṃ śatamabhiplavānāṃ daśarātro vratamiti etadahaḥ sahasraṃ trikadrukā jyotirgaurāyuriti catuḥṣaṣṭhyadhikaṃ śataṃ abhiplavānāṃ daśarātrovratamiti
10.15.1.[1]	sahasrasāvyamuktam anantaraṃ sārasvatānyucyante tatra brāhmaṇaṃ sarasvatyā vinaśane dīkṣeta iti yasmin deśe sarasvatyantarbhavati tadvinaśanamityucyate tasya vinaśanasya dakṣiṇe kūle tīre sārasvatāya tādarthye caturthī ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tithau pakṣasya paribhāṣitam udagayanapūrvapakṣapuṇyāhamiti gautama ācāryya āha
10.15.2.[1]	uktaṃ yadaharatirātro bhavati tadaharvatsānapākurvanti saṃsthite'tirātre sānāyyena yajanta iti tadvatsāpākaraṇena sānnāyyayogena ca atirātrasyaiva kālo jñāpyate vatsāpākaraṇaṃ hi amāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati tadanantare'hani sānnāyyena yāgaḥ so'yaṃ gautama ācāryya āha amāvāsyāyāmatirātraḥ syādevaṃ svasthānamāmāvāsyaṃ prayujyata iti āmāvāsyasya hi pūrvapakṣādisthānam uktañca saṃsthite'tirātre sānnāyyena yajanta iti tadyadyamāvāsyāyāmatirātro bhavati tatastasya svasthānaṃ pūrvapakṣādau bhavati / 2 /
10.15.2.[2]	saptamyāṃ vā dīkṣitvāmāvāsyāyā yajanīye 'hany atirātraḥ syād iti dhānañjapyaḥ / 10.15.3 /
10.15.2.[3]	<10.15.3 dhānañjapya ācāryya evamāha
10.15.4.[1]	vakṣyati hi teṣāṃ paurṇamāsyāṅgoṣṭomastomo bhavatīti yajanīye'hani syādityācāryyā iti tathaivāyuḥ pradekṣyate evantāvat āyuṣo yajanīye'hani kriyopadekṣyate tadyadyatirātro'pi yajanīye'hani kriyate tataḥ goāyurbhyāṃ samādhiḥ kṛto bhavati etadarthaṃ atirātro'pi yajanīya evāhani syāt iti kiñcānyat
10.15.5.[1]	yaduktamamāvāsyāyāmatirātra kriyamāṇe pūrvapakṣādau svasthānamāmāvāsyaṃ prayujyate itarathā hi kriyamāṇe na svasthānamāmāvāsyaṃ prayujyate kiṃ kāraṇam
10.15.6.[1]	kṛtsno hi pūrvapakṣa āmāvāsyasthānaṃ tadā darśitaṃ granthāntare
10.15.7.[1]	prāgrātrerārambhāt sāyandohaṃ dohayeran saṃsthite samāpte'tirātre prātardohaṃ dohayeran uktaṃ saṃsthite'tirātre sānnāyyena yajanta iti
10.15.8.[1]	uktaṃ sānnāyyeneṣṭvā'dhvaryuḥ śamyāṃ parāsyatīti tacchamyāprāśanaṃ kutra bhavatītyāha āhavanīyasamīpe tiṣṭhanniti kriyāpadeśaḥ na āsīnaḥ tiṣṭhan prāṅmukhaḥ nityamahanyahani iṣṭisaṃsthāsu iṣṭisamāptiṣu prāsyet prakṣipet śamyāṃ taduktaṃ brāhmaṇena sā yatra nipatati tadgārhapatyastataḥ ṣaṭtriṃśataṃ prakramān prakrāmati tadāhavanīyamiti nityagrahaṇam amāvāsyānantaraṃ prāśanaṃ prakṛtaṃ tatsarvamakṛtam iṣṭisaṃsthāsu ca tat syāditi nityagrahaṇam
10.15.9.[1]	patnīśālāpi tathaiva cakrīvati svāt patnīśālā prāgvaṃśā śāmitramapi cakrīvadeva syāt śāmitramuktalakṣaṇam
10.15.10.[1]	tāni sadaādīni yathādeśaṃ vartteran yo yasya deśo yathādeśaṃ svasvadeśena gaccheyuryadi samobhūmibhāgaḥ syāt
10.15.11.[1]	yadi viṣamo bhūmibhāgaḥ syāt ānupūryeṇa vartteran ānupūrvyamadhvaryyave siddhaṃ yathā vyavāyanam
10.15.12.[1]	vedyādīnānnayanamaśakyaṃ tatra teṣāmavayavā nīyante vederityapādānalakṣaṇā pañcamī tasyāḥ pāṃśūn grahītvā nayeyuḥ yathā vedestathottaravedeḥ pāṃśūn hareyuḥ dhiṣṇyebhyaśca pāṃśūn hareyuḥ
10.15.13.[1]	tān pāṃśūn niviśya upaviśya yathāyatanaṃ yadyasyāyatanaṃ tasminnivapeyuḥ
10.15.14.[1]	ulūkhalabudhnoyūpa iti brāhmaṇaṃ tatkathamulūkhalabudhna ityucyate pṛthubudhnaḥ syāt pṛthu vistāre vistīrṇabudhaḥ syāt
10.15.15.[1]	yapaḥ prakṛṣya iti brāhmaṇaṃ yūpasthānaṃ sarveṣāṃ pūrvaṃ karṣeyuḥ anudyachantaḥ anutkṣipantaḥ evaśabdaḥ kriyate karṣeyureva nainamutkṣipeyuḥ yathā granthāntare dṛṣṭaḥ prakṛṣya ityavasthāne prakṛṣyata ākṛtiko hyatyanta iti ākṛtiko bhavatu mā vābhūt prakṛṣṭavya eva prakṛṣya iti brāhmaṇam
10.15.16.[1]	upopta eveti brāhmaṇaṃ na nikhātastiṣṭhet upopta eveti pāṃśubhiḥ paryyuptaḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ
10.15.17.[1]	noparavān khanantīti brāhmaṇaṃ te uparavāḥ kasmin deśe iti ucyate somasyādhiṣavaṇārthau yau phalakau tayoradhastādbhūmau uparavānāmaśvabhrā vidyante śvabhraḥ khātaḥ teṣāmatra pratiṣedhaḥ ālekhanamātramevaiṣāṃ kuryuḥ na khaneyuḥ ālikheyurenānityevameva vaktavye evaśabdaḥ kimarthaṃ kriyate na khaneyuriti ucyate anyatrāpi yatrārthataḥ khāto na syāt tatra lekhanamātrameva syāt yathā sādyaḥkreṣu vaiśvadeve cātvālapāṃśubhiḥ prayojanaṃ nāsti tatrāpyālekhanamātraṃ syāditi
10.16.1.[1]	uktaṃ te tamāpūryamāṇamāmāvāsyena yanti teṣāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ goṣṭomaḥ stomo bhavatyuktho bṛhatsāmā saṃsthite goṣṭome paurṇamāsaṃ nirvapanta iti goṣṭomasaṃsthānantaraṃ paurṇamāsasya kriyāmādiśati paurṇamāsasya cāparapakṣādiḥ sthānaṃ tatkiṃ paurṇamāsakālavaśena yajanīye'hani goṣṭomo'stu atha pratyakṣatvāt paurṇamāsyāṃ goṣṭomaṃ kṛtvā tatkālānantaraṃ paurṇamāsaṃ nirūpyatāmiti ato'rthamācāryyaḥ parīkṣitumārabhate teṣāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ goṣṭomaḥ stomo bhavatīti sa goṣṭomo yajanīye'hani syāt ityevamācāryyā manyante kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt saṃsthānantaraṃ paurṇamāmasya kriyāṃ vidhatte yastvayaṃ paurṇamāsīśabdasteṣāṃ paurṇamāsyāmiti ayaṃ paurṇamāsīsannikṛṣṭe kāle
10.16.2.[1]	kiñcānyat yadidante tamāpūryyamāṇamāmāvāsyena yanti tetamapakṣīyamāṇaṃ paurṇamāsena yantītyetadabhidhānaṃ kṛtvā pakṣāvadhikṛtya kālādhvanoratyantasaṃyoge dvitīyeti yadi hyayaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ goṣṭomaṃ kuryyādamāvāsyāyāñcāyuṣṭomam āmāvāsyāpaurṇamāsābhyāṃ kṛtsnayoḥ pakṣayorvyāptirna syāt
10.16.3.[1]	tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣanivṛttyarthaḥ yaduktaṃ yajanīye'hani syāditi tanna parvaṇyeva syāt evaśabdo'vadhāraṇārthaḥ teṣāṃ paurṇamāsyānteṣāmamāvāsyāyāmeveti yasmāt pratyakṣeṇa vidadhāti yadidaṃ yajanīye'hanītyācāryyāṇāṃ vacanaṃ kalpanāmātramidam ayantvādyaḥ pratyakṣaśeṣaḥ kalpanāmātreṇa śakyaṃ pratyakṣaṃ vacanaṃ bādhituṃ kalpanāvacanayorvacanasya balīyastvāt vacanaṃ hi śrutiḥ
10.16.4.[1]	saṃsthite goṣṭome paurṇamāsamiti yaduktannāntarānyatkarma pravarttata ityetaduktaṃ bhavati sve sve kāla eva goṣṭomaḥ sve sve kāla eva paurṇamāsaḥ syāt vakṣyatyetenāyurvyākhyāta iti tatrā'pyeṣa eva vidhiḥ syāt
10.16.5.[1]	atha yaduktante tamāpūryyamāṇante tamapakṣīyamāṇamiti ca kṛtsnavatpakṣābhidhānamiti ayaṃ yathā bhūyasovādaḥ gṛhyatām asambhavāt kṛtsnabhāvasya
10.16.6.[1]	parvaṇi goṣṭomaṃ kṛtvā tasminnevāhani paurṇamāsena haviṣeṣṭvā udyuñjīranniti udyogaṃ kuryyuriti tadahareva pratiṣṭheranniti evaṃ saṃsthānantaraṃ paurṇamāsaṃ prayuktaṃ bhavatīti
10.16.7.[1]	gautama ācāryya āha parvaṇi goṣṭomeneṣṭvā ayajamānāḥ paurṇamāsena tasminneva deśe tāṃ rātriṃ vaseyuriti
10.16.8.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha iṣṭvā paurṇamāsyāṃ goṣṭomena pratitiṣṭheranneva śvo bhūte tu paurṇamāsena yajeran evaṃ paurṇamāsaṃ sve sthāne kṛtaṃ bhavati
10.16.9.[1]	etena gavā āyurvyākhyātaḥ yajanīye'hani syāt parvaṇi syādityetadādinā
10.16.10.[1]	tatra tasmin karmaṇi dhānañjapyena vidhānenātirātre kriyamāṇe amāvāsyāyāṃ yajanīye'hanyatirātraḥ syāditi tatra tasminnamāvāsyāyāṃ sāyandohaṃ dohayeran pūrvamatirātrasya prātaranuvākāt prātardohaṃ tataḥ saṃsthite'tirātre sānnāyyena yajeran
10.16.11.[1]	śāṇḍilyāyana ācāryya āha evaṃ kriyamāṇe yadyamāvāsyāyāṃ sānnāyyaṃ kriyate dvitīyāyāñca yāgaḥ aticiraṃ sānnāyyaṃ dugdhamavatiṣṭhediti tasmāditarayoreva goāyuṣoryajanīye'hani parvaṇi cetyetayorvidhānayoranyatarat kuryyuriti atirātrastvamāvāsyāyāmeva syāditi
10.16.12.[1]	iṣṭyayaneṣu kauṇḍapāyine satre bhojanamuktaṃ haviṣyam iṣṭyayaneṣūpāpadyeyuriti darśapūrṇamāsadharmāśca kauṇḍapāyina evoktāḥ amāvāsyena pūrvapakṣamitaraṃ paurṇamāsenetyādayaḥ
10.16.13.[1]	pramāṇaṃ evaṃ parvasu kauṇḍapāyine hi triṃśino māsāvihitāḥ iha candrapramāṇā eveti
10.17.1.[1]	uktaṃ dṛṣadvatyā apyaye'ponaptrīyaṃ carunnirūpyāthātiyantīti taccaruṇā iṣṭiścodyate dṛṣadvatyā nadyā apyayaḥ sarasvatyāsaṅgama ekībhāvastasminnapyaye'ponaptrīyāmiṣṭiṃ nirvaperan aponaptā devatā asyā ityaponaptrīyā nirvapatyālabhate yajatayaḥ pradhānaśabdāstatra pravarttakāḥ nirvapatiśabdeneṣṭiścodyate yadi tasmin deśe sodakā syāddṛṣadvatī
10.17.2.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryya āha anudakāyāmapi nirvaperan śrutisāmarthyāt
10.17.3.[1]	śate goṣvityādi brāhmaṇaṃ śate goṣvṛṣabhaṃ miśrayanti tāsāṃ vayaḥ ucyate vatsatarī śate garbhiṇīṣu vatsabhāvāduttīrṇā vatsataryyaḥ ayametāsāṃ vatsatvaṃ bahugotvaṃ vatsokṣāśvarṣabhebhyaśca tanutva iti ṭarac prathamagarbhāsvāsvityetaduktaṃ bhavati
10.17.4.[1]	tā gāvo yasmin deśe gavyaṃ tṛṇodakamabhayaṃ syāt gobhyohitaṃ gavyam abhayaṃ yatra bhayaṃ na syāt vyāghracaurādibhya etasmin deśe etā rakṣeyuḥ gopāḥ
10.17.5.[1]	ye tāsāṅgavāṃ puṅgavā utpadyeraṃstairbhuñjīran satriṇaḥ yatkiñcidannādyam upārjayitavyaṃ syāt taiḥ puṅgavaistadarjayeran te tatra nimittabhūtāḥ, apare brūvate ye tatra puṅgavāsteṣāṃ mātṝrdugdhvā tena kṣīreṇa bhuñjīran dadhnāvā yāḥ striyastāsāṃ mātaro na dogdhavyāḥ evaṃ varddhamānā kṣipraṃ sahasraṃ sampadyate eṣa evamukhyārthaḥ, apare brūvate ālabhyāste puṅgavā iti taiśca puṅgavairbhuñjīran sarpiṣā ca
10.17.6.[1]	uktaṃ yadā sahasraṃ sampadyate'thotthānaṃ yadā sarvajyāniñjīyante athotthānaṃ yadā gṛhapatirmriyate athotthānaṃ yadā plakṣaṃ prāśravaṇamāgacchantyathotthānamiti etānyevotthānanimittānyuktāni tatredantāvat prathamamutthānaṃ tāsu goṣu sahasraṃ saṃkhyātaḥ sampannāsu māsasya yaḥ pūrvapakṣastasmin gāmatirātrasaṃsthānaṃ kṛtvā datvā enāgāḥ uttiṣṭheyuḥ yasmai deyāstadupariṣṭādvakṣyate
10.17.7.[1]	tadyadā sarvajyānimiti kiṃ satriṇo yathā sarvajyāniñjīyante athānya ityatrāha tāsāmevādhikāraḥ prakaraṇabhūtatvāt tasmin hi prakaraṇe tasminnutthāne viśvajidatirātraḥ syāt
10.17.8.[1]	mṛte gṛhapatau āyuḥ syāt atirātra iti prakṛtam
10.17.9.[1]	etayorāpadoḥ sarvajyānigṛhapatimaraṇayoḥ prādurbhāvasamakālamevottiṣṭheyuḥ na pūrvapakṣamādriyeran aparapakṣe'pyuttiṣṭheyuḥ
10.17.10.[1]	sakṛdapi sarasvatyāmavabhṛthannābhyaveyuḥ
10.17.11.[1]	avidyamāne'nyatrodake sarasvatyā evoddhāraṃ kuryyāt pārśvatastu tasyā eva na dūre
10.17.12.[1]	prasravaṇe bhavaṃ prāsravaṇaṃ yadi tāvaddare sthāt plakṣaḥ sannikṛṣṭaśca pūrvapakṣaḥ tadā tena krameṇa prāsyeryuryathā pūrvapakṣe āgaccheyuriti gautama ācāryya āha
10.17.13.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryya āha caturṇāmutthānānāṃ yadenāt satriṇaḥ kiñcidutthānamāgacchet prāyaṇīyamevātirātraṃ jyotiṣṭomaṃ kṛtvottiṣṭheyuḥ ādyantasamādhyarthaṃ naiva gavādīn kuryyāditi
10.17.14.[1]	uktaṃ plakṣaṃ prāsravaṇamāgacchantīti tat plakṣaṃ prāsravaṇamāgamyāgnaye kāmāyeṣṭiḥ purastādatirātrasya syādityevaṃ śāṇḍilya ācāryo manyate
10.17.15.[1]	dhānajapya ācāryya āha iṣṭiḥ upariṣṭādatirātrasya syāditi tato'pyāhāvabhṛtham
10.17.16.[1]	tasyāmaśvāñca puruṣīñca dhenuke datteti tasyāmiṣṭau aśvāñca puruṣīñca dhenuke yajñopakaraṇaśeṣabhūtāṃśca abhirūpāya vidyādiguṇayuktāyānyasmai brāhmaṇāya datvā uttiṣṭheyuḥ
10.17.17.[1]	kasmādanyasmai dadyuḥ yasmāt satreṣu sarve svāminasteṣāṃ pratigrahaṃ na vidyate vidhānaṃ kimarthamiti cet anyasmai dadyuriti ucyate anyā api yāḥ kāścidaṅgadakṣiṇā naimittinyaḥ karttṛsaṃyuktāḥ satreṣvāgaccheyuḥ tā apyanyasmā eva dadyuḥ
10.17.18.[1]	avabhṛtha ukto brāhmaṇena kārapacavaṃ prati yamunāvabhṛthamabhyavayantīti
10.17.19.[1]	etat satraṃ sārasvatam apṛṣṭaśamanīyam atha kasmādayamaprāptapratiṣedhaḥ kriyate yadā naiva kaścit pṛṣṭhasamanīyaḥ satreṣvabhihitaḥ athāpi iha pratiṣedhe'nyatra prāptiṃ darśayati śrutyantaradṛṣṭatvāt tasmādudavasānīyajyotiṣṭomena agniṣṭomena rathantarapṛṣṭhena sahasradakṣiṇena pṛṣṭhaśamanīyena ca yajeteti
10.18.1.[1]	etenaiva uttare sārasvate vyākhyāte tayoḥ pūrvasmin paṭhati atirātrastrivṛtpañcadaśamityādi paratra trirātro jyotirgorāyustryaha ityādi darśapaurṇamāsikānāṃ haviṣāmebhistrivṛtpañcadaśatrikadrukaiḥ pratyāhuranyatsarvametenaiva vyākhyātamuttarayoḥ dakṣiṇe tīre sarasvatyā vinaśanasya dīkṣeran sārasvatāyetyārabhya
10.18.2.[1]	taddevatyau
10.18.3.[1]	prathame agnaye kāmāyeṣṭiḥ purastādatirātrasya upariṣṭādvai vibhāṣitaṃ tatra śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha yadyupariṣṭādatirātrasya syādiṣṭirevāgnaye kāmāya syānna sruvahomāviti
10.18.4.[1]	uktaṅgoāyuṣī indrakukṣī viśvajidabhijitāvindrakukṣī iti tāvindrakukṣī parvaṇoḥ syātāṃ tayorhi pūrvasmiṃsthāne dṛṣṭau indrakukṣī iti saṃjñā indrakukṣī kāle tu vadati tata indrakukṣīti coktam
10.18.5.[1]	ye adhikṛte tayoḥ sāmānyo vidhiruktaḥ sāmprataṃ pūrvasmiṃstāvadviśeṣa ucyate uttarayoḥ sārasvatayoḥ pūrvasya trivṛtī ahanī rāthantarabārhate agniṣṭomasaṃsthe syātāṃ pūrvapakṣe ukthasaṃsthe pañcadaśe rāthantarabārhate aparapakṣe iti gautama ācāryya āha
10.18.6.[1]	te ahanī na pakṣayoḥ sañcārayet tayoḥ pakṣavyatyāsaṃprayoge
10.18.7.[1]	sarvatra tveva pūrvapakṣe aparapakṣe ca trivṛtpañcadaśe eva vyatyāsaṃ svātām
10.18.8.[1]	tayostrivṛtpañcadaśayoryasmin anupete asaṃskṛte parvāgacchet cāndramasameva tenottaraṃ pakṣamārabheta uktaṃ hi candrapramāṇādeva parvasu syuriti
10.18.9.[1]	etenoktaṃ vidhānamuttarasya sārasvatasya trikadrukeṣu yasmin na saṃskṛte parvāgacchet tenottaraṃ pakṣamupakrameteti
10.18.10.[1]	anantaraṃ dārṣadvratataure paṭhati tayoḥ sāmānyato vidhānamucyate dārṣadvratañca taurañca tayorvratāni vakṣyanta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ vratāni niyamāḥ
10.18.11.[1]	tiṣṭheddivāsīta naktaṃ na saṃviśet ṣṭhāgatinivṛttau naktaṃ rātrāvāsīta upaviśeta nāpi saṃviśet havirucchiṣṭabhojī syāt adhaḥsaṃveśī adhaḥsaṃviśet na kṣamāyāṃ bhūmāvityarthaḥ amāṃsāśyalavaṇāśī na māṃsamaśnīyāt na lavaṇamiti kutaḥ punaḥ saṃśaya ucyate na punaḥ pravṛttiruparisaṃveśanasya māṃsalavaṇabhojanasya ca yenāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate yāvatā uktaṃ tiṣṭheddivāsīta naktaṃ havirucchiṣṭabhojī syāditi tadidamanarthakaṃ tasmāt na vaktavyam ucyamāne vā prayojanaṃ vaktavyam ucyate ārabdhavyameva uktaṃ hi saṃvatsaraṃ brāhmaṇasya gā rakṣet saṃvatsaraṃ vyarṇenaitandhave'gnimindhīta saṃvatsare parīṇahyagnīnādadhīteti tadgopālāgnīndhanayoretanna sambhavati gāḥ pālayataḥ sthānāsanaṃ sambhavati agnīndhane prāgagnyādhānāddhaviṣo'bhāvāddhavirucchiṣṭabhojitvaṃ na sambhavati etasmāt kāraṇādārabdhavyamidamanena niyamo yathā sambhavati striyannopeyāt maithunadharmeṇeti kuto vā pravṛttiḥ tatrāha vakṣyatyayaṃ yathā prakṛtyāhitāgnivṛttiṃ varttayediti tasyāṃ vṛttāvetat prakṛtamṛtāvupeyāditi tat pratiṣidhyate yathāprakṛti āhitāgneryyā prakṛtavṛttiḥ tāṃ varttayet agnihotradarśapūrṇamāsānāṃ karmaṇāmanuṣṭhānaṃ kuryyāt dārṣadvratataurayoḥ sāmānyāni vratānyuktāni sāmprataṃ dārṣadvratataurayoryovidhiḥ sa ucyate
10.18.12.[1]	dārṣadvrate paṭhati saṃvatsaraṃ brāhmaṇasya gā rakṣediti tadyoyasya brāhmaṇasya ṛtvik syāt ācāryyo vā tasya gā rakṣet na yasya kasyacidbrāhmaṇasya ṛtvigācāryyāvuktalakṣaṇau etau hi ṛtvigācāryyau sthānināvavicālinau
10.18.13.[1]	uktaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ vyarṇe naitandhave'gnimindhīteti naitandhavānā mārmāḥ sarasvatyāṃ mārmā hradāḥ teṣāmeko vyarṇaḥ arṇa ityudakanāma vigatodakaḥ tasmin vyarṇe hrade saṃvatsaramagnimindhīta ñiindhī dīptau kena nyāyena yā ekāgneḥ paricaryoktā
10.18.14.[1]	yadi purastādāhitāgniḥ syāt tatastasmin vyarṇe naitandhave mārme agnihotrameva juhvatsaṃvatsaramevāsīta tadeva syādagnīndhanam
10.19.1.[1]	uktaṃ saṃvatsare parīṇahyagnīnādadhīteti saṃvatsaramagnimindhitvā tasmādūrddhvaṃ parīṇhyagnīnādadhīta parīṇahīti deśaśrutiḥ parīṇaṃ nāma sthalī kurukṣetre bhūmerunnatapradeśaḥ tasyāṃ sthalyāmagnīnādhāya yathākālamanvārambhaṇīyo yaḥ kālaḥ tasminneva etayeṣṭvā prasṛjyeteti śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha
10.19.2.[1]	dhānañjapya ācāryya āha agnyādhānaṃ kṛtvā tasminneva deśe yathākālamanvārambhaṇīyayeṣṭvā darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajeteti
10.19.3.[1]	atha yadi purastādāhitāgniḥ sāyaṃ prātarāhutī eva hutvā prasṛjyeteti
10.19.4.[1]	brāhmaṇaṃ sadakṣiṇena tīreṇa dṛṣadvatyā āgneyenāṣṭākapālena śamyā parāsīyāditi tatsarasvatīdṛṣadvatyoḥ sambhedaṃ saṅgamaṃ prāpyāgneyena puroḍāśenāṣṭākapālena yaṣṭumupakrameta upakrama ārambhaḥ
10.19.5.[1]	tatra tasmin karmaṇi aṣṭākapālena yāgena śamyāprāsanaṃ śamyāprakṣepaḥ yena prakāreṇa sārasvateṣu āhavanīyanyantenetyādinā
10.19.6.[1]	na tviha prakramāt prakrāmet yathā sārasvateṣu tatra hi saumikañcaityāhavanīyam iha punaraiṣṭikaṃ tasmādiha prakramāt na prakrāmet
10.19.7.[1]	iha kāmamiṣṭitaḥ anekamiṣṭimekaikenāknā saṃsthāpayet kuryyāt viprakṛtya
10.19.8.[1]	dṛṣadvatyā dakṣiṇena kūlena iyādgacchet śamyāprāsaiḥ
10.19.9.[1]	uktaṃ triplakṣān prati yamunāmavabhṛthamabhyavaitīti tadeva manuṣyebhyastiro bhavatīti tasyā dṛṣadvatyāḥ prabhavyamarmaṃ prāpya yasmādasau prabhavati prāyāt taṃ prāpyaitayeṣṭvā āgneyenāṣṭākapālena triplakṣāvaharaṇaṃ deśaṃ prati yamunāmavabhṛthamabhyaveyāt triplakṣān pratīti brāhmaṇaṃ te plakṣā na jñāyante kasmin kāle avahṛtā iti āgamena tvavicchinnena pāramparyeṇādau vijñāyante tasmāt sūtrakāra evaṃ kalpayati
10.19.10.[1]	yadi tasmāddeśādyamunā dūre syāt tasmin kasmiṃściddeśe etayeṣṭyeṣṭvā svayaṃ sāma gāyannavabhthamabhyaveyādityarthādavagamyate svayamiti ucyate etaddhi avabhṛthasāma ṛtvikkartṛkaṃ tadanena liṅgenādriyetāpi ṛtviggānārtham evamādita ārabhya svayamiti athavā svayaṃ sāma gāyatīti asaṃpreṣito gāyet agāyanvā abhyaveyādavabhṛtham
10.19.11.[1]	idaṃ dārṣadvratamayanaṃ pravrajiṣyata evaṃ manya iti dhānajapyastadeva manuṣyebhyastiro bhavatīti eṣa tirobhāvastasya yannityamaraṇye vasanmanuṣyairdṛśyate
10.19.12.[1]	evamiva hi tadbrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
10.19.13.[1]	atha kriyāphalamidamucyate anena karmaṇā svargaṃ lokamākramate tato manuṣyebhyastirobhūto bhavati na manuṣyairupalabhyate
10.19.14.[1]	athavā vyāvarttata evāsau manuṣyebhyaḥ nāsau manuṣyaistulyo bhavati śreyān bhavati kiṃ punarmanuṣyebhyaḥ śreyaḥ brahmaprāptiḥ brahma prāpnotītyanena karmaṇā apavṛjyata ityarthaḥ ayamātyantikastirobhāvaḥ
10.19.15.[1]	athavā tirobhāva udakāntarddhānāt yadāsau avabhṛthamabhyavaityapsu nimajjati tadāsāvantarhito bhavati na dṛśyate tasmādudakāntarddhānāt tirobhavati yathā sarajasa iti dṛṣṭānta upādīyate yathā sarajaso'hani manuṣyalokādevainamantardadhātīti kuśapuṭairupayantīti
10.20.1.[1]	iha brāhmaṇamāgneyo'ṣṭākapāla aindra ekādaśakapālo vaiśvadevacarurityetadādyanukramyāha etena vai turo devamuniḥ sarvāmṛddhimārddhnot sarvāmṛddhimṛdhnoti ya etadupaitīti āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla ityādipradhānatvaṃ coditaṃ nāpyabhyāsaścodito nāpi kālaniyamaḥ kṛtaḥ so'yamācāryyo liṅgaṃ gṛhītvā etena vai turodevamuniḥ sa sarvāmṛddhimārdhnot sarvāmṛddhimṛdhnoti ya etadupaiti sāṃvatsarikaṃ satrāyaṇamupaitīti saṃvatsaramaharahastaureṇa yajeteti saṃvatsaramiti kālaniyamaḥ aharaharityabhyāsaścodyate taureṇeti karaṇalakṣaṇā tṛtīyā yajeteti kriyopadeśaḥ ayaṃ sūtrārthaḥ yadetadaiṣṭikaṃ vidhānaṃ vakṣyati anenāharahaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ yajeteti
10.20.2.[1]	ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tithau caitrīpakṣasya citrābhiryuktā paurṇamāsī caitrī yadetat karma vakṣyate etat ṣaṣṭyāṃ caitrīpakṣasyārabhya kuryyāt pañcamyāmiti gautama ācāryya āha pañcamyāṃ caitrīpakṣasya vratopāyanīyamodanamaśitvā odanaṃ bhuktvā vratamupaiti yena taṃ vratopāyanīyamodanamaupavasantikaṃ haviṣyamantraṃ bhuktvā keśān śmaśrūṇi ca vāpayitvā ahataṃ vasanaṃ paridhāya tāntukamanirṇiktamaprāvṛtapūrvaṃ tadvasanaṃ paridhāya parisamuhyāgnī paristīryya tretāgnīnāṃ paristaraṇamādhvaryyave siddhaṃ praṇītāḥ praṇīya praṇītāsaṃjñā mantrasaṃskṛtā āpaḥ mekhalāmābadhya mehanasya khalasya mālā mekhalā adharottarakāyavibhāgārthā raśanetyarthaḥ muñjādīnāṃ dravyāṇaṃ ekena nirvṛttā daṇḍaṃ pāṇau kṛtvā pālāśādīnāṃ yajñīyānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāmekasyāvayavabhūtaṃ gārhapatyasya paścime pradeśe upaviśya svayaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratiṣajeta tūṣṇīṃ kṛṣṇamṛgasya carma kṛṣṇājinaṃ tat svayaṃ skandhe pratiṣajeta adattamadhvaryuṇā etadādhvaryyavaṃ tadvacanāt svayaṃ bhavatīti adīkṣitaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratimuñceta iti tūṣṇīmiti mantreṇādhastādgrahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tasya pratiṣedhaḥ
10.20.3.[1]	kintu paścādgārhapatyasyopaviśyeti yaduktaṃ tasyāyaṃ vikalpaḥ
10.20.4.[1]	tasya tisra iṣṭayaḥ stomasaṃsthā vikṛtaṃ gavāmayanaṃ sarpasatraṃ syādityeke ācāryyā brūvate
10.20.5.[1]	aṣṭākapālaḥ ekādaśakapālaścaruḥ brāhmaṇoktametat sarvaṃ vakṣyamāṇaviśeṣavidhānārtham
10.20.6.[1]	kālatrayavihitahaviḥṣvekaiveṣṭiḥ na tisraḥ
10.20.7.[1]	svayaṃ gāyena vā gāyediti
10.20.8.[1]	prakṛtatvādubhayordārṣadvratataurayoravabhṛthottarakālamāgneyādibhiriṣṭvā somenāgniṣṭomena prayogaḥ
10.20.9.[1]	taddevatyaiḥ paśubhiḥ sāmarthyāt mantravarṇavikāraḥ
10.20.10.[1]	sarvo daśadaśīti stomo vikṛtaḥ agniṣṭomameva iti saṃsthāvikāraḥ śeṣaṃ samānaṃ gavāmayanena abhigarāpagarayoḥ kṛtatvāt
10.20.11.[1]	pratyakṣavihitametadārṣeyakalpena sarpasatraṃ tatra tasminnanumānaṃ na vidyate paraṃ naḥ pramāṇamārṣeyakalpe tena cedaṃ pratyakṣamuktasaṃśayaṃ vihitaṃ na ca śakyaṃ pratyakṣavihitamanumānena pratyākhyātuṃ vikalpayituṃ vā tadyathārṣeyakalpena kṛtaṃ tathaiva syāt kintu
10.20.12.[1]	abhigarāpagarāveva sarpasatrasyottame'hani bhavetāṃ taddhi vratasthānīyamupottamamahaḥ
10.20.13.[1]	paṭhati gavāmayanaṃ prathamaḥ saṃvatsaro'thādityānāmathāṅgirasāmiti tasya trisaṃvatsarasya paurṇamāsyāṃ prasavaḥ syāt tathopapādayeran yathā paurṇamāsyāṃ prasavo bhavati
10.20.14.[1]	yāvatya iṣṭayaḥ syustāvatīḥ kuryuriti
10.20.15.[1]	śāṇḍilya ācāryya āha ṣaṣṭi dīkṣāḥ syuriti
10.20.16.[1]	eke ācāryyā bruvate asmiṃstrisaṃvatsare prathamottamau saṃvatsarau vyatiharediti prathamottamayoḥ saṃvatsarayorvyatihāraḥ kathaṃ kuryyāditi gavāmayanam iti kimartham abhiplavastomapṛṣṭhyadeśarohaṇārtham evaṃ trivṛtstomā abhiplavāḥ prathame saṃvatsare bhavanti trivṛtpañcadaśastomā dvitīye cātuṣṭomyena tṛtīye abhiplavastomānāmeṣa rohaḥ pṛṣṭhyadeśasya ye pṛṣṭhyaḥ abhiplavānāṃ purastāt madhya upariṣṭādbhavati
10.20.17.[1]	yathaivāmnātāḥ saṃvatsarāstathaiva tānupeyuḥ ke hi pramāṇamāśritya pratyakṣaśrutiṃ pratyāmananti tasmādyathāmnāyamevopeyuḥ
10.20.18.[1]	uktaṃ trisaṃvatsaraṃ sahasrasaṃvatsare paṭhati ekaṃ prajāpateḥ anyadviśvasṛjāntayoḥ stotravidhirukto maśakena karmavidhiḥ sarvaḥ paribhāṣāsiddhaḥ kevalaṃ prasavakāla ucyate amāvāsyāprasave sahasrasaṃvatsare amāvāsyāyāṃ prasavo yayoste ime amāvāsyāprasave tadā dīkṣeran yathā amāvāsyāyāṃ prasavaḥ sampadyate ṣaṣṭhyāṃ pūrvapakṣasya dīkṣitānāṃ tṛtīyāyāmaparapakṣasya kramaḥ evamamāvāsyāyāṃ prasavaḥ sampadyate
